# NetPdf — Progress Status

**Current phase:** Phase 3 — Fragmentainer-aware layout + pagination 🚧 In progress (Task 17 cycle 5c.2d — recursive-site grid pagination wiring + production-pipeline coverage). **Cycle 5c.2d** wires the `EmitBlockSubtreeRecursive` grid dispatch site with the same clamp + F2 wrapper-resize + continuation-propagation pattern as the outer site (cycles 5c.2a–5c.2c). Production HTML fixtures (`<body><div class="grid">…</div></body>`) route grid containers through the recursive site, not the outer site; without this wiring, real documents never exercised the paginatable-grid path. **The mechanism**: (1) new local `bool paginateGridForChild = false` flag in `EmitBlockSubtreeRecursive` (mirrors the existing `paginateFlexForChild` at the same site); (2) new paginatable-grid extent clamp gated on `IsPaginatableGrid(child) && !_disableGridPagination && _capturedFragmentainer is not null && IsHeightAuto(child)` — shrinks `childBorderBoxBlockSize` to page-remaining + flips the gate; (3) wrapper cursor captured BEFORE the wrapper emit at line ~4112 (= `recursiveWrapperCursor = _sink.Cursor`); (4) at the IsGridContainer dispatch branch (line ~4357), incoming `GridContinuation` extracted from the recursion's `incomingBlockChain` via the same chain-consumption pattern as the multicol / flex branches; `DispatchGridInner` now passes `allowPagination: paginateGridForChild` + `incomingContinuation: incomingGridForChild` + captures `lastEmittedBlockExtent`; (5) F2 wrapper-resize fires when clamp activated OR incoming-continuation present — mutates wrapper BlockSize via `_sink.UpdateFragmentBlockSize` + recomputes cursor advance as `topShift + resizedWrapper + marginEnd`; (6) on `PageComplete(GridContinuation)`, wraps into `BlockContinuation(ResumeAtChild=childIdx, LayouterState=GridContinuation)` + returns up the recursion chain. The outer `AttemptLayout` then unpacks this nested chain to route the continuation back through the resume contract on the next page. **F1 NOT applied at recursive site**: the recursion doesn't propagate the attempt's strategy parameter, so F1's strategy-aware gate can't apply cleanly. Clamp + F2 + continuation propagation alone cover the recursive-site contract; F1's pre-empt is an optimization for the outer Strict-defer case. **Explicit-height grids stay atomic at the recursive site too**, per the `IsHeightAuto(child)` gate restored in cycle 5c.2c post-PR-#101 review P1#1 — waits for `grid-fragment-plan-shared-sizing-deferral`. **Tests**: 2 new production-pipeline tests in `GridLayouterProductionTests.cs` under `Cycle5c2d_*`: (a) `recursive_auto_height_grid_paginates_at_row_boundary` — 4-row auto-height grid inside `<body>` on a 350px page → page 1 emits rows 1–3 (= 300px), defers row 4 via a chained `BlockContinuation → GridContinuation(RowIndex=3)` walked via the new `FindGridContinuationLeaf` helper; (b) `recursive_explicit_height_grid_stays_atomic_pending_F3` — 200px explicit-height grid inside `<body>` on 150px page → no GridContinuation in result chain, both items emit atomically (= F3 regression test for the recursive site). Tests: **5122 unit** (+2 cycle-5c.2d production tests over 5120 baseline; +324 over 4798 cycle-0a baseline) + **97 RealDocs** + **30 LayoutSnapshots** + **4 AotJitParity** all green. AOT/JIT byte-parity preserved at sha256 `2942DD1E…30C3DE7`. Cycle 5c.3 picks up F3 (= explicit-height grid pagination via the deferred `grid-fragment-plan-shared-sizing-deferral` — shared immutable plan separating resolved geometry from fragment budget) + the orthogonal flex cycle 4f wrapper-resize consumer (= same `UpdateFragmentBlockSize` API now ships).

**Historical pointer — Task 17 cycle 5c.2c + post-PR-#101 review hardening** (superseded by cycle 5c.2d) — F3 REVERTED + 3 P1 findings closed + safety gates restored. **Cycle 5c.2c initial** attempted to resolve the `grid-explicit-height-paginate-deferral` by adding a subtree-extent clamp in `MeasureSubtreeVisualBlockExtent`'s outer consumer (= when `paginateGridForOuterChild`, cap subtree extent back to post-clamp `borderBoxBlockSize`) + removing the cycle-5c.2b-post-PR-#100-P1#3 `IsHeightAuto(child)` gate. **Post-PR-#101 review P1#1** correctly identified an architectural flaw: the subtree clamp + clamp-driven `borderBoxBlockSize` shrinkage fed the shrunk value into `GridSizing.Resolve` as `contentBlockSize`, causing fr / definite-height row sizing to redistribute against the smaller budget — e.g., `height: 400px; grid-template-rows: 100px 1fr` on a 250px page resolved rows as (100, 150) instead of the authored (100, 300), silently losing 150px of authored row geometry. **The fix REVERTS the F3 mechanism**: subtree-extent clamp removed; `IsHeightAuto(child)` safety gate restored on the outer-site clamp; `grid-explicit-height-paginate-deferral` remains `not-started`. F3 will ship when the `grid-fragment-plan-shared-sizing-deferral` (= shared immutable GridFragmentPlan separating resolved geometry from fragment budget) lands. **Post-PR-#101 review P1#2** (F2 authored-extent collapse) — resolved transitively by P1#1 revert: with `IsHeightAuto` gate restored, F2 doesn't fire for explicit-height grids → authored wrapper geometry preserved. **Post-PR-#101 review P1#3** (F1 must mirror dispatch's pagination decision) — added `paginateGridForOuterChild` to F1's gate condition so F1 can't synthesize a `GridContinuation` when the clamp didn't fire (= the dispatch would run atomically). Without this gate, F1 in a non-paginatable scenario could fabricate a continuation that the resume page's F2 (keyed off `incomingGridContinuation != null`) would mistakenly resize the wrapper against. **Post-PR-#101 review P2#1** (oversized-row test contract) — strengthened: the new `Cycle5c2c_post_PR_101_oversized_first_row_LastResort_emits_diagnostic_and_makes_progress` test asserts diagnostic code (`PaginationForcedOverflow001`), attempt outcome ≠ NeedsRewind, wrapper geometry preserved at authored 500, grid item emitted (= no row drop), no fabricated GridContinuation. **Tests** — replaced 3 F3-asserting tests with 5 safety-preserving tests under `Cycle5c2c_post_PR_101_*`: (a) `explicit_height_grid_atomic_until_GridFragmentPlan_ships` (= height 300, page 250 → wrapper preserves authored 300 via forced-overflow); (b) `explicit_height_grid_after_sibling_no_partial_clamp` (= sibling 150 + height 200 grid + page 300 → grid breaks to next page without partial-clamp + no GridContinuation); (c) `oversized_first_row_LastResort_emits_diagnostic_and_makes_progress` (= strengthened P2#1); (d) `explicit_height_with_fr_rows_preserves_authored_geometry` (= **P1#1 regression**: `height: 400` + `rows: 100px 1fr` on page 250 → items at row sizes 100 + 300, NOT 100 + 150); (e) `F1_does_not_fabricate_continuation_when_clamp_does_not_fire` (= **P1#3 regression**: explicit-height grid where clamp doesn't fire → F1 doesn't fabricate GridContinuation). Also updated `Cycle5c2a_F1_defers_paginatable_grid_when_first_row_exceeds_page_remaining` to use AUTO-HEIGHT grid (= the safety gate now requires this for F1/clamp activation). Tests: **5120 unit** (+2 net cycle-5c.2c post-PR-#101 over 5118 baseline; +322 over 4798 cycle-0a baseline) + **97 RealDocs** + **30 LayoutSnapshots** + **4 AotJitParity** all green. AOT/JIT byte-parity preserved at sha256 `2942DD1E…30C3DE7`. Cycle 5c.2d wires the recursive `EmitBlockSubtreeRecursive` site + nested-continuation propagation for cell / item / caption contexts + production-pipeline multi-page tests. The `grid-fragment-plan-shared-sizing-deferral` is the precondition for cycle 5c.3 (= F3 explicit-height re-attempt).

**Historical pointer — Task 17 cycle 5c.2c initial ship** (REVERTED per PR-#101 review P1#1): attempted F3 explicit-height grid pagination via subtree-extent clamp; conflated resolved geometry with fragment budget + silently corrupted fr row sizing. The cycle-5c.2b post-PR-#100 review P1#3 added an `IsHeightAuto(child)` gate to the outer-site clamp as a temporary safety guard pending F3; this cycle ships F3 + removes the gate, so explicit-height grids now flow through F1 (cycle 5c.2a) + F2 (cycle 5c.2b) pagination cleanly. **The mechanism**: new subtree-extent clamp at the outer-site break-check site (= where `effectiveBlockSize = Math.Max(borderBoxBlockSize, subtreeBlockExtent)` is computed). When `paginateGridForOuterChild` is true AND the recursive `MeasureSubtreeVisualBlockExtent` walk returned a value greater than the post-clamp `borderBoxBlockSize` (= happens for explicit-height grids because the recursive walk reads `parent.Style.ReadLengthPxOrZero(Height)` at line ~5893 → restores the authored 300px even after the clamp shrunk borderBoxBlockSize to 250), the subtree extent is CLAMPED back to the post-clamp wrapper extent. Mirrors the existing flex L3 + table cycle-1 subtree-extent clamps (= dominant-layouter-owned containers cap their recursive subtree contribution to the wrapper's already-shrunken `borderBoxBlockSize`). With F3, the break-check sees a fitting chunk → Continue → wrapper emit + dispatch with `allowPagination=true` → GridLayouter splits + F2 resizes the wrapper to the emitted-rows extent. **Tests**: 3 cycle 5c.2c tests under `Cycle5c2c_F3_*`: (a) `explicit_height_grid_paginates_on_fresh_page` — 300px explicit-height grid (3×100 rows) on 250px page → clamp shrinks to 250 + subtree clamp prevents 300 restore + emits rows 0+1 (= 200) → PageComplete with GridContinuation(RowIndex=2) + wrapper resized to 200; (b) `explicit_height_grid_after_sibling_paginates_correctly` — sibling 150 + 200px explicit-height grid + page 300 → clamp shrinks grid to 150 + emits row 0 → wrapper 100 + UsedBlockSize 250 + GridContinuation(RowIndex=1); (c) `explicit_height_grid_oversized_for_fresh_page_forced_overflow` — 500px row on 250px page (= oversized for any page) → falls through to forced-overflow with LayoutGridForcedOverflow001 diagnostic + wrapper at clamped extent (= LastResort progress contract preserved). The 2 prior cycle-5c.2b-P1#3 tests are replaced — they pinned the OLD "explicit-height grids never paginate" behavior; with F3 the assertions are inverted. Tests: **5118 unit** (+1 net cycle-5c.2c: +1 new test + 2 replaced over 5117 baseline; +320 over 4798 cycle-0a baseline) + **97 RealDocs** + **30 LayoutSnapshots** + **4 AotJitParity** all green. **Historical pointer — Task 17 cycle 5c.2b + post-PR-#100 review hardening** (superseded by cycle 5c.2c) — 4 findings closed: P1#1 + P1#2 + P1#3 + P2 deferral entry added. **Post-PR-#100 review P1#1** (nested-context grid pagination disabled): the cycle-5c.2b activation made the outer-site paginatable-grid path observable for ANY direct grid child of any `BlockLayouter`, including nested `BlockLayouter` instances created for table-cell content + grid-item content + table-caption content. Those nested callers (3 sites: `GridLayouter.DispatchGridItemContents` at line 1042; `TableLayouter` cell content at line 4986; `TableLayouter` caption content at line 3607) intentionally DISCARD the `AttemptLayout` result — a paginatable direct-child grid returning `PageComplete(GridContinuation)` would silently drop all rows past the split. Per CSS Fragmentation L3's "parallel flows" + table-cell / grid-item independent-fragmentation rules, this is non-conformant. Post-fix: new `disableGridPagination: bool = false` constructor parameter on `BlockLayouter`; the 3 nested callers explicitly pass `disableGridPagination: true`. When the flag is set, F1 pre-dispatch defer + the outer-site clamp + F2 wrapper-resize ALL no-op, leaving the cycle-1 atomic-dispatch contract intact for the nested context. Cycle 5c.2d will wire proper nested-continuation propagation. **Post-PR-#100 review P1#2** (F2 cursor uses topShift, not marginStart): the F2 cursor recomputation was `marginStart + resizedWrapperBlockSize + marginEnd`, but the standard block-flow cursor accounting is `topShift + borderBox + marginEnd` — `topShift` already encodes the ADDITIONAL distance after sibling margin collapse (per CSS 2.1 §8.3.1). For a preceding sibling with `margin-bottom: 80px` + grid with `margin-top: 10px`, the collapsed gap is 80 (= the 80 was already added by the prior block's emit, so `topShift = 0`); pre-fix F2 charged `10` again. Post-fix replaces `marginStart` with `topShift` so adjacent-sibling collapse is accounted for once. **Post-PR-#100 review P1#3** (explicit-height clamp gate): the cycle-5b clamp at the outer-site fired for ALL paginatable grids, but the F3 explicit-height deferral (`grid-explicit-height-paginate-deferral`) hasn't shipped yet — `MeasureSubtreeVisualBlockExtent` restores the authored `height: 300px` AFTER the clamp shrinks `borderBoxBlockSize`, causing forced-overflow at the corrupted (clamped) wrapper size. Post-fix: clamp gated by `IsHeightAuto(child)` so explicit-height grids preserve their authored geometry until cycle 5c.2c ships F3. **Post-PR-#100 review P2** (GridFragmentPlan dedup deferred): the multi-pass §11 sizing/placement is now explicitly tracked as a new `grid-fragment-plan-shared-sizing-deferral` entry in `docs/deferrals.md` rather than being claimed as fixed. The cache-hit path on resume avoids one Resolve (= cycle 5c.2a P1#2); pages without cache still triple-resolve. Triggers when a benchmark surfaces measurable regression vs cycle 5b atomic dispatch. **Tests** (6 new under `Cycle5c2b_P1_*`): (a) `nested_block_layouter_disables_grid_pagination` (= direct test of the `disableGridPagination` flag), (b) `table_cell_with_paginatable_grid_renders_all_rows` (= the P1#1 silent-content-loss regression — 4 rows in a 300 budget where pagination WOULD split, all 4 items emit + no GridContinuation in the result), (c) `F2_cursor_advance_honors_collapsed_margins` (= P1#2 regression with sibling `margin-bottom: 80` + grid `margin-top: 10` → `UsedBlockSize` = 280, not 290), (d) `F2_final_resume_fragment_with_margin_advances_correctly` (= resume page with grid `margin-top: 20` + emitted extent 200 → `UsedBlockSize` = 220), (e) `explicit_height_grid_not_clamped_until_F3_ships` (= P1#3 regression: 300px explicit-height grid on 250px page → wrapper at 300 via forced-overflow, NOT clamped to 250), (f) `explicit_height_grid_after_sibling_no_partial_clamp` (= sibling 150 + 200px explicit-height grid + page 300 → grid not partially clamped + breaks normally to next page). Tests: **5117 unit** (+13 cycle-5c.2b: 7 base + 6 review hardening over 5104 cycle-5c.2a baseline; +319 over 4798 cycle-0a baseline) + **97 RealDocs** + **30 LayoutSnapshots** + **4 AotJitParity** all green. AOT/JIT byte-parity preserved at sha256 `2942DD1E…30C3DE7` (= the `disableGridPagination` rollout makes nested-context pagination effectively a no-op, so production HTML fixtures stay byte-identical). Cycle 5c.2c picks up F3 (explicit-height grid handling); cycle 5c.2d wires the recursive site + nested-continuation propagation for cell / item / caption contexts + production-pipeline multi-page tests.

**Historical pointer — Task 17 cycle 5c.2b (initial ship)** (superseded by post-PR-#100 review hardening): F2 wrapper-resize consumer + cycle-5b outer-site clamp + gate-flip REACTIVATED. **Cycle 5c.2b** ships the consumer side of the `grid-fragment-extent-emitted-rows-only-deferral` (= PR-#97 review F2 architectural item) + reactivates the cycle-5b outer-site extent clamp + gate-flip that PR-#97 reverted. With cycle 5c.2a's F1 (pre-dispatch row-fit) + cycle 5c.2b's F2 (wrapper-resize) both in place, the outer-site clamp activation is safe: Strict-defer no longer leaves empty wrappers (F1) and partial-emit no longer leaves empty trailing space + cursor inflation (F2). **The mechanism**: (1) new `IBlockFragmentSink.UpdateFragmentBlockSize(int cursor, double newBlockSize)` API mutates a previously-emitted wrapper fragment's `BlockSize` in place — z-order preserved (= the wrapper stays at its sink-list index, ahead of its children); (2) `DispatchGridInner` gains `out double lastEmittedBlockExtent` exposing `gridLayouter.LastEmittedBlockExtent` (cycle 5c.1 producer); (3) at the outer-site IsGridContainer dispatch, the F2 consumer fires when EITHER `paginateGridForOuterChild` is on (= clamp fired this page) OR `incomingGridContinuation` is non-null (= resuming a previously-deferred grid; the AllDone-on-resume case from cycle 5c.1 PR-#98 review F1 needs the wrapper to size to remaining-rows extent, NOT the full grid's natural extent). When F2 fires, the wrapper is resized to `chrome + lastEmittedBlockExtent` via `sink.UpdateFragmentBlockSize(wrapperCursor, ...)` + the cursor advance is recomputed as `marginStart + chrome + lastEmittedBlockExtent + marginEnd` (= margin-box). (4) The cycle-5b outer-site extent clamp + gate-flip is REACTIVATED — when `IsPaginatableGrid(child)` + `pageRemaining > 0` + `pageRemaining < borderBoxBlockSize` + `pageRemaining > chrome`, clamp `borderBoxBlockSize` to remaining + flip `paginateGridForOuterChild=true` (mirrors paginatable-flex clamp at line ~1630). **Sink mutation API rollout**: `UpdateFragmentBlockSize` added to all 11 test sinks (BlockLayouterTests, BlockInlineIntegrationTests×2, FlexLayouterProductionTests, FlexLayouterTests, GridLayouterProductionTests, GridLayouterTests, MulticolLayouterProductionTests, MulticolLayouterTests, TableLayouterProductionTests, TableLayouterTests) — standard implementation `Fragments[cursor] = Fragments[cursor] with { BlockSize = newBlockSize }` (out-of-range = defensive no-op). Also added to 5 production helper sinks (`GridLayouter.TranslatingFragmentSink` forwards via baseline; `MulticolLayouter.DiscardingMeasureSink` + `BlockLayouter.MulticolDiscardingMeasureSink` = no-op since measure-only sinks discard fragments; `MulticolLayouter.ColumnFragmentSink` forwards to outer; `TableLayouter.MeasuringFragmentSink` mutates the buffered fragment so eventual FlushTo emits the resize). **Flex cycle 4f**: the API mirrors flex's deferred wrapper-resize need — flex's `FlexContinuation.EmittedBlockExtent` (cycle 4e) can consume the same `UpdateFragmentBlockSize` API in a future PR. **Tests**: 7 new direct unit tests under `Cycle5c2b_F2_*`: (a) `wrapper_resizes_to_emitted_extent_on_partial_emit` (= verifies wrapper BlockSize == emittedExtent + chrome on PageComplete with GridContinuation), (b) `wrapper_resize_eliminates_empty_trailing_space` (= the CRITICAL case: budget 250, emitted 240 → wrapper at 240 not 250), (c) `cursor_advance_uses_emitted_extent_not_budget` (= `ctx.UsedBlockSize` after the run reflects emitted-extent), (d) `gate_off_path_uses_unmodified_marginbox_cursor_advance` (= regression test for non-paginatable cases), (e) `AllDone_final_resume_page_resizes_wrapper` (= page 2 of split grid resizes wrapper to remaining-rows extent on AllDone), (f) `sink_UpdateFragmentBlockSize_replaces_blocksize_preserves_other_fields` (= API contract: mutate BlockSize only), (g) `sink_UpdateFragmentBlockSize_out_of_range_is_safe_noop` (= defensive bounds check). Tests: **5111 unit** (+7 cycle-5c.2b tests over 5104 cycle-5c.2a baseline; +313 over 4798 cycle-0a baseline) + **97 RealDocs** + **30 LayoutSnapshots** + **4 AotJitParity** all green. AOT/JIT byte-parity preserved at sha256 `2942DD1E…30C3DE7` (= production HTML fixtures route through the recursive `EmitBlockSubtreeRecursive` path which is unchanged; F2 + clamp fire only at the outer-site direct-construction path). Cycle 5c.2c picks up F3 (explicit-height grid handling — `MeasureSubtreeVisualBlockExtent` grid-aware); cycle 5c.2d wires the recursive site + forced-overflow re-route + production-pipeline multi-page tests.

**Historical pointer — Task 17 cycle 5c.2a + post-PR-#99 review hardening** (superseded by cycle 5c.2b) — F1 pre-dispatch row-fit decision for paginatable grids; post-PR-#99 review 4 findings closed: P1#1 + P1#2 + P2#1 + P2#2 partial. **Cycle 5c.2a** resolves the `grid-wrapper-rollback-for-pre-dispatch-deferral` (= PR-#97 review F1 architectural item) via the deferral's option (a) — BlockLayouter-owned pre-dispatch row-fit query — over option (b) sink rollback / wrapper backfill: cleaner semantics, no speculative emission, no new sink mutation contract, reuses the existing `GridSizing.Resolve` pattern. **The mechanism**: new `internal static` helper `BlockLayouter.PreMeasureGridRowExtentAt(box, rowIndex, contentInlineSize, contentBlockSize, incomingCache, ct)`. **Post-PR-#99 review P1#1** (progress guard): the original `pageRemaining < fullPage` proxy was unsound — a first-on-page grid with `margin-top > 0` has `topShift = marginStart`, making pageRemaining (which subtracts topShift) less than fullPage (which didn't), even on a fresh page; F1 could defer the row + the `LayoutRetryCoordinator` returns PageComplete WITHOUT escalating to LastResort (line 197 of LayoutRetryCoordinator.cs), so the zero-progress loop is unbounded — availability / DoS risk for authored or hostile CSS. Post-fix the guard is `emittedThisAttempt > 0` — F1 defers ONLY when prior content was committed on this attempt; when the grid is the first emittable child on the page, F1 falls through so atomic dispatch (or LastResort-§4.4 force-emit) makes progress. The next-page-fits predicate also subtracts `marginStart` (= mirrors the actual fresh-page topShift the deferred grid will see). **Post-PR-#99 review P1#2** (probe matches dispatch sizing): the original `(contentInlineSize: 1, contentBlockSize: 1)` dry-run didn't match the actual dispatch's content-box geometry, and the incoming `GridResumeCache` was preserved but never consulted — a hypocrisy that would silently diverge once fr / minmax tracks ship. Post-fix the helper takes the actual `gridGeom.ContentInlineSize / ContentBlockSize` (= `GridGeometryHelper.ComputeContentGeometry` at the F1 site) AND when a valid `GridResumeCache` (= identity + inline-size match) is supplied, reads `cache.RowBaseSizes[rowIndex]` directly — mirroring `GridLayouter`'s cache-reuse validation. **Post-PR-#99 review P2#1** (docs accuracy): the original "no production observable change" framing was incorrect — direct-construction callers observe the F1 routing immediately (the unit tests prove it). Production HTML fixtures route through the recursive `EmitBlockSubtreeRecursive` path (= unchanged until cycle 5c.2d), so existing AOT/JIT byte-parity is preserved — but the OUTER-SITE BlockLayouter contract is permanently changed from this ship forward. **Post-PR-#99 review P2#2** (sizing duplication): partial — the cache hit path on resume avoids the duplicate `GridSizing.Resolve`; the non-cached probe still duplicates sizing (= sizing also done in `PreMeasureGridRowExtent` + the dispatch's GridLayouter). Cycle 5c.2b will wire a shared `GridFragmentPlan` across pre-measure + F1 + dispatch so §11 work runs once per attempt. **Resume contract**: the probe's `startRow` is read from the incoming `BlockContinuation.LayouterState=GridContinuation`'s `RowIndex` when its `ResumeAtChild` matches the current childIdx, otherwise 0; the outgoing continuation preserves `incomingGridForProbe?.Cache` so the resume page's GridLayouter sees the same identity. **Tests**: 12 new direct unit tests under `Cycle5c2a_F1_*`: (a) `defers_paginatable_grid_when_first_row_exceeds_page_remaining`, (b) `does_not_defer_under_LastResort_strategy`, (c) `does_not_defer_when_first_row_fits_page_remaining`, (d) `does_not_defer_when_row_also_exceeds_fresh_page`, (e) `progress_guard_skips_defer_on_fresh_page`, (f) `does_not_apply_to_non_grid_children`, (g) `progress_guard_first_child_with_margin_top_does_not_defer` (= P1#1 direct regression), (h) `P1_first_child_terminates_via_coordinator` (= P1#1 round-trip via `LayoutRetryCoordinator`, page-loop iteration cap 8 to catch unbounded loops), (i) `helper_cache_hit_reads_from_cache_when_identity_and_inline_size_match` (= P1#2 cache-consultation), (j) `helper_cache_miss_when_inline_size_differs_falls_back_to_fresh_resolve`, (k) `helper_cache_miss_when_identity_differs_falls_back_to_fresh_resolve`, (l) `helper_handles_out_of_range_and_negative_row_indices`. Tests: **5104 unit** (+12 cycle-5c.2a tests over 5092 cycle-5c.1-hardening baseline; +306 over 4798 cycle-0a baseline) + **97 RealDocs** + **4 AotJitParity** all green. AOT/JIT byte-parity preserved at sha256 `2942DD1E…30C3DE7` (= production HTML fixtures route through the recursive path which keeps cycle-1 atomic dispatch; F1 is OBSERVABLE at the outer-site contract level but unreached by these fixtures). Cycle 5c.2b picks up F2 wrapper-resize consumer + reactivates the outer-site gate + ships the shared `GridFragmentPlan`; 5c.2c picks up F3 explicit-height; 5c.2d wires the recursive site + forced-overflow re-route + production-pipeline multi-page tests.

**Historical pointer — Task 17 cycle 5c.1 + post-PR-#98 deep-review hardening** (superseded by cycle 5c.2a) — 5 findings closed (F1 + F2 + F3 + F4 + F5). **F1 (CRITICAL design flaw)**: `GridContinuation.EmittedBlockExtent` only exists when `PageComplete` fires; the FINAL fragment of a split grid returns `AllDone` with no continuation but ALSO needs its wrapper resized to only the emitted rows. Per reviewer recommendation, the emitted-extent moved from continuation-only to a result-level channel via new `GridLayouter.LastEmittedBlockExtent` public property populated on EVERY outcome (PageComplete + AllDone + Strict-defer + early-return). The `GridContinuation.EmittedBlockExtent` field is kept as a redundant carrier when a continuation exists. **F2 (pre-existing dormant defect)**: when a resumed fragment Strict-defers its first remaining row, the returned `GridContinuation(startRow, Cache: null)` would make the next attempt see `Cache==null` → `identityMatches==false` → `startRow` reset to 0 → re-emission of prior-page rows. Post-fix preserves `_incomingContinuation?.Cache` on the Strict-defer path so identity + RowIndex both stay bound. **F3 (forward-compat trap)**: `sum(rowSizes)` is equal to occupied content-box span TODAY only because CSS Grid gutters / block-axis alignment aren't implemented; once `row-gap` lands, summing track sizes will under-report the fragment's occupied span. Replaced with GEOMETRY-based derivation: `lastEmittedRow.bottom - firstEmittedRow.top`. Today equivalent; remains correct under future spacing-bearing CSS Grid features. Eliminates the O(emitted rows) summation loop. **F4 (doc staleness)**: `grid-fragment-extent-emitted-rows-only-deferral` in `docs/deferrals.md` was still `not-started` despite the producer-side shipping in this PR. Updated to `approximated` (partial) with explicit producer-side-ships vs. cycle-5c.2-consumer-still-missing language + cross-link to the new `LastEmittedBlockExtent` property. **F5 (test gap)**: the prior `Cycle5c1_F2_AllDone_no_continuation_means_no_emitted_extent_record` test pinned the F1 gap as expected behavior — REPLACED with: (a) `Cycle5c1_F1_AllDone_layouter_property_carries_emitted_extent` (single-page fit case), (b) `Cycle5c1_F1_AllDone_final_fragment_of_split_grid_exposes_remaining_extent` (= the critical case: page 2 of split grid carries extent of remaining rows via `LastEmittedBlockExtent` since no continuation produced), (c) `Cycle5c1_F2_Strict_defer_from_resume_preserves_cache_no_double_emit` (= 3-step round-trip: emit row 0, Strict-defer row 1, retry with budget — only row 1 emits, NO re-emission of row 0), (d) `Cycle5c1_F3_emitted_extent_uses_geometry_not_sum_pins_today_equivalence` (= 3 different-sized rows, geometry derivation matches sum-of-sizes today; future row-gap will break sum but not geometry). Tests: **5092 unit** (+3 net cycle-5c.1 hardening tests: +4 new, -1 replaced; over 5089 cycle-5c.1-initial baseline; +294 over 4798 cycle-0a baseline) + **97 RealDocs** + **4 AotJitParity** all green. **Historical pointer — Task 17 cycle 5 + post-PR-#96 deep-review hardening — 6 findings closed (F1+F2 partial, F3, F4, F5, F6) + 1 deferred (F2 full IBreakResolver integration). **Post-PR-#96 hardening:** **F1+F2 partial — LastResort gating for forced-overflow** — pre-F1 the layouter ALWAYS force-emitted oversized first rows, which mispaginates common "grid starts below earlier content" layouts (80px remain on page 1, first row is 100px → spec says defer to page 2, old impl force-emitted on page 1). New `LayoutAttemptStrategy` parameter threaded through `ComputePaginatedRowRange`: `LastResort` strategy preserves the §4.4 progress-rule force-emit; any other strategy (= Strict / default) returns `PageComplete(GridContinuation(startRow, null))` signaling "defer entire grid" so the dispatching BlockLayouter rewinds + retries on a fresh page. Critical for cycle 5b dispatch safety. Full IBreakResolver integration (model rows as BreakOpportunity values, route through resolver, honor CSS `break-before`/`break-after`/`break-inside`) deferred — new `grid-break-resolver-integration-deferred` deferrals.md entry tracks F2 full scope, lands alongside CSS break-* property support. **F3 — relative offsets + inline-size mismatch detection** — pre-F3 the cache stored ABSOLUTE row/col positions baked from the original page's contentInlineOffset/contentBlockOffset; resume on a page with different origin (= left/right pages, nested fragmentainers) would mispaint. Post-F3: cache stores RELATIVE-FROM-CONTENT-ORIGIN positions (= 0-based). Resume adds current page's offsets at emit time. New `GridResumeCache.OriginalContentInlineSize` field — if resume page has a different inline size, the cached fr/Maximize'd column widths are stale → cache is invalidated + fresh §11 sizing + §8.5 placement pass runs + new `LayoutGridResumeInlineSizeMismatch001` diagnostic fires. **F4 — lazy cache build** — pre-F4 `BuildResumeCache` was called on EVERY fresh grid layout regardless of pagination, allocating 4 immutable arrays + placement copies that the dormant `allowPagination=false` production path could never consume (= avoidable GC pressure for grid-heavy invoice/report workloads). Post-F4: cache built only when `needsContinuation=true`. Atomic-mode + paginated-but-fits-on-one-page both skip the allocation. **F5 — cache identity + structural validation** — pre-F5 the cache had no ownership check; a continuation routed to the wrong grid container would emit boxes from grid A inside grid B's wrapper. Post-F5: new `GridResumeCache.GridIdentity` field (= original rootBox reference, typed `object` for the same Paginate-can't-reference-Layout circular-dep reason as `GridItemPlacement.Box`). New `ValidateCachePerF5` checks `GridIdentity == rootBox` + array length consistency + bounds-checks item placements + finite geometry + Box-type item payloads. Validation failure emits `LayoutGridResumeCacheRejected001` + falls back to fresh resolve (which also forces `startRow = 0` since the rejected continuation's RowIndex was for the wrong grid). **F6 — stale doc cleanup** — GridLayouter constructor XML, ConfigureEmission XML, DispatchGridInner XML, GridContinuation XML all updated to reflect the active cycle-5 contract instead of the cycle-1 throws-on-anything claim. **New diagnostic codes** (3 total in cycle 5 + hardening): `LayoutGridForcedOverflow001` (cycle 5 initial), `LayoutGridResumeInlineSizeMismatch001` (F3), `LayoutGridResumeCacheRejected001` (F5). All mirrored across PaginateDiagnosticCodes + NetPdf.Diagnostics.DiagnosticCodes + docs/diagnostics-codes.md + parity tests. **Tests**: 7 new hardening tests covering F1 (Strict-defers + LastResort-force-emits), F3 (mismatched inline size invalidates + same inline size uses cache), F4 (atomic mode + paginated-fit return null continuation), F5 (cross-grid continuation routing rejects cache + falls back to fresh resolve) + 2 new diagnostic parity tests. **Historical pointer — Task 17 cycle 5 (initial ship)** (merged: open PR-#96, awaiting review): **GridLayouter row-by-row pagination contract is ACTIVE**: cycle-5 promotes `allowPagination=true` from "throws" to "splits"; the layouter computes which rows fit the page budget + emits `[startRow, K]` inclusive + returns `PageComplete` with `GridContinuation(K+1, cache)`. Cache reuse is a real perf win on resume AND a correctness requirement (sparse auto-placement is order-sensitive + would yield a different placement if items were partially emitted on the prior page). Row offsets shift on resume so the first emitted row anchors at the wrapper's content-box top (= not at its absolute first-page position). **Architecture**: `GridContinuation.TrackSizingCache` field promoted from `object?` to typed `GridResumeCache?` (= immutable record of `ImmutableArray<double>` row/col sizes + positions + `ImmutableArray<GridItemPlacement>` per-item placement). **Historical pointer — Task 17 cycle 4 + post-PR-#95 deep-review hardening — 18 findings closed across 3 critical spec-violations + 4 hardening + 4 perf/cleanup + 4 doc + 9 deferral entries. **Post-PR-#95 hardening (the big-three critical fixes):** **C1** (§11.6 Maximize spec violation) — cycle-4 initial impl used `ratio = freeSpace / totalHeadroom; base += headroom × ratio` which is FLEXBOX semantics, NOT grid. Per CSS Grid §11.6 + §11.5.1 Maximize distributes EQUALLY to base sizes + freezes tracks as they hit growth limits. Counter-example: `minmax(50px, 100px) minmax(50px, 1000px)` in 400px → spec says A=100 (frozen), B=300; old impl said A=65, B=335. Rewritten `MaximizeTracks` mirrors the §11.7.1 iterative freezing pattern: mark non-eligible (fr, infinite-growth, growth≤base) frozen up-front; loop `share = freeSpace / liveCount; if newBase ≥ growth → clamp+freeze, else apply`; terminate when no track freezes. Bounded by unfrozenCount passes. Test `Cycle4_maximize_proportional_when_free_space_below_total_headroom` (which pinned the WRONG behavior) replaced with `Cycle4_maximize_equal_distribution_freezes_tracks_at_growth_limit` matching spec. **C2** (fit-content grown past computed size) — `ResolveIntrinsicTracks` set `BaseSize = effective = min(limit, contribution)` but left `GrowthLimit = FitContentLimit`. Maximize then saw headroom = limit-effective > 0 + grew the track past its §7.2.2 result. Fix: pin `GrowthLimit = effective` after intrinsic resolution → Maximize sees no headroom + leaves fit-content tracks alone. **C3** (percentage sub-args silently treated as pixels) — `ClassifyMinMax` never checked `MinSubIsPercentage`/`MaxSubIsPercentage`; FitContent never checked `entry.IsPercentage`. So `minmax(50%, 1fr)` silently became `minmax(50px, 1fr)` with no diagnostic. Fix: detect percentage at classify time + emit new `LayoutGridPercentageTrackApproximated001` + collapse the percentage side to 0 (= author sees clearly broken layout vs. authoritative-looking-wrong pixel value). Top-level `<percentage>` Length now hits a dedicated case + dedicated diagnostic (H3 — was the misleading "kind Length unsupported"). **Hardening fixes** (H1, H2, H7): H1 — new `SizesDiffer(a, b)` epsilon-comparison helper (`SizeEpsilon = 1e-9`) replaces fragile `!=` double-equality in intrinsic-resolution change detection. H2 — `ResolveFrTracks` loop bound corrected to `frTrackCount + 1` (was `infos.Count`); on safety-bound exhaustion emit `LayoutGridNonFiniteGeometry001` so a non-convergent algorithm bug doesn't silently fail. H7 — `MinBaseSize` mutation guarded so only fr-participating tracks update the floor; FitContent (non-fr) no longer touches MinBaseSize, keeping semantics clean. **Perf + cleanup** (P1, P3, Q1, Q3, P6): P1 — `CollectionsMarshal.AsSpan(infos)` ref-access pattern eliminates the 12+ copy-mutate-write-back sites for 72-byte `TrackSizingInfo` struct mutations; P2 — `stackalloc bool[N]` for the `frozen` array in fr distribution + Maximize (small-track-count common case bypasses heap); P3 — `MaterializeSizes` now called ONCE after Maximize (was twice — initially inside ResolveTrackSizes then overwritten); Q1 — deleted dead `kindsOut/rowKinds/colKinds` parameters (populated but never read); Q3 — kept `SizingContext` as class (documented why) + added new one-shot diagnostic flags. P6 — `CancellationToken.ThrowIfCancellationRequested()` at iteration boundaries in `ExpandTrackList` + `ResolveFrTracks` (hostile CSS like `repeat(10000, ...)` can spin tens-of-thousands of iterations). **Doc + diag clarity** (R1, R2, R3, R5): R1 — fr loop bound comment now matches implementation; R2 — new `LayoutGridMaxExpandedTracksTruncated001` for repeat() truncation (was misleading "Length unsupported"); R3 — fit-content xmldoc updated to reflect C2 fix; R5 — `SizingContext` xmldoc documents the per-axis-shared one-shot guard semantics. **New diagnostic codes** in both `PaginateDiagnosticCodes` + `NetPdf.Diagnostics.DiagnosticCodes`: `LayoutGridPercentageTrackApproximated001` + `LayoutGridMaxExpandedTracksTruncated001`. Updated `docs/diagnostics-codes.md` + 2 new parity tests in `DiagnosticCodesTests`. **Deferred to follow-up tasks** (each tracked as a dedicated `docs/deferrals.md` entry, all in `DeferralsParityTests.ExpectedDeferralIds`): `grid-maximize-extra-space-receiver-deferred` (H4 = §11.5.1 step 3 second-pass to infinite-growth tracks); `grid-box-sizing-border-box-deferred` (H6 = cross-cutting box-sizing audit, touches all layouters); `grid-sizing-perf-optimizations-deferred` (P2 ArrayPool, P4 per-item style cache, P5 inverted-index for placed items); `grid-sizing-architecture-followups-deferred` (Q2 strategy pattern non-decision, Q4 file split, Q5 AxisProperties refactor). **Tests**: 14 new hardening tests (T1 equal-distribute Maximize + below-all-limits variant, T2 fit-content without fr, T3 minmax percentage min + fit-content percentage limit + top-level percentage Length dedicated diagnostic, T4 DoS truncation diagnostic, T5 repeat with named lines in pattern, T6 sequential repeats, T7 multi-track simultaneous fr-freeze, T9 0fr in minmax, T11 production fr-removal, T12 production minmax min>max) + 2 new diagnostic parity tests. **Historical pointer — Task 17 cycle 4 (initial ship)** (merged at `48f3071`): — `minmax()` / `fit-content()` / `repeat(<integer>, ...)` track sizing per CSS Grid §7.2 + activates the §11.6 Maximize step + the §11.7.1 iterative fr-removal step. **Architecture**: introduced `TrackSizingInfo` private struct inside `GridSizing.cs` carrying `(BaseSize, MinBaseSize, GrowthLimit, IsFr, FrFactor, Kind, MinSubKind, MaxSubKind, FitContentLimit)` — replaces the cycle-2/3 parallel `sizes / isFr / frFactors / kinds` arrays. `ResolveTrackSizes` now returns `List<double>` (= MaterializeSizes from the info list) AND populates a side `List<TrackSizingInfo>` that the post-placement intrinsic + Maximize passes consume. **MinBaseSize** records the per-track floor (= the `minmax(min, fr)` min when fr; 0 for plain fr) so re-running fr distribution after intrinsic resolution doesn't mistake the prior pass's distributed value for the floor. **Repeat expansion**: new `ExpandTrackList` static helper walks `TrackList.Items`, unrolls positive-count `TrackListRepeat` into N inline pattern copies (pattern items: `TrackRepeatEntry` → `TrackListEntry`, `TrackRepeatNamedLine` → `TrackListNamedLine`), preserves auto-fill (count=0) + auto-fit (count=-1) for cycle-7 scope (they still emit unsupported diagnostic). Honors `TrackList.MaxExpandedTrackCount = 50_000` DoS cap. **minmax(min, max)**: per §7.2.4 — `ClassifyMinMax` reads min into BaseSize + MinBaseSize (Length pinned, intrinsic = 0 placeholder), max into GrowthLimit + IsFr + FrFactor (Length pinned, Fr → IsFr=true + uncapped GrowthLimit, intrinsic = ∞ placeholder). §11.5 invariant: when min > max (= invalid CSS like `minmax(200px, 100px)`), max = min (track sits at min). **fit-content(limit)**: per §7.2.2 the size = `max(auto-min, min(limit, max-content))`. Cycle 4 L19 approximation: auto-min = 0 → simplifies to `min(limit, max-content)`. Classified as base=0, growth=limit; intrinsic resolution writes base = min(limit, contribution). **§11.6 Maximize step** (new `MaximizeTracks` method): after fr distribution + intrinsic resolution, if free space > 0 AND tracks have finite GrowthLimit > BaseSize, distribute free space proportional to per-track headroom, capped at GrowthLimit. Fr tracks excluded (= §11.7 already consumed flex-derived space). **§11.7.1 iterative fr-removal step** (rewritten `ResolveFrTracks`): each pass computes nonFlexBase + leftover + hypoFr; any unfrozen fr track with `BaseSize > hypoFr × FrFactor` freezes at its base (= the "minimum prevents shrinkage" rule); recompute + iterate until no more removals. Pre-cycle-4 this never fired because all fr tracks had BaseSize=0 floor; cycle-4 `minmax(min, fr)` introduces non-zero floors that trigger removal. **Intrinsic resolution extended**: handles MinMax (intrinsic min → BaseSize from item contribution; intrinsic max → GrowthLimit from contribution; growth ≥ base invariant enforced) + FitContent (base = min(limit, contribution)). **Diagnostic update**: `LayoutGridTrackKindUnsupported001` message no longer lists minmax / fit-content / repeat as unsupported; still fires for auto-fill / auto-fit / percentage tracks + on MaxExpanded truncation. **Tests**: 10 direct + 4 production-pipeline cycle-4 tests covering: minmax(length, length) clamps to max via Maximize, minmax(length, fr) distributes via fr with min floor, minmax-fr-removal (`minmax(300px, 1fr) 1fr` in 400px → track 1 frozen at 300, track 2 gets 100), invalid-CSS minmax min > max → max = min, fit-content above + below limit, repeat(3, 100px) literal expansion, repeat(2, 100px 1fr) mixed-pattern expansion, Maximize full + proportional distribution paths, minmax-with-intrinsic-min → grows from placed item then Maximize, minmax-with-intrinsic-min pinned when container can't fit. Pre-existing 57 grid tests still pass unchanged. **Historical pointer — Task 17 cycle 2 + post-PR-#93 review hardening** (merged at `fdbf908`): — 6 review findings closed (3 P1, 2 P2, 1 P3). **Post-PR-#93 hardening:** F1 (spec-correct flexFactorSum) — the §11.7.1 floor applies to the TOTAL sum ONCE (`max(SUM(factors), 1.0)`), NOT per-track (`SUM(max(factor, 1))`) as the cycle-2 initial implementation did. The per-track floor produced materially wrong sizing for fractional factors: `0.25fr 0.25fr` in 400px yielded 50/50 instead of the spec's 100/100; `0fr 1fr` yielded 0/200 instead of 0/400; `0.5fr 1fr` yielded 100/200 instead of 133.33/266.67. All test expectations updated to match spec. F4 (non-finite flexFactorSum guard) — `1e308fr 1e308fr` overflows the sum to ∞ which would silently collapse tracks to 0 (`hypoFr = leftover / ∞ = 0`); the guard detects this BEFORE division and emits `LayoutGridNonFiniteGeometry001`. F2 (zero-sized cell content diagnostic) — new `LayoutGridZeroSizedCellContentSkipped001` diagnostic when an item has children but its cell resolves to a 0-width or 0-height area (= `0fr` column). The outer item fragment still emits at zero geometry but cycle 2 can't dispatch inner content (`FragmentainerContext` requires positive extent); the diagnostic surfaces the silent drop. Cycle 3 will ship the zero-area inner-layout strategy. F3 (fr under indefinite axis) — new `LayoutGridFrUnderIndefiniteApproximated001` diagnostic when fr tracks appear on an indefinite axis (= auto-height grid with fr rows). Per §11.7 these should resolve via intrinsic / max-content sizing (cycle 3 scope); cycle 2 emits the diagnostic + leaves fr tracks at 0. Detection: check `Height.Tag is Unset or Keyword` for rows, same for `Width` for columns. F5 (sizing helper drift) — documented in code (= cycle 3+ scope to fully extract a shared `GridTrackSizing` service; for cycle 2 both call paths use length-only for indefinite axes which is consistent). Updated `docs/diagnostics-codes.md` + parity tests in `DiagnosticCodesTests`. **Tests**: 5 existing fr tests updated with spec-correct expectations (= 0.25fr → 100, not 50; 0fr+1fr → 0+400, not 0+200; etc.); 5 new hardening tests covering F1 0.5fr+1fr unfloored sum, F2 zero-cell with-and-without inner content, F3 fr-in-auto-height-rows diagnostic, F4 overflow diagnostic. Tests: **5030 unit** (+10 hardening tests over 5020 cycle-2-initial baseline; +232 over 4798 cycle-0a baseline) + **97 RealDocs** + **6 PropertyCoverageCorpusTests** + **4 AotJitParity** all green. AOT/JIT byte-parity preserved at sha256 `2942DD1E…30C3DE7`. **Cycle 2 ships**: fr tracks via CSS Grid §11.7 "Find the Size of an fr" algorithm. Builds on cycle 1's GridLayouter by adding `<flex>` (fr) track sizing. The spec-correct algorithm (NOT the naive `flex / sumFlex` proportional split) handles fractional flex factors (`0.25fr`) and negative leftover correctly. **Algorithm** (per §11.7.1): (1) `leftover = containerExtent - sumOfNonFlexBases`; if ≤ 0, all fr tracks pin at 0 (= container may overflow). (2) `flexFactorSum = Σ max(flex, 1)` over fr tracks (= the divisor floors at 1; the numerator factor isn't floored). (3) `hypoFr = leftover / flexFactorSum`. (4) Each fr track's size = `hypoFr × flex` (raw factor). Cycle 2 ships with no content-derived base sizes (= L19 deferral; cycle 3 lands intrinsic sizing → the spec's iterative "remove fr track whose base > hypoFr × flex" step lands then). **Implementation**: `GridLayouter.ResolveTrackSizes` now takes a `containerExtent` parameter + classifies each track as Length / Fr / unsupported using parallel `isFr` + `frFactors` arrays (= the `isFr` boolean array correctly distinguishes 0fr from non-fr, which the initial-draft 0fr collision missed). New `ResolveFrTracks` helper applies the §11.7 distribution. The pre-cycle-1 fr-emit-diagnostic path now lands only for non-fr unsupported kinds. **Diagnostic refinement**: the `LayoutGridTrackKindUnsupported001` diagnostic no longer fires for fr (= fr is supported in cycle 2); still fires for auto / intrinsic / minmax / fit-content / repeat. **Tests**: 8 new tests (6 direct + 2 production) covering 2-equal-fr-split, fixed-plus-fr distribution, fractional-fr-below-1 floor-sum, negative-leftover pinning, 0fr edge case, fr-in-rows direction, full-pipeline. Cycle-1's "fr emits diagnostic + contributes zero" test rewritten to assert the new cycle-2 behavior (= fr now distributes correctly, no diagnostic). AOT/JIT byte-parity preserved at sha256 `2942DD1E…30C3DE7`. Cycle 3 ships intrinsic sizing (`auto` / `min-content` / `max-content`) with the spec's iterative fr-removal step.

**Historical pointer — Task 17 cycle 0c + post-PR-#91 review hardening** (merged at `eb96940`): — 6 review findings closed (3 P1, 2 P2, 1 P3). **Post-PR-#91 hardening:** F1 (atomic shorthand validation) — both grid expanders now pre-validate every `<grid-line>` component via the new `GridLineResolver.TryValidate(text)` static helper BEFORE emitting any longhand recovery record (per CSS Cascade L4 §4.2 invalid-shorthand-contributes-nothing rule). When validation fails, `CssPreprocessor` emits invalid-sentinel longhand recovery records (= raw shorthand value, which the resolver rejects); these override AngleSharp's per-longhand emit unconditionally (`IsFromShorthandExpansion=false`), so the cascade falls back to the property initial value. **Known-gap**: AngleSharp's per-rule property dedup discards earlier valid same-rule longhand values BEFORE recovery runs (= `grid-row-start: 3; grid-row: 2 / 0` ends up start=auto rather than the spec-correct start=3); preserving the earlier value requires extending `ExplicitLonghandRef` to carry raw values + rewriting the merge — tracked as a deferral. The three new expanders are: `GridLineShorthandExpander` for `grid-row` / `grid-column` (= 1-2 values separated by `/`, with the §8.4 omitted-pair rule); `GridAreaShorthandExpander` for `grid-area` (= 1-4 values, all four longhands written); `GridShorthandHelpers` for the shared `IsBareCustomIdent` + `IsCssWideKeyword` predicates. **§8.4 omitted-pair rule**: when the shorthand has fewer values than longhands, the omitted longhand inherits the corresponding original value IF it was a bare `<custom-ident>` (= a named line); OTHERWISE it falls back to `auto`. **Historical pointer — Task 17 cycle 0b + post-PR-#90 review hardening** (merged at `75e5e79`): — CSS parser/resolver for the grid AST + 8 review findings closed (4 P1, 4 P2). **Post-PR-#90 hardening:** F1 (tokenizer error path) — both `GridLineResolver` + `GridTemplateListResolver` tokenizers now emit explicit `Error` token kind (vs the prior empty-Ident sentinel that fed empty strings to validating factories + threw `ArgumentException`); parsers reject Error tokens early; Resolve catches `ArgumentException` as belt-and-braces. F3 (CSS-wide keywords) — both resolvers reject `initial` / `inherit` / `unset` / `revert` / `revert-layer` at the top level + the named-line parser rejects them in compound forms (= defense-in-depth; central cascade interception is a separate concern). F4 (unitless zero) — bare `0` is now accepted in `<length-percentage>` positions per CSS Values L4 §6.2 (track breadth, minmax args, fit-content limit); non-zero unitless numbers stay invalid. F5 (defer relative units) — em / rem / vw / ch / cqw / etc. now return `ResolverResult.Deferred(rawText)` (matches the `LengthResolver` pattern + the existing `ComputedStyle.SetDeferred` contract) instead of being diagnosed as malformed; the spec example `repeat(auto-fill, minmax(25ch, 1fr))` is no longer falsely diagnosed. `calc()` stays Invalid per the L19+ design-doc rejection. F2 (auto-fill / auto-fit grammar) — auto-repeat groups now enforce `<fixed-size>` tracks (= `<length-percentage>` OR `minmax()` with at least one fixed side); `repeat(auto-fill, 1fr)` / `repeat(auto-fit, auto)` / `repeat(auto-fill, min-content)` / `repeat(auto-fill, fit-content(100px))` now reject; the spec-canonical `repeat(auto-fill, minmax(100px, 1fr))` still parses. Also enforces the single-auto-repeat rule per §7.2.3. F8 (parser resource bounds) — `GridLineResolver` caps at 16 tokens (grid-line values have at most 3); `GridTemplateListResolver` caps at 50,000 tokens + 1024 top-level items + 64 items per `repeat()` pattern (combined with cycle-0a's `MaxRepeatCount = 10,000` + layout-time `MaxExpandedTrackCount = 50,000`, this bounds total CPU + allocation per declaration). F6 (ComputedStyle side-table invariant) — `Set(id, slot)` where `slot.Tag != SideTableIndex` now auto-clears any prior side-table payload; `SetDeferred` also clears. ComputedStyle owns the invariant; `MaterializeInto` simplified (no explicit `ClearSideTablePayload` call needed on the null-payload branch). **Original Task 16 cycle 1 + post-PR-#78 hardening** (historical pointer — superseded by cycle 2 above): Task 16 cycle 1 + post-PR-#78 review hardening — 3 P1 findings (pagination math uses align-content-adjusted coords; wrap-reverse pagination incorrect; LineIndex not validated) + 2 P2 (cycle-1 boundary too loose; missing boundary tests) + 1 P3 stale-doc cleanup. The post-PR-#78 rework moves fragment-range determination BEFORE align-content offsets are computed (per CSS Flexbox §10 "lay out as many lines as possible before finishing Cross Axis Alignment for each fragment"): a raw cursor sums only `line.LineCrossSize` (= ignoring align-content's `lineStartOffset` + `lineBetweenSpacing`) to identify the split point, then `lines` is sliced to the fragment's range before align-content + the emission loop run. Pagination is now strictly gated to `isWrapping && !isWrapReverse && !isColumn` so wrap-reverse falls through to atomic behavior (cycle 1 deferral — the CrossAxisFlow swap uses unfragmented containerCrossSize which would place resumed lines at the wrong physical offset). `FlexContinuation.LineIndex` validated against `[0, lines.Count]` with `ArgumentOutOfRangeException` on out-of-range. 8 new boundary tests added: too-tall first line still emits (CSS Fragmentation §4.4 progress rule); exact-fit returns AllDone; 3-line split at correct index; negative LineIndex throws; out-of-range LineIndex throws; `LineIndex == lines.Count` resumes as no-op AllDone; wrap-reverse pagination disabled emits atomically; align-content: center doesn't skew pagination fit. Original cycle-1 ships: the constructor accepts a non-null `FlexContinuation` (carrying `LineIndex`), AttemptLayout skips lines `[0, LineIndex)` at emission time + checks line-fit against `_contentBlockSize` (= the available block space from `ConfigureEmission`), splitting at the first line that doesn't fit + returning `LayoutAttemptResult.PageComplete` with a `FlexContinuation` for the next page. Gated behind a new `allowPagination: bool` parameter on `ConfigureEmission` (default `false`) so the L1-L17 fixtures (atomic mode, may overflow — the L7 hardening tests deliberately exercise this path) stay byte-identical. Row-direction wrap mode only for cycle 1; column-direction split (= inline-axis pagination) is sub-cycle 2+ scope. BlockLayouter dispatch integration (= capturing the PageComplete result + wiring the resume chain through outer pagination) is also sub-cycle 2 scope; cycle 1 ships the layouter-side contract so the data flow is testable in isolation. 4 new `Task16_*` unit tests verify: pagination off by default preserves atomic behavior; explicit pagination splits when lines exceed the available block; resuming with a continuation skips emitted lines; the constructor rejects non-FlexContinuation continuations. Tests: 4703 unit / 4834 solution-wide passing — PR open for review.

**Original L17 + post-PR-#77 hardening** (historical pointer — superseded by Task 16 cycle 1 above): Task 15 L17 + post-PR-#77 review hardening — proper CSS Cascade §5 importance + §7.4 source-order rules for shorthand-vs-explicit-longhand conflicts. The initial L17 used a per-property `ExplicitLonghandsAfterShorthand` set which couldn't represent multi-shorthand cases (`flex-flow ...; flex-wrap ...; flex-flow ...` where the LAST shorthand should win) or `!important` interactions. The post-PR-#77 rework replaces the set with per-declaration `SourceOrdinal` on `CssDeclarationRecovery` + a new `ExplicitLonghandRef` list on `CssStyleRuleRecovery` capturing (property, ordinal, importance) for every explicit longhand. The merge in `CssParserAdapter.AdaptDeclarationsWithRecovery` calls a new `ShouldShorthandWinAgainstExplicitLonghands(recovery, explicits)` helper that iterates the explicit list applying the cascade rules: an `!important` declaration beats a normal declaration regardless of order; within the same importance level the LATER source ordinal wins. P1 #1 inline-style wiring: `AdaptInlineStyleWithRecovery` now calls `ScanForModernDeclarationsWithOrder` instead of `ScanForModernDeclarations` + passes the ordinal list through to `CssStyleRuleRecovery`. P3 perf: the explicit-longhand list is LAZILY allocated only when a shorthand expansion has been seen (= shorthand-free rules don't allocate). 13 shorthand-recovery unit tests + 6 L17 production-pipeline tests pin the full cascade-correctness matrix: shorthand→explicit, multi-shorthand, important-shorthand-vs-normal-explicit, normal-shorthand-vs-important-explicit, inline-style shorthand→explicit. Tests: 4695 unit / 4826 solution-wide passing — PR open for review.

**Original L17 set-based fix** (historical pointer — superseded by post-PR-#77 hardening above): Task 15 L17 — shorthand cascade source-order tracking (closes the PR-#76 P1 known gap + the P2 comments-in-shorthand-value gap). Pre-L17 `.flex { flex-flow: row wrap; flex-wrap: nowrap; }` would silently end up with `flex-wrap: wrap` (the shorthand expansion's earlier value) instead of the spec-correct `flex-wrap: nowrap` (the later explicit longhand per CSS Cascade §7.4 last-decl-wins). Same issue for `.a { flex: 1; flex-grow: 0; }` — explicit longhand silently lost. L17 wires source-order tracking into the preprocessor's `ScanDeclarations`: each rule's recovery now carries an `ExplicitLonghandsAfterShorthand` set listing property names that appear at a later source position than a matching shorthand expansion. The merge in `CssParserAdapter.AdaptDeclarationsWithRecovery` checks this set and skips the shorthand-expansion override for those properties, letting AngleSharp's emit (which respects last-decl-wins natively for explicit longhands) survive. P2 comments-in-value: new `CssShorthandHelpers.StripBlockComments` pre-normalizes CSS `/* ... */` comments to single spaces before tokenization in both `FlexShorthandExpander` and `FlexFlowShorthandExpander`. Production CSS like `flex-flow: row /* gutter */ wrap` and `flex: 1 /* grow */ 0 /* shrink */ 100px` now parses correctly. The L16 `_known_gap_` regression tests are flipped to assert the spec-correct outcome. 2 new L17 production tests pin the cascade-correct outcome at the layout layer (3×200 items don't wrap when explicit `flex-wrap: nowrap` overrides `flex-flow: row wrap`; items don't grow when explicit `flex-grow: 0` overrides `flex: 1`). Tests: 4691 unit / 4822 solution-wide passing — PR open.

**Original L16 Hello World + post-PR-#76 hardening** (historical pointer — superseded by L17 above): Task 15 L16 — `flex-flow` shorthand parser per CSS Flexbox L1 §6.1 + post-PR-#76 review hardening — 1 P1 finding addressed via data-model wiring + known-gap regression tests; 2 P2 findings (revert-layer test, inline-style test) + P3 (behavioral assertions) directly fixed. Mirrors L13's `flex` shorthand pattern: AngleSharp.Css 1.0.0-beta.144 doesn't reliably round-trip the `flex-flow` shorthand into its two longhand declarations for the cascade. L16 adds a new `FlexFlowShorthandExpander.TryExpand(value) → (direction, wrap)` that decomposes `<flex-direction> || <flex-wrap>` per §6.1; the preprocessor's `ScanDeclarations` recovery pass now emits TWO longhand `CssDeclarationRecovery` records (`flex-direction` / `flex-wrap`) in place of the single dropped `flex-flow` declaration. The expander handles all 8 grammar branches plus CSS-wide keywords (now including `revert-layer` per CSS Cascade L5 §7.3) that pass through to both longhands. **Post-PR-#76 hardening:** the P1 cascade source-order finding was investigated. A naive append-only fix (= recoveries from shorthand expansion never override AngleSharp's emit) broke L13 production tests because AngleSharp's emit for `flex: auto` / `flex: 100px` is itself wrong + needs override. The proper fix requires source-position tracking on BOTH AngleSharp's emit + the recovery records so the merge interleaves them per CSS Cascade §7.4 — that's a substantial refactor pinned by 8 new `CssPreprocessorShorthandRecoveryTests` cases (`Mixed_flex_flow_then_explicit_flex_wrap_known_gap_*` + `Flex_shorthand_then_explicit_flex_grow_known_gap_*` document the LIMITATION; `Mixed_explicit_flex_wrap_then_flex_flow_pins_recovery_state` + the `Important_modifier_propagates_*` + `Inline_style_attribute_path_picks_up_flex_flow_recovery` test the working cases). The `IsFromShorthandExpansion` flag is wired through `CssDeclarationRecovery` so the future fix can switch on it without re-plumbing. P3 behavioral assertions: L16 production tests now check EXACT BlockOffsets (e.g., `flex-flow: row wrap` with 3 items × 200/50 in 300×300 → BlockOffsets 0/100/200 per align-content: stretch default) instead of "different". 18 expander unit tests + 3 production-pipeline tests + 8 shorthand-recovery cascade tests = 29 new tests. Tests: 4687 unit / 4818 solution-wide passing — PR open, awaiting re-review.

**Original L15 Hello World + post-PR-#75 hardening** (historical pointer — superseded by L16 above): Task 15 L15 — anonymous flex-item wrapping per CSS Flexbox L1 §4 + post-PR-#75 review hardening — 4 P1 findings + 2 P2 + 2 P3 on top of the initial L15 Hello World. Pre-L15 the FlexLayouter's per-item emission loop filtered out non-block-level children (TextRun / InlineBox / atomic inlines), so production HTML like `<div style="display:flex">Hello <span>world</span></div>` lost both the text "Hello" + the `<span>` — they never reached the sink. Per §4: "Each in-flow child of a flex container becomes a flex item, and each contiguous sequence of child text runs is wrapped in an anonymous block container flex item." The initial L15 implementation wrapped everything (text + inline elements together) into ONE anonymous flex item, which silently dropped per-item `order` / `flex-grow` / `align-self` properties on inline element children. The post-PR-#75 rework splits the pass into two concerns: (a) `BlockifyForFlexItem` builds a new Box with the block-level Kind equivalent for each inline element child (InlineBox → BlockContainer, InlineFlexContainer → FlexContainer, InlineBlockContainer → BlockContainer, etc.), preserving SourceElement + Style + Pseudo + children, so each direct element stays an INDEPENDENT flex item; (b) only TextRun runs get wrapped into anonymous flex items. Anonymous wrappers now use a freshly-rented `ComputedStyle` (defaults + inheritable subset via `CreateAnonBoxStyle`) so the wrapper does NOT inherit the container's `width` / `flex-grow` / `order` etc. Tests: 4658 unit / 4789 solution-wide passing.

**Original L15 Hello World** (historical pointer — superseded by post-PR-#75 hardening above): Task 15 L15 — initial implementation wrapped contiguous sequences of inline-level children into ONE anonymous flex item. The post-PR-#75 review caught that this is over-broad (per-item flex properties on inline elements silently lost) and that the wrapper style was wrong (parent style leaked layout properties). Replaced by the BlockifyForFlexItem-based split above.

**Original L14 Hello World** (historical pointer — superseded by L15 above): Task 15 L14 — `CrossAxisFlow` refactor (closes the L11 post-PR-#71 hardening F#9 TODO seam). Pre-L14 the wrap-reverse cross-axis SWAP formula was inline at the line-emission site in `FlexLayouter`: `var lineCrossCursor = isWrapReverse ? contentCrossOffset + containerCrossSize - swappedAxisCursor - line.LineCrossSize : contentCrossOffset + swappedAxisCursor`. L14 extracts the swap into a `CrossAxisFlow` record (encapsulating `IsReversed` + `ContentCrossOffset` + `ContainerCrossSize`) with one method `PhysicalLineOffset(swappedCursor, lineCrossSize)`. The emission loop now reads `crossFlow.PhysicalLineOffset(swappedAxisCursor, line.LineCrossSize)` — same formula, named expression. Pure refactor: zero behavior change (all 188 pre-existing flex tests pass unchanged + the L11 wrap-reverse production test pins identical output). 7 new `CrossAxisFlowTests` lock the contract directly (wrap = identity; wrap-reverse = end-anchored; respects contentCrossOffset padding; handles unequal line cross-extents). Tests: 4651 unit / 4782 solution-wide passing.

**Original L13 Hello World** (historical pointer — superseded by L14 above): Task 15 L13 — `flex` shorthand parser per CSS Flexbox L1 §7.4. AngleSharp.Css 1.0.0-beta.144 only partially handles the shorthand (it sets `flex-grow` from `flex: <number>` but doesn't expand the keyword / length-basis / two-value / three-value forms), so real-world stylesheets that write `flex: 1` / `flex: none` / `flex: auto` / `flex: 0 0 100px` would not produce the spec-correct (grow, shrink, basis) longhands at the cascade. L13 adds a new `FlexShorthandExpander.TryExpand(value) → (grow, shrink, basis)` that decomposes the shorthand per §7.4 grammar; the preprocessor's `ScanDeclarations` recovery pass now emits THREE longhand `CssDeclarationRecovery` records (`flex-grow` / `flex-shrink` / `flex-basis`) in place of the single dropped `flex` declaration. The expander handles: `none` → `0 0 auto`; `auto` → `1 1 auto`; `<number>` → `<num> 1 0`; `<basis>` → `1 1 <basis>`; `<number> <number>` → `a b 0`; `<number> <basis>` → `a 1 <basis>`; full three-value → `a b c`; CSS-wide keywords (`initial` / `inherit` / `unset` / `revert` / `revert-layer`) pass through to all three longhands per CSS Cascade §7. 21 new expander unit tests + 5 new production-pipeline tests covering every grammar branch + cascade-level proof that the three longhands are populated. Tests: 4644 unit / 4775 solution-wide passing.

**Original L12 Hello World** (historical pointer — superseded by L13 above): Task 15 L12 — §9.7 step-4 min/max-size clamping iteration. This closes the L8 known-gap pin: `min-width`/`max-width` (and `min-height`/`max-height` under column direction) now clamp the resolved main-size during the flexibility resolution and iterate per spec until convergence. New `MaxSize` PropertyType joins the dimension family (routes through LengthResolver, admits `none` keyword + percentage). New `ResolveFlexItemMinMaxMainSize(minSizeProperty, maxSizeProperty) → (Min, Max)` extension on `Boxes.Box` reads the constraints (`min-width: auto` defers to L13+ when intrinsic sizing lands; `max-width: none` → +∞). `ResolveFlexibleMainSizes` now delegates per line to `ResolveLineWithMinMaxClamping` which implements the full iterative algorithm: each iteration redistributes remaining free-space, clamps to [min, max], tracks totalViolation, and freezes min-violators (totalViolation > 0) or max-violators (totalViolation < 0). The L8 known-gap test `L8_known_gap_min_width_does_not_clamp_resolved_size_yet` is flipped to `L12_min_width_clamps_resolved_shrink_per_spec_step_4` asserting (250, 250, 250) instead of (200, 200, 200). 4 new L12 tests cover max-width clamp on grow, mixed min+max violations (terminates in 1 iteration), basis-below-min clamp, and column-direction max-height clamp on grow. Tests: 4617 unit / 4748 solution-wide passing.

**Original L11 Hello World** (historical pointer — superseded by L12 above): Task 15 L11 + post-PR-#71 review hardening — 6 P1/P2 findings + 3 P3 findings on top of the L11 wrap-reverse Hello World. The L11 Hello World shipped only `lines.Reverse()` after PackLines — this swapped iteration order but did NOT move the line stack to the swapped cross-start origin, and did NOT swap per-line align-items / align-self FlexStart/FlexEnd anchors. The hardening replaces the (incorrect) reversal with a proper cross-axis SWAP at offset-computation time: each line's physical cross-offset is computed as `contentCrossOffset + containerCrossSize - swappedAxisCursor - line.LineCrossSize` when isWrapReverse; the per-item ComputeAlignItemsPlacement helper now takes an `isCrossAxisReversed` parameter that flips FlexStart/FlexEnd within each line. The 5 L11 tests that pinned the wrong behavior are flipped to assert the spec-correct positions. 7 new tests added: align-content: flex-end + space-between under wrap-reverse; unequal item heights with align-items: flex-start / flex-end + align-self override (proves per-item swap); auto-height pre-measure parity; wrap-reverse × order interaction. Tests: 4613 unit / 4744 solution-wide passing.

Also threads `CancellationToken` through the helper (Copilot's cancellation note) and fixes 2 `<see cref="Boxes.Box.GetFlexChildrenInOrderSequence"/>` references that wouldn't resolve (extension methods belong to their declaring type, not the receiver). 4 new tests over PR #70 baseline (4589 → 4593 unit / 4720 → 4724 solution-wide). **Original Task 15 L8 Hello World** — `flex-grow` / `flex-shrink` / `flex-basis` per CSS Flexbox L1 §7 + §9.7: the flexibility algorithm. Distributes positive free space among items via `flex-grow` factors; absorbs negative free space (= overflow) via `flex-shrink × flex-basis` factors per the §9.7 ratio formula. `flex-basis` joins the resolved family (LengthResolver dispatch) — admits the `auto` (Keyword 0) / `content` (Keyword 1) keywords + the `<length-percentage>` production per §7.2; `min-content` / `max-content` / `fit-content` are L9+ scope. F#1 (P1) single-line gate corrected: `flex-wrap: nowrap` is the multi-line/single-line boundary per CSS Flexbox §9.4, NOT `lineCount <= 1` — a wrap container with one produced line now stretches per §8.4. F#2 (P1) per-mode overflow handling mirrors the L2 justify-content pattern per CSS Box Alignment L3 §5.3: positional values keep their natural (possibly-negative) offset on overflow under default mode; distribution + stretch fall back to safe-start; `safe X` forces safe-start fallback regardless of value family; `unsafe X` honors the natural offset. F#3 (P2) `align-content` added to `KnownDroppedProperties` so AngleSharp-dropped `safe/unsafe` compound forms are recovered through ScanDeclarations + KeywordResolver. F#4 (P3) cancellation tokens threaded through the sum-cross-extents + stretch-mutation loops. F#5 PROGRESS.md + deferrals.md wording corrected: stretch grows lines "equally" (not "proportionally"); per-mode overflow handling is implemented in L7 (not deferred to L8+). F#6 (P2) `<baseline-position>` triple (baseline / first baseline / last baseline) added to BuildAlignContentTable (29-entry table); reader maps all three to Stretch approximation per the align-items precedent. F#7 (P2) column-direction tests added (3 tests covering stretch / center / space-between with cross-axis = inline). ## Pending pre-v1.0 work

- **Coverage-guided fuzzing infrastructure** — deferred from Phase D (PR #18) to a dedicated post-Phase-3 milestone. Per the Phase D analysis (recommendation #8 from the threat-model audit), SharpFuzz + AFL++ harnesses for `HtmlParsingHost`, `CssPreprocessor` / `CssParserAdapter`, `SelectorCompiler`, `CalcResolver`, `VarSubstitution`, `ImageSafetyValidator`, `FontSafetyValidator`, and `PdfPreflightValidator` give continuous regression coverage of the parser surfaces our regression corpus can't exhaustively cover. Estimated 4-6 weeks dedicated effort (build-system integration, 8 harnesses + corpora, CI gate, crash triage runbook); deferred to land **after Phase 3 layout** so the eventual fuzz surface is more stable, with a 30-day no-new-crashes gate before the v1.0 tag. Phase A-D's regression corpus + threat-model coverage (215+ security tests) remains the primary defense in the interim.
**Last updated:** 2026-05-20 (**Phase 3 Task 15 L10 + post-PR-#70 review hardening — 6 findings + performance refactor + 3 Copilot review comments on top of the L10 `order` Hello World**. Roland's review of [PR #70](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/70) surfaced 6 findings (2 P2, 4 P3) + a performance recommendation; Copilot added 3 more concerns (stale align-self bullet, cancellation token, cref-to-extension). **F#1 (P2) — sink-order emission test.** Pre-fix the L10 unit tests only asserted final offsets; the emission order to the sink (= PDF painting order per CSS Display §3) was untested. **Fix:** new `L10_hardening_order_affects_sink_emission_order_for_painting` test asserts items with orders [2, 0, -1] emit to the sink in [c, b, a] order — protecting painting behavior if a future refactor decouples positioning from emission. **F#2 (P2) — pre-measure auto-height wrap test.** Pre-fix the L10 wrap test used explicit height, so `PreMeasureFlexMultiLineCrossExtent`'s line-packing path was bypassed. **Fix:** new `L10_hardening_order_with_auto_height_wrap_pre_measure_packs_in_effective_order` test uses `height: auto` on the wrapper + asserts wrapper BlockSize matches the SUM of effective-order line cross-extents + the following-sibling lands at that wrapper's bottom edge. Verifies pre-measure parity with the layout pass when `order` is in play. **F#3 (P3) — NumberResolver `order` tests.** Pre-fix the only `order` coverage was through the FlexLayouter layout assertions. **Fix:** 3 parametric tests in `NumberResolverTests` pin: `Order_accepts_signed_integer` (5 InlineData rows: -100, -1, 0, 2, 100); `Order_rejects_decimal` (1.5, -0.5, 3.14 → invalid); `Order_rejects_value_with_unit` (1px, 2em, 5% → invalid). Validates the cascade-side contract independent of the layout assertions. **F#4 (P3) — stale FlexLayouter xmldoc.** The class-level docs listed "align-self per-item override" as L4+ deferred (shipped in L9) + "No order property handling" (shipped in L10). PackLines + FlexLine docs still described `FirstItemIndex` as a DOM-children index (L10 changed it to a sorted-sequence position). **Fix:** updated all three sites — class-level Cycle 1 simplifications now reference L8/L9/L10 shipping; PackLines doc clarifies the L10 sorted-sequence semantics; FlexLine doc updated to "POSITION in `_sortedFlexChildIndices`, NOT a DOM-children index" + drops the per-item IsBlockLevel skip note (sorted sequence is pre-filtered). **F#5 (P3) — deferrals.md stale align-self.** The L10 commit accidentally re-introduced `align-self` as a Missing feature at line 1060 despite L9 shipping it. **Fix:** restored the post-L9 "shipped" annotation + added a cross-reference note. **F#6 (P3) — PROGRESS.md test counts + diff stats.** Pre-fix the L10 entry said "4588 unit / 4719 solution-wide" but GitHub reports 4589/4720; diff stats said "5 files / ~870 / ~80" but GitHub reports 8 files / 750 / 182. **Fix:** corrected the numbers + file count inline. **Performance refactor: cache `(domIndex, order)` in sort.** Pre-fix `GetFlexChildrenInOrderSequence`'s sort comparator called `ReadOrder()` (= a cascade slot lookup) on every comparison, producing O(n log n) cascade lookups during sort for large flex containers. **Fix:** the helper now reads each item's order ONCE during the initial scan + carries the `(domIndex, order)` pair in a tuple list; the comparator only touches the cached int fields + the int DOM index. Reduces order reads from O(n log n) to O(n) without changing the public contract. **Copilot review notes addressed:** (a) `CancellationToken` parameter added to `GetFlexChildrenInOrderSequence`; both call sites (FlexLayouter + BlockLayouter) thread their existing token; (b) 2 `<see cref="Boxes.Box.GetFlexChildrenInOrderSequence"/>` references corrected to `ComputedStyleLayoutExtensions.GetFlexChildrenInOrderSequence` (extension methods belong to their declaring type for cref resolution); (c) stale align-self bullet (= same as F#5). **Tests: 4593 unit / 4724 solution-wide passing + 6 skipped** (+4 unit / +4 solution-wide over PR #70 baseline at 4589 / 4720 — 2 new FlexLayouterTests hardening tests + 3 new NumberResolverTests parametric tests with 11 InlineData rows total). All 4 gates green: build (0 warnings, 0 errors), test, AOT/JIT byte-parity (4/4), `git diff --check` clean. **Diff:** ~8 files changed, ~640 insertions, ~110 deletions. Active-task pointer unchanged: Task 15 L11 next per Phase 3 plan (`flex` shorthand OR §9.7 step-4 min/max clamping OR `wrap-reverse` proper implementation OR proper `<baseline-position>` alignment).)

**Phase 3 Task 15 L10 Hello World shipped — `order` property per CSS Flexbox L1 §5.4** (historical entry; superseded by Task 15 L10 + post-PR-#70 review hardening above).

**Original L10 hardening detail (preserved for traceability):**. Continues from Task 15 L9 + post-PR-#69 review hardening ([PR #69](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/69) merged at `cc1b152`). Per CSS Flexbox §5.4 the `order` property changes the visual order of flex items WITHOUT modifying the DOM — items with lower order pack earlier on the main axis; items with equal order preserve DOM order (stable sort). Negative values are valid + place items before the default-0 items. **Implementation:** new `order` Integer property (default 0, applies_to FlexItems) in `properties.json`. New `ReadOrder` extension on `ComputedStyle` returns the cascaded integer (defensive fallback to 0 for non-Integer slots). New `GetFlexChildrenInOrderSequence` extension on `Boxes.Box` returns the block-level child indices in effective flex order via a two-key stable comparer (order asc, DOM index asc). Fast-path short-circuits to DOM order when no item declares a non-zero order — preserving L1-L9 behavior verbatim. **FlexLayouter refactor:** `PackLines` signature gained a `sortedChildIndices` parameter; the body walks the sorted sequence instead of building blockLevelIndices inline. `FlexLine.FirstItemIndex` semantics changed — now a POSITION in the sorted sequence (NOT a DOM-children index). The emission loop + `ResolveFlexibleMainSizes` + the LineMainSize-recompute loop all dereference via `_sortedFlexChildIndices[firstItemIndex + i]`. Non-block-level skip filter removed (the sorted sequence is pre-filtered). New `_sortedFlexChildIndices` instance field on FlexLayouter populated once per AttemptLayout entry. **BlockLayouter refactor:** `PreMeasureFlexMultiLineCrossExtent` walks `flexContainer.GetFlexChildrenInOrderSequence()` instead of `flexContainer.Children` directly — guarantees pre-measure line-boundary parity with the layout pass (same shared-helper pattern as the L8 F#1 hardening's `ResolveFlexItemHypotheticalMainSize`). **L1-L9 backward compat:** every existing FlexLayouter test (157 of 157 pre-L10 + 2 skipped) passes unchanged because items without explicit order get the cascade default 0 → `GetFlexChildrenInOrderSequence` short-circuits to DOM order → same iteration sequence as pre-L10. The refactor is purely a representation change for the L1-L9 surface. Tests: **4588 unit / 4719 solution-wide passing + 6 skipped** (+7 unit / +7 solution-wide over PR #69 baseline at 4581 / 4712 — 6 new unit tests + 1 new production-pipeline test).
