**Phase 3 Task 15 L9 + post-PR-#69 review hardening — 5 findings + architecture recommendation on top of the L9 align-self Hello World** (historical entry; superseded by Task 15 L10 Hello World above).

**Original L9 hardening detail (preserved for traceability):**. Roland's review of [PR #69](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/69) surfaced 5 findings (1 P1, 3 P2, 1 P3) plus an architecture recommendation to extract a shared self-position decoder. **F#1 (P1) — `align-self` added to `KnownDroppedProperties`.** Pre-fix, the L9 production tests only exercised the bare `align-self: flex-end` value because AngleSharp.Css drops the compound `safe X` / `unsafe X` forms for align-self (same precedent as justify-content / align-items / align-content). The safe-center test bypassed the CSS parser via `ComputedSlot.FromKeyword(14)` direct injection — so the production recovery path was unproven. **Fix:** added `"align-self"` to `CssPreprocessor.KnownDroppedProperties.Set` next to the four sibling alignment properties. 2 new production-pipeline tests prove the recovery: `L9_hardening_production_html_align_self_safe_center_overflow_recovers_through_cascade` (safe modifier forces safe-start fallback on cross-axis overflow); `L9_hardening_production_html_align_self_unsafe_flex_end_overflow_recovers_through_cascade` (unsafe modifier honors flex-end → natural -50 offset). **F#2 (P2) — pin all 28 align-self keyword IDs in `KeywordResolverTests`.** Pre-fix the 28-entry `BuildAlignSelfTable` was only exercised by the few hard-coded indices in FlexLayouter unit tests; a refactor that reordered the table would silently break `ReadAlignSelf`. **Fix:** new `AlignSelf_keyword_ids_are_pinned` test covers all 28 IDs (0=auto, 1-3 bare values, 4-6 baseline triple, 7-13 self-positions, 14-20 safe X, 21-27 unsafe X). Companion `AlignSelf_rejects_left_and_right_keywords` test pins that align-self uses `<self-position>` grammar (per CSS Align §6.2) and rejects the directional `left` / `right` keywords (which belong to `<content-position>` only). **F#3 (P2) — unsafe overflow tests for align-self.** Pre-fix only `safe center` overflow was tested; the symmetric `unsafe X` path was untested at the align-self call site. **Fix:** 2 new unit tests `L9_hardening_align_self_unsafe_center_overflow_honors_natural_negative_offset` (= natural -25 offset) + `L9_hardening_align_self_unsafe_flex_end_overflow_honors_alignment` (= natural -50 offset). **F#4 (P3) — stale `ReadAlignItems` xmldoc.** Pre-fix the L3 xmldoc still listed "align-self per-item override" as an L4+ deferral despite L9 shipping it. **Fix:** updated the L10+ deferrals paragraph to leave only baseline + anchor-center as the remaining fallback families. **F#5 (P3) — PROGRESS.md diff stats.** Pre-fix the L9 entry said "4 files changed, ~625 insertions, ~10 deletions" but GitHub reports 6 / 654 / 22. **Fix:** corrected the stats + listed the 6 file paths inline. **Architecture refactor: shared `DecodeSelfPositionGrid` helper.** Pre-fix `ReadAlignItems` and `ReadAlignSelf` held duplicate switch tables (27 entries vs. 28 entries with a +1 offset for align-self's leading `auto`). **Fix:** extracted `DecodeSelfPositionGrid(int keyword) → (AlignItemsValue, OverflowAlignmentMode)` as a private static helper next to `ReadAlignItems`. `ReadAlignItems` calls it directly + wraps in `ResolvedAlignItems`. `ReadAlignSelf` special-cases index 0 (= auto) + calls the shared helper with `keyword - 1` + converts AlignItemsValue → AlignSelfValue via a small mapping helper. **Phase 3 Task 15 L9 Hello World shipped — `align-self` per-item alignment override** (historical entry; superseded by Task 15 L9 + post-PR-#69 review hardening above; merged at `665e3ae` was the PR #68 baseline, this hardening continues on the PR #69 branch).

**Phase 3 Task 15 L9 Hello World original detail:**. Continues from Task 15 L8 + post-PR-#68 review hardening ([PR #68](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/68) merged at `665e3ae`). L1-L8 implemented every flex primitive except per-item alignment override (= align-self): justify-content (L2), align-items (L3), flex-direction column + reverse (L4-L5), flex-wrap (L6), align-content (L7), the flexibility algorithm (L8). Per CSS Box Alignment L3 §4.3 "If the value of align-self is auto, its used value is the value of align-items on the parent" — the L1-L8 behavior IS the auto case. **Implementation:** new `AlignSelfValue` enum (Auto / FlexStart / FlexEnd / Center / Stretch) + `ResolvedAlignSelf` record-struct (Value, Mode) + `ReadAlignSelf` extension decode the 28-entry `BuildAlignSelfTable` (auto / normal / stretch / anchor-center / baseline triple / 7 self-positions / 7 safe+self-positions / 7 unsafe+self-positions). The reader mirrors `ReadAlignItems`' decoder shape but adds the auto variant at index 0; baseline / anchor-center / baseline-triple approximate to Stretch (= the same approximation as align-items pending L10+ intrinsic-sizing integration). New `ResolveAgainstContainerAlignItems` extension method on `ResolvedAlignSelf` folds the per-item value into the effective `ResolvedAlignItems` tuple passed to the existing `ComputeAlignItemsPlacement` helper: when align-self is Auto, returns the container's (value, mode) unchanged; else converts the AlignSelfValue → AlignItemsValue + uses the item's own overflow mode. **FlexLayouter integration:** at the per-item placement site (in the emission loop's cross-axis math), `var alignSelf = item.Style.ReadAlignSelf();` + `var effectiveAlign = alignSelf.ResolveAgainstContainerAlignItems(alignItems);` replaces the L1-L8 direct read of the container's alignItems. The L1-L8 tests pass unchanged because every item without an explicit align-self gets Auto → falls back to alignItems → the same effective tuple as before. **Phase 3 Task 15 L8 + post-PR-#68 review hardening — 5 findings on top of the L8 flex-grow/shrink/basis Hello World** (historical entry; superseded by Task 15 L9 Hello World above; merged at `665e3ae`).

**Original L8 hardening detail (preserved for traceability):** Roland's review of PR #68 surfaced 5 findings on top of the L8 flex-grow/shrink/basis Hello World. Roland's review of [PR #68](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/68) surfaced 5 findings (1 P1, 3 P2, 1 P3) plus an architecture recommendation for a shared FlexItemSizing model. **F#1 (P1) — wrap line packing now uses flex-basis-driven hypothetical main-size.** Pre-fix, `PackLines` (FlexLayouter) and `PreMeasureFlexMultiLineCrossExtent` (BlockLayouter) both used `ReadLengthPxOrZero(mainProp)` for the per-item contribution to wrap-boundary decisions; the L8 §9.7 algorithm THEN used a flex-basis-driven hypothetical in `ResolveFlexibleMainSizes` so the layout-pass sizes differed from the line-packing-pass sizes. Concretely: 3 items with `width: 300; flex-basis: 0; flex-grow: 1` in a 300px wrap container packed into 3 separate lines (because PackLines saw width=300) but each line then had only one item to grow to 300 (= the spec-correct end-state SHOULD be one line of 3 items × 100px each). **Fix:** extracted `ResolveFlexItemHypotheticalMainSize` to a shared extension on `Boxes.Box` (next to `ReadFlexGrow` / `ReadFlexShrink` / `ReadFlexBasis`); both layouters now call it. PackLines + the BlockLayouter pre-measure pack the same lines the §9.7 pass distributes across. The architecture recommendation for a broader `FlexItemSizing` struct unification is L9+ scope; the extension method is the minimum surface that closes the line-boundary drift. New tests pin the fix (`L8_hardening_wrap_with_flex_basis_zero_packs_into_single_line`, `L8_hardening_wrap_with_flex_basis_length_overrides_width_for_packing`, `L8_hardening_wrap_with_flex_basis_percentage_drives_line_packing`, `L8_hardening_pre_measure_and_layout_pack_into_same_lines_with_flex_basis`). **F#2 (P2) — fractional flex-grow sum &lt; 1.** Pre-fix, the grow distribution divided by `sumFlexGrow` unconditionally, so 2 items with `flex-grow: .25` each (sumFlexGrow = .5) each received `(.25 / .5) * freeSpace = 50% of freeSpace` — consuming 100% of free space. Per CSS Flexbox L1 §9.7 when sumFlexGrow &lt; 1, items take only `sumFlexGrow * freeSpace` total (= the literal fraction); the remainder stays as alignment-axis free-space for justify-content. **Fix:** divisor is now `max(sumFlexGrow, 1)`. New test `L8_hardening_fractional_flex_grow_sum_below_one_only_takes_fraction` pins 2 items at .25/.25 in 400px (200 hypothetical, 200 free) → each grows to 150 (= 0.25 * 200 added), leaving 100 for justify-content. **F#3 (P2) — negative flex-basis invalidation.** Pre-fix, `flex-basis: -10px` / `-10%` resolved successfully through LengthResolver (because FlexBasis joined the resolver dispatch in L8 without joining `NonNegativeProperties`), then floored silently at the layout `ResolveHypotheticalMainSize` helper. Per CSS Flexbox §7.2 + Sizing §5 negative values are spec-invalid. **Fix:** added `PropertyId.FlexBasis` to `NonNegativeProperties.Set` so the LengthResolver path now emits CSS-PROPERTY-VALUE-INVALID-001 + the cascade falls back to the property's initial value (`auto`). New tests `Flex_basis_rejects_negative_length` / `Flex_basis_rejects_negative_percentage` / `Flex_basis_accepts_zero_length` in LengthResolverTests + `L8_hardening_negative_flex_basis_length_is_invalid_falls_back_to_auto` in FlexLayouterTests (= defense-in-depth pin that layout's floor-at-0 still works if a buggy upstream resolver delivers a negative slot). **F#4 (P2) — flex-basis: content honesty.** Pre-fix, the `Content` variant was preserved on `ResolvedFlexBasis` but the FlexLayouter delegated it to the same path as `Auto` (= read the declared main-size) — a silent approximation per spec §7.2.1 which says Content forces the intrinsic content size REGARDLESS of declared width/height. **Fix:** explicit known-gap pin (`L8_hardening_known_gap_flex_basis_content_approximates_to_auto`) documenting that an item with `width: 200; flex-basis: content` currently produces a hypothetical of 200 (= the declared width via the Content → Auto approximation); spec-correct would be 0 (= intrinsic content size of an item with no children). When L9+ wires intrinsic sizing through BlockLayouter pre-measure, the test should flip. XML doc on `FlexBasisKind.Content` updated to make the approximation loud. **F#5 (P3) — test coverage gaps.** Added: 3 wrap+flex-basis tests; 1 fractional-grow test; 1 content-known-gap pin; 1 row-reverse-with-flex-grow direction-parity test; 1 heterogeneous-shrink test exercising the proportional-shrink math; 1 negative-flex-basis defense-in-depth pin; 1 pre-measure × layout line-packing parity test; 2 production-pipeline tests (`L8_hardening_production_html_flex_shrink_absorbs_overflow`, `L8_hardening_production_html_flex_basis_percentage_drives_size`); 3 LengthResolver negative-basis tests. **Copilot review notes addressed:** (a) PropertyResolverDispatch.cs "dimension family has 5 members" → updated to "all six" + clarified the FlexBasis joining + the F#3 hardening; (b) FlexLayouter.cs LineMainSize-recompute inner-loop cancellation token added per the low-confidence note; (c) ResolveHypotheticalMainSize's `containerMainSize <= 0` guard relaxed to `!IsFinite` only — definite 0 is now treated as valid (percentage of 0 = 0) per the low-confidence note. **Tests: 4566 unit / 4697 solution-wide passing + 6 skipped** (+12 unit / +12 solution-wide over PR #68 baseline at 4554 / 4685 — 9 new unit tests + 3 LengthResolver tests; 2 new production tests counted in the unit total). All 4 gates green: build (0 warnings, 0 errors), test, AOT/JIT byte-parity, `git diff --check` clean. **Diff:** 8 files changed, ~870 insertions, ~50 deletions. **`docs/deferrals.md` updated:** L9+ scope clarified — the shared `FlexItemSizing` struct unification is a broader L9+ refactor; the `ResolveFlexItemHypotheticalMainSize` extension is the L8 hardening minimum. Active-task pointer advances to **Task 15 L9** (`align-self` OR `order` OR `flex` shorthand OR §9.7 step-4 min/max clamping OR intrinsic flex-basis: content) OR begin **Task 16+** (Grid layouter per Phase 3 plan).)

**Original Task 15 L8 Hello World shipped — `flex-grow` / `flex-shrink` / `flex-basis` (the flexibility algorithm)** (historical entry; superseded by Task 15 L8 + post-PR-#68 review hardening above; the Hello World work is in [PR #68](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/68), this hardening updates the same branch in-place.). Continues from Task 15 L7 + post-PR-#67 review hardening ([PR #67](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/67) merged at `37eb6e6`). L1-L7 implemented item placement (justify-content + align-items + align-content), the 4 flex-direction variants, multi-line wrap, and cross-axis line distribution — but items always used their declared widths as the main-axis size. CSS Flexbox L1 §7 + §9.7 specifies the flexibility algorithm that distributes free space among items via the `flex-grow` / `flex-shrink` factors with `flex-basis` as the input — this is the foundation of "flexible box layout." **Implementation:** the cascade-side `flex-grow` (Number type, default 0) + `flex-shrink` (Number type, default 1) properties are already in `properties.json` and resolve through `NumberResolver`. L8 wires the `flex-basis` (`FlexBasis` type, default `auto`) property through `LengthResolver` by joining the dimension family in `PropertyResolverDispatch` — the resolver admits `auto` (KeywordIdAuto = 0) + `content` (new KeywordIdContent = 1) keywords + the generic `<length-percentage>` production per §7.2. Three new reader extensions (`ReadFlexGrow` / `ReadFlexShrink` / `ReadFlexBasis`) decode the Number / Number / typed `ResolvedFlexBasis` slots. New `FlexBasisKind` enum (`Auto` / `Content` / `LengthPx` / `Percentage`) + `ResolvedFlexBasis` record-struct (Kind, Value) mirror the L2/L3/L7 resolved-* patterns. **Algorithm:** new `ResolveFlexibleMainSizes` helper runs between `PackLines` and the per-line emission loop. Per line: (1) compute each item's hypothetical main-size from its `flex-basis` (Auto/Content → ReadLengthPxOrZero, LengthPx → use directly, Percentage → resolve against container main-size); (2) compute `freeMainSpace = containerMainSize - sum(hypothetical)`; (3) if positive AND any item has `flex-grow > 0`, each item grows by `(item.flexGrow / sumFlexGrow) * freeMainSpace`; (4) if negative AND any item has `flex-shrink > 0`, each item shrinks by `(item.flexShrink * hypothetical / sumScaledShrinks) * |freeMainSpace|`; (5) otherwise items keep hypothetical sizes. Resolved sizes are stored in a `double[]` indexed by child index in `_rootBox.Children`; the emission loop reads `resolvedItemMainSizes[itemIdx]` instead of `ReadLengthPxOrZero(mainSizeProperty)`. After resolution each line's `LineMainSize` is updated to the sum of resolved sizes so `justify-content`'s `freeSpace = containerMainSize - line.LineMainSize` calculation sees the post-flex layout. Min/max-width clamping per §9.7 step 4 is L9+ scope; the L8 algorithm distributes free space in a single pass without iteration. **Existing-test retrofit:** the 9 L1-L7 overflow tests (6 L2 justify-content overflow tests + 1 L5 row-reverse overflow test + 1 L6 single-oversized-item test + 2 L2 production overflow tests) pre-dated L8 and assumed items never shrink. Post-L8 the cascade default `flex-shrink: 1` would shrink items to fit, defeating the overflow assertions. Retrofitted each test with explicit `flex-shrink: 0` on every item — preserves the pre-L8 "items never shrink" behavior + the overflow assertions unchanged. Same pattern as the L7 retrofit that added `align-content: flex-start` to L6 tests. The `LayoutNItemsWithJustifyContent` helper sets `flex-shrink: 0` by default (covers 7 of the 9 retrofitted tests with a single change); the L5 + L6 + 2 production tests opted in individually. **Tests: 4554 unit / 4685 solution-wide passing + 6 skipped** (+13 unit / +13 solution-wide over PR #67 baseline at 4541 / 4672 — 12 new unit tests + 1 new production-pipeline test). All 4 gates green: build (0 warnings, 0 errors), test, AOT/JIT byte-parity, `git diff --check` clean. **New unit tests** in `FlexLayouterTests` (12): `L8_flex_grow_distributes_positive_free_space_proportionally` (3 items × flex-grow:1 in 600px); `L8_flex_grow_weighted_distributes_proportionally` (grow values 1/2/3 → final sizes 150/200/250); `L8_flex_grow_zero_items_do_not_grow` (grow values 1/0/1 → only growable items absorb the free space); `L8_flex_grow_no_growable_items_keeps_natural_sizes` (sumFlexGrow == 0 → grow branch skipped, free space falls through to justify-content); `L8_flex_shrink_absorbs_negative_free_space_proportionally` (3 items × 300 in 600 → each shrinks to 200); `L8_flex_shrink_zero_items_do_not_shrink` (shrink values 1/0/1 → only shrinkable items absorb the deficit); `L8_flex_basis_explicit_length_overrides_declared_width` (flex-basis: 100 overrides width: 50); `L8_flex_basis_zero_with_grow_one_equally_fills_container` (the canonical `flex: 1 1 0` recipe — items equally partition regardless of declared widths); `L8_flex_basis_percentage_resolves_against_container_main_size` (flex-basis: 25% in 600 container → hypothetical 150); `L8_flex_basis_auto_delegates_to_declared_width` (flex-basis: auto delegates to width property — sanity); `L8_flex_grow_column_direction_distributes_along_block_axis` (direction parity — grow distributes on block axis when flex-direction: column); `L8_known_gap_min_width_does_not_clamp_resolved_size_yet` (PIN — §9.7 step 4 min/max clamping is L9+ scope; current behavior produces 200 even when min-width: 250; will flip to 250 when clamp lands). **New production test** `L8_production_html_flex_grow_one_equally_partitions_container` exercises `flex-grow: 1` + `flex-basis: 0` (longhand for the canonical `flex: 1` recipe) through the full HTML → cascade → layout pipeline — 3 items in a 600px container equally partition to 200px each. **Diff:** 6 files changed, ~620 insertions, ~30 deletions. **`docs/deferrals.md` updated:** flex-grow/shrink/basis removed from the Missing list (now shipped). New deferrals added for the L9+ scope: the `flex` shorthand parser; `min-content` / `max-content` / `fit-content` intrinsic flex-basis keywords; the §9.7 step-4 min/max clamping iteration; cross-axis flexibility (= align-items stretch with intrinsic cross-axis sizing); the `align-self` per-item override. **Flex L9+ scope (updated):** the `flex` shorthand (`flex: 1` longhand-equivalent `flex: 1 1 0`); intrinsic flex-basis keywords; §9.7 step-4 min/max clamping; `align-self`; `order` (PackLines pre-sort); `flex-wrap: wrap-reverse` proper implementation; multi-page flex split; inline-flex-item anonymous wrapping; **BlockLayouter explicit-width honoring** (F#2 from PR #64); writing-mode/direction integration (F#1 from PR #65); cross-axis margins + auto-margins. Active-task pointer advances to **Task 15 L9** (`align-self` OR `order` OR `flex` shorthand OR `wrap-reverse` proper implementation OR §9.7 step-4 min/max clamping) OR begin **Task 16+** (Grid layouter per Phase 3 plan).)

**Phase 3 Task 15 L7 + post-PR-#67 review hardening — 10 findings on top of the L7 align-content Hello World** (historical entry; superseded by Task 15 L8 Hello World above; merged at `37eb6e6`). Roland's review of [PR #67](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/67) surfaced 10 findings (2 P1, 5 P2, 3 P3) plus a wording correction (F#5). **F#1 (P1) — single-line gate corrected.** Pre-fix, `ComputeAlignContentOffsets` short-circuited on `lineCount <= 1`. Per CSS Flexbox L1 §9.4 a flex container is "single-line" iff `flex-wrap: nowrap` — NOT iff `flex-wrap: wrap` produced exactly one line. A wrapping container whose content happens to fit on one line is still a multi-line container, and align-content still applies (the default `normal → stretch` from §8.4 stretches that single line to fill the container). **Fix:** gate is now `lineCount == 0 || !isWrapping`. New test `L7_hardening_wrap_container_with_single_line_stretches_per_spec` pins the fix. **F#2 (P1) — per-mode overflow handling.** Pre-fix, the overflow branch returned `(0,0,0)` for all values regardless of overflow modifier. Per CSS Box Alignment L3 §5.3 + the L2 hardening precedent: `safe X` falls back to safe-start; `unsafe X` honors natural (possibly-negative) offset; default mode gives distribution values + stretch the safe-start fallback while positional values keep their natural offset. **Fix:** mirrors the `ComputeJustifyContentOffsets` pattern — compute natural offset for the value, then if `freeCrossSpace < 0` branch on mode + value family. New tests pin all three modes: `L7_hardening_default_center_overflow_keeps_natural_negative_offset` (replaces the original L7 `L7_align_content_overflow_falls_back_to_flex_start` which pinned wrong behavior); `L7_hardening_default_space_between_overflow_falls_back_to_flex_start`; `L7_hardening_safe_center_overflow_falls_back_to_flex_start`; `L7_hardening_unsafe_center_overflow_keeps_natural_negative_offset`. **F#3 (P2) — production CSS recovery for compound align-content.** Pre-fix, AngleSharp.Css 1.0.0-beta.144 drops `align-content: safe center` / `unsafe flex-end` compound declarations before they reach KeywordResolver — same precedent as `justify-content` / `align-items`. **Fix:** added `align-content` to `CssPreprocessor.KnownDroppedProperties` so the recovery path through ScanDeclarations preserves the raw declaration text. New parametric KeywordResolver test `Align_content_accepts_compound_keywords` (13 InlineData rows) covers `space-*`, `stretch`, the baseline triple, and 6 safe/unsafe compound forms. **F#4 (P3) — cancellation in line-distribution loops.** Pre-fix, the sum-cross-extents foreach + the stretch-addend mutation for-loop didn't check `cancellationToken`. **Fix:** added `cancellationToken.ThrowIfCancellationRequested()` inside both loops so very-large hostile flex inputs exit promptly between packing and distribution. **F#5 — docs/progress wording corrected.** Pre-fix, PROGRESS.md / deferrals.md said L7 "ships in full" with overflow refinement deferred to L8+ AND said stretch grows lines "proportionally." Both statements were inaccurate post-fix: F#2 now implements per-mode overflow (so the L8+ deferral closes); stretch grows lines by an EQUAL share of free-space (= `freeCrossSpace / lineCount` per line), not "proportionally" (which would imply weighted by some other quantity). **Fix:** PROGRESS.md + deferrals.md reworded — stretch is "equally," overflow refinement is L7-complete (not L8+). **F#6 (P2) — `<baseline-position>` keyword family.** Pre-fix, `BuildAlignContentTable` produced a 26-entry table mirroring `justify-content`, omitting the three `<baseline-position>` keywords that CSS Box Alignment L3 §6.3 admits for align-content (same as align-items). Authoring `align-content: baseline` invalidated to `normal → stretch` silently. **Fix:** BuildAlignContentTable expanded to 29 entries (added `baseline` / `first baseline` / `last baseline` at indices 5-7); `ReadAlignContent` maps all three to Stretch (the safe approximation — proper baseline alignment is text-shaping integration, L8+ scope). All keyword indices renumbered downstream — KeywordResolverTests `AlignContent_keyword_ids_are_pinned` test pins all 29 IDs; existing L7 tests updated for the new positional-keyword indices (5→8, 8→11, 9→12, etc.). New smoke test `L7_hardening_baseline_keyword_resolves_to_stretch_approximation` exercises baseline → stretch through the layout. **F#7 (P2) — column-direction proof.** Pre-fix, 100% of L7 tests were row-direction. **Fix:** 3 new column-direction tests verify align-content distributes lines along the INLINE axis when `flex-direction: column`: `L7_align_content_column_direction_stretch_grows_lines_along_inline_axis`; `L7_align_content_column_direction_center_centers_lines_inline`; `L7_align_content_column_direction_space_between_distributes_along_inline`. **F#8 (P2) — align-items × align-content interaction.** Pre-fix, no tests pinned how stretched lines (from align-content: stretch) interact with align-items on auto-cross-size items. **Fix:** 2 new interaction tests — `L7_align_content_stretch_with_align_items_center_auto_items_stay_at_natural_size` (positional align-items + auto items stay at natural cross-size, centered within the stretched line); `L7_align_content_stretch_with_align_items_stretch_auto_items_grow_to_stretched_line` (align-items: stretch + auto items grow to the stretched line's cross-extent, per the L3 post-PR-#63 IsCrossSizeAuto detection). **F#9 (P2) — wrap-reverse × align-content interaction.** Pre-fix, no tests pinned that align-content still applies when `flex-wrap: wrap-reverse` triggers the L6 hardening approximation diagnostic. **Fix:** new test `L7_align_content_wrap_reverse_emits_diagnostic_and_applies_distribution` verifies (a) the `LAYOUT-FLEX-WRAP-REVERSE-APPROXIMATED-001` diagnostic still fires; (b) align-content distribution still applies on top of the wrap approximation. Cross-axis line-stacking reversal remains L8+ scope (documented in the test). **F#10 (P3) — NaN/Infinity defensive guard.** Pre-fix, a non-finite `freeCrossSpace` from upstream geometry blow-up would propagate NaN through stretchAddend → BoxFragment offsets. **Fix:** explicit `!double.IsFinite(freeCrossSpace)` check at the top of `ComputeAlignContentOffsets`; non-finite values fall back to safe-start `(0,0,0)`. **Source-code cleanup:** `using System.Collections.Generic;` added to FlexLayouter.cs — fully-qualified `System.Collections.Generic.List<T>` references replaced. The `lineCount <= 1` short-circuit collapsed into `lineCount == 0 || !isWrapping` (the spec-correct gate). **Phase 3 Task 15 L7 Hello World shipped — `align-content` multi-line cross-axis alignment** (historical entry; superseded by Task 15 L7 + post-PR-#67 review hardening above; the Hello World work is in [PR #67](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/67), this hardening updates the same branch in-place.) Continues from Task 15 L6 + post-PR-#66 review hardening ([PR #66](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/66) merged at `5e70d7c`). L6 introduced multi-line flex via `flex-wrap: wrap` but stacked lines at cross-start at natural sizes (= effectively `flex-start` approximation per the PR #66 F#3 deferral). L7 closes that deferral by adding the full `align-content` property pipeline. **Implementation:** new `align-content` property in `properties.json` (Keyword type, default `normal`); new `BuildAlignContentTable()` in `KeywordResolver` produces a 26-entry table mirroring `justify-content` (0=normal, 1-4=ContentDistributions {space-between, space-around, space-evenly, stretch}, 5-11=ContentPositions {center, start, end, flex-start, flex-end, left, right}, 12-18=safe X, 19-25=unsafe X). New `AlignContentValue` enum (FlexStart/FlexEnd/Center/SpaceBetween/SpaceAround/SpaceEvenly/Stretch) + `ResolvedAlignContent` record-struct (Value, Mode) + `ReadAlignContent()` extension mirror the L2 `ResolvedJustifyContent` / L3 `ResolvedAlignItems` patterns. **Spec-default behavior:** `normal` resolves to `Stretch` per CSS Flexbox §8.4 — line cross-extents grow by an equal share of the free cross-space (= `freeCrossSpace / lineCount` per line) when sum of natural extents < container cross-extent. (Post-PR-#67 F#5 — original wording said "proportionally," which incorrectly implied weighted distribution; the spec defines equal-share growth.) **Algorithm:** new `ComputeAlignContentOffsets` helper returns `(startOffset, betweenSpacing, stretchAddend)`. FlexLayouter applies stretchAddend BEFORE the per-line emission loop by mutating each `FlexLine.LineCrossSize` (items within a stretched line use the larger cross-extent for align-items per spec). startOffset advances the lineCrossCursor; betweenSpacing extends it after each emitted line. For overflow (freeCrossSpace ≤ 0) the early return falls back to flex-start (= safe-start fallback regardless of mode — refinement deferred to L8+). **Single-line nowrap containers:** unchanged — align-content has no effect (only one line, no distribution). **Phase 3 Task 15 L6 + post-PR-#66 review hardening — 6 findings on top of the L6 flex-wrap: wrap Hello World** (historical entry; superseded by Task 15 L7 Hello World above; [PR #66](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/66) merged at `5e70d7c`.) Roland's review of PR #66 surfaced 6 findings (2 P1, 3 P2, 1 P3). **F#1 (P1) — column-wrap pagination over-reserved.** Pre-fix, the L6 skip-main-extent-grow prevented the WRAPPER from growing past declared height, but the outer BlockLayouter's `MeasureSubtreeVisualBlockExtent` walked children as block-flow and reserved the un-wrapped sum (e.g., 240px for 4×60px items in `height: 150px` column-wrap). Outer cursor + pagination used the over-measure → siblings landed too low, false page breaks. **Fix:** mirror the L3 row pre-measure's `subtreeBlockExtent` clamp at both BlockLayouter flex dispatch sites — when column+wrap+explicit-LengthPx-height, clamp `subtreeBlockExtent` to the wrapper's `borderBoxBlockSize`. Predicate is strictly narrower than the existing row clamp (only fires for known absolute pixel heights — Percentage column-wrap will surface in a follow-up if needed). 2 new tests pin sibling positioning + near-page-boundary clean emission. **F#2 (P1) — production wrap test masked BlockLayouter explicit-width bug.** The L6 production test set `contentInlineSize: 250` matching the declared `width: 250px` — artificially narrowed the fragmentainer to make wrap activate. On a real 600px page, `.flex { width: 250px; flex-wrap: wrap; }` doesn't wrap (4×100px all fit in the 600px wrapper) because BlockLayouter doesn't honor declared `width` on block containers (= the pre-existing `BlockLayouter-flex-explicit-width` deferral from PR #64 F#2). **Fix:** new `L6_hardening_known_gap_narrow_flex_in_wide_page_does_not_wrap_yet` production test uses the default 600px page width with `width: 250px` flex; pins the current incomplete behavior (all 4 items on one line at BlockOffset 0). When BlockLayouter explicit-width support lands, this test should flip to assert the spec-correct 2 lines. Added cross-reference in the existing `BlockLayouter-flex-explicit-width` deferral entry. **F#3 (P2) — align-content default behavior + property not actually parsed.** Pre-fix the deferrals.md claimed `align-content` was "parsed and carried by the cascade" — but `align-content` is NOT in `properties.json`/`KeywordResolver`. CSS Flexbox `align-content`'s initial value is `stretch`, so a definite-height multi-line container should stretch line cross-sizes when sum < container. L6 approximates as `flex-start` (lines stack at natural sizes; extra space empty). **Fix:** corrected the deferrals.md bullet (`align-content` NOT yet in property pipeline; needs both properties.json+KeywordResolver entries + the stretch-lines pass; L7+ scope); new pinning test `L6_hardening_known_gap_align_content_stretch_not_implemented` locks the current flex-start approximation; FlexLayouter class XML doc updated. **F#4 (P2) — wrap-reverse silently rendered as wrap.** Pre-fix `flex-wrap: wrap-reverse` decoded successfully but rendered identically to `wrap` — silent wrong behavior. **Fix:** new diagnostic `LAYOUT-FLEX-WRAP-REVERSE-APPROXIMATED-001` (Warning severity) emitted ONCE per `AttemptLayout` invocation when WrapReverse is used. Registered in `PaginateDiagnosticCodes` + public `DiagnosticCodes` mirror + `docs/diagnostics-codes.md` registry row + 3 parity tests in `DiagnosticCodesTests` + 1 integration test verifying the diagnostic fires (and only once per layout despite multiple items). New field `_emittedWrapReverseDiagnostic` resets per AttemptLayout entry. **F#5 (P2) — wasted work + line-packing duplication.** Pre-fix BlockLayouter called `PreMeasureFlexMainExtent()` then ignored the result when `skipMainExtentGrow` was true (column+wrap+explicit-height path). Also `PackLines()` algorithm duplicated between BlockLayouter's premeasure path and FlexLayouter's emission path. **Fix:** short-circuited both dispatch sites — only call `PreMeasureFlexMainExtent` when the result will be used. Added TODO comments at both line-packing sites citing L7+ shared-helper extraction (full refactor deferred to avoid regression risk). **F#6 (P3) — stale "L6+ scope" wording.** L6 has shipped; updated 4 deferrals.md sites + 3 source-code sites to "L7+ scope". **Phase 3 Task 15 L6 Hello World shipped — `flex-wrap: wrap` multi-line layout** (historical entry; superseded by Task 15 L6 + post-PR-#66 review hardening above; the Hello World work is in [PR #66](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/66), this hardening updates the same branch in-place.) Continues from Task 15 L5 + post-PR-#65 review hardening ([PR #65](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/65) merged at `b323101`). L1-L5 implemented the single-line flex algorithm with all 4 `flex-direction` values + justify-content + align-items + stretch + overflow modes. L6 adds the multi-line algorithm per CSS Flexbox L1 §6.3 + §9.3 + §9.4: items wrap onto additional lines when they don't fit on the main axis. **Implementation:** new `FlexWrapValue` enum (NoWrap / Wrap / WrapReverse) + `ReadFlexWrap()` extension + `IsFlexWrapping()` predicate (returns true for Wrap AND WrapReverse — the latter falls through to Wrap for L6, the cross-axis line-stacking reversal is L7+ scope). FlexLayouter refactored to two-phase: (1) `PackLines()` greedy line-packing pre-pass groups items into a list of `FlexLine` records `(FirstItemIndex, ItemCount, LineMainSize, LineCrossSize)`; (2) per-line emission loop runs the existing L1-L5 single-line algorithm against EACH line. Greedy algorithm per spec: walk items, accumulate main-axis sizes; when adding the next item would exceed `containerMainSize`, commit the current line + start a new one. First item on a line ALWAYS lands even if it overflows (= the "single oversized item" rule). Per-line cross-extent = max(item cross-size on that line). Lines stack on cross axis at cross-start: `line[i]` anchored at `contentCrossOffset + sum(line[0..i-1].LineCrossSize)`. Each line's `align-items` placement targets the LINE'S cross-extent (NOT the container's full cross extent) — items in different lines align relative to their own line's max-cross-size. Per-line `justify-content` operates on the container's main-extent (= `containerMainSize`); the line's `LineMainSize` is informational. **BlockLayouter pre-measure updated:** new `PreMeasureFlexMultiLineCrossExtent` helper at both dispatch sites (outer + recursion). For row + wrap: replaces the L3 `PreMeasureFlexCrossExtent` (which finds max-item-block-size for single-line); the new helper runs the same greedy line-packing logic + returns sum(line cross-extents). For column + wrap: SKIPS the L4 `PreMeasureFlexMainExtent` grow when `height` is explicit (otherwise the grow would defeat wrap by sizing the wrapper past the declared height so all items fit in one column). For column + wrap + auto-height: falls through to the L4 main-extent path (single column, no wrap activation; the column extends to contain all items). Tests: **4498 unit / 4629 solution-wide passing + 6 skipped** (+9 unit / +9 solution-wide over post-PR-#65 baseline at 4489 / 4620 — 8 new unit tests + 1 new production-pipeline test; 6 skipped includes the pre-existing 5 + 1 from L5 hardening F#1 RTL/writing-mode pin). All 4 gates green: build (0 warnings, 0 errors), test, AOT/JIT byte-parity, `git diff --check` clean. **New unit tests** in `FlexLayouterTests`: `L6_flex_wrap_packs_items_into_two_lines_when_natural_widths_exceed_container` (4×100px in 250px → lines [0,1] + [2,3]); `L6_flex_wrap_three_items_per_line_with_remainder` (7×80px in 250px → lines of 3+3+1); `L6_flex_wrap_single_oversized_item_still_emits_on_its_line` (500px item in 100px container — emits despite overflow per spec); `L6_flex_wrap_with_justify_content_center_centers_each_line` (per-line justify-content); `L6_flex_wrap_container_auto_height_sums_line_extents` (wrapper BlockSize = sum of line cross-extents); `L6_flex_wrap_align_items_center_per_line` (varying item heights aligned per-line); `L6_flex_direction_column_flex_wrap_packs_into_columns` (column-direction wrap); `L6_flex_wrap_nowrap_default_behavior_unchanged` (sanity: default flex-wrap produces L1-L5-identical output). **New production test** `L6_production_html_flex_wrap_with_4_items_two_per_line` exercises `<div style="display: flex; flex-wrap: wrap; width: 250px;">` with 4 100px items through the full HTML → cascade → BoxBuilder → BlockLayouter → FlexLayouter pipeline. Added optional `contentInlineSize` parameter to `RenderViaFullPipelineAsync` to enable narrow-page tests for wrap scenarios. **No existing tests broke** — `flex-wrap: nowrap` is the default; `PackLines` for nowrap returns a single line containing all items with the same total main-size + max cross-size as the L1-L5 single-line algorithm. The per-line loop then runs exactly once with `line-cross-extent == container-cross-extent` (= the L1-L5 path) producing byte-identical output. All 87 L1-L5 flex tests pass unchanged. **Diff:** 6 files changed, ~1406 insertions, ~259 deletions; concentrated in FlexLayouter (two-phase refactor + PackLines + per-line emission) + BlockLayouter (new multi-line pre-measure + dispatch wiring + column-wrap skip rule) + ComputedStyleLayoutExtensions (new enum + extensions) + the 2 test files + deferrals.md. **`docs/deferrals.md` updated**: `flex-layouter-features` Missing list removed `flex-wrap: wrap`; added narrower bullets for `flex-wrap: wrap-reverse` (cross-axis line stacking reversal — L7+) and `align-content` (multi-line cross-axis alignment per CSS Box Alignment L3 §6 — L7+). Behavior section gains L6's multi-line algorithm description. **Flex L7+ scope (updated):** `flex-wrap: wrap-reverse`; `align-content` (multi-line cross-axis alignment); `flex-grow` / `flex-shrink` / `flex-basis` (flexibility computation per CSS Flexbox L1 §7-§9); `order` property; baseline alignment family; `anchor-center`; `align-self` per-item; multi-page flex split; inline-flex-item anonymous wrapping; **BlockLayouter explicit-width honoring** (F#2 from PR #64); writing-mode/direction integration (F#1 from PR #65); cross-axis margins + auto-margins; stretch with margin-box + min/max; outer-main-size + auto-margins in justify-content; writing-mode-aware logical-axis aliases. **Phase 3 Task 15 L5 Hello World + post-PR-#65 review hardening — `flex-direction: row-reverse` + `column-reverse`** (historical entry; superseded by Task 15 L6 Hello World above; [PR #65](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/65) merged at `b323101`.) Continues from Task 15 L4 + post-PR-#64 review hardening ([PR #64](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/64) merged at `b41bf4f`). L1-L4 shipped `row` + `column` (axis swap + container measurement); L5 ships the orthogonal AXIS REVERSAL completing all 4 `flex-direction` values per CSS Flexbox L1 §5.1. **Spec semantics:** "row-reverse: Same as row but main-start and main-end are swapped"; same for column-reverse. Item ORDER reverses along the main axis — last DOM item appears at the main-start edge of the container (= the original main-end edge); first DOM item at the original main-start. Cross-axis behavior is UNCHANGED — `row-reverse` still has block as cross axis; `column-reverse` still has inline as cross axis. **Minimal implementation** — a single offset-flip at the emission site rather than reversed iteration: `mainOffsetForEmission = isReverse ? (contentMainOffset + containerMainSize) - (mainCursor - contentMainOffset) - itemMainSize : mainCursor;`. The per-item math (`ComputeJustifyContentOffsets`, `ComputeAlignItemsPlacement`, stretch overrides, safe/unsafe overflow modes) is UNCHANGED. Only the final main-axis offset assigned to each fragment flips around the container's main-extent. Iteration order stays in DOM order. **Verification by example:** for 3×50px items in a 600px container with `flex-direction: row-reverse; justify-content: flex-start` (= the L5 production test fixture): cursor at 0/50/100 (= L1-L4 math); after flip, items emit at 600-0-50=550, 600-50-50=500, 600-100-50=450. So DOM item 0 lands at InlineOffset 550 (rightmost), item 1 at 500 (middle), item 2 at 450 (leftmost) — packed against the right edge in reverse DOM order. For `justify-content: center` in the same fixture: cursor at 225/275/325; flipped: 325/275/225 (centered, reverse DOM order). For `column-reverse`: same algorithm but applied to BlockOffsets. **New API:** `IsFlexReverseDirection()` predicate extension on `FlexDirectionValue`. **Pre-existing pre-measure helpers** (`PreMeasureFlexCrossExtent` row, `PreMeasureFlexMainExtent` column) work for reversed variants WITHOUT change — both gate on `IsFlexColumnDirection()` which returns true for both Column AND ColumnReverse; max/sum operations are direction-agnostic. Tests: **4483 unit / 4614 solution-wide passing** (+8 unit / +8 solution-wide over post-PR-#64 baseline at 4475 / 4606 — 7 new unit tests + 1 new production-pipeline test; 5 skipped). All 4 gates green: build (0 warnings, 0 errors), test, AOT/JIT byte-parity, `git diff --check` clean. **New unit tests** in `FlexLayouterTests`: `L5_flex_direction_row_reverse_with_flex_start_packs_at_right_edge` (3×50px in 400px container → InlineOffsets 350/300/250); `L5_flex_direction_row_reverse_with_justify_content_center_centers_cluster` (3×50px in 400px → 225/175/125 = centered visual layout in reverse DOM order); `L5_flex_direction_column_reverse_with_flex_start_packs_at_bottom` (column equivalent → BlockOffsets 350/300/250); `L5_flex_direction_column_reverse_with_justify_content_center_centers_cluster`; `L5_flex_direction_row_reverse_preserves_cross_axis_alignment` (align-items unaffected by main-axis reversal); `L5_flex_direction_row_baseline_unchanged_for_non_reverse` (sanity: row direction unchanged); `L5_flex_direction_column_baseline_unchanged_for_non_reverse` (sanity: column direction unchanged). **New production test** `L5_production_html_flex_direction_row_reverse` exercises `<div style="display: flex; flex-direction: row-reverse; width: 600px;">` with 3×50px items → InlineOffsets 550/500/450 through the full HTML → cascade → BoxBuilder → BlockLayouter → FlexLayouter pipeline. **No existing tests broke** — the offset flip is transparent for non-reverse directions (`isReverse == false` falls through to the unchanged `mainCursor` value). **Phase 3 Task 15 L4 + post-PR-#64 review hardening — 5 findings on top of the L4 flex-direction: column Hello World** (historical entry; superseded by Task 15 L5 Hello World above; [PR #64](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/64) merged at `b41bf4f`.) Roland's review of PR #64 surfaced 5 findings (2 P1, 2 P2, 1 P3). **F#1 (P1) — column auto-height wrapper sized incorrectly.** Pre-fix, the L4 column path correctly skipped the L3 row pre-measure (`PreMeasureFlexCrossExtent`) but lacked any replacement for column main-axis sizing. The wrapper's `borderBoxBlockSize` stayed at the auto-resolved default; `FlexLayouter.ConfigureEmission` received an undersized `_contentBlockSize`; `justify-content: center` on column computed `freeSpace = small - sum(item heights)` → negative → spurious overflow handling. **Fix:** new `PreMeasureFlexMainExtent` helper in BlockLayouter sums items' main-axis (block) sizes for column direction; wired into BOTH dispatch sites (outer at ~line 1391, recursion at ~line 2822). The wrapper's `borderBoxBlockSize` now grows to `max(declared, flexMainExtent + wrapper border + padding)`. 3 new pinning tests: wrapper BlockSize == sum(item heights); justify-content: center on auto-height column packs cleanly (no negative offsets); sibling lands after the full column stack. **F#2 (P1) — explicit width not honored.** Verified the bug: `BlockLayouter.cs:1138` derives `borderBoxInlineSize` from the available inline range, ignoring declared `width`. The L4 unit tests used `FragmentainerContext(contentInlineSize: 200)` matched to the declared `width: 200px`, masking the bug. New `L4_hardening_column_explicit_width_smaller_than_page_centers_correctly` test (page=600, flex.width=200, align-items: center) confirms item lands at InlineOffset=250 (= centered against 600px page) instead of the spec-correct 50 (centered against 200px). **Fix scope:** BlockLayouter width-resolution pipeline refactor is too large for L4 hardening — added `BlockLayouter-flex-explicit-width` Missing bullet to `flex-layouter-features` deferral. Per CSS Flexbox §7.2, stretch applies only to auto cross-size. **Fix:** match the canonical `IsHeightAuto` predicate — auto iff `slot.Tag is Unset or Keyword`. Percentage / SideTableIndex (calc/em/rem) slots are now correctly treated as EXPLICIT declarations (even if unresolved at cascade time). 2 new pinning tests: row direction with `height: 50%` doesn't stretch; column direction with `width: 50%` doesn't stretch. **F#4 (P2) — cancellation threading.** Pre-fix the L3 `PreMeasureFlexCrossExtent` looped all flex children without checking the token. Hostile inputs with millions of items could continue through after cancellation. **Fix:** added `CancellationToken` parameter to BOTH pre-measure helpers (L3's `PreMeasureFlexCrossExtent` AND the new L4 `PreMeasureFlexMainExtent`); per-iteration `ThrowIfCancellationRequested()` calls; both call sites updated to pass the token already in scope. **F#5 (P3) — stale docs/comments.** Cleaned 3 sites: `docs/deferrals.md` flex section's "not yet honored" wording + the `flex-direction: column` future-scope claim (L4 shipped it); `FlexLayouterTests.cs:1475` region comment that incorrectly described "auto-width stretch" while the fixture set explicit item widths. The new comment accurately describes explicit-width-items-keep-declared-size (per CSS Flexbox §7.2 stretch only applies when cross-size computes to auto). Per-item emission maps the `(mainCursor, itemMainSize, itemCrossOffset, itemEffectiveCrossSize)` tuple to physical `(inlineOffset, blockOffset, inlineSize, blockSize)` per direction — for row, mainCursor → InlineOffset; for column, mainCursor → BlockOffset. **Container cross-axis derivation:** column direction with `width: auto` falls back to `max(item natural inline-size)` (parallel to L3's row-direction `max(item natural block-size)`); column direction with explicit `width` uses that value (already present via `_contentInlineSize`). **BlockLayouter pre-measure dispatch:** L3's `PreMeasureFlexCrossExtent` + subtree-extent clamp now gated on `!IsFlexColumnDirection()` at BOTH dispatch sites (outer-loop + recursion). Column-direction wrappers use the natural block-flow stacking sum from `MeasureSubtreeVisualBlockExtent` — spec-correct for main-axis-block because column direction's main axis IS the block axis (= sum of item block-sizes). **Phase 3 Task 15 L3 + post-PR-#63 review hardening — 7 findings on top of the L3 align-items Hello World** (historical entry; superseded by Task 15 L4 Hello World above; [PR #63](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/63) merged at `f4f439f`.) Continues from Task 15 L3 Hello World ([PR #63](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/63) opened on 2026-05-16, this hardening updates the same branch in-place). Roland's review of PR #63 surfaced 7 findings (2 P1, 3 P2, 2 P3). **F#1 (P1) — auto-height flex wrapper measured incorrectly.** Pre-fix, BlockLayouter measured the flex wrapper before dispatching to FlexLayouter using `MeasureSubtreeVisualBlockExtent`, which stacks children vertically as if they were block-flow. A height-auto flex row with items 50/100/75 reserved ~225px of wrapper height + advanced the outer cursor by 225px, while FlexLayouter (correctly) emitted the flex line at only 100px. CSS Flexbox §9.4 says single-line auto-height = max(item hypothetical cross-size), not vertical stacking. **Fix:** new `PreMeasureFlexCrossExtent` static helper in BlockLayouter mirrors the `PreMeasureMulticolColumnExtent` precedent — walks `flexContainer.Children`, computes `max(item.Height)`. Wired into BOTH dispatch sites (outer-loop at line ~1356, recursion at line ~2762). Also needed a `subtreeBlockExtent` clamp at line ~1499 (mirroring the table precedent) because `MeasureSubtreeVisualBlockExtent` ALSO over-measures by block-flow stacking; without the clamp `effectiveBlockSize = Math.Max(borderBoxBlockSize=100, subtreeBlockExtent=225) = 225` and the bug persisted. 2 new pinning tests: wrapper BlockSize matches max-item-height; sibling cursor advance respects the flex line extent. **F#2 (P1) — explicit `height: 0` mistaken for auto.** Pre-fix stretch branch used `effectiveCross = itemCrossSize > 0 ? itemCrossSize : containerCrossSize` — but `0` could be EITHER explicit `height: 0px` (LengthPx slot with value 0) OR `height: auto` (Unset / Keyword slot which `ReadLengthPxOrZero` returns 0 for). These are semantically different per CSS Flexbox §7.2 (stretch applies ONLY when cross-size computes to auto). **Fix:** new `IsCrossSizeAuto(Box)` private static helper on FlexLayouter checks `style.Get(PropertyId.Height).Tag != ComputedSlotTag.LengthPx`. `ComputeAlignItemsPlacement` signature gains a `bool itemIsCrossSizeAuto` parameter; the stretch branch uses it instead of the value-based heuristic. 3 new tests pin explicit-zero / auto / explicit-positive cases. **F#3 (P2) — safe/unsafe align-items compounds not production-pinned.** Pre-fix, only unit tests covered the L3 safe/unsafe compounds (via raw keyword indices). PR #62 had added `justify-content` to `KnownDroppedProperties` because AngleSharp.Css drops compound keywords; the same issue exists for `align-items`. **Fix:** 2 new production tests (`safe center` overflow falls back; `unsafe flex-end` overflow honors). The `unsafe flex-end` test failed without the preprocessor fix (expected -50, got 0); added `"align-items"` to `KnownDroppedProperties` in `CssPreprocessor.cs` (same precedent as the cycle-2-prior `justify-content` entry). **F#4 (P2) — cross-axis margins ignored.** Per CSS Flexbox §8.4, align-items operates on the MARGIN BOX, and cross-axis `margin: auto` overrides align-items/align-self. L3 uses border-box. Implementing requires plumbing margin reads through FlexLayouter (sub-cycle L4+ scope). **Fix:** explicit deferral in `docs/deferrals.md#flex-layouter-features` + 1 pinning test (`L3_hardening_known_gap_cross_axis_margins_ignored_in_alignment`) that locks the current (incomplete) behavior; sub-cycle L4+ should flip the test. **F#5 (P2) — stretch ignores margin-box + min/max.** Per CSS Flexbox §7.2, stretch sets the item's margin-box as close as possible to the line size, respecting min/max constraints. L3 sets `BlockSize = containerCrossSize`, ignoring all of those. **Fix:** explicit deferral + 1 pinning test (`L3_hardening_known_gap_stretch_ignores_min_max_constraints`). **F#6 (P3) — missing cancellation check.** The new cross-size pre-pass loop didn't call `cancellationToken.ThrowIfCancellationRequested()` (the main-axis pre-pass + emit loop do). Hostile inputs with millions of items could continue through after cancellation. **Fix:** added the check inside the cross-size derivation loop. **F#7 (P3) — deferrals.md contradicted implementation.** The Missing list still claimed "safe/unsafe overflow containment for align-items" was deferred even though L3 decodes + applies the modes correctly. **Fix:** removed the contradictory bullet; added narrower future-work bullet (baseline-family overflow semantics + parser recovery coverage). Tests: **4462 unit / 4593 solution-wide passing** (+9 unit / +9 solution-wide over PR #63 baseline at 4453 / 4584 — 5 hardening fixes + 2 deferral pins + 2 production tests; 4 skipped). All 4 gates green: build (0 warnings, 0 errors), test, AOT/JIT byte-parity, `git diff --check` clean. **Diff:** 6 files changed, ~763 insertions, ~27 deletions. **Existing tests unchanged** — the F#2 fix preserves the existing `L3_align_items_stretch_resizes_items_to_container_cross_size` test because it uses Unset slots (= auto) for items 0+2 and explicit `Height: 50` for item 1; the new `IsCrossSizeAuto` returns the same answer for both shapes as the old `> 0` heuristic in those specific cases. **Flex L4+ scope (updated):** baseline alignment family, anchor-center, align-self per-item, flex-direction: column / row-reverse / column-reverse, flex-wrap: wrap / wrap-reverse, flex-grow / flex-shrink / flex-basis, order, multi-page flex split, inline-flex-item anonymous wrapping, **cross-axis margins + auto-margins** (F#4 deferral), **stretch with margin-box + min/max** (F#5 deferral), outer-main-size + auto-margins in justify-content free-space calc (F#3 from PR #62 hardening), writing-mode-aware logical-axis aliases for both axes, baseline-family overflow semantics. Active-task pointer advances to **Task 15 L4** (baseline OR flex-direction: column OR flex-wrap: wrap OR flex-grow/shrink/basis OR align-self) OR begin Task 16+ (Grid layouter).)

**Phase 3 Task 15 L3 Hello World shipped — `align-items` cross-axis alignment** (historical entry; superseded by Task 15 L3 + post-PR-#63 review hardening above; the Hello World work is in [PR #63](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/63), this hardening updates the same branch in-place.) Continues from Task 15 L2 + post-PR-#62 review hardening ([PR #62](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/62) merged at `0888ffe`). L1 + L2 emitted items at `contentBlockOffset` regardless of `align-items` (= implicit cycle-1 default); L3 honors the full cross-axis alignment matrix per CSS Flexbox L1 §8.3 + CSS Box Alignment L3 §6. **Implementation reuses L2's two-channel pattern:** new `AlignItemsValue` enum (FlexStart / FlexEnd / Center / Stretch) + new `ResolvedAlignItems` record-struct (Value, Mode) using the existing `OverflowAlignmentMode` enum from L2. `ReadAlignItems` extension decodes all 27 keyword indices (0=normal, 1=stretch, 2=anchor-center, 3-5=baseline variants, 6-12=SelfPositions, 13-19=safe-X compounds, 20-26=unsafe-X compounds). For L3 Hello World: `normal` resolves to `Stretch` per spec; `anchor-center` and the 3 baseline variants fall through to `Stretch` (safe default) — dedicated handling is L4+ scope. SelfPositions decoded per cycle-1 LTR-row mapping: `center` → Center; `start` / `self-start` / `flex-start` → FlexStart; `end` / `self-end` / `flex-end` → FlexEnd. Writing-mode-aware mapping deferred to L4+. **Algorithm:** pre-pass derives `containerCrossSize` from the container's `height` slot — explicit `LengthPx` → use it; else `max(item natural block-size)` across block-level items. Per-item placement via new `ComputeAlignItemsPlacement` helper: `Stretch` resizes items with `height: 0` (auto) to `containerCrossSize` while items with explicit `height > 0` keep their declared size; positional values compute `crossSpace = containerCrossSize - itemCrossSize` and place items at `contentBlockOffset + (crossSpace / 2)` (Center), `contentBlockOffset + crossSpace` (FlexEnd), or `contentBlockOffset` (FlexStart). Overflow handling per CSS Box Alignment L3 §5.3 mirrors L2's per-family branches: `safe` modifier always falls back to flex-start (= `contentBlockOffset`); `unsafe` always honors natural; default mode allows positional values to keep their natural (possibly-negative) offset — items with cross-size larger than the container overflow equally on both sides for Center. **`AlignItemsValue.Stretch` semantics:** the spec says stretch items get a cross-size equal to the container's cross extent (clamped against min/max). Hello World L3 simplification: only items with `height: 0` (= unset / auto) get the override; explicit-height items honor their declaration per CSS Flexbox L1 §7.2. Per-item min/max content checks are L4+ scope. Tests: **4453 unit / 4584 solution-wide passing** (+14 unit / +14 solution-wide over Task 15 L2 baseline at 4439 / 4570 — 13 new unit tests + 1 production-pipeline test; 4 skipped). All 4 gates green: build (0 warnings, 0 errors), test, AOT/JIT byte-parity, `git diff --check` clean. **New unit tests** in `FlexLayouterTests`: `L3_align_items_flex_start_packs_items_at_cross_start` (offset 0); `L3_align_items_flex_end_packs_items_at_cross_end` (offset 150 in 200px container with 50px items); `L3_align_items_center_centers_items_on_cross_axis` (offset 75); `L3_align_items_stretch_resizes_items_to_container_cross_size` (auto-height items get effective height 200); `L3_align_items_overflow_center_keeps_negative_offset` (-25 for 250px items in 200px container); `L3_align_items_safe_center_overflow_falls_back_to_flex_start` (offset 0); `L3_align_items_unsafe_flex_end_overflow_honors_alignment` (offset -50); `L3_align_items_logical_alias_maps_to_physical_for_ltr_row` (Theory with 4 alias rows: start/end/self-start/self-end → flex-start/flex-end); `L3_align_items_baseline_falls_back_to_stretch_for_l3` (deferral pin); `L3_align_items_container_height_auto_uses_max_item_height` (mixed item heights 50/100/75 → containerCrossSize=100). **New production test** `L3_production_html_align_items_center` exercises `<div style="display: flex; align-items: center; height: 200px">` with 3 items of height 50 → all 3 emit at block offset 75 through the full HTML → cascade → BoxBuilder → BlockLayouter → FlexLayouter pipeline. **No existing tests broke** — the default `align-items: normal` resolves to `stretch`, and stretch with explicit `itemCrossSize > 0` keeps the item's declared height, so the existing L1+L2 tests (which all set explicit item heights) see no behavior change. **Diff:** 5 files changed, ~865 insertions, ~25 deletions. **`docs/deferrals.md` updated**: `flex-layouter-features` Missing list now reflects L3's progress — removed the "`align-items` values beyond default stretch" bullet; inline-flex-item anonymous wrapping for stray TextRun whitespace; outer-main-size + auto-margins in `justify-content` free-space calc (F#3 deferral from PR #62); writing-mode-aware logical-axis aliases for both axes. **Phase 3 Task 15 L2 + post-PR-#62 review hardening — 5 findings on top of the L2 Hello World** (historical entry; superseded by Task 15 L3 Hello World above; [PR #62](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/62) merged at `0888ffe`.) Continues from Task 15 L2 Hello World ([PR #62](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/62) opened on 2026-05-16, this hardening updates the same branch in-place). Roland's review of PR #62 surfaced 5 findings (2 P1, 2 P2, 1 P3). **F#1 (P1) — `safe`/`unsafe` compound keywords decoded incorrectly.** Pre-fix indices 12-25 (the 14 `safe X` / `unsafe X` compounds) all fell through to `FlexStart` — `safe center` rendered like flex-start; `unsafe flex-end` rendered like flex-start. Per CSS Box Alignment L3 §5.3, `unsafe` HONORS the specified alignment; `safe` ONLY changes behavior in overflow cases. **Fix:** adopted a two-channel decoding — new `OverflowAlignmentMode` enum (Default / Safe / Unsafe) + new `ResolvedJustifyContent` record-struct (Value, Mode). `ReadJustifyContent` rewritten to decode ALL 26 keyword indices into the struct: bare indices map to `(Value, Default)`; safe indices 12-18 map to `(Value, Safe)` for their base position (center/start/end/flex-start/flex-end/left/right); unsafe indices 19-25 map to `(Value, Unsafe)`. **F#2 (P1) — overflow handling wrong for positional values.** Pre-fix `ComputeJustifyContentOffsets` returned `(0, 0)` for ALL values when `freeSpace <= 0`. Per CSS Box Alignment L3 §5.3, the overflow behavior differs by family: distribution values (space-between/space-around/space-evenly) fall back to safe-start on overflow; positional values (flex-start/flex-end/center) keep their natural offset (which may be negative — `center` with negative free-space puts items at `freeSpace/2` < 0, so items overflow equally on both sides). The `safe X` modifier forces safe-start regardless of value; the `unsafe X` modifier honors the natural offset. **Fix:** rewrote `ComputeJustifyContentOffsets` per-family: always compute the natural offset first; on overflow, branch on mode (Safe → (0,0); Unsafe → natural) then on value family (distribution → (0,0); positional → natural). **F#3 (P2) — outer-main-size + auto-margins gap.** Per CSS Flexbox L1 §9.5, `justify-content` free-space uses each item's resolved margin-box main-axis size + auto margins consume free space BEFORE distribution. L2's pre-pass sums only `width`. **Fix:** explicit deferral — implementing the margin-box outer-size pre-pass requires plumbing margin/padding/border reads through FlexLayouter (sub-cycle 3+ scope). Added Missing bullet in `docs/deferrals.md#flex-layouter-features` + a pinning test `L2_justify_content_known_gap_item_margins_ignored_in_free_space_calc` that pins the current (incomplete) behavior; sub-cycle 3+ will make this test fail, prompting an update to the spec-correct margin-box-aware assertion. **F#4 (P2) — tests bypass CSS pipeline.** Pre-fix most L2 tests wrote raw keyword ordinals directly into ComputedSlot; only 1 production test covered `space-between`. The F#1 compound-keyword bug was hidden because no test exercised the parser→cascade→layout chain for safe/unsafe variants. **Fix:** 4 new production-pipeline tests cover the full HTML→cascade→layout chain for `center`, `flex-end`, `safe center` overflow, and `unsafe flex-end` overflow. **Important supporting fix:** discovered AngleSharp.Css 1.0.0-beta.144 silently drops `justify-content: safe center` and `justify-content: unsafe flex-end` declarations entirely (compound-keyword recovery not implemented). Added `justify-content` to `KnownDroppedProperties` in `CssPreprocessor.cs` (same precedent as existing `white-space` / `overflow-wrap` entries at lines 78-96); the preprocessor's `ScanDeclarations` recovery layer captures the raw declaration text + routes it to `KeywordResolver.BuildJustifyContentTable` which correctly handles all 26 indices. Without this fix, F#4 tests 3 + 4 would have always rendered as default flex-start. **F#5 (P3) — docs drift fixed.** `docs/deferrals.md#flex-layouter-features` Behavior section rewritten to reflect L2's full justify-content matrix (6 base values × 3 overflow modes); F#3 added as a Missing bullet; stale "items packing from start edge only" wording removed. **Existing tests modified:** `L2_justify_content_overflow_falls_back_to_flex_start` (at `FlexLayouterTests.cs:331`) rewritten in place to `L2_justify_content_center_with_overflow_keeps_centered_negative_offset` — the old test pinned the WRONG behavior per F#2 (center overflow should keep its natural centered offset, not collapse to flex-start). Tests: **4427 unit / 4558 solution-wide passing** (+10 unit / +10 solution-wide over PR #62 baseline at 4417 / 4548 — 4 new production + 6 new unit + 1 existing rewritten in place = +10 net; 4 skipped). All 4 gates green: build (0 warnings, 0 errors), test, AOT/JIT byte-parity, `git diff --check` clean. **Diff:** 6 files changed, ~690 insertions, ~88 deletions. **Flex L3+ scope (updated):** outer-main-size + auto-margins in free-space calc (F#3 deferral); writing-mode-aware `left`/`right` mapping; `flex-direction: column` / `row-reverse` / `column-reverse`; `flex-wrap: wrap` / `wrap-reverse`; `align-items` values beyond default; `flex-grow` / `flex-shrink` / `flex-basis`; `order`; baseline alignment; multi-page flex split; inline-flex-item anonymous wrapping. Active-task pointer advances to **Task 15 L3** OR revisit multicol cycle 5+ deferrals.)

**Phase 3 Task 15 L2 Hello World shipped — `justify-content` main-axis alignment** (historical entry; superseded by Task 15 L2 + post-PR-#62 review hardening above; the Hello World work is in [PR #62](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/62), this hardening updates the same branch in-place.) Continues from Task 15 L1 Hello World ([PR #61](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/61) merged at `fc7320f`). L1 shipped single-line row-packing with items packed at `flex-start` (the implicit cycle-1 default); L2 honors the full content-position + content-distribution value set per CSS Box Alignment L3 §4.5. **Algorithm:** pre-pass computes `totalItemInlineSize` + `freeSpace = contentInlineSize - totalItemInlineSize`; resolves the keyword via new `ReadJustifyContent()` extension on `ComputedStyleLayoutExtensions` (decodes the 26-entry keyword table that `KeywordResolver.BuildJustifyContentTable` produces — verified indices 0=normal, 1=space-between, 2=space-around, 3=space-evenly, 4=stretch, 5=center, 6=start, 7=end, 8=flex-start, 9=flex-end, 10=left, 11=right, 12-25=safe/unsafe compounds — into a new `JustifyContentValue` enum with 6 cases); computes `(startOffset, betweenSpacing)` via the new `ComputeJustifyContentOffsets` static helper; the existing L1 cursor loop becomes `cursor = _contentInlineOffset + startOffset` advancing by `itemInlineSize + betweenSpacing`. **Spec edge cases honored:** overflow (freeSpace ≤ 0) → all keywords fall back to flex-start (items overflow at start). N=1 with `space-between` → fall back to flex-start per spec (no gaps between single item). N=1 with `space-around` / `space-evenly` → degenerate to center naturally via the formulas. **Logical aliases** (CSS Box Alignment L3 §4.5 admits `start`/`end`/`left`/`right` for cross-spec compatibility): map to `flex-start`/`flex-end` for the L1 default `flex-direction: row`; writing-mode-aware mapping deferred to L3+. **`safe`/`unsafe` overflow modifiers** (24 compound keywords in the table): treated as bare position for L2; safe-mode overflow containment deferred to L3+. **`stretch` value**: not applicable to flex per spec (it's grid-specific); maps to `flex-start` (= the same default `normal` resolves to). **`normal` keyword** (the computed default): maps to `flex-start` for flex per CSS Flexbox L1 §8.2. Tests: **4417 unit / 4548 solution-wide passing** (+9 unit / +9 solution-wide over Task 15 L1 baseline at 4408 / 4539 — 8 new unit tests + 1 new production-pipeline test; 4 skipped). All 4 gates green: build (0 warnings, 0 errors), test, AOT/JIT byte-parity, `git diff --check` clean. **New unit tests** in `FlexLayouterTests`: `L2_justify_content_flex_end_packs_items_at_main_end` (offsets 150/200/250 for 3×50 items in 300px); `L2_justify_content_center_centers_items_on_main_axis` (75/125/175); `L2_justify_content_space_between_distributes_equal_gaps` (0/125/250 — gap=75); `L2_justify_content_space_around_half_space_at_edges` (25/125/225 — gap=50, half at edges); `L2_justify_content_space_evenly_equal_space_everywhere` (37.5/125/212.5 — gap=37.5 everywhere); `L2_justify_content_overflow_falls_back_to_flex_start` (5×100 in 300px → 0/100/200/300/400); `L2_justify_content_single_item_space_between_uses_flex_start` (1 item at offset 0); `L2_justify_content_normal_keyword_maps_to_flex_start` (3 items at 0/50/100). **New production test** `L2_production_html_justify_content_space_between` exercises `<div class="flex">` with three 50px-wide `<div>` block children → offsets 0/275/550 through the full HTML → cascade → BoxBuilder → BlockLayouter → FlexLayouter pipeline. **Diff:** 5 files changed, ~518 insertions, ~17 deletions. **`docs/deferrals.md` updated**: `flex-layouter-features` Missing list now reflects L2's progress — removed the bare "`justify-content` values beyond `flex-start`" bullet; added the still-deferred edge cases (`safe`/`unsafe` overflow-position modifiers; writing-mode-aware `left`/`right` mapping). **Flex L3+ scope (updated):** `flex-direction: column` / `row-reverse` / `column-reverse`; `flex-wrap: wrap` / `wrap-reverse`; `align-items` values beyond default stretch; `flex-grow` / `flex-shrink` / `flex-basis`; `order` property; baseline alignment; multi-page flex container splitting (atomic to outer pagination in L1+L2); inline-flex-item anonymous wrapping for stray TextRun whitespace; `safe`/`unsafe` overflow-position modifiers for `justify-content`; writing-mode-aware logical-axis aliases. **Phase 3 Task 15 Hello World shipped — `FlexLayouter` L1 single-line** (historical entry; superseded by Task 15 L2 above; [PR #61](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/61) merged at `fc7320f`.) Continues from Task 14 cycle 4 + post-PR-#60 review hardening ([PR #60](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/60) merged at `68c0a96`). Task 15 opens **CSS Flexbox L1** with the simplest possible Hello World: `display: flex` containers lay their direct block-level children out in a horizontal row, each item at its declared `width` × `height`, packed left-to-right from the container's content origin. **New layouter:** `src/NetPdf.Layout/Layouters/FlexLayouter.cs` (~342 LOC), `internal sealed class FlexLayouter : ILayouter, IDisposable`. Constructor signature mirrors `MulticolLayouter` cycle 1: `(rootBox, sink, incomingContinuation: null, diagnostics: null, shaperResolver: null)`. Rejects non-null `incomingContinuation` (multi-page flex split is L2+ scope; mirrors MulticolLayouter cycle 1's safety rejection). **Algorithm (cycle 1):** read flex container properties (defaults: `flex-direction: row` + `flex-wrap: nowrap` + `justify-content: flex-start` + `align-items: stretch`); iterate `_rootBox.Children`; for each block-level child emit a `BoxFragment` at `(currentInlineCursor, contentBlockOffset, itemInlineSize, itemBlockSize)` then advance the cursor by the item's inline-size. Non-block-level children (whitespace `TextRun`s injected by BoxBuilder between item elements) are skipped — the BoxBuilder pipeline injects them between `<span>` items in real HTML; an inline anonymous-flex-item wrapping pass is sub-cycle 2+ scope (documented in the `flex-layouter-features` deferral). **`BlockLayouter` dispatch** added at TWO sites: the outer-loop site (`BlockLayouter.cs:1920-2018`, after the existing multicol dispatch) + the recursion site (`BlockLayouter.cs:2814-2880`, after the nested-multicol dispatch). Both sites mirror the multicol pattern — caller emits the wrapper fragment, then `FlexLayouter.ConfigureEmission(...)` + `AttemptLayout`. New `IsFlexContainer` static helper at `BlockLayouter.cs:3435` (adjacent to `IsMulticolContainer`); BoxKind-gated (`FlexContainer or InlineFlexContainer`) — contrast with multicol which is property-based. **New deferral entry** `docs/deferrals.md#flex-layouter-features` (lines 833-892) catalogs the 9 deferred Flexbox L1 features: `flex-direction: column` / `row-reverse` / `column-reverse`; `flex-wrap: wrap` / `wrap-reverse`; `justify-content` values beyond `flex-start`; `align-items` values beyond default stretch; `flex-grow` / `flex-shrink` / `flex-basis`; `order` property; baseline alignment; multi-page flex container splitting (atomic to outer pagination in L1); inline-flex-item anonymous wrapping for stray TextRun whitespace. `DeferralsParityTests.ExpectedDeferralIds` updated. **Task 14 cycle 5 (`column-span: all`) deferred.** The sub-agent assigned to cycle 5 correctly identified that column-span: all requires plumbing a "max-child-index" through BlockLayouter (or equivalent cross-layouter coordination) — beyond Hello World scope. Documented as remaining-deferred in `docs/deferrals.md#multicol-balancing-pagination` alongside column-rule paint, font-relative widths, and break-*-column honoring.
