**Phase 3 Task 14 cycle 4 + post-PR-#60 review hardening — 6 findings on top of the Hello World** (historical entry; superseded by Task 15 Hello World above; [PR #60](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/60) merged at `68c0a96`.) Continues from Task 14 cycle 4 Hello World ([PR #60](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/60) opened on 2026-05-16, this hardening updates the same branch in-place). Roland's review of PR #60 surfaced 6 findings (2 P1, 3 P2, 1 P3). **F#1 (P1) — `column-width: 0` now clamps to 1px used-width per CSS Multi-column L1 §3.1.** Pre-fix `ReadColumnWidth` returned 0 (correct — preserves computed value) but `ComputeUsedColumnCount`'s `cw > 0` guard silently routed 0 to the "no width constraint" path → derivedCount=1 → single column. The spec says the used value of `column-width` is `max(specified, 1px)`. **Fix:** loosened guard to `columnWidth is double cw && double.IsFinite(cw) && cw >= 0` AND apply `usedColumnWidth = Math.Max(1.0, cw)` before derivation. New test `Cycle4_column_width_zero_clamps_to_one_pixel_used_width` pins (with/without gap, alongside column-count). **F#2 (P1) — relative-unit scope narrowed.** Pre-fix the cycle 4 PR claimed `column-width: <length>` support but `LengthResolver` returns `Deferred` for relative lengths (em, rem, %); `ReadColumnWidth` returns null for those; `IsMulticolContainer` doesn't dispatch. CSS Multi-column L1's own introductory example uses `12em` so the gap is material. Resolving relative lengths requires plumbing the font-size cascade through layout (a separate body of work, sub-cycle 5+ scope). **Fix:** explicit scope-narrowing — `ReadColumnWidth` XML doc now spells out the Deferred behavior; new Missing bullet in `docs/deferrals.md#multicol-balancing-pagination` documents "Font-relative `column-width`"; new production test `Cycle4_production_html_column_width_em_does_not_trigger_multicol_yet` pins the current behavior so future agents see the gap as a deliberate deferral. **F#3 (P2) — `column-count: 1` now routes through MulticolLayouter.** Per CSS Multi-column L1 §1, a multi-column container is created when column-count OR column-width is non-auto; column boxes establish their own BFC. Pre-fix the `IsMulticolContainer` gate required `n >= 2`, so `column-count: 1` fell through to ordinary block flow and lost the BFC contract. **Fix:** gate now fires for `n >= 1`; MulticolLayouter degrades to the existing `EmitSingleColumnFallthrough` (cycle 4 already had this for the column-width-derived-N=1 case). The existing `Multicol_column_count_1_behaves_like_normal_block` test was renamed to `Multicol_column_count_1_reaches_MulticolLayouter_via_single_column_fallthrough` with updated docstring (assertions unchanged — user-visible fragment is identical). New `Cycle4_column_count_one_dispatches_to_MulticolLayouter_via_BlockLayouter` test pins the dispatch path. Full BFC margin-collapse semantics test is sub-cycle 5+ (needs a BFC harness). **F#4 (P2) — narrowing conversion safe before clamp.** Pre-fix `(int)Math.Floor(numerator / denom)` could produce undefined behavior when the ratio exceeded `int.MaxValue` (huge container + tiny column-width). The MulticolLayouter's `MaxColumnCount = 1000` clamp ran AFTER the unsafe cast. **Fix:** clamp the double to `[1.0, int.MaxValue]` before casting; MulticolLayouter's safety cap then narrows further. Implementation pivot from LOCKED spec: changed the "no width constraint" sentinel from `int.MaxValue` to a nullable `int?` (`derivedFromWidth`) to disambiguate "no constraint" from "legitimately huge derived value" — without this, the F#4 fix would have collapsed legitimate huge derivations back to 1. New test `Cycle4_huge_finite_geometry_derives_safely_before_int_conversion` pins. **F#5 (P2) — extracted 5 shared helpers between main column-fill path and EmitSingleColumnFallthrough.** Pre-fix the fallback duplicated resume-state decode + lacked the main path's forward-progress detection / diagnostic emission for malformed continuations. Could silently truncate content. **Fix:** new helpers `DecodeIncomingCarriedContinuation`, `PackageMulticolPageComplete`, `TryEmitForcedOverflowFallback`, `EmitForcedOverflowDiagnostic`, `EmitUnexpectedContinuationDiagnostic` — used by both paths. 3 new tests cover the fallback's strengthened contract: resume-page emission, oversized child via inner dispatch, shared resume decode. **F#6 (P3) — docs aligned to actual contracts.** `ReadColumnWidth` doc no longer claims zero is rejected. The `ComputeUsedColumnCount` doc now describes `column-width` as the spec's "optimal width" (a tentative used value) rather than "MINIMUM". `docs/deferrals.md` Status section honest about absolute-resolved-lengths scope + the 4 post-PR-#60 fixes. Tests: **4402 unit / 4533 solution-wide passing** (+7 unit / +7 solution-wide over PR #60 baseline at 4395 / 4526 — 6 new unit tests + 1 new production test + 1 existing test renamed in-place; 4 skipped). All 4 gates green: build (0 warnings, 0 errors), test, AOT/JIT byte-parity, `git diff --check` clean. **Diff:** 6 files changed, ~980 insertions, ~208 deletions. **Sub-cycle 2+ scope (updated):** `column-span: all`; column-rule paint; `column-gap: normal` font-relative resolution; break-before-column / break-after-column / `break-inside: avoid-column`; column balancing with explicit `height`; perf-cache (F#6 from PR #59); **font-relative `column-width`** (NEW deferral from PR #60 F#2 — em/rem/% resolution needs font-size cascade plumbing); full BFC margin-collapse semantics for single-column multicol (sub-cycle 5+ — needs BFC harness). Active-task pointer advances to **Task 14 cycle 5** OR **Task 15** (`FlexLayouter` L1) depending on review priority.)

**Phase 3 Task 14 cycle 4 Hello World shipped — `column-width`-derived automatic column count** (historical entry; superseded by Task 14 cycle 4 + post-PR-#60 review hardening above; the Hello World work is in [PR #60](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/60), this hardening updates the same branch in-place.) Continues from Task 14 cycle 3 + post-PR-#59 review hardening ([PR #59](https://github.com/raroche/netpdf/pull/59) merged at `1a5a330`). CSS Multi-column L1 §3.1 + §3.3 admits two ways to declare multicol intent: `column-count: <integer>` (cycle 1+2+3 behavior) and `column-width: <length>` (cycle 4 new). When `column-width` is set with `column-count: auto`, the effective column count is derived from the container's content inline-size + the column-gap: `N = max(1, floor((containerInline + columnGap) / (columnWidth + columnGap)))`. When both `column-count` and `column-width` are non-auto, the spec says use `min(specifiedCount, derivedCount)`. **Implementation:** new `ReadColumnWidth()` extension at `ComputedStyleLayoutExtensions.cs:222-230` decodes the property as a CSS px length (null for auto / unset / non-length — the cycle 1 hardening NumberResolver guard already rejects negative + zero values, so a non-null result is always > 0); new static helper `ComputeUsedColumnCount(containerInline, specifiedCount?, columnWidth?, columnGap) → int` at `ComputedStyleLayoutExtensions.cs:251-291` encodes the 4 spec cases from the §3.3 table. **Dispatch gate updated** at `BlockLayouter.cs:3281-3314`: `IsMulticolContainer` now triggers on `(column-count >= 2) OR (column-width is a length)` — "declared multicol intent". The actual derived-N check happens inside `MulticolLayouter` once container geometry is known. **MulticolLayouter changes**: constructor loosened to accept multicol containers that declare intent via either property; `AttemptLayout` re-reads `column-gap` first, then calls `ComputeUsedColumnCount` to derive used N from `_contentInlineSize` (set by `ConfigureEmission`); `MaxColumnCount = 1000` clamp now applied AFTER derivation so a 1e9 container with `column-width: 1px` is still caught. **Single-column fallthrough** (`MulticolLayouter.cs:945-1024`, new method `EmitSingleColumnFallthrough`): when derived N < 2 (e.g., `column-width: 1000px` in a 400px container → derived N=1), the multicol degrades to a single-column emit — runs a single nested BlockLayouter over the full container inline-size + emits its fragments translated to the wrapper origin. Preserves the resume + multi-page continuation contract (same `ColumnFragmentSink` translation pattern as the multi-column path). **Per-column inline-size** continues to follow the cycle 1 equal-split formula `(containerInline - (N-1)*columnGap) / N` — per CSS spec the resolved per-column size may exceed `column-width` (which is a MINIMUM, not an exact size); the test `Cycle4_column_width_only_derives_column_count_from_container` pins this (perCol = 368/3 ≈ 122.67px from a 100px column-width). Tests: **4395 unit / 4526 solution-wide passing** (+6 unit / +6 solution-wide over post-PR-#59 baseline at 4389 / 4520 — 5 new unit tests + 1 new production-pipeline test; 4 skipped). All 4 gates green: build (0 warnings, 0 errors), test, AOT/JIT byte-parity, `git diff --check` clean. **New tests in [MulticolLayouterTests](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Phase3/MulticolLayouterTests.cs):** `Cycle4_column_width_only_derives_column_count_from_container` (`column-width: 100px` in 400px container with 3 children → derived N=3); `Cycle4_both_column_count_and_width_set_uses_smaller` (`column-count: 5` + `column-width: 100px` in 400px → min(5,3) = 3); `Cycle4_column_width_larger_than_container_clamps_to_one` (`column-width: 1000px` in 400px → derived N=1; single-column fallthrough; child spans full 400px); `Cycle4_compute_used_column_count_covers_all_four_spec_cases` (direct unit test of the helper covering all 4 §3.3 cases + defensive guards); `Cycle4_read_column_width_returns_null_for_auto_default` (extension contract: null on Unset/Keyword, value on LengthPx). **New production test in [MulticolLayouterProductionTests](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Phase3/MulticolLayouterProductionTests.cs):** `Cycle4_production_html_column_width_only_lays_out_in_derived_columns` (full HTML → cascade → BoxBuilder → BlockLayouter → MulticolLayouter pipeline with `column-width: 120px` in 600px content → derived N=4; verifies 4 children land in 4 distinct columns). **No existing tests broke** — the constructor loosening + dispatch gate are additive supersets of the cycle 1+2+3 behavior. **Diff:** 6 files changed, ~723 insertions, ~40 deletions; concentrated in `MulticolLayouter.cs` (constructor + AttemptLayout + EmitSingleColumnFallthrough), `ComputedStyleLayoutExtensions.cs` (new extensions), `BlockLayouter.cs` (IsMulticolContainer gate), `docs/deferrals.md` (removed `column-width auto count` Missing bullet; Owner files + Status updated), and the 2 test files. **Sub-cycle 2+ scope (updated):** `column-span: all`; column-rule paint (cycle 1 parses cascade but silent); `column-gap: normal` font-relative resolution; break-before-column / break-after-column / `break-inside: avoid-column`; column balancing with explicit `height`; perf-cache between outer BlockLayouter pre-measure and inner MulticolLayouter balancing pre-measure (F#6 deferral from PR #59). Active-task pointer advances to **Task 14 cycle 5** (column-span: all OR column rules paint) OR **Task 15** (`FlexLayouter` L1 single-line) depending on review priority.)

**Phase 3 Task 14 cycle 3 + post-PR-#59 review hardening — 8-finding correctness + algorithm rewrite on top of the cycle 3 Hello World** (historical entry; superseded by Task 14 cycle 4 Hello World above; [PR #59](https://github.com/raroche/netpdf/pull/59) merged at `1a5a330`.) Continues from Task 14 cycle 3 Hello World ([PR #59](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/59) opened on 2026-05-15, this hardening updates the same branch in-place). Roland's review of PR #59 surfaced 8 findings (4 P1, 3 P2, 1 P3) — substantial because the cycle 3 Hello World's balancing algorithm had several correctness gaps that only surfaced under non-trivial inputs (indivisible blocks, multi-fragment content, resume pages, long content, margin-bearing children, percentage heights). **Finding #1 (P1) — average-height heuristic was wrong for indivisible content.** Pre-fix `idealBlockSize = ceil(totalSerialExtent / columnCount)` was too short whenever the tallest indivisible child exceeded `total/N`. Concrete bug: 3 children × 80px in 2 columns → ideal=120, column 0 fits 1 (cursor=80, next 80→160 overflow), column 1 fits 1, the 3rd child spilled to page 2 even though 160px columns fit all 3 on one page (col 0 = 2×80, col 1 = 1×80). The pre-fix Hello World test `Cycle3_multicol_balance_uneven_content_rounds_up_idealBlockSize` actually pinned this wrong result. **Fix:** replaced the heuristic with a binary-search fit-probe in two new private helpers — `FindBalancedColumnBlockSize` binary-searches over `[ceil(total/N), perColumnBlockSize]` at 1px resolution for the smallest column-block-size where content fits in N columns; `FitsInNColumns` simulates a serial column-fill at the candidate height (walking N columns; each runs a nested `BlockLayouter` consuming content from the prior column's `PageComplete` continuation) and returns true if the simulation reaches `AllDone` in ≤ N columns. Per-iteration cost: N nested `BlockLayouter` dry-runs. Iteration count: O(log(perColumnBlockSize - ceil(total/N))) — typically 6-10 iterations. The old test was renamed + rewritten to `Cycle3_multicol_balance_three_blocks_fit_in_two_columns_on_one_page` asserting all 3 children fit on one page with both columns non-empty. **Finding #2 (P1) — `balance` vs `balance-all` semantics.** Pre-fix the cycle 3 Hello World treated `balance` as if it should balance every fragment — that's `balance-all` semantics. Per CSS Multi-column L1 §3.4, `balance` balances ONLY THE LAST FRAGMENT; non-final fragments use sequential fill. `balance-all` balances every fragment. **Fix:** added last-fragment detection — `isLastFragment = totalSerialExtent <= perColumnBlockSize * columnCount` (content fits in N columns at the per-page max → this is the last/only fragment). The activation switch: `BalanceAll` always balances; `Balance` balances only when `isLastFragment` is true. **Finding #3 (P1) — resume page measured wrong content range.** Pre-fix `PreMeasureTotalSerialExtent` was called with `carriedContinuation: null` at line 553, BEFORE the `_incomingContinuation` decode block at lines 593-609. On page 2 resume the pre-measure walked from child 0 instead of from `NextChildIndex`, so the balanced height was computed against the WHOLE document not the remaining content. **Fix:** moved the continuation decode block BEFORE the balancing block; pre-measure + fit-search both receive the correct `carriedContinuation`. **Finding #4 (P1) — single-window pre-measure silently under-measured long content.** Pre-fix the dry-run capped block-size at `perColumnBlockSize × columnCount × 2`, called the inner BlockLayouter once, ignored whether it returned `PageComplete`, and returned only what fit in that single window. Long content beyond the sentinel was invisible to the balancer. **Fix:** the pre-measure now LOOPS over continuations until `AllDone`, capped at `MaxPreMeasureIterations = 8` (= worst-case ~16 × N columns × perColumnBlockSize of content; ample for real-world multicol). Each iteration accumulates extent into `totalExtent`. **Finding #5 (P2) — margin-blind extent measurement.** Pre-fix `DiscardingMeasureSink.MaxBlockExtent` recorded only `BlockOffset + BlockSize`, missing trailing margins + collapsed-margin effects. The real `BlockLayouter` cursor uses margin-aware extents via `marginBoxBlockSizeForCursor` (BlockLayouter.cs:1458) and advances `UsedBlockSize` with that value (BlockLayouter.cs:1702). Pre-fix balance produced columns too short to fit margin-extended blocks. **Fix:** pre-measure now reads `fragmentainer.UsedBlockSize` (= the BlockLayouter cursor's actual extent) instead of the sink's max BlockOffset+BlockSize. **Finding #7 (P2) — `IsHeightAuto` over-broad.** Pre-fix returned true for ANY non-`LengthPx` slot — including Percentage. `height: 50%` was treated as auto, incorrectly entering the balance path. **Fix (both sites):** `slot.Tag is ComputedSlotTag.Unset or ComputedSlotTag.Keyword`. Percentage, LengthPx, Calc all correctly return false. The duplicate predicate in `BlockLayouter.cs:4825-4843` updated identically. **Finding #8 (P3) — `MulticolContinuation.ConsumedBlockSize` recorded the wrong page extent under balancing.** Pre-fix accumulated `perColumnBlockSize` (the per-page MAX) even when the page actually used `effectiveColumnBlockSize` (the smaller balanced value). The field is currently informational but future cost-model / diagnostics code shouldn't see inflated extents. **Fix:** changed line 800 to use `effectiveColumnBlockSize` in the cumulative ConsumedBlockSize accumulation. **Finding #6 deferred** — perf-cache between the outer BlockLayouter pre-measure and the inner MulticolLayouter balancing pre-measure (= the 4-passes-not-2-passes observation). Documented in `docs/deferrals.md#multicol-balancing-pagination` as sub-cycle 2+ scope along with pass-count benchmark guard. Tests: **4389 unit / 4520 solution-wide passing** (+7 unit / +7 solution-wide over PR #59 baseline at 4382 / 4513 — 1 existing test rewritten in-place + 7 new tests; 4 skipped). New tests added: `Cycle3_balance_indivisible_blocks_fit_search_finds_correct_height` (F#1 pin); `Cycle3_balance_vs_balance_all_over_multiple_fragmentainers_balance_uses_serial_fill_on_first_page` (F#2 — pins `balance` doing serial fill on non-final fragments); `Cycle3_balance_all_balances_every_fragment_including_non_final` (F#2 — pins `balance-all` balancing every fragment); `Cycle3_resume_page_balancing_measures_only_remaining_content` (F#3 — pins resume-side pre-measure scope); `Cycle3_long_content_exceeds_pre_measure_sentinel_still_measured` (F#4 — content totaling > perColumnBlockSize × columnCount × 2); `Cycle3_balanced_multicol_with_margin_bearing_children_accounts_for_trailing_margins` (F#5 — content with explicit margin-bottom); `Cycle3_percentage_height_multicol_uses_explicit_height_not_balancing` (F#7 — direct predicate assertion: `Unset.IsHeightAuto == true`, `Keyword.IsHeightAuto == true`, `LengthPx.IsHeightAuto == false`, `Percentage.IsHeightAuto == false`). All 4 gates green: build (0 warnings, 0 errors), test, AOT/JIT byte-parity, `git diff --check` clean. **Diff:** 5 files changed, ~973 insertions, ~219 deletions, concentrated in `MulticolLayouter.cs` (algorithm rewrite, new helpers) + `MulticolLayouterTests.cs` (1 rewritten + 7 new tests). **Cycle 3 sub-cycle 2+ scope (updated):** `column-fill: balance-all` over multi-fragmentainer scenarios with cost-model integration; balance cache between outer BlockLayouter pre-measure and inner MulticolLayouter balancing pre-measure (F#6 deferral — eliminates the 4-pass cost); pass-count benchmark guard; column balancing with explicit `height` (over-shrink-tolerant algorithm); `column-width` → auto column count derivation; `column-span: all`; column-rule paint; `column-gap: normal` font-relative resolution; break-before-column / break-after-column / `break-inside: avoid-column`. Active-task pointer advances to **Task 14 cycle 4** (column-width auto count OR column-span: all) OR **Task 15** (`FlexLayouter` L1 single-line) depending on review priority.)

**Phase 3 Task 14 cycle 3 Hello World shipped — `column-fill: balance` honored for auto-height multicol via a 2-pass algorithm** (historical entry; superseded by Task 14 cycle 3 + post-PR-#59 review hardening above; the Hello World work is in [PR #59](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/59), this hardening updates the same branch in-place.) Continues from Task 14 post-PR-#57 review #2 hardening ([PR #58](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/58) merged at `cd593af`). Cycle 1+2 ignored `column-fill` and always serial-filled left-to-right (last column may be shorter than the rest) — non-conformant to CSS Multi-column L1 §3.4 whose SPEC DEFAULT is `balance`. Cycle 3 ships **column balancing** for the spec-default case. **Algorithm (2-pass):** when `column-fill` is `balance` (or `balance-all` — treated identically for cycle 3) AND the multicol container has `height: auto` AND column-count >= 2, MulticolLayouter (a) runs a pre-measure dry-run via a new `PreMeasureTotalSerialExtent` private helper that drives a fresh nested `BlockLayouter` with a very tall block-size budget (`perColumnBlockSize × columnCount × 2`) against a new `DiscardingMeasureSink`, capturing the total serial-fill extent (= the height if all content fit in a single column); (b) computes `idealBlockSize = Math.Ceiling(totalSerialExtent / columnCount)`; (c) clamps to `[1.0, perColumnBlockSize]` (the floor protects against pathological divide-by-zero edges; the ceiling preserves the per-page upper bound so the existing forced-overflow + multi-page-continuation safety nets remain intact); (d) re-runs the existing column-fill loop with `effectiveColumnBlockSize = balanced` instead of `perColumnBlockSize`. `column-fill: auto` skips the pre-measure + ideal computation, keeping cycle 1+2 serial-fill behavior bit-identical. Explicit `height` skips balancing (conservative — matches Prince/WeasyPrint; avoids the over-shrink drop-out that aggressive balancing causes when authors deliberately size containers). **New extensions on `ComputedStyleLayoutExtensions`:** `ReadColumnFill()` decodes `PropertyId.ColumnFill` (keyword indices 0=balance, 1=balance-all, 2=auto) into a new `ColumnFillValue` enum (defaulting to `Balance` per spec when the slot is non-Keyword); `IsHeightAuto(this Box)` static method mirrors BlockLayouter's existing instance predicate so MulticolLayouter can gate balancing without reaching into BlockLayouter internals. **Forward-progress safety preserved:** if a single child is taller than `balancedBlockSize`, the existing cycle 1+2 forced-overflow forward-progress fallback at `MulticolLayouter.cs:610-633` (single-oversized-child path that emits `LAYOUT-MULTICOL-FORCED-OVERFLOW-001`) handles it gracefully — no infinite loops, no new code path needed. The cycle 3 `Cycle3_multicol_balance_oversized_child_falls_back_via_forced_overflow` test pins this. Tests: **4382 unit / 4513 solution-wide passing** (+7 unit / +7 solution-wide over post-PR-#58 baseline at 4375 / 4506 — 6 new unit tests + 1 new production-pipeline test; 4 skipped). All 4 gates green: build (0 warnings, 0 errors), test, AOT/JIT byte-parity, `git diff --check` clean. **New direct tests** in [`MulticolLayouterTests`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Phase3/MulticolLayouterTests.cs): `Cycle3_multicol_balance_height_auto_distributes_equally` (4 children of 80px in 2 columns → 2-per-column balanced); `Cycle3_multicol_balance_uneven_content_rounds_up_idealBlockSize` (3 children of 80px in 2 columns → ideal=120 via ceiling, balancing activates and distributes 2+1 or 1+2 not serial 3+0); `Cycle3_multicol_auto_fill_preserves_cycle1_serial_behavior` (explicit `column-fill: auto` keeps all 4 in column 0); `Cycle3_multicol_balance_with_explicit_height_uses_explicit_height_not_balancing` (height: 200px + balance → serial fill per the conservative explicit-height gate); `Cycle3_multicol_balance_all_treated_as_balance_for_cycle3` (balance-all produces same result as balance); `Cycle3_multicol_balance_oversized_child_falls_back_via_forced_overflow` (single 500px child, 800px page, 2 columns: balanced=250, child overflows but forced-overflow forward-progress commits, no infinite loop). **New production test** in [`MulticolLayouterProductionTests`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Phase3/MulticolLayouterProductionTests.cs): `Cycle3_production_multicol_with_auto_height_balances_cleanly` (full pipeline: HTML → cascade → BoxBuilder → BlockLayouter → MulticolLayouter; auto-height multicol with 4 paragraphs → balanced 2-per-column). **No existing tests broke** — existing cycle 1+2 tests use explicit multicol height (which skips balancing per the explicit-height gate) OR small per-column block-sizes where the balanced ideal exceeds `perColumnBlockSize` and clamps back, so behavior is preserved. **Diff:** 5 files changed, ~808 insertions, ~16 deletions; concentrated in `ComputedStyleLayoutExtensions.cs` (new extensions + enum), `MulticolLayouter.cs` (balancing block + `PreMeasureTotalSerialExtent` helper + `DiscardingMeasureSink`), `docs/deferrals.md` (`multicol-balancing-pagination` Status updated; "Column balancing" Missing bullet replaced with sub-cycle 2+ deferrals for `balance-all` last-fragmentainer semantics + balancing with explicit height; new owner-files entry), and the 2 test files. **Cycle 3 sub-cycle 2+ scope:** `column-fill: balance-all` last-fragmentainer semantics (content fragmented across pages); column balancing with explicit `height` (over-shrink-tolerant algorithm); `column-width` → auto column count derivation; `column-span: all`; column-rule paint; `column-gap: normal` font-relative resolution; break-before-column / break-after-column / `break-inside: avoid-column`. Active-task pointer advances to **Task 14 cycle 4** (column-width-derived auto count OR column-span: all) OR **Task 15** (`FlexLayouter` L1 single-line) depending on review priority.)

**Phase 3 Task 14 post-PR-#57 review #2 hardening — 3-finding correctness + docs/test cleanup on top of the cycle 2 + 5-finding hardening** (historical entry; superseded by Task 14 cycle 3 Hello World above; [PR #58](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/58) merged at `cd593af`.) Continues from Task 14 cycle 2 + 5-finding hardening ([PR #57](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/57) merged at `8f7788f`). Roland's second review of PR #57 surfaced 3 findings; this entry covers their fixes in a focused follow-up PR. **Finding #1 (P1) — chain-flatten correctness fix.** The cycle 2 hardening's top-level recursion-return wrap at `BlockLayouter.cs:1993` (and forced-overflow path at `1674`) used `LayouterState: deepRet.LayouterState ?? deepRet` to flatten the chain by one layer — preserving the cycle-1 protocol shape for depth==1 cases. The flatten silently DROPPED the recursion's wrap layer, which carried the `ResumeAtChild` index of the intermediate container (e.g., for `<body><spacer/><multicol/>`, the flatten dropped the "body in root" layer; the inner `BC(rc=1 [multicol in body], ls=Mc)` would then be interpreted against the wrong child list on resume, miss its target, and the multicol would restart from column 0 on page 2 — duplicating page-1 content). The hardcoded `ResumeAtChild=0` re-wrap branches at `BlockLayouter.cs:1955-1960` (top-level switch) and `BlockLayouter.cs:2722-2738` (recursion chain-unwrap) compounded the issue: when the flatten produced a chain shorter than DOM depth, those branches re-wrapped Table/MulticolContinuation leaves with `rc=0`, which happened to work only when the leaf was at idx 0 in its parent. The reviewer flagged that existing resume-chain tests at `MulticolLayouterTests.cs:1563-1568` and `TableLayouterTests.cs:6500-6503` used `rc=0` chains throughout, so the bug was untested. Fix: (a) remove the flatten — top-level and forced-overflow paths now use `LayouterState: deepRet` directly, preserving the full DOM-depth chain; (b) remove the hardcoded-rc=0 leaf-re-wrap branches — the chain now always has the leaf's parent BC layer with the correct rc, so re-wrap is unnecessary (and silently misroutes if applied); (c) add `var startIdx = incomingBlockChain?.ResumeAtChild ?? 0;` to the recursion's for loop at `BlockLayouter.cs:2222` — pre-fix, even if the chain routed correctly the recursion would re-emit children at indices `[0, ResumeAtChild)` (because the loop always started at 0); the new startIdx mirrors the top-level `AttemptLayout` loop's `startChildIdx`. 2 new regression tests pin the non-zero-intermediate-index resume contract: `Cycle2_multicol_at_non_first_position_in_parent_resumes_correctly` (multicol at body idx 1 with a spacer at idx 0) and `Cycle2_table_at_non_first_position_in_parent_resumes_correctly` (same shape for tables); both assert (i) the chain shape has the correct intermediate-index BC layer + (ii) on page 2 the spacer is NOT re-emitted + the multicol/table resumes at the correct NextChildIndex/NextRowIndex. 2 existing tests updated: `Cycle2_production_multicol_at_depth_3_splits_cleanly` now asserts a 4-layer BC > BC > BC > MulticolContinuation chain (was 3-layer assumption from the pre-fix flatten); `Cycle2_table_resume_chain_routes_back_to_inner_layouter` now constructs a 4-layer BC > BC > BC > TableContinuation chain (was 3-layer pre-fix). **Finding #2 (P2) — docs cleanup.** Pre-fix, `PaginateDiagnosticCodes.cs:219-231`, `DiagnosticCodes.cs:393-406`, and `docs/diagnostics-codes.md:122` still listed the deep-nested branch (b) of `LAYOUT-MULTICOL-FORCED-OVERFLOW-001` even though that branch was removed in the cycle 2 hardening Finding #1's multi-level continuation propagation lift. All three sites updated to describe only the surviving forward-progress safety fallback for single-oversized-child resume pages. **Finding #3 (P2) — rewind test gap.** `Deep_nested_table_rewind_preserves_wrapper_state` at `TableLayouterTests.cs:6700+` previously stopped after page-1 assertions and did NOT exercise the resume path. The test now drives a page-2 attempt with the page-1 continuation and asserts (a) row 3 emits, (b) wrapper-count on page 2 is exactly 1, (c) no `PAGINATION-FORCED-OVERFLOW-001` was emitted on either leg — pinning chain routing across page boundaries. Tests: **4375 unit / 4506 solution-wide passing** (+2 unit / +2 solution-wide over PR #57 baseline at 4373 / 4504 — 2 new regression tests; 1 existing test extended in-place; 4 skipped). All 4 gates green: build (0 warnings, 0 errors), test, AOT/JIT byte-parity, `git diff --check` clean. **Diff:** ~120 net insertions across `BlockLayouter.cs` (Finding #1 code fix), `MulticolLayouterTests.cs` (new test + chain-shape comment), `TableLayouterTests.cs` (new test + extended test + chain construction update), `MulticolLayouterProductionTests.cs` (4-layer chain assertion), `PaginateDiagnosticCodes.cs` + `DiagnosticCodes.cs` + `docs/diagnostics-codes.md` (docs cleanup). Active-task pointer advances unchanged to **Task 14 cycle 3** — column balancing OR `column-width`-derived auto column count — OR **Task 15** — `FlexLayouter` L1 single-line — depending on review priority.)

**Phase 3 Task 14 cycle 2 + 5-finding hardening shipped — multi-page multicol via `MulticolContinuation`, with multi-level recursion-continuation propagation lifted for both `MulticolLayouter` AND `TableLayouter`** (historical entry; superseded by Task 14 post-PR-#57 review #2 hardening above; [PR #57](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/57) merged at `8f7788f`.) Continues from Task 14 cycle 1 + hardening ([PR #56](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/56) merged at `8f51100`). Cycle 2 ships **CSS Multi-column L1 §3.5 — fragmentation across pages**: when multicol content exceeds N × column-block-size, the outer container fragments across pages via `MulticolContinuation` instead of truncating with a forced-overflow diagnostic; the resume side unpacks `MulticolContinuation.PerChildLayouterState` as the FIRST column's `incomingContinuation` so content resumes at the exact child the prior page deferred at — parallels Task 13 cycle 1's row-pagination pattern for tables. Post-ship review (5 findings: 2 P1, 3 P2) drove the hardening in this same PR (#57). **Finding #1 (P1) — multi-level recursion-continuation propagation lifted (architectural):** cycle 2 originally shipped with `EmitBlockSubtreeRecursive`'s depth==1-only callback pattern (mirroring Task 13 cycle 2's `onTablePageComplete` / `onMulticolPageComplete` hooks). Real HTML `html > body > div.multicol` is depth 2; the original cycle 2 emitted `LAYOUT-MULTICOL-FORCED-OVERFLOW-001` and truncated. Roland's review elected to lift this limit NOW rather than continue the documented sub-cycle 3+ deferral, and to do so symmetrically for TableLayouter (which had the IDENTICAL depth==1-only limit from Task 13 cycle 2 hardening, tracked under `docs/deferrals.md#table-auto-fixed-spans-borders`'s "Deeper-nesting recursion-continuation propagation"). Refactor: `EmitBlockSubtreeRecursive` changes from `void` with 4 depth-gated callback args (`incomingTableContinuationAtDepth1`, `onTablePageComplete`, `incomingMulticolContinuationAtDepth1`, `onMulticolPageComplete`) to `LayoutContinuation?` return-based contract with a single `incomingContinuation` arg. **Routing protocol (down):** the recursion walks `BlockContinuation` chains downward — `BlockContinuation(rc=k, ls=BlockContinuation(rc=0, ls=TableContinuation))` passes the inner `BlockContinuation` as `incomingContinuation` to depth+1; leaf-kind continuations (Table/Multicol) get unwrapped at their owning layouter's dispatch site. **Stitching (up):** each level wraps non-null returns into a fresh `BlockContinuation(ResumeAtChild=childIdx, ConsumedBlockSize=0, LayouterState=<returned>)`; the depth==0 top-level dispatch fills in real `ConsumedBlockSize` and applies a `LayouterState ?? deepRet` flatten that preserves cycle-1 protocol back-compat for depth==1 cases. `NoBreakBreakResolver` is no longer used for depth>=2 nested tables (the class stays — captions still use it); the propagating resolver flows through any depth, with TableLayouter's own forward-progress guard (single-oversized-row forced-overflow at `TableLayouter.cs:3490+`) preventing infinite loops. `useDryRunCommittedHeight: true` added at the nested-table pre-measure site (`BlockLayouter.cs:2419`) AND at `MeasureNestedTableContentExtent` (so the outer subtree-measure also reports per-page committed extents — pre-fix the outer pre-measure saw full natural table extent and triggered `PAGINATION-FORCED-OVERFLOW-001` even though the deep table now splits cleanly). `AttemptLayout` entry validators relaxed to accept `LayouterState is BlockContinuation` (the recursion-chain case) with a chain-depth cap at `MaxRecursionDepth=256` (DoS guard for malformed pathological chains; new test `MaxRecursionDepth_chained_continuation_throws_or_truncates` pins this). Float-helper recursion sites (`EmitNestedFloat`, `EmitFloat`) DISCARD their non-null returns and emit a one-shot-per-page `LAYOUT-FLOAT-BREAK-INSIDE-NESTED-001` warning — floats remain atomic per the Phase 3 Task 8 cycle 3+ float-continuation deferral; new `docs/deferrals.md#float-continuation-propagation` entry tracks. Deleted: the `LAYOUT-MULTICOL-FORCED-OVERFLOW-001` deep-nested-truncation emission block at `BlockLayouter.cs:2659-2673` (the diagnostic code itself stays defined; it now ONLY fires from MulticolLayouter's no-forward-progress guard at `MulticolLayouter.cs:610-633`) + the `NoBreakBreakResolver` else-branch at `BlockLayouter.cs:2771-2793`. **Finding #2 (P1) — `MulticolContinuation` invariant validation tightened:** `MulticolLayouter` constructor adds 4 fail-fast checks at `MulticolLayouter.cs:255-326` (mirroring `TableLayouter.cs:300-319`'s `ArgumentOutOfRangeException` pattern): `ConsumedBlockSize` finite + non-negative; `PerChildLayouterState` is null OR `BlockContinuation` only; terminal index (`NextChildIndex == Children.Count`) requires `PerChildLayouterState is null` (producer-bug guard); when `PerChildLayouterState is BlockContinuation bc`, `bc.ResumeAtChild == NextChildIndex` (symmetric-index guard). 5 new negative tests cover each invariant. **Finding #3 (P2) — column-count clamp surfaced:** the silent `MaxColumnCount=1000` clamp at `MulticolLayouter.cs:330` now emits `LAYOUT-MULTICOL-COLUMN-COUNT-CLAMPED-001` Warning at `MulticolLayouter.cs:402-432` naming the requested + clamped values + DoS rationale; new code registered in `PaginateDiagnosticCodes` + public `DiagnosticCodes` mirror + `docs/diagnostics-codes.md` registry row + 3 parity tests + 1 integration test (`Multicol_with_excessive_column_count_clamps_and_emits_diagnostic`). **Finding #4 (P2) — weak oversized-child test split:** the loose `AllDone or PageComplete` assertion at `MulticolLayouterTests.cs:1032-1122` replaced with 3 deterministic tests mapping to the 3 production paths (oversized-first-page → `PageComplete` + NO diagnostic; resume-with-no-forward-progress pinned as a "no spurious emission" guard since cycle 2's normal paths can't trigger the in-MulticolLayouter forced-overflow emission directly — the path requires deep-nested triggering pinned by `MulticolLayouterProductionTests`; resume-with-partial-progress → `PageComplete` + NO diagnostic). **Finding #5 (P2) — `MulticolGeometryHelper` extracted:** private static helper class at `BlockLayouter.cs:4697-4811` with `ContentBox` record + `ComputeContentGeometry` method consolidates the 4 duplicated multicol content-box geometry sites (outer dispatch ~1724, recursion dispatch ~2552, premeasure outer ~1216, premeasure recursion ~2474); pure mechanical extraction, byte-identical behavior verified by the full test suite passing with NO test deltas from F#5 alone. **Tests flipped (2):** `Cycle2_production_multi_page_multicol_via_full_pipeline` at `MulticolLayouterProductionTests.cs:254-344` — old pin (asserted `hasForcedOverflow == true` + `itemFragmentCount >= 2` for truncation) inverted to assert clean multi-page split (no diagnostic + `PageComplete` continuation chain shape). `Cycle1_production_multi_page_table_does_not_crash_full_pipeline` at `TableLayouterProductionTests.cs:788-855` — old pin (asserted all 3 rows committed atomically with `PAGINATION-FORCED-OVERFLOW-001`) inverted to assert page-1 rowCount=2 + clean `PageComplete` with chained `TableContinuation`. **Tests added (9):** `Cycle2_production_multicol_at_depth_3_splits_cleanly` (direct construction); `Cycle2_production_multicol_via_html_body_splits_cleanly` (positive replacement for the flipped pin); `Cycle2_multicol_resume_chain_routes_back_to_inner_layouter` (resume-side chain routing); `Cycle2_production_table_at_depth_3_splits_cleanly`; **Phase 3 Task 14 cycle 2 shipped — multi-page multicol via `MulticolContinuation`** (historical entry; superseded by Task 14 cycle 2 + 5-finding hardening above; both bundled in [PR #57](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/57).) Continues from Task 14 cycle 1 + hardening ([PR #56](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/56) merged at `8f51100`). Cycle 1 shipped Hello World multi-column layout + the cycle 1 hardening REJECTED non-null `MulticolContinuation` at the constructor as a forward-progress safety check. Cycle 2 ships **CSS Multi-column L1 §3.5 — fragmentation across pages**: when multicol content exceeds N × column-block-size, the outer container now fragments across pages via `MulticolContinuation` instead of truncating with a forced-overflow diagnostic. This parallels Task 13 cycle 1's row-pagination work for tables (single-table multi-page). **`MulticolContinuation` final shape:** `record (int NextChildIndex, double ConsumedBlockSize = 0.0, object? PerChildLayouterState = null)`. `NextChildIndex` names the multicol child where content emission resumes; `PerChildLayouterState` is the opaque mirror of `LayoutContinuation.LayouterState` — carries the LAST column's overflowing `BlockContinuation` so the FIRST column on the resumed page resumes that nested layouter at the exact spot. **Algorithm:** on `AttemptLayout` entry, when `_incomingContinuation is MulticolContinuation mc`, `resumeAtChild = mc.NextChildIndex` + `priorConsumedBlock = mc.ConsumedBlockSize` + the first column gets `mc.PerChildLayouterState` as `incomingContinuation` to its nested `BlockLayouter`. The column-emit loop proceeds normally. When the LAST column overflows (cycle 1 truncated), cycle 2 instead returns `PageComplete(MulticolContinuation(NextChildIndex: <captured>, ConsumedBlockSize: <updated>, PerChildLayouterState: <captured-inner>))`. **Constructor accepts MulticolContinuation:** cycle 1 hardening Finding 5's rejection is relaxed; cycle 2 accepts MulticolContinuation as resume state, rejects other kinds (mirrors TableLayouter's pattern). `_incomingContinuation` field re-introduced. **BlockLayouter dispatch / propagation:** mirrors Task 13 cycle 1's `BlockContinuation.LayouterState = TableContinuation` pattern. The main-loop dispatch wraps `PageComplete(MulticolContinuation)` into `PageComplete(BlockContinuation(ResumeAtChild=multicolChildIdx, LayouterState=MulticolContinuation))`. Resume side: `incomingBlock.LayouterState is MulticolContinuation` → pass to `MulticolLayouter` via constructor. New `_consumedIncomingMulticolContinuation` one-shot flag prevents siblings inheriting it. **Recursion-continuation propagation extended (cycle 2 originally):** `EmitBlockSubtreeRecursive`'s Task 13 cycle 2 hardening Finding 1 callback pattern (`onTablePageComplete` for tables) extended to also handle MulticolContinuation — new `onMulticolPageComplete` callback. Single-level depth==1 propagation only at cycle-2 ship time; deeper nesting (real HTML `html > body > div.multicol` is depth 2) emitted the diagnostic to surface the truncation — deliberate cycle 3+ deferral. (NOTE: this single-level limit was LIFTED in the cycle 2 hardening above — see the superseding entry.) Mirrors the `Cycle1_production_table_as_root_child_splits_cleanly_at_outer_path` pattern from Task 13. **Diagnostic semantics narrowed:** `LAYOUT-MULTICOL-FORCED-OVERFLOW-001` from cycle 1 was emitted for ANY content overflow. Cycle 2 SUPPRESSES it for clean multi-page splits (no longer an "error"). At cycle-2 ship time the diagnostic still fired when: (a) MulticolLayouter resume-page makes no forward progress (single-child block taller than per-page multicol block-size — mirrors TableLayouter single-row-oversize); (b) deep-nested multicol whose `PageComplete` can't propagate (depth ≥ 2 recursion fallback). (NOTE: branch (b) was REMOVED in the cycle 2 hardening above when multi-level propagation was lifted — only branch (a) survives.) Updated `docs/diagnostics-codes.md` row + `PaginateDiagnosticCodes` doc-comment to reflect narrower semantics. Tests: **4349 unit / 4480 solution-wide passing** (+10 unit / +10 solution-wide over PR #56 baseline at 4339 / 4470 — 8 new direct cycle 2 tests + 2 new production tests; 2 cycle 1 tests renamed/rewritten to cycle 2 contract; 4 skipped). New direct tests in [`MulticolLayouterTests`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Phase3/MulticolLayouterTests.cs): overflow returns PageComplete with continuation; resume round-trip emits all content across 2 pages; constructor accepts MulticolContinuation (cycle 1 rejection inverted); continuation kind validation; no-overflow no-continuation; overflow diagnostic suppressed on clean split; cancellation on resume; resumeAtChild=0 equivalent to first page; single-oversized-child forced-overflow fallback. **Phase 3 Task 14 cycle 1 shipped + post-PR-#56 review hardening — `MulticolLayouter` Hello World with columnized-extent outer cursor advance, auto-height multicol from fragmentainer remaining, validated multicol property values, non-finite geometry guard, `MulticolContinuation` rejection until sub-cycle 2, and 6 review findings + 4 Copilot inline comments + Finder-copy artifact cleanup** (historical entry; superseded by Task 14 cycle 2 above. [PR #56](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/56) opened at `7304ce7`; this hardening updates the same branch in-place. **Post-PR-#56 review hardening (6 findings, 2 P1 + 3 P2 + 1 P3, plus 4 Copilot perf/cleanup + Finder-copy artifact cleanup):** (1) [P1 #1] **Outer cursor advance uses columnized extent** — pre-hardening, `BlockLayouter` measured the multicol child via normal recursive block flow (`MeasureSubtreeVisualBlockExtentRecursive`), then advanced `UsedBlockSize` with the serial subtree extent. A 2-column container with two 90px children + height 100px reserved ~180px (serial sum) instead of ~90px (columnized) — false blank space + wrong page breaks for siblings after multicol. Fix: new `PreMeasureMulticolColumnExtent` helper (mirrors `PreMeasureTableIfNeeded`) does a dry-run multicol layout into a `MulticolDiscardingMeasureSink` that captures max(BlockOffset + BlockSize) across all emitted fragments (the columnized extent = the longest column's bottom edge, anchored at 0,0 in the discarding sink's coordinate space so the returned value is column-relative). Two integration points: (a) `MeasureSubtreeVisualBlockExtentRecursive` returns the columnized extent for multicol parents (fixes outer cursor advance); (b) the dispatch site uses the pre-measure to grow `borderBoxBlockSize` so the wrapper's PAINTED fragment also reflects columnized content (mirrors table wrapper auto-height fold-in). Cost: 2× per multicol container (measure + emit); cycle 2+ may cache. New regression: `Multicol_followed_by_paragraph_does_not_overlap` direct test + `Production_multicol_followed_by_paragraph_no_overlap` full-pipeline analog. (2) [P1 #2] **Auto-height multicol derives column size from fragmentainer remaining** — pre-hardening, `BlockLayouter.cs:1600`'s `contentBlockSize` came from `borderBoxBlockSize`; for `height: auto`, that resolved to 0 → MulticolLayouter clamped to 1px → multicol immediately force-overflowed. Cycle 1 production test only worked because it set `height: 100px`. Fix: new `IsHeightAuto(Box)` predicate reads `box.Style.Get(PropertyId.Height).Tag != ComputedSlotTag.LengthPx` — the `LengthResolver` resolves `auto` to a Keyword slot (`Tag = Keyword`) vs explicit `0px` resolves to `LengthPx` with value 0, so the tag check cleanly distinguishes auto vs explicit zero. When `IsHeightAuto(multicolContainer)`, derive the per-column block-size from `fragmentainer.BlockSize - blockOffset - wrapper's vertical border+padding`. Applied at THREE sites (pre-measure block-size, main-loop dispatch's emit block-size, recursion dispatch's emit block-size) so measure + emit produce consistent geometry. New tests: `Multicol_auto_height_derives_column_size_from_fragmentainer_remaining` + `Production_multicol_without_explicit_height_renders_full_column_space`. (3) [P2 #3] **Invalid multicol values validated** — pre-hardening, `column-count: 0` / negative integers were silently accepted (NumberResolver didn't enforce positive); `column-gap` / `column-width` weren't in `NonNegativeProperties`. Fix: `NumberResolver` (line 61 area) extended to enforce `column-count` as positive integer → values `< 1` emit `CSS-PROPERTY-VALUE-INVALID-001` + fall back to `auto` (MulticolLayouter dispatch doesn't fire); `NonNegativeProperties` extended with `ColumnWidth` + `ColumnGap` so negative values fall back to default + emit the invalid diagnostic. New resolver tests for `column-count: 0` / `-5` + `column-gap: -10px` + `column-width: -50px`. (4) [P2 #4] **Non-finite geometry guard** — pre-hardening, `MulticolLayouter.cs:286`'s `perColumnInlineSize` was clamped, but `totalGap` + `columnInlineOffset` weren't finite-guarded; `column-gap: 1e308` × 100 columns = `Inf`. Fix: explicit `double.IsFinite` checks; when `totalGap` is non-finite, clamp to `containerInlineSize / 2` (so `totalGap < half-container`); `columnInlineOffset[c]` finite-check is a no-op in practice after the gap clamp but defends future operand changes. New `LAYOUT-MULTICOL-NON-FINITE-GEOMETRY-001` Warning emitted at the clamp site + 3 parity tests. New test: `Multicol_with_non_finite_column_gap_clamps_and_emits_diagnostic`. (5) [P2 #5] **`MulticolContinuation` rejected at constructor** — pre-hardening, constructor accepted a `MulticolContinuation` but `AttemptLayout` never read it → accidental resume restarted from column 0 (duplicates/drops content). Fix: constructor now throws `ArgumentException` when `incomingContinuation is MulticolContinuation`; mirrors the cycle 1 `TableLayouter` pattern. The unused `_incomingContinuation` field had to be removed entirely (not just set null) to satisfy the 0-warnings build gate. Sub-cycle 2 will re-introduce when multi-page multicol lands. New test: `Multicol_rejects_non_null_continuation_until_subcycle_2`. (6) [P3 #6] **Compatibility matrix marked partial** — `docs/compatibility-matrix.md:43` updated from "supported" to "partial/approximated" with link to `docs/deferrals.md#multicol-balancing-pagination`. **Plus Copilot 4 stale-docs/inaccuracy fixes**: Copilot #1 — XML doc at MulticolLayouter.cs:82 referenced non-existent `ReadColumnWidth` extension; corrected to `ReadColumnGap` / `ReadColumnCount`. Copilot #2 — XML doc at MulticolLayouter.cs:195 said "When content overflows the FIRST column the layouter advances to the next" but the implementation advances when ANY non-last column overflows; doc rewritten accurately. Copilot #3 — `docs/diagnostics-codes.md:121` claimed the LAYOUT-MULTICOL-FORCED-OVERFLOW-001 message "names ... the leftover content extent" but the emitted message didn't include that; doc aligned with actual message. Copilot #4 — PROGRESS.md:10 claimed constructor required `>= 2` but impl accepts `>= 1` (BlockLayouter bypasses for 1); entry updated to accurately describe the constructor's `>= 1` predicate + dispatch's `>= 2` gate as distinct contracts. **Plus Finder-copy artifact cleanup**: removed 15+ untracked `* 2.md` / `* 2.cs` / `* 2.json` files (macOS Finder duplicates) from source + test directories that PR #56's `git status` showed in Roland's Finding 7. **Phase 3 Task 14 cycle 1 shipped — `MulticolLayouter` Hello World** (historical entry; superseded by hardening review above. Continues from Task 13 cycle 2 + hardening ([PR #55](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/55) merged at `d1157b3`). Task 13 (multi-page row splitting + `<thead>`/`<tfoot>` repetition) closed out the table layout pipeline for typical invoices; Task 14 opens **CSS Multi-column Layout L1** per the Phase 3 plan §"MulticolLayouter". Cycle 1 ships **Hello World multi-column layout** for the most common case: a block container with `column-count: N` splits its in-flow content equally across N parallel columns, each acting as a sub-fragmentainer. **New types in [`src/NetPdf.Layout/Layouters/`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Layouters/):** [`MulticolLayouter`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Layouters/MulticolLayouter.cs) — `internal sealed class : ILayouter, IDisposable` (489 LOC). Constructor signature mirrors `BlockLayouter`/`TableLayouter`: `(rootBox, sink, incomingContinuation: null, diagnostics: null, shaperResolver: null)` where `rootBox` MUST satisfy `Style.ReadColumnCount() >= 1` (the constructor's predicate is `>= 1` so direct-construction tests of the `column-count: 1` edge case work + so future sub-cycles with `column-width`-derived counts that round to 1 can construct a layouter; the `BlockLayouter` dispatch gate that decides whether to invoke MulticolLayouter at all is the stricter `>= 2` — `column-count: 1` lays out as a normal block per the locked design — validates + throws `ArgumentException` otherwise). Plus internal `ColumnFragmentSink` decorator that translates each emitted fragment's `InlineOffset` by `c * (columnInlineSize + columnGap)` so per-column content lands at the correct column origin. Plus a reserved `MulticolContinuation` record in `src/NetPdf.Paginate/LayoutContinuation.cs` (cycle 2+ work — not produced by cycle 1). **Algorithm:** (1) Read `column-count: N` (clamp `[1, 1000]`) + `column-gap: <length>` (default 16px via cycle 1 hard-code; `normal` keyword resolves via cycle 2's font-size cascade). (2) Compute per-column inline size = `(containerContentInlineSize - (N-1) * columnGap) / N`. (3) For each column `c` in `[0, N)`: construct a sub-`FragmentainerContext` with `contentInlineSize = columnInlineSize` + `blockSize = containerContentBlockSize`; construct a nested `BlockLayouter` with `rootBox = _rootBox` (the multicol container) + a `ColumnFragmentSink` wrapping the outer sink with `inlineOffsetTranslation = c * (columnInlineSize + columnGap)`; lay out content into the column. When the nested BlockLayouter returns `PageComplete(BlockContinuation)`, the continuation describes "resume content emission at child index X" — captured for the next column. The next column's nested layouter is constructed with that continuation as `incomingContinuation`, picking up where the previous column left off. (4) Outer multicol box: emit ONE `BoxFragment` for the multicol container at the parent's allocated geometry — the columns' content fragments land INSIDE the multicol box (the parent BlockLayouter doesn't see the per-column structure). (5) **Cycle 1 overflow simplification**: if content overflows N columns, emit new `LAYOUT-MULTICOL-FORCED-OVERFLOW-001` Warning + truncate remaining content. Multi-page multicol (the outer multicol box fragmented across pages) is sub-cycle 2 work. **`BlockLayouter` integration:** new dispatch sites in BOTH the main `AttemptLayout` child-emit loop AND `EmitBlockSubtreeRecursive` (the recursion is needed because real HTML `<body><div class="multicol">...</div></body>` reaches multicol via the body-wrap recursion — verified by the production test, which would emit full-width content otherwise). When `child.Style.ReadColumnCount() >= 2`, dispatch through `MulticolLayouter` instead of laying out children directly. `column-count: 1` bypasses MulticolLayouter (predicate gates on `>= 2`) — content lays out as normal block flow. **CSS property pipeline:** added `column-count` / `column-width` / `column-gap` / `column-fill` / `column-rule-width` / `column-rule-style` / `column-rule-color` to `src/NetPdf.Css/properties.json`. `column-count` (Integer, default `auto`, NOT inherited); `column-gap` (Length, default `normal`, NOT inherited); `column-fill` (Keyword `auto | balance | balance-all`, default `balance`); `column-rule-style` (Keyword — border-style values). New per-property keyword paths in `KeywordResolver` + `LengthResolver` + `NumberResolver` for the `auto` / `normal` defaults (default-resolve previously hit `CSS-PROPERTY-VALUE-INVALID-001`). New `ReadColumnCount(this ComputedStyle) → int?` + `ReadColumnGap(this ComputedStyle) → double` extensions on `ComputedStyleLayoutExtensions`. **`column-gap` removed from RealDocuments `UnsupportedAllowlist`** (now supported). **New diagnostic** `LAYOUT-MULTICOL-FORCED-OVERFLOW-001` Warning added to `PaginateDiagnosticCodes` + `NetPdf/Diagnostics/DiagnosticCodes` + `docs/diagnostics-codes.md` + 3 parity tests. **Docs:** new `multicol-balancing-pagination` deferral entry in `docs/deferrals.md` documenting cycle 1 Behavior + sub-cycle 2+ Missing (column balancing, `column-span: all`, column rules paint, multi-page multicol, `column-width`-derived auto column count, `column-gap: normal` resolution via cascade, fragmentation interaction with `avoid-break`, per-column resolver isolation). `DeferralsParityTests` updated with the new ID. Tests: **4323 unit / 4454 solution-wide passing** (+15 unit / +15 solution-wide over PR #55 baseline at 4308 / 4439 — 11 direct `MulticolLayouterTests` + 1 production test + 3 diagnostic-codes parity tests; 4 skipped). AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green; `git diff --check` clean. New direct tests in [`MulticolLayouterTests`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Phase3/MulticolLayouterTests.cs): 2-column emit + outer wrapper; equal-split minus gaps; content distribution across columns; overflow → forced-overflow diagnostic; `column-count: 1` bypasses multicol; rejects invalid column counts (zero/negative); default gap = 16px; empty container emits outer only; cancellation observed; + 2 more pinning fragment count + ordering. New production test in [`MulticolLayouterProductionTests`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Phase3/MulticolLayouterProductionTests.cs): `<div style="column-count: 2; width: 200px;">` lays out content into 2 columns end-to-end through the full HTML → BoxBuilder → BlockLayouter pipeline. **Sub-cycle 2+ scope:** multi-page multicol (outer fragmented across pages via the reserved `MulticolContinuation`); column balancing (`column-fill: balance`); `column-width`-derived automatic column count; `column-span: all`; column rules paint (cycle 1 parses the cascade but doesn't paint); `column-gap: normal` resolving to 1em via cascaded font-size (cycle 1 hard-codes 16 px); fragmentation interaction with `avoid-break`; per-column resolver isolation for `break-inside: avoid-column`. Active-task pointer advances to **Task 14 cycle 2** — column balancing OR multi-page multicol, depending on review priority. Plus all remaining Task 12 sub-cycle 6+ items + Task 13 deeper-nesting recursion-continuation propagation deferrals.)

**Phase 3 Task 13 cycle 2 shipped + post-PR-#55 review hardening — `<thead>` / `<tfoot>` repetition with production-path recursion-continuation propagation, oversized header+footer skip-body policy, header/footer cell diagnostic flush-once, `RepeatHead`/`RepeatFoot` flags honored on resume, `<tfoot>`-before-`<tbody>` reordering in `CollectRows`, test rigor for row identity/order/offsets, and 7 review findings** (historical entry; superseded by Task 14 cycle 1 above. [PR #55](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/55) opened at `595a9f3`; this hardening updates the same branch in-place. **Post-PR-#55 review hardening (7 findings, 2 P1 + 4 P2 + 1 P3, plus 5 Copilot perf/cleanup):** (1) [P1 #1] **Production HTML path now exercises multi-page repetition** — pre-hardening, `<html><body><table>` recursion used `NoBreakBreakResolver` → atomic commit. Cycle 2's `<thead>`/`<tfoot>` repetition only worked in direct-construction tests. Same gap deferred by cycle 1's Finding 1. Fix: implemented **single-level recursion-continuation propagation** via the *forwarded-parameter + capturing-callback* approach. `EmitBlockSubtreeRecursive` accepts four optional parameters (`propagatingResolver`, `propagatingFragmentainer`, `incomingTableContinuationAtDepth1`, `onTablePageComplete`); when a depth-1 nested Table is found and propagation hooks are provided, the recursion uses the OUTER resolver (not `NoBreakBreakResolver`) and feeds any captured `TableContinuation` back through the callback. The main `AttemptLayout` Continue branch wraps the captured continuation in `BlockContinuation(ResumeAtChild=childIdx, LayouterState=tc)` and returns `PageComplete`. Validation relaxed (line 468-482) to allow `ResumeAtChild` to point at a block-flow container so the resume page walks INTO it. Single-level only: deeper nesting (`body > div > table`) still uses the atomic fallback. New production test `Cycle2_production_html_table_with_thead_tfoot_repeats_across_pages_via_full_pipeline` proves header/footer repeat end-to-end through the full pipeline. Deeper-nesting propagation documented as continued sub-cycle 6+ deferral. (2) [P1 #2] **Oversized header+footer branch enforces skip-body policy** — pre-hardening, `LAYOUT-TABLE-HEADER-FOOTER-OVERSIZED-001` diagnostic said body rows are skipped but flow continued into the body loop with a negative body budget (Copilot #1 caught the same). Fix: when `headerStackHeight + footerStackHeight > availableBlockSize`, emit headers + footers atomically and **return `LayoutAttemptResult.AllDone` WITHOUT entering the body loop** (the "skip body" policy). Test `Cycle2_table_with_header_and_footer_exceeding_fragmentainer_skips_body_rows` replaced the diagnostic-only assertion with assertions for NO body row fragments emitted + AllDone returned. (3) [P2 #3] **Header/footer cell diagnostics flushed once (Copilot #2 + #3)** — pre-hardening, header/footer cells emitted via `FlushKeepingBuffer` (preserves content for repeat) but `DiagnosticsBuffer` was never flushed. Fix: per-instance one-shot `_diagnosticsFlushedOnce: bool` flag set at construction for resume-page layouters (prior layouter already drained); first-page TableLayouter drains the diagnostics buffer once on its first header/footer emit. Resume pages do NOT re-emit the same diagnostics. New test `Cycle2_header_cell_diagnostics_flush_once_across_multi_page` pins the behavior. (4) [P2 #4] **`RepeatHead`/`RepeatFoot` flags honored on resume** — pre-hardening, the flags were SET on `PageComplete` but ignored on resume (TableLayouter resumed based only on measured header/footer counts). Fix: on resume, when `_incomingTableContinuation.RepeatHead == false`, DO NOT emit Phase A-pre headers; same for `RepeatFoot == false`. Default flow unchanged (continuations are built with `RepeatHead = (_headerRowCount > 0)` + `RepeatFoot = (_footerRowCount > 0)`); the flag is consulted on the resume side. Authors / future CSS opt-out paths can construct continuations with `false` flags. New test `Cycle2_continuation_with_repeathead_false_does_not_repeat_header`. (5) [P2 #5] **DP optimizer scope-limited per time-pressure guidance** — row pagination still streams `ConsiderBreakAt` (greedy fallback) rather than `ResolveBreaks` (bounded DP). Documented inline as sub-cycle 6+ TODO at `TableLayouter.cs:~1605`. The greedy path is correct for cycle 2's atomic-row semantics; the optimizer's benefit emerges with row-internal splitting + `break-inside: avoid` (also deferred). (6) [P2 #6] **Tests strengthened for row identity/order/offsets** — pre-hardening, cycle-2 tests counted `TableRow` fragments but didn't prove WHICH row repeated, footer-follows-body, or offset correctness. Fix: existing 11 cycle-2 tests strengthened in-place to assert fragment order (header before body before footer per page), source-box identity (same header Box appears in both pages' fragment lists when repeated), block offsets (header at rowStackOrigin; body starts at rowStackOrigin + headerStackHeight; footer at rowStackOrigin + headerStackHeight + bodyEmittedHeight), and page grouping. (7) [P3 #7] **Stale docs/XML cleanup** — TableLayouter.cs:155 + :167 + :195 + class doc thead/tfoot-deferred wording updated to reflect cycle 2's shipping. Remaining gaps centralized in `docs/deferrals.md`. **Plus Copilot extras:** Copilot #4 — unused `rowKinds` array at line 2374 removed (truly dead post-collection — only `headerCount`/`footerCount` are consumed). Copilot #5 — **PROGRESS.md / implementation claim about BoxBuilder reordering CORRECTED**. Verification confirmed Copilot is right: `GridLevelFixup` (`BoxBuilder.cs:1019`) preserves source order; it does NOT reorder `<tfoot>` to the end. The reordering happens INSIDE `TableLayouter.CollectRows` itself via 3-way partition into headers/bodies/footers buffers (assembled in headers → body → footers order). Critical fix because HTML5 allows `<tfoot>` before `<tbody>` in source order. New test `Cycle2_table_with_tfoot_before_tbody_in_source_renders_footer_at_end` pins the in-TableLayouter reordering. **Existing test update**: `Cycle1Hardening_Finding9_LayouterState_TableContinuation_on_non_table_child_throws` updated to use `FlexContainer` instead of `BlockContainer` (Finding 1 legitimately relaxes the validation for block-flow containers — they're now valid resume targets via the recursion-propagation path). AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green; `git diff --check` clean. **Sub-cycle 6+ scope (still deferred):** deeper-nesting recursion-continuation propagation (`body > div > table`); DP optimizer integration for table-row pagination; footer bottom-anchoring; row-internal splitting; spec-strict §11 rowspan distribution across pages; per-row checkpoint capture for `break-inside: avoid`; plus all remaining Task 12 sub-cycle 6+ items (border-collapse, percentages, etc.). Active-task pointer advances to **Task 14** — `MulticolLayouter` — OR **Task 12 sub-cycle 6** — border-collapse + percentage widths + spec-strict proportional-weight distribution, depending on review priority.)

**Phase 3 Task 13 cycle 2 shipped — `<thead>` / `<tfoot>` repetition at page boundaries** (historical entry; superseded by hardening review above. Continues from Task 13 cycle 1 + hardening ([PR #54](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/54) merged at `8c84c30`). Cycle 1 shipped row-level pagination via `TableContinuation`; the `RepeatHead` / `RepeatFoot` fields on the continuation were reserved for cycle 2. Cycle 2 ships **CSS Tables L3 §3.6 / §11 header + footer repetition**: when a `<thead>` (TableHeaderGroup) or `<tfoot>` (TableFooterGroup) exists in the source HTML, those rows now repeat at the top + bottom of EACH page where the table appears (not just page 1). **Row classification:** `CollectRows` extended to tag each row with its source group kind (`Header` / `Body` / `Footer`); rows from `TableHeaderGroup` get `Header`, rows from `TableFooterGroup` get `Footer`, all others (direct `TableRow` or `TableRowGroup` children) get `Body`. BoxBuilder's `GridLevelFixup` (`src/NetPdf.Layout/Boxes/BoxBuilder.cs:1019`) preserves source order — it does NOT reorder `<tfoot>` to the end of the row sequence. The reordering happens inside `TableLayouter.CollectRows` itself: after walking grid children in document order into per-kind buffers (`headers`, `bodies`, `footers`), the final row list is assembled in headers → body → footers order. This handles the HTML5 case where `<tfoot>` is declared before `<tbody>` in source. Per cycle 2 hardening Copilot #5 + new test `Cycle2_table_with_tfoot_before_tbody_in_source_renders_footer_at_end`. After collection: header rows occupy `[0, headerCount)`, body rows occupy `[headerCount, rows.Count - footerCount)`, footer rows occupy `[rows.Count - footerCount, rows.Count)`. **New fields:** `_measuredHeaderStackHeight` + `_measuredFooterStackHeight` cache the cumulative row heights for the header/footer slices — stable across pages since the same headers/footers repeat. **Per-page emit phases extended from 5 to 7 phases:** (Phase 0) top captions (first page only); (Phase A-pre) **header rows** (every page if `_headerRowCount > 0` — re-emitted at row stack origin on resume pages); (Phase A) **body rows** (cycle 1's row-pagination loop, but bounded to `[headerCount, rows.Count - footerCount)`); (Phase B / C) cells + content interleaved with body row emit; (Phase A-post) **footer rows** (every page if `_footerRowCount > 0` — emitted immediately after the last body row that fit on this page); (Phase D) bottom captions (last page only). **Body block budget reservation:** before the body-row pagination loop, `fragmentainer.UsedBlockSize = rowStackOrigin + headerStackHeight + footerStackHeight` — the body loop now sees the correct remaining space (excludes header above + footer reservation below). Body row chunk-size = body row height (unmodified); the resolver naturally sees overflow when adding the next body row would exceed `BlockSize - footerStackHeight`. After the body loop, `UsedBlockSize` is restored to `initialUsedBlockSize` so the outer BlockLayouter's cursor advance doesn't double-count. **Footer positioning:** footers emit IMMEDIATELY AFTER the last body row that fit on this page (NOT anchored at the absolute page bottom). This is the simpler "footer follows body" rendering; sub-cycle 3+ may add bottom-anchoring if needed (documented inline + in deferrals). **`RepeatHead` / `RepeatFoot` flags consumed:** on the first page (`_incomingTableContinuation == null`), `repeatHead` / `repeatFoot` are `false` (headers emit naturally as part of the row stack). When the body-row loop returns `PageComplete`, the new `TableContinuation` is built with `RepeatHead = (_headerRowCount > 0)` + `RepeatFoot = (_footerRowCount > 0)` — signals to the next page: "I have headers/footers that need to repeat". On the resume page, `_incomingTableContinuation.RepeatHead == true` triggers Phase A-pre fresh-emit of headers at the row-stack-origin; `RepeatFoot == true` triggers Phase A-post fresh-emit of footers after the last body row. **New diagnostic** `LAYOUT-TABLE-HEADER-FOOTER-OVERSIZED-001` Warning fires for the catastrophic case where `headerStackHeight + footerStackHeight > fragmentainer.BlockSize - rowStackOrigin` (no room for any body content); cycle 2 still emits the headers + footers but skips body rows on that page to avoid infinite-resume loops. New diagnostic added to `PaginateDiagnosticCodes` + `NetPdf/Diagnostics/DiagnosticCodes` + `docs/diagnostics-codes.md` + 3 parity tests. **Edge cases handled:** (a) no `<thead>` / `<tfoot>` → cycle 1 behavior preserved (`_headerRowCount = _footerRowCount = 0`; budget reservation no-ops). (b) header taller than fragmentainer → emit headers atomically + existing `PAGINATION-FORCED-OVERFLOW-001`. (c) footer taller than fragmentainer → similar. (d) header + footer combined > fragmentainer → new `LAYOUT-TABLE-HEADER-FOOTER-OVERSIZED-001`. (e) table with ONLY headers (no body) → emit headers + `AllDone`. (f) table with ONLY footers → symmetric. (g) body row taller than `availableBodyBlockSize` → existing forced-overflow path. (h) top captions on resume pages → cycle 1 behavior preserved (skipped). (i) bottom captions follow the footer on the last page. **Caveat:** under `<html><body><table>` the recursive-atomic fallback from cycle 1 Finding 1 keeps the table on a single page; cycle 2's per-page repetition is fully exercised by direct-construction unit tests + a direct-construction outer-path production test. Cycle 6+ may generalize `EmitBlockSubtreeRecursive` to propagate continuations end-to-end. Tests: **4304 unit / 4435 solution-wide passing** (+15 unit / +15 solution-wide over PR #54 baseline at 4289 / 4420 — 11 new direct cycle-2 tests + 1 new production test + 3 new diagnostic-codes parity tests; 4 skipped). New direct tests in [`TableLayouterTests`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Phase3/TableLayouterTests.cs): `Cycle2_table_with_thead_repeats_header_on_each_page`, `Cycle2_table_with_tfoot_repeats_footer_on_each_page`, `Cycle2_table_with_thead_and_tfoot_repeats_both`, `Cycle2_continuation_repeathead_repeatfoot_flags_set_correctly`, `Cycle2_no_thead_or_tfoot_preserves_cycle_1_behavior`, `Cycle2_table_with_only_thead_emits_only_headers`, `Cycle2_table_with_only_tfoot_emits_only_footers`, `Cycle2_table_with_oversized_header_emits_forced_overflow`, `Cycle2_table_with_header_and_footer_exceeding_fragmentainer_emits_diagnostic`, `Cycle2_top_caption_skipped_on_resume_pages`, `Cycle2_bottom_caption_emitted_only_on_last_page_after_footer`. New production test: `Cycle2_production_html_table_with_thead_tfoot_emits_header_and_footer_fragments` (pins recognition + emission through the full pipeline; under the body-wrap atomic fallback the multi-page repetition isn't exercised, but the header + body + footer rows all flow through BoxBuilder + emit as TableRow fragments). AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green; `git diff --check` clean. **Docs:** `docs/deferrals.md`'s `table-auto-fixed-spans-borders` entry's Behavior gains a paragraph describing the header/footer repeat algorithm; Missing drops "per-page header/footer repeat (Task 13)"; retains all the remaining sub-cycle 6+ items (border-collapse, percentages, spec-strict §11 rowspan, RTL, recursive continuation propagation, etc.). **Sub-cycle 3+ / sub-cycle 6+ scope (still deferred):** footer bottom-anchoring (cycle 2 emits footer immediately after last body row); recursive-emission continuation propagation past single-level (cycle 1 Finding 1 deferral); row-internal splitting; spec-strict §11 rowspan distribution-proportional algorithm across pages; per-row checkpoint capture for `break-inside: avoid` (cycle 1 Finding 5 deferral); plus all remaining Task 12 sub-cycle 6+ items (border-collapse, percentages, etc.). Active-task pointer advances to **Task 14** — `MulticolLayouter` — OR **Task 12 sub-cycle 6** — border-collapse + percentage widths + spec-strict proportional-weight distribution, depending on review priority.)

**Phase 3 Task 13 cycle 1 shipped + post-PR-#54 review hardening — multi-page row splitting in `TableLayouter` with outer wrapper fragment-aware sizing, zero-progress committed-non-row-content guard, per-row-window diagnostic flush, Rewind diagnostic, rowspan-crosses-page atomic-with-diagnostic, `ColumnLayoutCache` resume perf, `LayouterState` validation, and 10 review findings** (historical entry; superseded by Task 13 cycle 2 above. [PR #54](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/54) opened at `c900a15`; this hardening updates the same branch in-place. **Post-PR-#54 review hardening (10 findings, 3 P1 + 6 P2 + 1 P3, plus 6 Copilot perf/cleanup):** (1) [P1 #1] **Production HTML tables via `<html><body><table>`** — pre-hardening, the recursive `EmitBlockSubtreeRecursive` path forced `NoBreakBreakResolver` so all rows still emitted atomically; the cycle 1 production test only pinned "does not crash". Full recursion-level `LayoutAttemptResult` propagation was too risky for this sub-cycle's scope (touches recursion-emit semantics + would require generalized continuation chaining); per the locked design's contingency clause, took the documentation-only path: kept the nested-recursion atomic fallback (existing `NoBreakBreakResolver`) + added new direct-construction production test `Cycle1_production_table_as_root_child_splits_cleanly_at_outer_path` that exercises the OUTER dispatch path (table as root child, not nested under `<body>`). The pre-existing nested-atomic test is retained as a regression for the fallback. Single-level + deeper-nesting recursive propagation documented as continued sub-cycle 6+ deferral. (2) [P1 #2] **Outer wrapper fragment-aware sizing** — pre-hardening, `PreMeasureTableIfNeeded` returned the full natural table height; outer block wrapper sized + scored as if all rows belonged to the current page, emitting a false `PAGINATION-FORCED-OVERFLOW-001` even on clean splits. Fix: `PreMeasureTableIfNeeded` extended with a dry-run pagination pass — when natural height > available, also reports `CommittedRowsBlockSize` (the block extent of rows that DO fit + their captions/borders). Outer wrapper's emitted `BoxFragment.BlockSize` uses `CommittedRowsBlockSize` (not natural) when splitting. Forced-overflow diagnostic suppressed when split is clean; still fires for single-row oversize. `MeasureSubtreeVisualBlockExtentRecursive` clamps `subtreeBlockExtent` at the outer dispatch site so the recursive measure pass doesn't defeat Finding 2. (3) [P1 #3] **Zero-progress committed-non-row-content guard** — pre-hardening, forward-progress check `fragmentainer.UsedBlockSize == initialUsedBlockSize` was load-bearing on an UNCHANGED check, but the line bumps `UsedBlockSize` to `rowBlockOffsets[r]` for the resolver consult (Copilot #1 caught the same bug). Combined with table content starting after wrapper padding/border or top caption, an oversized first row could return `PageComplete(NextRowIndex: same row)` without emitting → infinite loop. Fix: explicit `_committedNonRowContent` flag tracks whether captions emitted on this page; emitted-rows counter tracks rows. PageComplete is safe iff `(r > resumeAtRow)` OR `(r == resumeAtRow AND _committedNonRowContent == true)`; else force-emit the row + emit forced-overflow diagnostic. (4) [P2 #4] **Per-row-window diagnostic flush** — pre-hardening, cell + caption diagnostic buffers flushed BEFORE the row-pagination loop; deferred rows' diagnostics emitted on the wrong page or duplicated. Fix: top-caption diagnostics flush at Phase 0 (first page only); per-row cell-content diagnostics flush inside `EmitRowWindow` AFTER each row commits (deferred rows' diagnostics stay buffered); bottom-caption diagnostics flush at Phase D (last page only). (5) [P2 #5] **`BreakAction.Rewind` diagnosed** — pre-hardening, the row loop silently treated Rewind as Continue. Fix: new `LAYOUT-TABLE-REWIND-NOT-SUPPORTED-001` Warning emitted when the resolver returns Rewind at a row boundary; fall back to Continue (current behavior preserved with explicit diagnostic). New diagnostic added to `PaginateDiagnosticCodes` + facade + docs + 3 parity tests. Per-row checkpoint support is Task 14+ scope. (6) [P2 #6] **Rowspan crossing page boundary** — pre-hardening, a `rowspan>1` cell whose origin row committed but whose span crossed the break was emitted with full height on the origin page; the continuation row later emitted without the spanning cell → visual overflow. Fix: detect when a break cuts through any rowspan cell; force break BEFORE the origin row so the rowspan cell stays atomic on the next page + emit new `LAYOUT-TABLE-ROWSPAN-CROSSES-PAGE-001` Warning naming the rowspan + row index. If forcing-before would be zero-progress, fall through to forced-overflow path. New diagnostic + 3 parity tests. (7) [P2 #7] **`NextRowIndex == rows.Count` OOR handled** — pre-hardening, validation allowed `NextRowIndex == rows.Count` (Copilot #2 caught the same) but `rowBlockOffsets[resumeAtRow]` was OOR. Fix: explicitly treat `NextRowIndex == rows.Count` as "all rows emitted; emit bottom captions if needed + return AllDone" without indexing. New direct validation test. (8) [P2 #8] **`ColumnLayoutCache` implemented for resume perf** — pre-hardening, `TableContinuation.ColumnLayoutCache` was null in practice; resume reconstructed the whole table measurement including auto-layout intrinsic passes — O(pageCount × totalRows × intrinsicMeasurementCost). Fix: populate cache on PageComplete with `MeasuredRows`, `ColumnWidths`, `ColumnOffsets`, `Placements`, `IntrinsicMeasurementCache`. On resume, check cache first + skip measurement entirely when present. The cache holds REFERENCES to existing `MeasuringFragmentSink` buffers (no deep cloning); deferred cells' buffers haven't flushed yet so they have content for page 2. Resume cost is now O(rows on this page) not O(total rows). (9) [P2 #9] **`LayouterState` validation** — pre-hardening, if `BlockContinuation.LayouterState is TableContinuation` but `ResumeAtChild` no longer pointed to a Table/InlineTable, the state was silently ignored. Fix: at AttemptLayout entry, when `_incomingBlockContinuation?.LayouterState is TableContinuation`, validate `_rootBox.Children[_incomingBlockContinuation.ResumeAtChild].Kind is Table or InlineTable`; throw `InvalidOperationException` otherwise. New direct test for the violation. (10) [P3 #10] **Stale docs / XML comment cleanup** — `TableLayouter.cs:157` class XML doc multi-fragmentainer-splitting-is-deferred wording updated to reflect cycle 1's row-pagination support; lines 167 + 195 + Copilot #4 + #5 + #6 stale `ResumeAtRowIndex` → `NextRowIndex` references corrected; `LayoutContinuation.cs:74-78` (Copilot #3) `TableContinuation` XML doc inaccuracies fixed; `BlockLayouter.cs:3716` (Copilot #6) inconsistent `Dispose()` comment rewritten; `PROGRESS.md:10` (Copilot #5) `ResumeAtRowIndex` → `NextRowIndex` fixed. **Two new diagnostic codes added** (LAYOUT-TABLE-REWIND-NOT-SUPPORTED-001 + LAYOUT-TABLE-ROWSPAN-CROSSES-PAGE-001) with 6 total parity tests. Tests: **4289 unit / 4420 solution-wide passing** (+16 unit / +16 solution-wide over PR #54 baseline at 4273 / 4404 — 12 new TableLayouter hardening tests + 1 new production test + 6 new diagnostic-codes parity tests; 4 skipped). AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green; `git diff --check` clean. **Cycle 2+ scope:** Task 13 cycle 2 — `<thead>`/`<tfoot>` repetition at page boundaries; recursive-emission continuation propagation past single-level (Finding 1 deferral); row-internal splitting; spec-strict §11 rowspan distribution across pages; per-row checkpoints for `BreakAction.Rewind` honoring. Plus all remaining Task 12 sub-cycle 6+ items. Active-task pointer advances to **Task 13 cycle 2** — `<thead>` / `<tfoot>` repetition at page boundaries.)

**Phase 3 Task 13 cycle 1 shipped — multi-page row splitting in `TableLayouter`** (historical entry; superseded by hardening review above. Continues from Task 12 sub-cycle 5 + hardening ([PR #53](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/53) merged at `f59e892`).
