Sub-cycle 5 closed out the core CSS Tables L3 §3 algorithm (Hello-World → spans → captions → fixed → auto); the table now correctly walks Table → TableGrid → row/group → cell, handles colspan + rowspan via 2D occupancy grid, lays out captions with full box model, computes column widths via fixed-layout (3-pass + Pass D reconciliation) OR auto-layout (shrink-to-fit via min/max-content), honors cell padding/border in intrinsic sizing, and treats `OverflowWrap.BreakWord` distinct from `Anywhere` for min-content correctness. **What was still missing**: when the table's row stack exceeded the fragmentainer's remaining block-size, `TableLayouter` emitted ALL rows on the current page + a `PAGINATION-FORCED-OVERFLOW-001` Warning — no actual multi-page row splitting; rows overflowed off the bottom of the page. Task 13 cycle 1 ships **row-level pagination**: rows that don't fit defer to the next page via the standard `LayoutAttemptResult.PageComplete` + continuation mechanism the rest of the layout system uses. This is the prerequisite for cycle 2's `<thead>` / `<tfoot>` repetition (which only makes sense for tables that span pages). **`TableContinuation` extended:** the existing `TableContinuation` record (in `src/NetPdf.Paginate/LayoutContinuation.cs`) gains `ConsumedBlockSize` field for cumulative-across-pages bookkeeping (the existing `RepeatHead` / `RepeatFoot` fields stay reserved for cycle 2). Named-only argument convention preserves backward compatibility for any future cycle-2 cache plumbing. **Algorithm:** `TableLayouter`'s constructor now accepts a `TableContinuation` via `incomingContinuation` (rejecting other kinds with `ArgumentException`); `_incomingTableContinuation` field stores it. In `AttemptLayout`: `resumeAtRow = _incomingTableContinuation?.NextRowIndex ?? 0`; `priorConsumedBlock = _incomingTableContinuation?.ConsumedBlockSize ?? 0`. **Phase 0 (top captions)** only emits when `resumeAtRow == 0` (first page); on resume pages, captions are skipped (already emitted on page 1). **Row-emit loop** (new `EmitRowWindow` helper): walks rows starting at `resumeAtRow`; for each row, bumps `fragmentainer.UsedBlockSize = rowBlockOffsets[r]` (the cumulative bottom edge); consults the resolver via `BreakOpportunity.Block`; on `BreakHere` returns `LayoutAttemptResult.PageComplete(new TableContinuation(NextRowIndex: rowIdx, ConsumedBlockSize: priorConsumedBlock + (rowBlockOffsets[r] - rowStackOrigin)))`; on `Continue` emits Phase A row + Phase B cells + Phase C content for that row; restores `initialUsedBlockSize` on return so the outer BlockLayouter's cursor advance doesn't double-count. **Phase D (bottom captions)** only emits on the LAST page (when the loop completes all rows without `BreakHere`). **Outer BlockLayouter integration:** `EmitTableInner` was previously `private static void`; now returns `LayoutAttemptResult` so callers see the table's PageComplete. `BlockLayouter`'s outer child-loop sniffs `incomingBlock.LayouterState is TableContinuation` once on resume + passes it through `PreMeasureTableIfNeeded` to the new `TableLayouter`. Uses the existing opaque `LayouterState : object?` slot on `BlockContinuation` (the field exists exactly for this case per Phase 3 review fix #7's doc — no new continuation subtype). New `_consumedIncomingTableContinuation` one-shot field ensures the continuation is consumed exactly once. **Nested-recursion atomic fallback:** `EmitBlockSubtreeRecursive` has no continuation-emission route (it walks descendants of an already-committed block), so `<html><body><table>` (the common BoxBuilder shape) routes the table through the recursion. Cycle 1 keeps nested tables atomic by promoting `NoBreakBreakResolver` from private (caption-internal use, sub-cycle 3 hardening) to internal + using it for the nested-recursion `EmitTableInner`; the forced-overflow diagnostic still fires for over-tall nested cases. Cycle 2+ generalize `EmitBlockSubtreeRecursive` to carry continuations. **Page-relative offset re-anchoring:** rather than recompute `rowBlockOffsets` from scratch on resume, AttemptLayout shifts all entries by `(rowBlockOffsets[resumeAtRow] - rowStackOrigin)` so the rest of the emit math (row offsets, cell anchors, prefix-sums) stays identical to page 1 (saves ~80 lines of duplicated arithmetic). **Single-oversized-row fallback:** if a row exceeds fragmentainer.BlockSize on a fresh page, the resolver's `LastResort` strategy returns `Continue` (forward progress); the row emits + overflows + existing `PAGINATION-FORCED-OVERFLOW-001` Warning still fires. Row-internal splitting is cycle 2+ scope. **Rowspan + multi-page**: rowspan cells stay atomic across pages — a rowspan cell that crosses a page boundary commits in full on its origin row's page + may overflow (CSS Tables L3 §11 strict rowspan-distribution is sub-cycle 6+). Tests: **4273 unit / 4404 solution-wide passing** (+9 unit / +9 solution-wide over PR #53 baseline at 4264 / 4395 — 8 new direct tests + 1 new production test + 1 existing `Table_oversized_for_fragmentainer` test updated to expect `PageComplete` (was `AllDone + overflow diagnostic`); 4 skipped). New direct tests in [`TableLayouterTests`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Phase3/TableLayouterTests.cs): `Table_with_multi_page_rows_splits_at_resolver_break_point`, `Table_continuation_round_trip_emits_all_rows_across_two_pages`, `Table_with_single_oversized_row_falls_back_to_forced_overflow`, `Table_top_caption_emits_only_on_first_page`, `Table_bottom_caption_emits_only_on_last_page`, `Table_continuation_validates_incoming_kind`, `Table_resume_at_row_index_skips_emitted_rows`, `Table_rejects_negative_or_out_of_range_resume_index`. New production test: `Cycle1_production_multi_page_table_does_not_crash_full_pipeline`. AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green; `git diff --check` clean. **Docs:** `docs/deferrals.md`'s `table-auto-fixed-spans-borders` entry's Behavior gains a multi-page-splitting paragraph; Missing drops "multi-fragmentainer row splitting"; retains row-internal splitting (cycle 2+), `<thead>`/`<tfoot>` repetition (cycle 2), nested-recursion continuations, and the existing sub-cycle 6+ items (border-collapse, percentages, spec-strict §11 rowspan, etc.). **Cycle 2+ scope:** Phase 3 Task 13 cycle 2 — `<thead>` / `<tfoot>` repetition at page boundaries (consume the existing `TableContinuation.RepeatHead` / `RepeatFoot` fields); row-internal splitting; nested-recursion continuation propagation; per-row checkpoint capture for `break-inside: avoid` support (cycle 1 ignores `BreakAction.Rewind`). Plus all remaining Task 12 sub-cycle 6+ items. Active-task pointer advances to **Task 13 cycle 2** — `<thead>` / `<tfoot>` repetition at page boundaries.)

**Phase 3 Task 12 sub-cycle 5 shipped + post-PR-#53 review hardening — `table-layout: auto` shrink-to-fit with direct-cell-text fix, `<col>`/first-row constraint feed-in, padding/border in intrinsic sizing, intrinsic-measurement budget, `OverflowWrap.BreakWord` distinct from `Anywhere`, wrapper/caption widening on overflow, and 7 review findings** (historical entry; superseded by Task 13 cycle 1 above. [PR #53](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/53) opened at `e995dce`; this hardening updates the same branch in-place. **Post-PR-#53 review hardening (7 findings, 4 P1 + 2 P2 + 1 P3, plus 2 Copilot perf/cleanup):** (1) [P1 #1] **Direct `<td>X</td>` text now measures** — pre-hardening, `MeasureCellContent` passed the TableCell as the BlockLayouter root, but `BlockLayouter` only lays out children + relies on `IsInlineOnlyBlockContainer(parent)` to dispatch inline content. `TableCell` was NOT a member of that predicate, so direct `TextRun` children of TableCells were skipped — common invoice HTML like `<td>Description</td>` contributed ZERO intrinsic width. Production tests had been working around this by wrapping cell text in `<div>`. Fix: BoxBuilder's `FixupAnonymousBlocks` now wraps inline-only TableCell children in `AnonymousBlock` (Option B from the locked design — Option A alone was insufficient because the predicate is called on the CHILD of `_rootBox`, not on `_rootBox` itself; for inline-only TableCells dispatched via `MeasureCellContent`, the child is a TextRun which isn't a block container regardless). The Option A predicate change is kept as defense-in-depth. 2 new production tests + the `<div>` workarounds in existing tests removed. (2) [P1 #2] **`<col>` widths feed into auto-layout as constraints** — pre-hardening, `ComputeColumnWidthsAuto` only used intrinsic content measurements; CSS Tables L3 §3 specifies author column/cell `width` constraints should be inputs to column min/preferred sizing. Fix: `ComputeColumnWidthsAuto` now calls the existing `CollectColumnsFromGridLevel` + `ApplyFirstRowCellWidths` first to capture `declaredColumnWidths` + `columnHasDeclared`; then `colMinContent[c] = max(intrinsic min, declaredColumnWidths[c])` + `colMaxContent[c] = max(intrinsic max, declaredColumnWidths[c])` when declared. The 3-branch distribution operates on the constraint-aware arrays. Tests replaced — `Auto_layout_keeps_existing_fixed_layout_behavior_intact` (which pinned the wrong behavior "auto ignores `<col>`") is gone; new tests pin the constraint interaction. (3) [P1 #3] **Cell padding + border in intrinsic sizing** — pre-hardening, `MeasureCellContent` passed full column width as inner content fragmentainer; `MaxInlineExtentFromCellOrigin` tracked only child content. TD padding/border should contribute to cell's min-content/max-content AND inset inner content. Fix: `MeasureCellContent` reads cell's box-model (padding + border per edge) via `ReadLengthPxOrZero`; inner fragmentainer inline-size = `max(1.0, cellInlineSize - inlineEdges)`; inner-content `MeasuringFragmentSink.inlineTranslation` includes `paddingInlineStart + borderInlineStart`; intrinsic min/max widths add back `inlineEdges` so column aggregation sees full cell extent. (4) [P1 #4] **Intrinsic-measurement budget** — pre-hardening, every cell ran 3 nested BlockLayouter passes (min speculative + max speculative + final). Large hostile tables amplified work 3×. Fix: new `MaxIntrinsicMeasurementOps = 10_000` budget tracked across `MeasureCellIntrinsicWidths` calls (2 ops per cell). Exceeded → emit new `LAYOUT-TABLE-INTRINSIC-MEASUREMENT-BUDGET-EXCEEDED-001` Warning + fallback: remaining cells get `minContent = 0, maxContent = contentInlineSize`. New diagnostic added to `PaginateDiagnosticCodes` + facade + docs + 3 parity tests. (5) [P2 #5] **`OverflowWrap.BreakWord` distinct from `Anywhere`** — pre-hardening, the materializer folded `overflow-wrap: break-word` AND `word-break: break-word` to `OverflowWrap.Anywhere`. Per CSS Text L3 §3.5, `anywhere` soft opportunities COUNT for min-content but `break-word` opportunities DON'T. Auto-layout's 1px min-content speculative wrap caused `break-word` cells to incorrectly shrink to glyph width. Fix: new `OverflowWrap.BreakWord` enum variant; materializer maps `overflow-wrap: break-word` AND `word-break: break-word` to `BreakWord` (not `Anywhere`); `LineBuilder.Wrap` accepts the new variant + treats it like `Anywhere` for normal line-wrap; new `intrinsicSizingMode: bool` parameter on `LineBuilder.Wrap` + `InlineLayouter.Layout` / `LayoutPerRun` downgrades `BreakWord` → `Normal` when true (no forced glyph-level wrap during min-content speculative). `TableLayouter.MeasureCellIntrinsicWidths` sets `BlockLayouter._intrinsicSizingMode = true` via new `SetIntrinsicSizingMode` setter before the min-content pass; BlockLayouter threads through to inline layouter calls. 2 new tests: anywhere reduces min-content; break-word does NOT. Migration impact: existing `InlineTextPolicyTests` + `InlineTextPolicyEndToEndTests` updated to assert the new `BreakWord` mapping. (6) [P2 #6] **Wrapper + caption widen on auto overflow** — pre-hardening, auto overflow set row/cell inline-size to min-content column sum (`MeasuredUsedInlineSize`), but BlockLayouter still emitted the outer Table wrapper at containing inline size + captions measured at wrapper content width. Backgrounds/borders/captions ended narrower than the actual grid. Fix: TableLayouter measures rows/cells first, computes `MeasuredUsedInlineSize`, THEN measures captions at the wider extent. `BlockLayouter.PreMeasureTableIfNeeded` returns `tableMeasuredUsedInlineSize` out param; when the measured used inline-size exceeds the wrapper's content-inline-size, the wrapper's emitted `BoxFragment.InlineSize` widens to `MeasuredUsedInlineSize + paddingInline + borderInline`. New tests pin wrapper + caption geometry consistency on overflow. (7) [P3 #7] **Stale docs / duplicate XML summary cleanup** — refreshed XML doc class summary at TableLayouter.cs:16-22 (was "splits columns equally" — both fixed + auto now implemented); stale auto-layout-as-future-work comment at 496-502; stale doc at 1125-1129; duplicate `<summary>` block on `ComputeColumnWidths` at 2070-2128. Remaining gaps centralized in `docs/deferrals.md`. **Plus Copilot inline cleanup**: deferrals.md:400 incorrectly claimed sub-cycle 4 hardening "wires `IsSet(Width)` to gate the fallback" — implementation actually kept the pre-fix behavior (cascade-aware was infeasible per the `ApplyDefaults` constraint); deferral entry updated to accurately describe what shipped. The other Copilot finding (MeasureCellIntrinsicWidths DoS — same as Roland's Finding 4) is addressed via the budget. **LayoutSnapshots:** `tests/NetPdf.LayoutSnapshots/Fixtures/03-table-with-caption/box-tree.txt` regenerated to reflect Finding 1's AnonymousBlock wrapping under TableCell (desired side-effect of the fix). Tests: **4264 unit / 4395 solution-wide passing** (+14 unit / +14 solution-wide over PR #53 baseline at 4250 / 4381 — 8 new TableLayouter tests + 4 new production tests + 1 replacement + 3 diagnostic-codes parity tests for the new budget diagnostic, minus 2 obsolete tests retired (the "auto ignores `<col>`" tests); 4 skipped). AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green; `git diff --check` clean. **Sub-cycle 6+ scope (still deferred):** CSS Tables L3 §3 spec-strict proportional-weight distribution (sub-cycle 5 uses linear interpolation); percentage column widths; cell intrinsic-width caching across re-layout passes (sub-cycle 5 measures fresh each time); §6.3 border-collapse model + `border-spacing`; §6.4 column-group widths beyond Pass A fallback; per-page header/footer repeat (Task 13); multi-fragmentainer row splitting; §11 spec-strict rowspan distribution-proportional algorithm; HTML5 `colspan="0"` / `rowspan="0"` remainder semantics; RTL writing modes / row reversal / caption inline-axis keyword routing; HTML width attribute cascade precedence (requires `ApplyDefaults` rework); block-level fixed-`width` children in cell intrinsic measurement + replaced-element intrinsic widths (sub-cycle 5 uses line-width signal only — block boxes use border-box fallback); `BlockLayouter::EmitBlockSubtreeRecursive` honoring child `width` declarations (orthogonal pre-existing gap). Active-task pointer advances to **Task 13** — `<thead>`/`<tfoot>` repetition across pages — OR **Task 12 sub-cycle 6** — border-collapse + percentage widths + block-level intrinsic-width refinement, depending on review priority.)

**Phase 3 Task 12 sub-cycle 5 shipped — `table-layout: auto` shrink-to-fit algorithm via min/max-content** (historical entry; superseded by hardening review above. Continues from Task 12 sub-cycle 4 + hardening ([PR #52](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/52) merged at `8222bdc`). Sub-cycle 4 shipped `table-layout: fixed` + `<col>` widths + Pass D reconciliation + 6-finding hardening; `table-layout: auto` (the default) was still equal-split — the most-visible deficiency for real invoices ("a table renders with equal columns when it shouldn't" per the deferral Trigger). Sub-cycle 5 ships **CSS Tables L3 §3 auto-table-layout** so column widths derive from each cell's intrinsic content size rather than naive equal-split. **Algorithm:** (1) **Per-cell intrinsic widths** — extended `MeasuringFragmentSink` with `MaxInlineExtentFromCellOrigin` property (tracked from each forwarded `BoxFragment`'s `InlineOffset + InlineSize`, but PREFERRING `InlineLayout.Lines[i].TotalAdvance` (actual shaped-text width) when the buffered fragment carries an inline layout — the cell's nested BlockLayouter recursion fills its border-box with the AVAILABLE width, so the line-width signal is the only way to differentiate min vs max for text content; block-level fixed-width content + replaced elements stay on the border-box fallback, documented as sub-cycle 6+ gap). New `MeasureCellIntrinsicWidths(cell, fragmentainer, layout, ct)` returns `(double MinContent, double MaxContent)` via TWO speculative cell-content layouts at `cellInlineSize = 1.0` (min) and `cellInlineSize = 1e6` (max); the buffered content is discarded after each measurement (no fragment emission). Defensive clamp in `MeasureCellContent`: `cellInlineSize < 1.0` clamps to 1.0 before constructing the inner `FragmentainerContext` (which rejects zero/negative widths) — empty cells legitimately produce `colMin = colMax = 0` so the prefix-sum yields zero. (2) **Per-column min/max aggregation** — for each column `colMinContent[c] = max(cell.minContent for cells with colspan=1 anchored at c)`, similarly for max-content. Colspan > 1 cells DISTRIBUTE their min/max-content across the spanned columns (deterministic equal-split of any excess — the §3 spec-strict proportional-weight allocation is approximated; documented inline + in deferrals). (3) **Table width determination** — `tableWidth = clamp(contentInlineSize, sum(colMinContent), sum(colMaxContent))`. (4) **3-branch distribution**: if `tableWidth >= sum(colMaxContent)`, give each column its max-content + distribute the extra (`tableWidth - sum(colMaxContent)`) equally across all columns; if `tableWidth <= sum(colMinContent)`, give each column its min-content + emit `LAYOUT-TABLE-INLINE-OVERFLOW-001` Warning (table overflows wrapper inline-axis); otherwise, linear interpolation — `widths[c] = colMinContent[c] + (tableWidth - sum(colMinContent)) * (colMaxContent[c] - colMinContent[c]) / (sum(colMaxContent) - sum(colMinContent))`. Floating-point tolerance `1e-9` on the saturated branch; degenerate `range ≈ 0` (all-equal-min-max) falls back to equal-split of excess. **`ComputeColumnWidthsAuto` method** called from `ComputeColumnWidths` when `mode == TableLayoutMode.Auto`. Caches intrinsic measurements alongside `_measuredColumnWidths` so emit doesn't re-measure. **Cancellation**: `MeasureCellIntrinsicWidths` + `ComputeColumnWidthsAuto` honor `CancellationToken` (per-cell + per-column checks). **Diagnostic reuse**: existing `LAYOUT-TABLE-INLINE-OVERFLOW-001` now fires under BOTH `table-layout: fixed` (declared sum > wrapper) AND `table-layout: auto` (min-content sum > wrapper); message rephrased generically (sub-cycle 4's overflow test still passes — it asserts the numeric content + columnsum substrings only). Tests: **4250 unit / 4381 solution-wide passing** (+10 unit / +10 solution-wide over PR #52 baseline at 4240 / 4371 — 8 new direct tests + 2 new production tests; 4 skipped). New direct tests in [`TableLayouterTests`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Phase3/TableLayouterTests.cs): `Auto_layout_short_content_uses_max_content_columns`, `Auto_layout_long_content_shrinks_to_min_content_when_table_too_narrow`, `Auto_layout_distributes_extra_above_max_content_equally`, `Auto_layout_columns_overflow_when_below_min_content`, `Auto_layout_colspan_cell_distributes_intrinsic_widths`, `Auto_layout_observes_cancellation_during_measurement`, `Auto_layout_linear_interpolation_between_min_and_max`, `Auto_layout_keeps_existing_fixed_layout_behavior_intact`. New production tests in [`TableLayouterProductionTests`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Phase3/TableLayouterProductionTests.cs): `Production_auto_layout_with_real_text_renders_per_content`, `Production_auto_layout_invoice_style_columns`. AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green; `git diff --check` clean. One pre-existing test (`Rowspan_2_cell_spans_two_rows`) implicitly depended on equal-split column behavior — updated to add block content to the span cell so auto-layout produces symmetric widths matching the original 200/200 expectation. **Docs:** `docs/deferrals.md`'s `table-auto-fixed-spans-borders` entry's Behavior section gains a paragraph describing the auto-layout algorithm; Missing section drops "§3 auto-table-layout"; retains percentage widths, border-collapse, header/footer repeat, multi-fragmentainer row splitting, spec-strict §11 rowspan, RTL writing modes, HTML width attribute cascade precedence (requires ApplyDefaults rework), block-level fixed-width child + replaced element intrinsic widths (sub-cycle 5 gap surfaced during implementation). **Sub-cycle 6+ scope (still deferred):** percentage column widths (CSS Tables L3 §17.5.2); block-level fixed-`width` children in cell intrinsic measurement + replaced-element intrinsic widths (sub-cycle 5 used line-width signal only — block boxes use border-box fallback); cell intrinsic-width caching across re-layout passes; §3 spec-strict proportional-weight distribution (sub-cycle 5 uses linear interpolation as an approximation); §6.3 border-collapse model + `border-spacing`; §6.4 column-group widths beyond Pass A fallback; per-page header/footer repeat (Task 13); multi-fragmentainer row splitting; §11 spec-strict rowspan distribution-proportional algorithm; HTML5 `colspan="0"` / `rowspan="0"` remainder semantics; RTL writing modes / row reversal / caption inline-axis keyword routing; HTML width attribute cascade precedence; `BlockLayouter::EmitBlockSubtreeRecursive` honoring child `width` declarations (orthogonal pre-existing gap). Active-task pointer advances to **Task 13** — `<thead>`/`<tfoot>` repetition across pages — OR **Task 12 sub-cycle 6** — border-collapse + percentage widths + block-level intrinsic-width refinement — depending on review priority.)

**Phase 3 Task 12 sub-cycle 4 shipped + post-PR-#52 review hardening — `table-layout: fixed` + `<col>` widths + Pass D column-sum reconciliation, first-row colspan partial-declare fixed, HTML width cascade limitation documented, definite-width policy documented, cancellation threading, new `LAYOUT-TABLE-INLINE-OVERFLOW-001` diagnostic, and 6 review findings** (historical entry; superseded by Task 12 sub-cycle 5 above. [PR #52](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/52) opened at `6ce94e2`; this hardening updates the same branch in-place. **Post-PR-#52 review hardening (6 findings, 2 P1 + 3 P2 + 1 P3, plus 6 Copilot perf/cleanup):** (1) [P1 #1] **Pass D column-sum reconciliation** — pre-hardening, declared column widths were used as-is; `<col width="100"><col width="200">` in a 600px table left cells totaling 300px while row/caption fragments spanned 600px (visual gap), and declared widths > content width caused cell overflow past wrapper geometry. CSS 2.1 §17.5.2.1: "If, when the calculation is done, the total width of the columns is less than the width of the table, the extra space should be distributed over the columns." Fix: new Pass D after Pass A+B+C — compute `columnSum`; if `< contentInlineSize`, distribute leftover EQUALLY across ALL columns so widths sum exactly to `contentInlineSize`; if `> contentInlineSize`, keep declared widths + record `_measuredUsedInlineSize = columnSum` + emit new `LAYOUT-TABLE-INLINE-OVERFLOW-001` Warning naming the spec deviation. Row + caption fragment `InlineSize` now uses `_measuredUsedInlineSize = max(columnSum, contentInlineSize)` so rendered geometry matches actual column extent. `ComputeColumnWidths` promoted from static to instance to record state. New `MeasuredUsedInlineSize` public property; `MeasureContentHeight` signature unchanged so BlockLayouter doesn't need updates. (2) [P1 #2] **First-row colspan partial-declare semantics fixed** — pre-hardening, `ApplyFirstRowCellWidths` used `anyUndeclared` + divided cell width by full colspan. Example: col 0 from `<col width="100">`, first-row cell `colspan=2 width=400` gave col 1 = 200 (=400/2), not the spec-correct 300 (=400 - 100). Fix: rewrote helper to compute `alreadyDeclared = sum(_measuredColumnWidths[c..c+colspan-1] where columnHasDeclared[c])`, `undeclaredCount = count of undeclared columns in span`, `remainingWidth = max(0, cellWidth - alreadyDeclared)`; distribute `remainingWidth / undeclaredCount` to each undeclared column in the span. (3) [P2 #3] **HTML width attribute cascade precedence — investigated + documented** — pre-hardening, `ReadColumnWidthPx` fell back to HTML `width` attribute whenever CSS `width` read as 0, conflating "no CSS authored" with "CSS explicit `width: auto`". Investigated `ComputedStyle.IsSet(PropertyId)`: it could distinguish "explicitly set" from "never set" in isolation, BUT `BoxBuilder.ApplyDefaults` eagerly fills every `ComputedStyle` slot with the property's initial value (via `PropertyResolverDispatch.Resolve` over `meta.DefaultValue`), so `IsSet(Width)` returns `true` for EVERY box regardless of whether author CSS fired. Cascade-aware fix infeasible without restructuring `ApplyDefaults`. Per the locked design's contingency clause: kept the pre-fix HTML-attribute fallback behavior; documented the limitation inline in `ReadColumnWidthPx` + the `docs/deferrals.md` Missing section ("HTML width attribute cascade precedence per CSS 2.1 §17.5: presentational attributes should NOT override explicit author CSS"). 2 new tests pin the current documented behavior. Sub-cycle 5+ may rework `ApplyDefaults` to enable the cascade-aware fix. (4) [P2 #4] **Fixed-without-definite-width policy documented** — CSS 2.1 strictly requires a definite table width for `table-layout: fixed`. NetPdf currently treats the wrapper's resolved content-inline-size (from CSS `width` or the containing-block width) as the effective table width, even when `table.width` is `auto`. Added explicit paragraph to `docs/deferrals.md`'s Behavior section naming this as a deliberate NetPdf approximation; new test `Fixed_layout_with_auto_width_applies_as_documented_approximation` pins the behavior. (5) [P2 #5] **Cancellation threading through column-width computation** — pre-hardening, column-width helpers didn't observe cancellation. Hostile tables with many columns/spans could run unobservably long. Fix: `CancellationToken` threaded through `ComputeColumnWidths`, `CollectColumnsFromGridLevel`, `VisitColumnishChild`, `ApplyDeclaredWidthToColumns`, `ApplyFirstRowCellWidths`; checks per direct child + per span-iteration. New regression test with pre-cancelled token + 1000-column table throws `OperationCanceledException` before completing. (6) [P3 #6] **Stale docs cleanup** — `docs/deferrals.md`'s `table-auto-fixed-spans-borders` Owner/Removal text still said "replace equal-split with auto + fixed layout passes"; updated to list current remaining items (auto layout + percentage widths + content-shrink reconciliation + border models + header/footer + pagination + spec-strict rowspan distribution + remainder semantics + RTL + HTML width cascade precedence). Plus Copilot stale-docs: `docs/deferrals.md:294` rowspan-distribution reference "sub-cycle 4+" → "sub-cycle 5+"; `docs/deferrals.md:303` caption RTL/vertical writing-mode "deferred to sub-cycle 4" → "deferred to a future sub-cycle"; `TableLayouter.cs:16` XML doc class summary "sub-cycle 1+2+4" → "sub-cycle 1+2+3+4" (caption was missing); `TableLayouter.cs:639` stale comment about `MeasureContentHeight` nulling `_measuredColumnWidths` (multiple inaccuracies — rewrote to describe the actual `rows is null` bail signal). **Plus Copilot inline #4 — negative-width rejection in `ReadColumnWidthPx`**: pre-hardening, `int.TryParse(s, NumberStyles.Integer, ...)` accepted leading `+`/`-` so `<col width="-100">` parsed to `-100`. Fix: explicit `if (parsed < 0) return 0;` after parse; updated comment. New test `Fixed_layout_negative_html_width_attribute_treated_as_zero`. **New diagnostic code:** `LAYOUT-TABLE-INLINE-OVERFLOW-001` Warning added to `PaginateDiagnosticCodes` + `NetPdf/Diagnostics/DiagnosticCodes` + `docs/diagnostics-codes.md` + 3 parity tests. Existing tests re-pinned: 6 sub-cycle 4 tests (e.g., `Fixed_layout_col_width_drives_column_widths`) that pinned cells at 100/200 inside 600px row now assert post-distribution geometry (cell 0 at offset 0 width 250; cell 1 at offset 250 width 350; same source declarations, post-Pass-D distribution). Tests: **4240 unit / 4371 solution-wide passing** (+14 unit / +14 solution-wide over PR #52 baseline at 4226 / 4357 — 11 new TableLayouter tests + 3 diagnostic-codes parity; 4 skipped). AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green; `git diff --check` clean. **Sub-cycle 5+ scope (still deferred):** CSS Tables L3 §3 auto-table-layout (shrink-to-fit columns via min/max-content) — the highest-leverage remaining gap for real invoices; percentage column widths; full grid/table used-inline-size reconciliation for content-shrink scenarios; §6.3 border-collapse model + `border-spacing`; §6.4 column-group widths beyond Pass A fallback; per-page header/footer repeat (Task 13); multi-fragmentainer row splitting; §11 spec-strict rowspan distribution-proportional algorithm; HTML5 `colspan="0"` / `rowspan="0"` remainder semantics; RTL writing modes / row reversal / caption inline-axis keyword routing; HTML width attribute cascade precedence (requires `ApplyDefaults` rework). Active-task pointer advances to **Task 12 sub-cycle 5** — auto-table-layout via min/max-content, OR **Task 13** — `<thead>`/`<tfoot>` repetition across pages, depending on review priority.)

**Phase 3 Task 12 sub-cycle 4 shipped — `table-layout: fixed` algorithm + `<col>` / `<colgroup>` widths** (historical entry; superseded by hardening review above. Continues from Task 12 sub-cycle 3 + hardening ([PR #51](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/51) merged at `5f8fb77`). Sub-cycle 3 shipped captions actually laid out (top/bottom emit phases, caption box model, no-break resolver, 6 hardening fixes); sub-cycle 4 implements **CSS Tables L3 §3.5 fixed-table-layout algorithm** plus `<col>` / `<colgroup>` `width` declarations + `width` attribute on first-row cells. Today, the scalar `_measuredColumnWidth` becomes a `double[] _measuredColumnWidths` array plus a `double[] _measuredColumnOffsets` prefix-sum (so per-cell `inlineSize = offsets[col + colspan] - offsets[col]` is a single subtraction). **3-pass algorithm** (CSS Tables L3 §3.5 fixed-layout method) — runs only when `table-layout: fixed`; `table-layout: auto` (default) keeps the existing equal-split (the actual §3 shrink-to-fit auto algorithm via min/max-content is sub-cycle 5 work): (1) **Pass A — `<col>` / `<colgroup>` widths**: walk the wrapper + the synthesized `TableGrid` for `BoxKind.TableColumn` / `BoxKind.TableColumnGroup` children in document order. New `CollectColumnsFromGridLevel` walks both anchor points defensively (BoxBuilder's `GridLevelFixup` puts them under the grid; some authored HTML edge cases could still attach to the wrapper). For each `<col>`, read `width` style + `span` HTML attribute (default 1, clamp [1, 1000]); contribute the width to `span` consecutive columns. A `<colgroup>` with no `<col>` children contributes its own `width` × `span` consecutive columns (Pass A fallback). (2) **Pass B — first-row cell widths**: for cells anchored at `(0, c)` with `colspan=S` where `columnWidths[c..c+S-1]` are still 0 (Pass A left undeclared), read `cell.Style.ReadLengthPxOrZero(PropertyId.Width)` + the HTML `width` attribute; distribute the declared width equally across the S spanned columns. (3) **Pass C — equal-distribute remainder**: count columns still undeclared; equal-distribute `contentInlineSize - sum(declared)` (clamped non-negative) across them. **Column-width reading helper** — new `ReadColumnWidthPx(box)` returns CSS `width` style → HTML `width` attribute integer-px fallback → 0 (for percentages, invalid, or missing). Percentages (`<col width="20%">`) silently fall back to 0 (column then enters Pass C remainder distribution) — sub-cycle 5+ work; documented inline + in `docs/deferrals.md`. New `ParseColumnSpan` is intentionally separate from `ParseSpanAttribute` (cell `colspan`/`rowspan`): `<col span="0">` does NOT admit the HTML5 "remainder" semantic — different valid ranges, different malformed-handling. **CSS property pipeline:** `table-layout` added to `src/NetPdf.Css/properties.json` (Keyword, NOT inherited, default `auto`, applies to TableElements); `KeywordResolver.cs` admitted keywords `auto | fixed`; new `TableLayoutMode` enum (`Auto = 0, Fixed = 1`) on `ComputedStyleLayoutExtensions` with `ReadTableLayout` extension. Removed `table-layout` from `tests/NetPdf.RealDocuments/Css/PropertyCoverageCorpusTests.cs`'s `UnsupportedAllowlist` (self-check test enforces "anything in properties.json must NOT be in the allowlist"). **Edge cases**: more `<col>` declarations than columns are silently ignored; fewer fall through to Pass B/C; `<col>` width wins over first-row cell `width` (Pass A precedence per spec); `table-layout: fixed` with NO `<col>` + NO first-row widths falls back to equal-split. **Emit phase** unchanged structurally — cell fragments now use `_measuredColumnOffsets[col]` for `InlineOffset` + `(offsets[col + colspan] - offsets[col])` for `InlineSize`; caption inline-size still anchors at `contentInlineOffset` width `contentInlineSize` (CSS spec says caption width = grid outer inline-size which is `contentInlineSize` until auto-layout ships). Tests: **4226 unit / 4357 solution-wide passing** (+12 unit / +12 solution-wide over PR #51 at 4214 / 4345 — 10 new direct tests + 2 new production tests; 4 skipped). AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green; `git diff --check` clean. New direct tests in [`TableLayouterTests`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Phase3/TableLayouterTests.cs): `Fixed_layout_col_width_drives_column_widths`, `Fixed_layout_col_with_span_applies_to_multiple_columns`, `Fixed_layout_first_row_cell_width_used_when_no_col`, `Fixed_layout_col_width_wins_over_first_row_cell_width`, `Fixed_layout_undeclared_columns_equal_split_remaining`, `Fixed_layout_colspan_2_cell_spans_two_columns_widths`, `Fixed_layout_with_no_declared_widths_falls_back_to_equal_split`, `Auto_layout_keeps_equal_split_for_now`, `Fixed_layout_percentage_col_width_treated_as_zero`, `Fixed_layout_colgroup_width_fallback_when_no_col_children`. New production tests in [`TableLayouterProductionTests`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Phase3/TableLayouterProductionTests.cs): `Production_table_with_fixed_layout_and_col_widths_renders_correctly`, `Production_table_with_auto_layout_ignores_col_widths_for_now`. **Docs:** `docs/deferrals.md`'s `table-auto-fixed-spans-borders` entry updated — Behavior describes the 3-pass fixed-layout algorithm; Missing drops §3.5 fixed-table-layout; adds percentage column widths to Missing. **Sub-cycle 5+ scope (still deferred):** CSS Tables L3 §3 auto-table-layout (shrink-to-fit columns via min/max-content) — the highest-leverage remaining gap for real invoices; percentage column widths; §6.3 border-collapse model + `border-spacing`; §6.4 column-group widths beyond Pass A fallback; per-page header / footer repeat (Task 13); multi-fragmentainer row splitting; §11 spec-strict rowspan distribution-proportional algorithm; HTML5 `colspan="0"` / `rowspan="0"` remainder semantics; RTL writing modes / row reversal / caption inline-axis keyword routing. Active-task pointer advances to **Task 12 sub-cycle 5** — auto-table-layout via min/max-content, OR **Task 13** — `<thead>`/`<tfoot>` repetition across pages, depending on review priority.)

**Phase 3 Task 12 sub-cycle 3 shipped + post-PR-#51 review hardening — Table captions actually laid out with full CSS box model, no-break caption resolver, inline-axis caption-side diagnosed, overflow check in early-return paths, inherited caption-side production test, and 6 review findings** (historical entry; superseded by Task 12 sub-cycle 4 above. [PR #51](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/51) opened at `d52e34d`; this hardening updates the same branch in-place. **Post-PR-#51 review hardening (6 findings, 2 P1 + 3 P2 + 1 P3):** (1) [P1 #1] **Caption box model honored** — pre-hardening, caption fragment size + stacking was based solely on measured child content; caption's own margin / border / padding / explicit height were ignored. `caption { padding:10px; border:2px solid; margin-bottom:8px; height:40px }` would place row content too high + flush text at the caption border edge. Fix: `CaptionMeasurement` extended with 11 box-model fields (margin/border/padding per edge + declared height) + computed `BorderBoxBlockSize` + `MarginBoxBlockSize` properties. `MeasureCaptionContent` now reads box-model from `captionBox.Style` via `ReadLengthPxOrZero` (mirroring BlockLayouter), lays inner content at `(captionInlineOffset + BorderInlineStart + PaddingInlineStart, inner content-box top)` with `ContentBoxInlineSize` clamped at 1; records all metrics. Emit phases (Phase 0 + Phase D + missing-grid early-return) use the margin-box cursor algorithm: cursor advances by MarginBlockStart, fragment BlockSize = BorderBoxBlockSize, content flushes at cursor + BorderBlockStart + PaddingBlockStart, cursor advances by BorderBoxBlockSize + MarginBlockEnd. Stacking totals sum margin-box sizes. `BlockSizeContent` is the floor; explicit `height` raises (`max(declared, content)`). 5 new tests pin padding / border / margin / explicit-height / shorter-height behavior. (2) [P1 #2] **No-break caption resolver guarantees full content measurement** — pre-hardening, `MeasureCaptionContent` ignored the nested BlockLayouter's `LayoutAttemptResult`. If caption content returned `PageComplete` with continuation, remaining children were silently dropped. Fix: new internal `NoBreakBreakResolver : IBreakResolver` that always returns `BreakAction.Continue` — captures the existing `BreakResolver` lease semantics for safety, then short-circuits any break decision. Caption layout uses this resolver so the entire caption subtree walks in one pass. Defense-in-depth assert at the attempt boundary: if the result is somehow `PageComplete`, emit `PAGINATION-FORCED-OVERFLOW-001` Warning into the buffered diagnostic sink (caption content still emits whatever BlockLayouter managed to lay out before the break). The existing `BreakResolver` + `LastResort` strategy combo did NOT guarantee Continue — `LastResort` only suppresses `NeedsRewind`; chunk-too-tall still triggers `BreakHere`. Custom resolver was necessary. New regression test: 2 known-height caption blocks whose combined height exceeds the page — both children emit fragments + the diagnostic fires. (3) [P2 #3] **Inline-axis `caption-side` diagnosed** — pre-hardening, `inline-start` / `inline-end` keywords were admitted by the keyword table but silently mapped to `Top` by `ReadCaptionSide`, turning valid CSS into wrong layout once vertical writing modes start landing. Fix: `MeasureCaptions` reads the raw keyword via `ReadKeywordOrDefault`; index 4 (`inline-start`) / index 5 (`inline-end`) emit `LAYOUT-TABLE-FEATURE-UNSUPPORTED-001` Warning naming the deferred axis. Falls back to `top` per the unchanged `ReadCaptionSide` mapping (graceful render under LTR). 2 new tests pin diagnostic fire + fallback behavior. (4) [P2 #4] **Overflow check in early-return paths** — pre-hardening, the row-stack emit path emitted `PAGINATION-FORCED-OVERFLOW-001` when content extended past the fragmentainer; the missing-TableGrid / zero-row / zero-column early-return path returned before the overflow check. A caption-only table with a tall caption silently overflowed. Fix: new private helper `EmitOverflowDiagnosticIfNeeded(fragmentainer, tableBottomBlockOffset, ref layout)` called from BOTH the row-stack emit path AND each early-return path that emitted any caption content. New regression: missing-TableGrid table with tall caption fires the diagnostic. (5) [P2 #5] **Inherited `caption-side` production test** — pre-hardening, the production test set `caption-side` on the caption element directly. Per CSS, `caption-side` is INHERITED, so `table { caption-side: bottom; } <caption>...` should also work via inheritance. Fix: new `Production_caption_side_inherits_from_table_to_caption` test — HTML sets `caption-side: bottom` on the table only; verifies the caption inherits + renders below the row. Protects the property pipeline, inheritance, BoxBuilder table-caption placement, and TableLayouter end-to-end. (6) [P3 #6] **Patch hygiene + docs drift** — `git diff --check origin/main..HEAD` previously failed on PROGRESS.md:16 trailing whitespace; sub-cycle 3 implementation had 3 stale "sub-cycle 3" references in TableLayouter.cs (lines 41-42 + 109-110 + 1042) + 1 in `docs/deferrals.md`:294 referring to the spec-strict rowspan distribution-proportional algorithm. Fix: stripped trailing whitespace; rewrote all 4 stale references to "sub-cycle 4+ — see docs/deferrals.md#table-auto-fixed-spans-borders" so future agents don't target the wrong sub-cycle. Tests: **4214 unit / 4345 solution-wide passing** (+10 unit / +10 solution-wide over PR #51 baseline at 4204 / 4335 — 9 Finding-1-to-4 direct tests + 1 Finding-5 production test; 4 skipped). AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green; `git diff --check` clean. Active-task pointer advances to **Task 12 sub-cycle 4** — auto-table-layout column widths (shrink-to-fit via min/max-content; the highest-leverage remaining gap for real invoices), OR **Task 13** — `<thead>`/`<tfoot>` repetition across pages, depending on review priority.)

**Phase 3 Task 12 sub-cycle 3 shipped — Table captions actually laid out** (historical entry; superseded by hardening review above. Continues from Task 12 sub-cycle 2 + hardening ([PR #50](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/50) merged at `f3f015c`). Sub-cycle 2 shipped colspan/rowspan + 8-finding hardening; captions were still emitting `LAYOUT-TABLE-FEATURE-UNSUPPORTED-001` with the caption's text content captured in the diagnostic message via `DiagnosticTextSanitizer`. Sub-cycle 3 ships **actual caption layout per CSS Tables L3 §11.5.1–§11.5.2** — `<caption>` elements render as block fragments above (`caption-side: top`, default) or below (`caption-side: bottom`) the table grid. **CSS property pipeline:** `caption-side` added to `src/NetPdf.Css/properties.json` (Keyword, inherited, default `top`, applies to `TableElements`); `KeywordResolver.cs` admitted-keyword tables registered for `top | bottom | block-start | block-end | inline-start | inline-end`; new `CaptionSide` enum (`Top = 0, Bottom = 1`) on `ComputedStyleLayoutExtensions` with `ReadCaptionSide` extension that maps writing-mode-relative keywords (`block-start`, `block-end`) to physical (`top`, `bottom`) under LTR horizontal mode; inline-axis keywords (`inline-start`, `inline-end`) currently fall back to `top` (RTL + vertical-axis routing deferred to sub-cycle 4). **Algorithm:** during the measure phase, after collecting rows + placing cells onto the occupancy grid, the layouter walks the Table wrapper's direct children (NOT inside TableGrid — that's where BoxBuilder attaches captions) for `BoxKind.TableCaption`. Each caption is laid out via a nested `BlockLayouter` into a buffered `MeasuringFragmentSink` (same pattern as cells); the resulting block-extent + caption-side are cached in a new `CaptionMeasurement` struct + the `_measuredCaptionList` / `_measuredTopCaptionsTotal` / `_measuredBottomCaptionsTotal` fields. Caption inline-size = table wrapper's content-inline-size (sub-cycle 4 will switch to grid outer-inline-size once auto-table-layout ships; documented as inline TODO). The `MeasureContentHeight` API still returns the single total `topCaptionTotal + rowStackTotal + bottomCaptionTotal` — BlockLayouter consumes it as before; no public API breakage. **Emit phase extended to 5 phases** (was 3 in sub-cycle 2):
  - **Phase 0 (new) — Top captions**: emit each top caption's `BoxFragment` + flush buffered content in document order, cumulative top-caption offset.
  - **Phase A — Rows** (existing, shifted): row block-offsets now anchor at `contentBlockOffset + topCaptionTotal`.
  - **Phase B — Cells** (existing): follow shifted row offsets automatically.
  - **Phase C — Cell content** (existing): unchanged.
  - **Phase D (new) — Bottom captions**: emit at `contentBlockOffset + topCaptionTotal + rowStackTotal + cumulative bottom-caption offset` + flush.

Final outer-sink order: `[wrapper] [top captions + content] [rows] [cells] [cell content] [bottom captions + content]` — paint-safe ordering (backgrounds → boxes → text) preserved end-to-end including across captions. **Diagnostic removed:** the `LAYOUT-TABLE-FEATURE-UNSUPPORTED-001` Warning emit for captions is gone; the `CollectCaptions` + `ExtractCaptionTextSnippet` helpers + the `using System.Text;` import that supported the diagnostic are removed. The diagnostic code itself stays (still fires for missing-TableGrid + `rowspan="0"` / `colspan="0"` deferral). 2 sub-cycle 1 caption-diagnostic tests renamed + inverted (`Caption_no_longer_emits_LAYOUT_TABLE_FEATURE_UNSUPPORTED_001`); 1 production test replaced with `Production_table_with_top_caption_renders_via_full_pipeline`. **Diagnostic plumbing:** caption-internal diagnostics use the same `BufferingDiagnosticsSink` flush-on-commit / discard-on-rewind contract as cell content (Finding 5 of PR #50 hardening). **Edge cases**: captions still emit in the "missing-TableGrid / zero rows / zero columns" early-return paths so authors who hand-craft malformed tables still see their caption content. **Docs:** `docs/deferrals.md`'s `table-auto-fixed-spans-borders` entry updated — Behavior section now describes caption rendering; Missing section drops the captions line. `docs/diagnostics-codes.md` `LAYOUT-TABLE-FEATURE-UNSUPPORTED-001` row updated to drop the captions reference. `tests/NetPdf.RealDocuments/Css/PropertyCoverageCorpusTests.cs` `UnsupportedAllowlist` drops `caption-side`. Tests: **4204 unit / 4335 solution-wide passing** (+8 unit / +8 solution-wide over PR #50 baseline at 4196 / 4327 — 8 new direct tests + 2 new production tests minus 2 removed; 4 skipped). New direct tests in [`TableLayouterTests`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Phase3/TableLayouterTests.cs): `Caption_top_renders_above_rows`, `Caption_bottom_renders_below_rows`, `Multiple_top_captions_stack_vertically`, `Caption_content_renders_via_nested_BlockLayouter`, `Caption_no_longer_emits_LAYOUT_TABLE_FEATURE_UNSUPPORTED_001`, `Caption_block_extent_feeds_into_table_total_height`, `Caption_with_default_no_caption_side_falls_back_to_top`, `Caption_block_start_maps_to_top`. New production tests: `Production_table_with_top_caption_renders_via_full_pipeline`, `Production_table_with_bottom_caption_renders_below_rows`. AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green. **Sub-cycle 4+ scope:** CSS Tables L3 §3 auto-table-layout column widths (shrink-to-fit via min/max-content) — the highest-leverage remaining gap for real invoices; §3.5 fixed-table-layout; §6.3 border-collapse model + `border-spacing`; §6.4 column-group widths; per-page header/footer repeat (Task 13); multi-fragmentainer row splitting; §11 spec-strict rowspan distribution-proportional algorithm; HTML5 `colspan="0"` / `rowspan="0"` remainder semantics; RTL writing modes / row reversal / caption inline-axis keyword routing. Caption inline-size will switch to grid outer-inline-size once auto-table-layout ships. Active-task pointer advances to **Task 12 sub-cycle 4** — auto-table-layout, OR **Task 13** — `<thead>`/`<tfoot>` repetition across pages, depending on review priority.)

**Phase 3 Task 12 sub-cycle 2 shipped + post-PR-#50 review hardening — `colspan` + `rowspan` cell merging with real fragmentainer threading, recursive measure pass, 3-phase paint-safe emit, DoS-resistant interval-list occupancy + slot budget, buffering diagnostics for speculative measure, and 8 review findings** (historical entry; superseded by Task 12 sub-cycle 3 above. [PR #50](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/50) opened at `710b533`; merged at `f3f015c` after hardening. **Post-PR-#50 review hardening (8 findings, 4 P1 + 3 P2 + 1 P3, plus 3 Copilot perf/cleanup):** (1) [P1 #1] **Real fragmentainer threading** — pre-hardening `BlockLayouter.EmitBlockSubtreeRecursive` measured + emitted nested tables with `new FragmentainerContext(..., blockSize: 1)` — any positive-height nested table emitted false `PAGINATION-FORCED-OVERFLOW-001` Warnings, and cell content with multiple/tall block children could hit BlockLayouter's forced-overflow `PageComplete` (TableLayouter ignored the continuation, losing content). Fix: new `_capturedFragmentainer` field on BlockLayouter retains the active outer fragmentainer; the recursion + nested-table dispatch now use it instead of synthesizing a 1px context. (2) [P1 #2] **Recursive measure pass includes table content extent** — `MeasureSubtreeVisualBlockExtentRecursive` previously returned the table wrapper's own border-box for `Table`/`InlineTable` (auto-height = 0). Parent block pagination undercounted. Fix: extracted `MeasureNestedTableContentExtent` helper (mirrors `PreMeasureTableIfNeeded` from sub-cycle 1 hardening); the measure pass dispatches through it with a per-`Box` content-height cache. Emit pass re-measures via fresh TableLayouter (acceptable — content buffers couldn't be reused without anchored offsets; mirrors cycle-2c duplicate-walk pattern). (3) [P1 #3] **3-phase paint-safe emit for rowspan** — pre-hardening, the row-emit loop emitted row + cells + flushed content per row before moving to the next row. For `rowspan>1` cells, later rows' backgrounds/borders could paint OVER the spanning cell's content (which was flushed at the origin row). Fix: split `AttemptLayout`'s emit into THREE phases over the whole table — Phase A emits all row fragments; Phase B emits all cell `BoxFragment`s (only at origin row/col); Phase C flushes all cells' buffered content. Backgrounds → boxes → text invariant holds across rowspan. Built `placementsByRow[]` bucket once + `rowEndBlockOffset[]` prefix-sum once to make Phase B/C O(placement count) rather than O(rowCount × placementCount); knocks out Copilot perf findings #1 + #2. (4) [P1 #4] **DoS-resistant interval-list occupancy grid + slot budget** — pre-hardening, `PlaceCellsOntoGrid` stored slots as per-row `HashSet<int>` + looped every `rowspan × colspan` cell. HTML5 allows `rowspan` up to 65534 + `colspan` up to 1000 — a single hostile cell could force 65M hash insertions. Fix: replaced per-slot HashSet with **per-row interval list** (`List<(int StartCol, int EndColExclusive)>`, kept sorted + non-overlapping); occupied-check via binary search; insertion via linear find-then-merge (small list so cheap). Plus new `MaxOccupiedSlots = 1_000_000` budget tracked across all placements; exceeded → emit new `LAYOUT-TABLE-SLOT-BUDGET-EXCEEDED-001` Warning + cap remaining cells at 1×1 (no crash, truncate). New diagnostic added to `PaginateDiagnosticCodes` + `NetPdf/Diagnostics/DiagnosticCodes` + parity tests + `docs/diagnostics-codes.md`. Cancellation now checked per row-iteration inside the slot-marking loop (Copilot finding #5). Current row's own colspan slots no longer marked (cursor advances past them naturally; only mark slots in rows BELOW for rowspan>1). (5) [P2 #5] **Buffering diagnostics during speculative measure** — pre-hardening, cell-content measurement passed the live diagnostic sink to the nested BlockLayouter. If the outer resolver discarded the table (rewind), cell-level diagnostics for uncommitted work could leak. Fix: new `src/NetPdf.Paginate/Diagnostics/BufferingDiagnosticsSink.cs` (97 LOC) — `IPaginateDiagnosticsSink` decorator that captures `Emit` calls into a `List<PaginateDiagnostic>` + exposes `FlushTo(target)` / `Discard()`. TableLayouter wraps `layout.Diagnostics ?? _diagnostics` per cell during measure, passes the buffering sink BOTH as `LayoutContext.Diagnostics` AND as the nested BlockLayouter's `diagnostics:` ctor arg so cell-internal `OptimizingBreakResolver.SafeEmit` lands in the buffer regardless of path. On commit (Phase C), each cell's buffered diagnostics flush to the outer sink. (6) [P2 #6] **`rowspan="0"` / `colspan="0"` documented + diagnosed** — HTML5 specifies `rowspan="0"` = "span all remaining rows in the row group/table section"; sub-cycle 2 clamped `<1` silently to 1. Fix: `ParseSpanAttribute` returns `0` distinguishably; placement loop clamps to 1 + emits `LAYOUT-TABLE-FEATURE-UNSUPPORTED-001` with explicit deferral message naming the HTML5 semantic. `docs/deferrals.md` Missing section adds `rowspan="0"`/`colspan="0"` remainder semantics. (7) [P2 #7] **Caption diagnostic uses `DiagnosticTextSanitizer`** — pre-hardening, `ExtractCaptionTextSnippet` only replaced CR/LF + trimmed. Other control characters could be injected into diagnostics/logs. Fix: invoke `DiagnosticTextSanitizer.Sanitize(text, maxLength: 80)` (internal to `NetPdf.Css`; accessible via existing InternalsVisibleTo) for the caption snippet. Caption diagnostic message also updated — dropped "sub-cycle 1" wording, added "captions are not yet laid out per CSS Tables L3 §11; sub-cycle 3 work" + link to the deferral doc. (8) [P3 #8] **Stale docs / dead helpers cleanup** — refreshed `TableLayouterTests.cs` test-class XML doc, `TableLayouter.cs` XML docs at lines 147-148 + 184-185 + 1007-1021 (sub-cycle 1 references → sub-cycle 2 reality), comment at line 399 referencing fictional `_rowBlockOffsets[R]` field (Copilot finding #1), comment at line 782 about rowSpan clamping (Copilot finding #6). Removed `CountTableCells` helper (sub-cycle 1 leftover; sub-cycle 2's placement grid renders it redundant). Tests: **4196 unit / 4327 solution-wide passing** (+12 unit / +12 solution-wide over PR #50 baseline at 4184 / 4315 — 9 hardening regression tests (one per Finding 1-7 + a direct `BufferingDiagnosticsSink` contract test) + 3 diagnostic-codes parity tests for the new `LAYOUT-TABLE-SLOT-BUDGET-EXCEEDED-001`; 4 skipped). AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green. Active-task pointer advances to **Task 12 sub-cycle 3** — auto-table-layout column widths + border-collapse + captions actually laid out + `<col>` widths + multi-page row splitting + spec-strict §11 rowspan distribution-proportional algorithm + HTML5 `colspan="0"`/`rowspan="0"` remainder semantics, OR **Task 13** — `<thead>`/`<tfoot>` repetition across pages, depending on review priority.)

**Phase 3 Task 12 sub-cycle 2 shipped — `colspan` + `rowspan` cell merging** (historical entry; superseded by hardening review above. Continues from Task 12 sub-cycle 1 + hardening ([PR #49](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/49) merged at `5a69240`). Sub-cycle 1 shipped the equal-column Hello-World layouter; sub-cycle 2 implements **CSS Tables L3 + HTML5 cell-placement algorithm** so cells with `colspan="N"` or `rowspan="M"` attributes actually merge across the appropriate grid slots — previously these attributes triggered a `LAYOUT-TABLE-FEATURE-UNSUPPORTED-001` Warning + were silently ignored. **Algorithm (2D occupancy grid):** for each row in document order, walk `TableCell` children; for each cell, read `colspan` (default 1, clamp to [1, 1000]) + `rowspan` (default 1, clamp to [1, 65534]) from the element's HTML attributes via `ParseSpanAttribute`. Maintain a per-row `HashSet<int>? occupiedCols[rowCount]` (lazily allocated for non-empty rows). For each cell, scan the column cursor starting at 0 in the current row, advancing past any occupied slot until a free one is found; reserve `(rowspan × colspan)` slots starting at that anchor. Record `CellPlacement(cell, originRow, originCol, rowspan, colspan)`. Column count = max occupied column index + 1 across all rows (extends correctly when a `colspan` pushes past the natural row width). HTML5 `colspan="0" = "remainder"` is clamped to 1 for now (sub-cycle 3 will implement; documented in `ParseSpanAttribute` doc-comment). `rowspan` values that would extend past the table's end are clamped to the available rows so emit-pass index access stays in-bounds. **Column-width with spans:** equal-split still applies (`columnWidth = contentInlineSize / columnCount`); a cell with `colspan=N` occupies `N × columnWidth` of inline space at its anchor. **Row-height with rowspan:** naive distribution — pass A sets `rowHeight[i] = max(content extent of cells with rowspan=1 starting at row i)` (rows with no `rowspan=1` cells start at 0). Pass B processes `rowspan>1` placements sorted by ascending `rowSpan` (small spans before long spans so heights settle): for each spanning cell with content extent C at origin row `i` with span `S`, if `sum(rowHeight[i..i+S-1]) < C`, the excess lands on `rowHeight[i+S-1]` (last row of the span). The cell's emit-time `BlockSize = sum(rowHeight[originRow..originRow+rowspan-1])`. This isn't the CSS Tables L3 §11 spec-strict distribution-proportional algorithm but it's deterministic + simple; deferred to sub-cycle 3 (flagged inline + in `docs/deferrals.md`). **Emit phase:** per row in document order — emit ONE row fragment per row at full content-inline-width × `rowHeight[r]`; for each cell whose `originRow == r`, emit ONE cell fragment at `(contentInlineOffset + originCol × columnWidth, rowCursorBlock)` with `(colspan × columnWidth) × cellBlockSize`, then flush its buffered content via the `MeasuringFragmentSink.FlushTo(target, additionalBlockOffset)` method (extended to accept a deferred block-offset translation since sub-cycle 2 can't pre-compute the final cell block-offset before the rowspan distribution pass completes). Continuation slots (occupied but not origin) are skipped. The paint-safe ordering invariant from sub-cycle 1 hardening (row → cells → cell content) still holds for each row's emit batch. **Diagnostic removed:** the `LAYOUT-TABLE-FEATURE-UNSUPPORTED-001` emit + `sawColspanAttribute` flag that fired once per table when any cell had `colspan`/`rowspan` is gone (the codes themselves stay — still emitted for captions + missing-TableGrid). 2 sub-cycle 1 tests asserting the diagnostic fires were renamed + inverted to assert it does NOT fire. **Docs:** `docs/deferrals.md`'s `table-auto-fixed-spans-borders` entry updated — Behavior section gains "spans work via 2D occupancy-grid + naive row-height distribution"; Missing section drops "cell merging (colspan / rowspan)" + retains the spec-strict distribution-proportional algorithm gap. `docs/diagnostics-codes.md` row updated to drop the colspan/rowspan reference. Tests: **4184 unit / 4315 solution-wide passing** (+8 unit / +8 solution-wide over PR #49 at 4176 / 4307 — 6 new direct tests + 2 new production tests + 2 sub-cycle 1 tests renamed-and-inverted; 4 skipped). New tests in [`TableLayouterTests`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Phase3/TableLayouterTests.cs): `Colspan_2_cell_spans_two_columns`, `Rowspan_2_cell_spans_two_rows`, `Colspan_and_rowspan_combined`, `Rowspan_cell_content_taller_than_natural_rows_extends_last_row`, `Colspan_overflowing_row_extends_column_count`, `Cells_with_invalid_colspan_attribute_fall_back_to_1`. New tests in [`TableLayouterProductionTests`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Phase3/TableLayouterProductionTests.cs): `Production_colspan_table_renders_correctly`, `Production_rowspan_table_renders_correctly`. AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green. **Sub-cycle 3+ scope:** CSS Tables L3 §3 auto-table-layout (shrink-to-fit columns via min/max-content); §3.5 fixed-table-layout (column widths from `<col>` + first-row cell widths); §6.3 border-collapse model + `border-spacing`; §11 captions actually laid out (not just diagnosed); §6.4 column-group widths; per-page header / footer repeat; multi-fragmentainer row splitting; §11 spec-strict rowspan distribution; HTML5 `colspan="0" = remainder` semantic; RTL writing modes. Active-task pointer advances to **Task 12 sub-cycle 3** — auto-table-layout column widths + border-collapse, OR **Task 13** — `<thead>`/`<tfoot>` repetition across pages, depending on review priority.)

**Phase 3 Task 12 sub-cycle 1 shipped + post-PR-#49 review hardening — `TableLayouter` Hello-World with two-phase measure+emit protocol, paint-safe ordering, resolver isolation, caption diagnostic, and 6 review findings** (historical entry; superseded by Task 12 sub-cycle 2 above. [PR #49](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/49) opened at `77120ca`; merged at `5a69240` after hardening. **Post-PR-#49 review hardening (6 findings, 4 P1):** (1) [P1 #1] **Table height fed back into block flow** — pre-hardening `TableLayouter` left `fragmentainer.UsedBlockSize` unchanged after emitting rows because BlockLayouter "already advanced by the wrapper" — but for auto-height tables that wrapper extent is 0 (CSS `height: auto` reads as 0), so siblings overlapped the rows + tables near the page bottom didn't trigger break-before. Fix: split TableLayouter into a **two-phase measure+emit protocol**. New public `MeasureContentHeight(...)` pre-computes the row stack height (cell content laid out into a buffered MeasuringFragmentSink — no outer-sink emits during measure); the result is cached on the layouter. `AttemptLayout` reuses the cached measurements. BlockLayouter's child-processing loop (BOTH the Continue + forced-overflow paths PLUS `EmitBlockSubtreeRecursive`'s nested-table dispatch) now constructs the TableLayouter once, calls MeasureContentHeight to get `tableContentHeight`, uses `max(cssHeight, tableContentHeight)` as the effective wrapper height for the resolver consult + the emitted BoxFragment.BlockSize. `fragmentainer.UsedBlockSize` advances by the wrapper's actual border-box reflecting the measured content. (2) [P1 #2] **Paint-safe fragment order** — MeasuringFragmentSink previously forwarded translated cell content to the outer sink DURING measurement; row + cell fragments were emitted AFTER. Phase 4 painter walks fragment order, so backgrounds/borders would paint OVER text. Fix: rewrite MeasuringFragmentSink to BUFFER fragments. New public `FlushTo(target)` drains the buffer to the outer sink in order. TableLayouter's row-emit loop now: measure cells (buffered) → compute row height → emit row fragment → emit each cell fragment → flush each cell's buffered content. Final outer-sink order: [wrapper] [row N] [cells N] [cell content N] [row N+1] ... — backgrounds before text. (3) [P1 #3] **Resolver isolation** — `LayoutCellContent` previously passed the OUTER `IBreakResolver` to the nested BlockLayouter. Inner checkpoint registration would replace/return the outer's checkpoint lease, corrupting later outer pagination/rewind decisions. Fix: each cell layout constructs `using var cellResolver = new BreakResolver();` — fresh instance scoped to the cell, dispose returns the cell-local lease to the pool. The outer resolver is never passed to nested layouters. (4) [P1 #4] **Captions emit feature diagnostic** — BoxBuilder keeps `<caption>` as a direct child of the Table wrapper (NOT inside TableGrid). Pre-hardening, captions were never walked + silently dropped. Fix: after finding TableGrid, walk the Table wrapper's direct children for `TableCaption`; for each, emit `LAYOUT-TABLE-FEATURE-UNSUPPORTED-001` Warning with the caption's text content (recursive TextRun walk, ~80 char cap, embedded newlines collapsed) included in the diagnostic message so users see what got dropped. (5) [P2 #5] **Missing-TableGrid uses correct diagnostic code** — pre-hardening emitted `PAGINATION-FORCED-OVERFLOW-001`, but a missing TableGrid is a malformed-box-tree invariant violation, not pagination overflow. Fix: changed to `LAYOUT-TABLE-FEATURE-UNSUPPORTED-001` with an explicit "box-generation invariant violation" message. (6) [P2 #6] **Production-pipeline integration tests** — pre-hardening tests bypassed BoxBuilder by constructing Table → TableGrid → row → cell hierarchies directly. Fix: new `tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Phase3/TableLayouterProductionTests.cs` (357 LOC) with 6 tests routing real HTML through `HtmlParsingHost` → `CssPreprocessor` → `CssParserAdapter` → `CascadeResolver` → `BoxBuilder` → `BlockLayouter`: simple table renders via full pipeline; table-followed-by-paragraph doesn't overlap (Finding 1 regression); table-with-caption emits feature diagnostic; thead/tbody collects rows via row groups; colspan emits feature diagnostic via full pipeline; cell with real inline text lays out via inline-only-block. Plus 5 new direct-construction tests in TableLayouterTests covering Findings 1-5 each. **Plus Copilot inline-review cleanup: removed unused `_incomingContinuation` field** — the constructor parameter is validated against null + then discarded; no field needed (sub-cycle 2 will re-introduce when `TableContinuation` lands). **Nested-table dispatch in `EmitBlockSubtreeRecursive`** — discovered during Finding 6 integration testing: pre-hardening only the top-level child loop in BlockLayouter dispatched TableLayouter, so nested tables (e.g., `body > table` which BoxBuilder produces by default) had their rows/cells silently dropped. The hardening symmetrically adds the same MeasureContentHeight + EmitTableInner protocol to the recursion's transient LayoutContext. Tests: **4176 unit / 4307 solution-wide passing** (+12 unit / +12 solution-wide over PR #49 baseline at 4164 / 4295 — 5 Finding-1-to-5 direct tests + 6 Finding-6 production-pipeline tests + 1 capturing-resolver test double; 4 skipped). AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green. Active-task pointer advances to **Task 12 sub-cycle 2** — `table-layout: auto`/`fixed` algorithms + `colspan`/`rowspan` cell merging + border-collapse model + captions actually laid out (not just diagnosed) + `<col>` widths + multi-page row splitting + thead/tfoot repetition — OR **Task 13** depending on review priority.)

**Phase 3 Task 12 sub-cycle 1 shipped — `TableLayouter` Hello-World** (historical entry; superseded by hardening review above. Continues from Task 11 sub-cycle 1 + post-PR-#48 review hardening ([PR #48](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/48) merged at `a21f5a8`). Task 11 sub-cycle 1 wired the block ↔ inline integration seam for `<p>`-style inline-only block containers; Task 12 sub-cycle 1 ships the first **non-block-flow layouter** — `TableLayouter` — handling the `Table → TableGrid → row → cell` hierarchy that `BoxBuilder` produces for HTML `<table>` content. **New types in [`src/NetPdf.Layout/Layouters/`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Layouters/):** [`TableLayouter`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Layouters/TableLayouter.cs) — `internal sealed class : ILayouter, IDisposable`. Constructor signature mirrors `BlockLayouter`: `(rootBox, sink, incomingContinuation: null, diagnostics: null, shaperResolver: null)` where `rootBox.Kind` MUST be `Table` or `InlineTable` (validates at the constructor + throws `ArgumentException` otherwise). The outer `Table` / `InlineTable` `BoxFragment` is emitted by the parent `BlockLayouter` via its standard block-flow path; `TableLayouter` is dispatched AFTER that emit + adds the inner row + cell fragments at fragmentainer-relative offsets so the painter sees the complete table geometry. **Algorithm (equal-column "Hello World"):** (1) Find the wrapper's `TableGrid` child (defensive — `BoxBuilder`'s table fixup is supposed to insert it; missing grid emits a diagnostic + returns AllDone). (2) Walk the TableGrid's children in document order, recursing into `TableRowGroup` / `TableHeaderGroup` / `TableFooterGroup` to collect their `TableRow` children. Captions, column groups, columns are SKIPPED (sub-cycle 1 deferral). (3) Column count = max number of `TableCell` children across all rows. Sub-cycle 1 assumes no `colspan` (cell count == column count); cells declaring `colspan` / `rowspan` emit `LAYOUT-TABLE-FEATURE-UNSUPPORTED-001` Warning + the attribute is silently ignored (cell occupies one column × one row). (4) Equal-split inline-size: `columnWidth = contentInlineSize / columnCount`. No author column widths, no shrink-to-fit, no min/max-content sizing. (5) For each row: measure each cell's content extent via a nested `BlockLayouter` with a `MeasuringFragmentSink` wrapping the outer sink — the row height resolves to the maximum measured cell extent. Cell-content fragments land at fragmentainer-relative coordinates via the nested `BlockLayouter`; `TableLayouter` then emits one `BoxFragment` per row spanning the full inline width at the computed row height, then one `BoxFragment` per cell at the column offset with the row height. (6) `FragmentainerContext.UsedBlockSize` advances by the row height as each row is committed. **`BlockLayouter` integration:** new private `DispatchTableInnerIfNeeded(child, parentInlineOffset, parentContentTop, parentContentInlineSize, ctx, ref layoutCtx, resolver, ct)` helper wired at TWO sites — the normal Continue path (after the outer Table fragment is emitted) + the forced-overflow path (so oversized tables still render inner geometry alongside the diagnostic). The helper resolves the wrapper's border + padding via the existing inline/block edge readers, computes the inner content-top-left + content-inline-size, constructs a `TableLayouter`, and calls `AttemptLayout` with `LastResort` strategy (sub-cycle 1 doesn't propagate rewind / break inside the table). **Diagnostics:** new `LAYOUT-TABLE-FEATURE-UNSUPPORTED-001` Warning code added to `PaginateDiagnosticCodes` + `NetPdf/Diagnostics/DiagnosticCodes` + `docs/diagnostics-codes.md`; emitted once per cell carrying `colspan` / `rowspan` attributes. Existing `PAGINATION-FORCED-OVERFLOW-001` is emitted when the row stack exceeds the fragmentainer's remaining block size (sub-cycle 1 doesn't split tables across pages). **Sub-cycle 1 scope limits + sub-cycle 2+ TODOs** (documented inline + in `docs/deferrals.md#table-auto-fixed-spans-borders`): CSS Tables L3 §3 auto-table-layout (shrink-to-fit columns via min/max-content); §3.5 fixed-table-layout (column widths from `<col>` + first-row cell widths); §6.3 border-collapse model + `border-spacing`; cell merging (`colspan` / `rowspan`); §11 captions; §6.4 column-group widths; per-page header / footer repeat across pages; multi-fragmentainer table splitting + row-level `break-inside: avoid`; RTL writing modes / row reversal. **Tests: 4164 unit / 4295 solution-wide passing** (+12 unit / +12 solution-wide over PR #48's 4152 / 4283 baseline — 9 new `TableLayouterTests` + 3 diagnostic parity tests; 4 skipped). New tests: [`TableLayouterTests`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Phase3/TableLayouterTests.cs) — 9 tests pinning: simple 2×2 emit order (outer + nested cell-content fragments + 2 row fragments + 4 cell fragments); row height equals max cell extent; equal-column-split offsets; empty table emits only the outer wrapper; `colspan` cell triggers `LAYOUT-TABLE-FEATURE-UNSUPPORTED-001`; oversized table triggers `PAGINATION-FORCED-OVERFLOW-001`; non-table rootBox kind rejected via `ArgumentException`; non-null incoming continuation rejected; rows nested inside `<thead>` / `<tbody>` collected via row-group recursion. Plus 3 diagnostic parity tests added to `DiagnosticCodesTests` (registry match, value stable, facade vs paginate agree). Plus new `table-auto-fixed-spans-borders` entry in `docs/deferrals.md` + `DeferralsParityTests.ExpectedDeferralIds`. AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green. Active-task pointer advances to **Task 12 sub-cycle 2** — `table-layout: auto`/`fixed` algorithms + `colspan` / `rowspan` cell merging + border-collapse model + captions + `<col>` widths — OR **Task 13** depending on review priority.)

**Phase 3 Task 11 sub-cycle 1 shipped + post-PR-#48 review hardening — Block + inline integration with InlineLayoutResult bundle, recursive nested dispatch, pagination integration, CSS box model, and 8 review findings** (historical entry; superseded by Task 12 sub-cycle 1 above. PR #47 (deferrals doc) merged at `988e63a`; this branch rebased on it. **Post-PR-#48 review hardening (8 findings, 5 P1):** (1) [P1 #1] **InlineLayoutResult bundle** — Phase 4 painter needs `ShapedRun[]` + preprocessed `TextRun[]` to resolve `LineFragment.Slices.ShapedRunIndex` into concrete `ShapedGlyph` data. New `src/NetPdf.Layout/Inline/InlineLayoutResult.cs` record struct bundles `Lines + ShapedRuns + PreprocessedRuns`. `InlineLayouter.Layout` (both overloads) + `LayoutPerRun` return this struct; `BoxFragment.InlineLines` renamed to `InlineLayout: InlineLayoutResult?`. Migrated 5 inline-layouter test files to use `.Lines` accessor. New painter-contract resolution test walks slices to concrete glyphs. (2) [P1 #2] **Recursive nested dispatch** — `EmitBlockSubtreeRecursive` now has an inline-only branch (`EmitInlineOnlyBlockInRecursion`) so `<div><p>Hello</p></div>` correctly emits the p's `InlineLayout`. `MeasureSubtreeVisualBlockExtentRecursive` includes inline block-axis extent via new `MeasureInlineOnlyBlockExtent`. (3) [P1 #3] **Pagination integration** — new `DispatchInlineOnlyBlock` captures `LayoutCheckpoint`, consults `IBreakResolver` via `BreakOpportunity.Block`, handles Rewind / BreakHere (forced overflow + clean PageComplete) / Continue. Oversized inline content emits `LAYOUT-FORCED-OVERFLOW` diagnostic. (4) [P1 #4] **`CollectInlineTextRuns` content handling** — `LineBreak` (`<br>`) injects synthetic U+2028 LINE SEPARATOR TextRun (survives `Normal` whitespace collapse + triggers mandatory break); `Marker` (list bullets) recurses into children with the marker's own Style; atomic inline (`InlineBlockContainer` / `InlineFlexContainer` / `InlineGridContainer` / `InlineTable` / `InlineReplacedElement`) emit new `LAYOUT-INLINE-ATOMIC-NOT-SUPPORTED-001` diagnostic + skip. (5) [P1 #5] **CSS box model honored** — new `ReadInlineOnlyBlockMetrics` reads margin/border/padding/width/`line-height`; new `ComputeInlineOnlyBlockLayout` resolves border-box from declared width (or full range when `auto`), places lines inside the content box, computes block-size = content + padding-vertical + border-vertical. `line-height` from CSS overrides the 1.2 × font-size fallback. (6) [P2 #6] **`NotSupportedException` catch** — `try/catch` around `InlineLayouter.LayoutPerRun` in `LayoutInlineContent`; falls back to Warning `LAYOUT-INLINE-UNSUPPORTED-001` diagnostic + no fragment emitted. Induced via `word-break:keep-all` vs `normal` mismatch test. (7) [P2 #7] **Diagnostic parity** — 9 new parity tests (3 codes × 3 checks each: registry match, value stable, facade vs paginate); `docs/diagnostics-codes.md` footer bumped + LAYOUT-* section extended. (8) [P2 #8] **End-to-end tests** — 12 new tests in `BlockInlineIntegrationTests.cs` covering all findings + painter-contract resolution. Plus follow-up commit adding `inline-atomic-boxes` entry to `docs/deferrals.md` + `DeferralsParityTests.ExpectedDeferralIds` (PR #47's enforcement, now ratified by this PR's branch via rebase). **Per-run mismatch acceptance matrix unchanged from sub-cycle 4** (WhiteSpace all 6, OverflowWrap Normal+Anywhere, WordBreak Normal+BreakAll with KeepAll throw, Hyphens all 3). **Sub-cycle 2+ TODOs documented inline:** margin-collapse between inline-only block + block siblings; per-line splitting for oversized inline; cache inline-pass across measure + emit; per-run line-height + CSS Text L3 strut/ascent-descent; atomic inline placeholder injection. AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green. **Phase 3 Task 11 sub-cycle 1 shipped — Block + inline integration** (historical entry; superseded by hardening review above. Continues from Task 10 cycle 3d sub-cycle 4 ([PR #46](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/46) merged at `23612c9`). Task 10 cycle 3d's per-source-run policy plumbing is now consumed by `BlockLayouter`: when the layouter encounters a block container whose children are entirely inline-level (e.g., a `<p>` containing only text + inline `<span>`s, or the `AnonymousBlock` boxes that `BoxBuilder` wraps inline runs in), it dispatches into `InlineLayouter.LayoutPerRun` and emits ONE `BoxFragment` for the inline-only block with the wrapped `LineFragment[]` carried on the new `BoxFragment.InlineLines` field. The Phase 4 painter consumes the line array to position shaped-glyph slices at successive baselines inside the fragment's border box. **Wiring (`BlockLayouter`):** new optional `IShaperResolver? shaperResolver = null` constructor parameter — when supplied, drives the inline pass; when null + inline content encountered, emits a `LAYOUT-INLINE-SKIPPED-NO-SHAPER-RESOLVER-001` diagnostic + skips (mirrors the pre-sub-cycle-1 behavior for back-compat with existing test fixtures). New `IsInlineOnlyBlockContainer` predicate detects the dispatch target. New private `LayoutInlineContent` method collects `TextRun`s via `CollectInlineTextRuns` (walks the subtree, picks up `BoxKind.TextRun` leaves with non-empty text; atomic inline-replaced / inline-block / inline-flex / inline-grid / inline-table / `<br>` are recognized but silently skipped — sub-cycle 2+ scope), calls `InlineLayouter.LayoutPerRun` with hard-coded `"Latn"` / `"en"` + `ParagraphDirection.LeftToRight` (UAX #24 + RTL deferred per `docs/deferrals.md`), computes a placeholder block extent (`lineCount × 1.2 × fontSize`, default 16 px when font-size unset — line-height property wiring deferred), emits the BoxFragment, advances `fragmentainer.UsedBlockSize`. **Margin chain reset semantics** for inline-only block: matches the existing non-block-level skip (line box breaks margin adjacency per CSS 2.1 §8.3.1). **`BoxFragment`** gains an optional `LineFragment[]? InlineLines` field (default null for back-compat with cycles 1-2c pure-block fragments). **Diagnostics:** new `LAYOUT-INLINE-SKIPPED-NO-SHAPER-RESOLVER-001` code added to `PaginateDiagnosticCodes` + `NetPdf/Diagnostics/DiagnosticCodes` + `docs/diagnostics-codes.md`. **Sub-cycle 1 scope limits + sub-cycle 2+ TODOs** (documented inline in the new `LayoutInlineContent` XML doc): mixed block + inline children inside one BFC; margin / border / padding honoring on the inline-only block itself; margin-collapse chain participation; widows / orphans (CSS Fragmentation L3 §4.3); `line-height` from `ComputedStyle`; `text-align` / `vertical-align`; RTL fragment-level slice reversal; UAX #24 script + BCP 47 language detection; inline content flowing around floats; atomic inline-replaced / inline-block / inline-flex / inline-grid / inline-table / `<br>` descendants.
