**Phase 3 Task 10 cycle 3d sub-cycle 4 shipped + post-PR-#46 review hardening — per-source-run Hyphens with per-position Liang gating + SH suppression per-run + lazy posToSrcRun**. **Post-PR-#46 review hardening (6 findings):** (1) [P1 Finding #1] **Per-position Liang gate** — sub-cycle 4 originally gated Liang application by the WORD's first letter's source-run Hyphens, but a word can span source runs with different Hyphens values. A Liang break position landing INSIDE a None/Manual segment (because the word started in Auto) would be wrongly recorded; conversely an Auto-tail word starting in None would skip Liang entirely. Fix: (a) `ApplyLiangPatterns` now runs Liang when ANY letter in the word is in a Hyphens=Auto source run (not just the first letter); (b) each returned Liang break position is gated by `posToSrcRun[concatIdx].Hyphens == Auto` before being recorded. Cross-run words now produce correct Liang break geometry. (2) [P1 Finding #2] **Disabled soft-hyphens don't suppress Liang** — CSS Text L3 §6.1.1's "soft-hyphen suppresses elsewhere-in-word Liang" rule should only count ACTIVE soft hyphens. A U+00AD whose source run has Hyphens=None is demoted + excluded from `hyphenationAfter[]`; suppressing Liang because of it would unfairly lose valid Auto opportunities in the same tokenized word. Fix: the suppression scan in `ApplyLiangPatterns` now checks `posToSrcRun[shConcatIdx].Hyphens != None` for each U+00AD in the word — only ACTIVE soft hyphens trigger the suppression. (3) [P2 Finding #3] **Lazy `posToSrcRun` allocation** — previously built unconditionally whenever `inlineTextPolicyPerRun` was supplied, even for non-hyphenation paths (mixed WhiteSpace / OverflowWrap / WordBreak). For large inline content this wasted 4 bytes per UTF-16 code unit. Fix: build the map ONLY when `inlineTextPolicyPerRun is not null && (hasSoftHyphen || anyHyphensAuto)` — the actual conditions that need per-position Hyphens decisions. (4) [P2 Finding #4] **Exact-geometry mixed-word Liang tests** — replaced loose assertions with 4 new tests pinning per-position behavior: Liang-breaks-inside-None-segment-suppressed; Liang-runs-when-only-later-letters-Auto; disabled-SH-does-NOT-suppress-Liang-in-Auto-segment; Manual-alongside-Auto-no-Liang-inside-Manual. (5) [P3 Finding #5] **Stale `LineBuilder.cs` XML docs refreshed** — the old "LineBuilder-only scope (cycle 3b stopgap)" + "CSS-property pipeline deferral" sections claimed overflow-wrap/word-break/hyphens weren't wired through ComputedStyle. That pipeline shipped in Task 10 cycles 2-4; docs now describe the production path (KeywordResolver → ComputedStyle → InlineTextPolicyMaterializer → LayoutPerRun → per-run array). (6) [P3 Finding #6] **Removed unused `sourceTextRuns` parameter** from `ComputeHyphenationPositions` (the per-run policy data flows via `inlineTextPolicyPerRun` + `posToSrcRun` directly). **Per-run mismatch acceptance matrix unchanged from sub-cycle 4:** WhiteSpace all 6, OverflowWrap Normal+Anywhere, WordBreak Normal+BreakAll (KeepAll throws), Hyphens all 3. Tests: **4125 unit / 4256 solution-wide passing** (+4 unit / +4 solution-wide over pre-hardening sub-cycle 4 at 4121; 4 skipped). New tests: 4 in `InlineLayouterCycle3dTests` covering Finding #1 (Liang-inside-None suppression, Liang-runs-when-later-Auto) + Finding #2 (disabled-SH doesn't suppress Liang) + Manual+Auto interaction. AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green. Active-task pointer advances to **Task 11** (Phase 4 painter cycle / `LineFragment[]` → `BoxFragment` conversion) — the per-run mismatch matrix is now complete enough for the painter to consume `LineFragment[]` end-to-end. KeepAll CJK suppression (UAX #24) and BreakSpaces-distinctive semantics are the remaining sub-cycle 5+ items.)

**Phase 3 Task 10 cycle 3d sub-cycle 4 shipped — per-source-run Hyphens via hyphenation pipeline** (historical entry; superseded by hardening review above. Continues from Task 10 cycle 3d sub-cycle 3 ([PR #45](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/45) merged at `9637137`). The `inlineTextPolicyPerRun` array already carried `Hyphens` through (sub-cycle 2 refactor + sub-cycle 3 validation); sub-cycle 4 wires the per-source-run decisions into the hyphenation pipeline. **Algorithm:** when `inlineTextPolicyPerRun` is supplied, `LineBuilder.Wrap` builds a `posToSrcRun: int[concatTotal]` map (lazy) so each concat position can look up its source run's Hyphens value. Two pipeline stages use this map: (1) **Soft-hyphen Allowed demotion** — the existing global "Hyphens=None demotes U+00AD breaks to Prohibited" pass becomes per-position; only positions whose source run has Hyphens=None get demoted. Positions in Manual/Auto runs keep their UAX #14 LB10 Allowed classification. (2) **`ComputeHyphenationPositions` + `ApplyLiangPatterns`** — per concat position, the soft-hyphen inclusion in `hyphenationAfter[]` is gated by source-run Hyphens (include if != None). The Liang per-word check uses the FIRST letter's source-run Hyphens (apply only if Auto). The sub-cycle 3 defense-in-depth guard (Wrap-side "per-run Hyphens must equal global") is REMOVED — direct callers can now pass a Hyphens mix freely. `InlineLayouter.LayoutPerRun` removes the throw on Hyphens mismatch; only WordBreak.KeepAll mismatch still throws (CJK semantics still pending UAX #24). **Per-run mismatch acceptance matrix as of sub-cycle 4:** WhiteSpace all 6 mixable, OverflowWrap Normal+Anywhere mixable, WordBreak Normal+BreakAll mixable (KeepAll on mismatch throws), Hyphens ALL 3 mixable. **Cycle 3d sub-cycle 4 deferrals (sub-cycle 5+ / Task 11):** WordBreak.KeepAll CJK inter-character break suppression (UAX #24 script detection + LB30b); BreakSpaces-distinctive semantics; UAX #24 + RTL fragment-level reversal; `LineFragment[]` → `BoxFragment` conversion (cycle 4); bidi-aware glyph painting. Tests: **4121 unit / 4252 solution-wide passing** (+4 unit / +4 solution-wide over PR #45 hardening at 4117; 4 skipped). New tests: 4 in `InlineLayouterCycle3dTests` covering soft-hyphen-in-None-run-not-wrap-candidate, soft-hyphen-in-Manual-run-IS-wrap-candidate, uniform-Auto regression, direct LineBuilder.Wrap Hyphens.None demotion proof. 4 prior throws-tests (cycle 3b, 3c, 3d sub-cycle 2, 3d sub-cycle 3) updated to assert handled behavior. AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green. Active-task pointer advances to **Task 11** (Phase 4 painter cycle / `LineFragment[]` → `BoxFragment` conversion) OR continue cycle 3d sub-cycle 5 (KeepAll CJK support via UAX #24 script detection) depending on review priority.)

**Phase 3 Task 10 cycle 3d sub-cycle 3 shipped + post-PR-#45 review hardening — per-source-run WordBreak.BreakAll with KeepAll throw + cross-run boundary + per-run Hyphens guard**. **Post-PR-#45 review hardening (5 findings):** (1) [P2 Finding #1] **KeepAll mismatch throws** — uniform KeepAll has always behaved like Normal (CJK inter-character break suppression needs UAX #24 script detection + LB30b), but accepting a KeepAll vs. {Normal, BreakAll} mismatch in per-run mode would silently lose KeepAll's intent. LayoutPerRun now throws NotSupportedException for KeepAll mismatches; uniform-KeepAll continues to silently approximate as Normal (documented). (2) [P2 Finding #2] **Per-run Hyphens defense-in-depth in Wrap** — LineBuilder.Wrap's per-run validation now rejects inlineTextPolicyPerRun entries whose Hyphens field differs from the global `hyphens` argument. Until sub-cycle 4 ships per-source-run Liang application, hyphenationAfter[] is built from the global hyphens arg only; direct callers (tests + future block-layouter wires) can't pass a Hyphens mix without triggering this guard. LayoutPerRun's caller-side check + the Wrap-side check together provide layered protection. (3) [P2 Finding #3] **Cross-run BreakAll boundary uses "either side may opt in"** — mirrors OverflowWrap's cross-run rule from sub-cycle 2. For the LAST glyph of a shaped run whose NEXT source run has BreakAll, perGlyphBreakAll is upgraded to true. This lets a Normal prefix wrap immediately at the run boundary of a following BreakAll span (instead of overflowing into the first BreakAll glyph before BreakAll's own upgrades take effect). (4) [P2 Finding #4] **Broader test coverage** — 8 new tests in InlineLayouterCycle3dTests: BreakAll-first-then-Normal-no-whitespace-boundary (Finding #3); Normal-immediately-followed-by-BreakAll-no-whitespace boundary (Finding #3 positive control); NoWrap+BreakAll interaction (NoWrap wins, downgrade after BreakAll upgrade); KeepAll mixed-with-Normal throws (Finding #1); invalid WordBreak/Hyphens enum values throw at Wrap entry (Finding #4); per-run Hyphens-must-match-global enforcement (Finding #2); direct LineBuilder.Wrap call with InlineTextPolicy[] proving end-to-end behavior. (5) [P3 Finding #5] **Stale docs refreshed** — InlineLayouter.cs adds an explicit per-run-mismatch acceptance matrix table (WhiteSpace all 6 / OverflowWrap Normal+Anywhere / WordBreak Normal+BreakAll / Hyphens throws + KeepAll throws); InlineTextPolicy.cs integration-status item for sub-cycle 3 + KeepAll/Hyphens deferral notes; LineFragment.cs shipped-capabilities ladder extended through sub-cycle 3; LineBuilder.Wrap's inlineTextPolicyPerRun XML doc documents WordBreak (sub-cycle 3 per-glyph) + Hyphens (sub-cycle 4 throws on mismatch with global). **Cycle 3d sub-cycle 3 deferrals (sub-cycle 4+):** per-source-run hyphens (Liang application per-run); KeepAll CJK semantics (UAX #24 script detection); BreakSpaces-distinctive semantics; UAX #24 + RTL fragment-level reversal; `LineFragment[]` → `BoxFragment` conversion (cycle 4); bidi-aware glyph painting. Tests: **4117 unit / 4248 solution-wide passing** (+8 unit / +8 solution-wide over pre-hardening sub-cycle 3 at 4109; 4 skipped). AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green. Active-task pointer advances to **Phase 3 Task 10 cycle 3d sub-cycle 4** — per-source-run hyphens (Liang per-run), OR **Task 11** (Phase 4 painter cycle) depending on review priority.)

**Phase 3 Task 10 cycle 3d sub-cycle 2 shipped + post-PR-#44 review hardening — per-source-run OverflowWrap plumbing + refactor to single InlineTextPolicy[] parameter + grapheme-cluster gate + cross-run wrap-friendly gate**. **Post-PR-#44 review hardening (5 recommendations):** (1) [P1 Rec #1] **Grapheme-cluster boundary gate** on the overflow-wrap:anywhere forced-break fallback. Per CSS Text L3, anywhere must keep grapheme clusters (UAX #29) together. The new `IsGraphemeBoundaryBetweenFlatGlyphs` helper checks the cursor-1 → cursor break point's UTF-16 position against the existing `graphemeBreakAfter` array + applies `IsBreakAllProtected` for ZWJ/WJ/NBSP adjacencies. Multi-glyph single-cluster shapes (combining marks, ZWJ emoji, regional-indicator flag pairs) are detected via `clusterEnd <= prevCluster` and protected. Anywhere now snaps to grapheme boundaries instead of mid-cluster. (2) [P1 Rec #2] **Cross-run wrap-friendly gate** on anywhere. Two adjacent non-wrap-friendly source runs (e.g., NoWrap+Pre or Pre+NoWrap with overflow-wrap=anywhere) cannot become anywhere break sites at their style boundary — per CSS Text L3 §5.1 overflow-wrap only has effect when white-space allows wrapping. Cross-run gate now requires at least ONE side to be wrap-friendly per WhiteSpace; if both sides are Pre/NoWrap, the boundary stays unbreakable. (3) [P2 Rec #4] **Refactor parallel per-run arrays to a single InlineTextPolicy[] parameter**. `LineBuilder.Wrap` no longer takes `whiteSpacePerRun: IReadOnlyList<WhiteSpace>?` + `overflowWrapPerRun: IReadOnlyList<OverflowWrap>?` separately. Replaced with one `inlineTextPolicyPerRun: IReadOnlyList<InlineTextPolicy>?` that bundles all 4 dimensions (WhiteSpace + OverflowWrap + WordBreak + Hyphens) in one coherent struct. Future sub-cycles (word-break, hyphens) can plumb through the same array without adding nullable parameters. `LayoutPerRun` builds one array lazily on first mismatch + extracts a `WhiteSpace[]` for the preprocessor when needed. Validation: length match + every entry's WhiteSpace/OverflowWrap/WordBreak/Hyphens enums must be defined. (4) [P2 Rec #3] **Strengthened sub-cycle 2 tests** with exact line/slice/glyph assertions. Previously `>= 2` patterns; now `Assert.Equal(6, result.Length)` + per-line glyph-range + advance assertions. Added 4 new tests: combining-mark cluster preserved under anywhere (Rec #1), NoWrap+Pre cross-run boundary not broken (Rec #2), Pre+NoWrap symmetry, Normal+Anywhere boundary IS broken when at least one side wrap-friendly (positive control). (5) [P3 Rec #5] **Stale docs refreshed** in InlineLayouter.cs (full cycle 3a→3d sub-cycle 2 capability ladder), InlineTextPolicy.cs (integration status reflects sub-cycle 2 refactor), LineFragment.cs (sub-cycle deferrals point to word-break/hyphens, not overflow-wrap). **Cycle 3d sub-cycle 2 deferrals (sub-cycle 3+):** per-source-run word-break (BreakAll per-glyph); per-source-run hyphens (Hyphens.Auto Liang per-run); BreakSpaces-distinctive semantics; UAX #24 script detection; RTL fragment-level reversal; `LineFragment[]` → `BoxFragment` conversion (cycle 4); bidi-aware glyph painting. Tests: **4107 unit / 4238 solution-wide passing** (+4 unit / +4 solution-wide over pre-hardening at 4103; 4 skipped). New tests: 4 in `InlineLayouterCycle3dTests` covering Rec #1 (combining-mark cluster preserved) + Rec #2 (NoWrap+Pre, Pre+NoWrap cross-run gates) + positive control (Normal+Anywhere boundary IS broken). Prior sub-cycle 2 tests' `>= 2` assertions replaced with exact 6-line/per-glyph geometry. AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green. Active-task pointer advances to **Phase 3 Task 10 cycle 3d sub-cycle 3** — per-source-run word-break + hyphens, OR **Task 11** (Phase 4 painter cycle) depending on review priority.)

**Phase 3 Task 10 cycle 3d sub-cycle 2 shipped — per-source-run OverflowWrap plumbing broadens LayoutPerRun matrix to accept overflow-wrap mismatches** (historical entry; superseded by hardening review above. Same-run breaks fire only when the run's OverflowWrap is Anywhere; cross-run breaks fire when EITHER side enables anywhere (boundary is a natural anywhere site for the affected run). **`InlineLayouter.LayoutPerRun`** now builds the per-source-run OverflowWrap array (lazily on first mismatch) + passes through to `LineBuilder.Wrap`. The cycle 3b/3c/3d-sub1 throw on overflow-wrap mismatch is REMOVED; only word-break + hyphens mismatches still throw. **Result:** mixed-mode `<span style="overflow-wrap:anywhere">` inside `overflow-wrap:normal` text now works without throwing — the anywhere span splits per Anywhere semantics while the surrounding Normal text stays intact. **Phase 3 Task 10 cycle 3d sub-cycle 1 shipped + post-PR-#43 review hardening — per-source-run WhiteSpace preprocessor with per-glyph trim + per-glyph anywhere gate + cancellation + soft-hyphen Liang suppression**. Continues from Task 10 cycle 3c ([PR #42](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/42) merged at `0f05fba`). Cycle 3c narrowed the accepted mixed-WhiteSpace matrix to {Normal, NoWrap}-only because the preprocessor was uniform-mode; cycle 3d sub-cycle 1 ships **`LineBuilder.PreprocessTextRunsPerRun(runs, modes[])`** — each source run is preprocessed with its OWN WhiteSpace mode. Cross-run state managed per the "preserve runs are atomic; collapse runs chain via `inWs`" rule: two consecutive collapse-mode runs (Normal/NoWrap/PreLine) chain their `inWs` state across the boundary so trailing+leading SPs collapse; preserve-mode runs (Pre/PreWrap/BreakSpaces) emit content character-for-character and reset `inWs=false` for the next collapse run. Document-leading SP strip applies only when Run 0 is a collapse mode; document-trailing SP strip applies only when the last run is a collapse mode. **`InlineLayouter.LayoutPerRun`** updated to call the new preprocessor when per-run WhiteSpace varies — removing the cycle-3c Normal/NoWrap matrix-narrowing throw. **Result:** mixed-mode inputs like `<pre>` inside `white-space:normal` text now work without throwing. **Algorithm change in LayoutPerRun:** when a WhiteSpace-only mismatch is detected, build the per-source-run `WhiteSpace[]` array (lazily) + delegate via `PreprocessTextRunsPerRun` instead of the uniform `PreprocessTextRuns`. All 6 WhiteSpace values participate; the cycle-3c IsCollapseModeMatrixMember predicate is removed. **Cycle 3d sub-cycle 1 deferrals (subsequent cycles):** per-glyph overflow-wrap / word-break / hyphens for mixed-mode descendants (currently throws); UAX #24 script detection; RTL fragment-level reversal; `LineFragment[]` → `BoxFragment` conversion (cycle 4); bidi-aware glyph painting via Phase 4 painter integration. New tests: 15 in [`InlineLayouterCycle3dTests`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Phase3/InlineLayouterCycle3dTests.cs) — `PreprocessTextRunsPerRun` length-mismatch + invalid-enum + null-arg validation (4 tests); uniform-Normal regression equivalence with `PreprocessTextRuns`; Pre+Normal preserves Pre + collapses Normal at boundary; Normal+Pre preserves both; preserve-only doesn't strip document-trailing SP; collapse-only strips document-trailing SP; LayoutPerRun Normal+Pre / NoWrap+PreWrap / Normal+PreLine / Normal+BreakSpaces / Pre+Normal-first all-handled (5 tests); overflow-wrap mismatch still throws. Plus 4 cycle 3c matrix-narrowing-throw tests REMOVED (the mixes are now handled — see cycle 3d tests for replacements with exact assertions). **Post-PR-#43 review hardening (6 recommendations):** (1) [P1] **Per-glyph IsBreakSpace from source-run WhiteSpace** — previously the global wrap-time `collapsesSpaces` flag tagged Pre/PreWrap/BreakSpaces SP glyphs as IsBreakSpace too (because LayoutPerRun passes wrapWhiteSpace=Normal globally to defer wrap decisions to the per-glyph downgrade), causing soft-wrap snap-back to TRIM preserved spaces. Fix: derive IsBreakSpace per-glyph by looking up `whiteSpacePerRun[shaped.Source.SourceTextRunIndex]` + checking `IsCollapseModeWhiteSpace`. New regression test pins PreWrap "AAA "+Normal " BBB" preserves the PreWrap trailing SP at the soft-wrap boundary. (2) [P1] **Per-glyph gate on overflow-wrap:anywhere fallback** — previously the global `wrapsAtAllowed=true` in per-run mode let the anywhere forced-break fallback fire INSIDE NoWrap/Pre source runs when all runs shared overflow-wrap:anywhere. Per CSS Text L3 §5.1 "overflow-wrap only has an effect when white-space allows wrapping". Fix: when whiteSpacePerRun is supplied AND cursor>lineStart, check if break point (cursor-1 → cursor) is INSIDE a NoWrap/Pre source run; if so, gate the anywhere fallback to NOT fire. New regression tests for Pre(anywhere)+Normal(anywhere) and NoWrap(anywhere)+Normal(anywhere). (3) [P2] **BreakSpaces docs clarified as approximation** — the prior "deferred to a subsequent cycle" framing implied a cleaner ladder than reality. Now WhiteSpace.cs + InlineTextPolicy.cs explicitly document that BreakSpaces is APPROXIMATED as PreWrap (preserve + wrap at UAX #14 Allowed); distinguishing CSS Text L3 §6.4 semantics (forced wrap candidates at every preserved SP + trailing-space wrap-vs-hang) are NOT implemented and tracked as a known fidelity gap. (4) [P2] **PreprocessTextRunsPerRun CancellationToken** — added optional `CancellationToken cancellationToken = default` parameter checked at method entry + once per source-run boundary. LayoutPerRun's per-run path now passes the token + checks immediately after preprocessing (before the potentially-expensive ShapeForLayout call). New tests for pre-cancelled token in both `PreprocessTextRunsPerRun` direct API + `LayoutPerRun` per-run mode. (5) [P3] **Stale LineFragment.cs cycle-3d docs updated** — removed the claim that LayoutPerRun only handles Normal/NoWrap matrix; added cycle 3d sub-cycle 1 capabilities (per-source-run preprocessor + per-glyph IsBreakSpace + anywhere gate); per-glyph overflow-wrap/word-break/hyphens deferred to sub-cycle 2. (6) [P2] **Liang positions suppressed inside soft-hyphen-containing words** — pre-existing CSS Text L3 §6.1.1 gap surfaced during review. The word tokenizer in `ApplyLiangPatterns` now treats U+00AD as a word-internal character (via new `IsAsciiLetterOrSoftHyphen` predicate) so "hyphen­ation" is identified as ONE word; per-word check then SKIPS Liang for any word containing U+00AD (only the explicit soft-hyphen position is used). New regression test pins "hyphen­ation" with budget 30 wraps at the soft-hyphen position (line 0 = 6 glyphs "hyphen"), NOT at a Liang position (which would give line 0 = 2 glyphs "hy"). **Cycle 3d sub-cycle 1 deferrals (subsequent cycles):** per-glyph overflow-wrap / word-break / hyphens for mixed-mode descendants (currently throws); BreakSpaces-distinctive semantics (forced wraps at every preserved SP + trailing-space wrap-vs-hang per §6.4); UAX #24 script detection; RTL fragment-level reversal; `LineFragment[]` → `BoxFragment` conversion (cycle 4); bidi-aware glyph painting via Phase 4 painter integration. Tests: **4098 unit / 4229 solution-wide passing** (+7 unit / +7 solution-wide over pre-hardening cycle 3d at 4091; 4 skipped). New tests: 5 new in `InlineLayouterCycle3dTests` (Rec #1 PreWrap trim guard, Rec #2 anywhere NoWrap/Pre gates × 2, Rec #4 cancellation × 2) + 2 new in `LineBuilderHyphenationTests` (Rec #6 soft-hyphen Liang suppression + regression guard). AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green. Active-task pointer advances to **Phase 3 Task 10 cycle 3d sub-cycle 2** — per-glyph overflow-wrap/word-break/hyphens metadata threading, OR **Task 11** (Phase 4 painter cycle / `LineFragment[]` → `BoxFragment` conversion) depending on review priority.)

**Phase 3 Task 10 cycle 3c shipped + post-PR-#42 review hardening — per-glyph WhiteSpace honoring (NoWrap-inside-Normal) with narrowed Normal/NoWrap matrix** [PR #42] (historical entry, superseded by Task 10 cycle 3d sub-cycle 1 above). Continues from Task 10 cycle 3b ([PR #41](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/41) merged at `c507a21` + post-merge review pass at `d26222b`). Cycle 3b shipped `LayoutPerRun(...)` that threw `NotSupportedException` on any policy mismatch; cycle 3c **relaxes mixed-mode WhiteSpace** by building a per-source-run WhiteSpace array + plumbing to a new `LineBuilder.Wrap` `whiteSpacePerRun` parameter. Glyphs in NoWrap/Pre runs get their UAX #14 Allowed opportunities downgraded to Prohibited at flat-build time. **Result:** mixed-mode `<span style="white-space:nowrap">` inside `white-space:normal` text now works without throwing. **Algorithm:** in `LayoutPerRun`, walk source runs + check each policy against the first non-empty's policy; on first mismatch, verify only WhiteSpace differs (other 3 fields must match) — else throw with explanatory message; if WhiteSpace-only, lazily build a `WhiteSpace[]` array indexed by source-run-index + plumb through `LineBuilder.Wrap`'s new optional `whiteSpacePerRun` parameter. The wrap-loop's flat-build pass uses `shaped.Source.SourceTextRunIndex` to look up per-glyph WhiteSpace + downgrades Allowed → Prohibited for NoWrap/Pre runs. Empty-run handling preserved (cycle 3b hardening) — empty runs ignored in the policy walk, all-empty input returns empty result. **Post-PR-#42 review hardening (7 recommendations, fixed in one squashed pass):** (1) [P1] **Narrowed accepted matrix to Normal/NoWrap-only** — Pre/PreWrap/PreLine/BreakSpaces mixed with collapse modes now throws `NotSupportedException` with explanatory message (collapse-vs-preserve cannot be reconciled post-shape; needs cycle 3d per-source-run preprocessing). Both Normal + NoWrap share collapse semantics per CSS Text L3 §4.1 so they're the safe subset. (2) [P1] **Per-glyph wrapsAtAllowed when whiteSpacePerRun supplied** — the global `wrapsAtAllowed` gate inside `LineBuilder.Wrap` now defers authoritatively to the per-glyph downgrade when per-run mode is active. Previously a leading NoWrap source run made `wrapsAtAllowed=false` globally, suppressing wraps even in a TRAILING Normal source run (Normal-after-NoWrap order bug). New regression test pins the fix. (3) [P1] **Preprocess pass uses `WhiteSpace.Normal` (not PreWrap)** for mixed mode — since the matrix is now Normal/NoWrap-only, both collapse identically + Normal is the correct unified mode. The earlier PreWrap-everywhere preprocess would preserve whitespace from NoWrap-source-runs that should have been collapsed. (4) [P2] **Compute `preprocessed` ONCE** + pass to both `ShapeForLayout` + `LineBuilder.Wrap` (previously called `PreprocessTextRuns` twice with identical args). (5) [P2] **Strengthened cycle 3c tests** — replaced `Assert.NotEmpty(result)` with exact `Slices.Length` / `ShapedRunIndex` / `GlyphStart` / `GlyphLength` / `SliceAdvance` / `EndsWithMandatoryBreak` assertions. New tests pin: NoWrap-span-inside-Normal wraps at outer boundary (line geometry + advance); Normal-run-after-NoWrap still wraps at its own boundary (Rec #2 fix); uniform-NoWrap collapses spaces correctly; matrix-narrowing throws for 4 illegal mixes (Pre/PreWrap/PreLine/BreakSpaces); per-run enum validation rejects undefined values. (6) [P2] **`whiteSpacePerRun` enum validation** — invalid enum values now throw `ArgumentException` at entry. (7) [P3] **Docs refresh** — `WhiteSpace.cs` / `InlineTextPolicy.cs` / `LineFragment.cs` summaries updated to reflect shipped 3a/3b/3c capabilities + deferred cycle-3d items (was claiming BreakSpaces / hyphenation / overflow-wrap were "deferred to cycle 3b/c" — those shipped). Plus [Copilot #4] **fixed misleading "only LAST glyph" comment** in `LineBuilder.Wrap`'s per-glyph WhiteSpace downgrade — the loop visits + downgrades EVERY glyph in a NoWrap/Pre source run independently. **Cycle 3c deferrals (cycle 3d+):** per-source-run preprocessing for Pre/PreWrap/PreLine/BreakSpaces mixed with Normal/NoWrap (collapse-vs-preserve); per-glyph overflow-wrap / word-break / hyphens for fully heterogeneous mixed-mode; UAX #24 script detection; RTL fragment-level reversal; `LineFragment[]` → `BoxFragment` conversion (cycle 4); bidi-aware glyph painting via Phase 4 painter integration. Tests: **4080 unit / 4208 solution-wide passing** (+7 unit / +7 solution-wide over pre-hardening cycle 3c at 4073; 4 skipped). AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green. Active-task pointer advances to **Phase 3 Task 10 cycle 3d** — per-source-run preprocessing for the broader WhiteSpace matrix + per-glyph overflow-wrap/word-break/hyphens, OR **Task 11** (Phase 4 painter cycle / `LineFragment[]` → `BoxFragment` conversion) depending on review priority.)

**Phase 3 Task 10 cycle 3b shipped — `InlineLayouter.LayoutPerRun(...)` per-source-TextRun policy** [PR #41] (historical entry, superseded by Task 10 cycle 3c above). Continues from Task 10 cycle 3 ([PR #40](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/40) merged at `2b575ea` + post-merge review pass at `1c4bd7a`). Cycle 3 shipped the containing-block-style `Layout` overload that applies a uniform policy; cycle 3b adds **`LayoutPerRun(...)` — reads each source-TextRun's policy + verifies they all match**, throwing `NotSupportedException` on mixed-mode descendants. **Why this is the right shape:** CSS Text L3 §3-§6 properties all inherit, so for the 95% case all source TextRuns share the same policy (inherited from the containing block) + the new overload silently delegates to the cycle-3a uniform path. For mixed-mode descendants (e.g., `<span style="white-space:nowrap">` inside `white-space:normal` text) the overload throws loudly with a descriptive message — the failure mode is loud + deterministic instead of silently using the wrong policy. Full per-glyph metadata for mixed-mode is scheduled for cycle 3c. **Algorithm:** read `InlineTextPolicy` from each TextRun's `Style.ReadInlineTextPolicy()`; check that all match the first via record-struct equality; if all match, delegate to the cycle-3a explicit-args path; if any differs, throw `NotSupportedException` with run-index + both policies in the message. **Cycle 3b deferrals (cycle 3c+):** per-glyph metadata stream threaded through `LineBuilder.Wrap` so mixed-mode descendants work without throwing; UAX #24 script detection; RTL fragment-level reversal; `LineFragment[]` → `BoxFragment` conversion (cycle 4); bidi-aware glyph painting via Phase 4 painter integration. New tests: 8 in [`InlineLayouterCycle3bTests`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Phase3/InlineLayouterCycle3bTests.cs) — null arg, empty input, uniform default policy, uniform NoWrap, mixed-white-space-throws, mixed-overflow-wrap-throws, mixed-hyphens-throws, singleton run. Tests: **4055 unit / 4191 solution-wide passing** (+8 unit / +8 solution-wide over PR #40 hardening at 4047; 4 skipped). AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green. Active-task pointer advances to **Phase 3 Task 10 cycle 3c** — per-glyph metadata stream for mixed-mode descendants (the actual implementation behind the cycle 3b "throws" guard), OR **Task 11** (Phase 4 painter cycle / display-list IR / `LineFragment[]` → drawn glyphs) depending on review priority.)

**Phase 3 Task 10 cycle 3 shipped — `InlineLayouter.Layout(...,ComputedStyle,...)` overload** [PR #40] (historical entry, superseded by Task 10 cycle 3b above). Continues from Task 10 cycle 2 ([PR #39](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/39) merged at `eadc9f5` + post-merge review pass at `941a959`). The cycle-2 materializer's cross-property folds (`word-break:break-word` → bumps overflow-wrap to Anywhere; `overflow-wrap:break-word` → folds to Anywhere; `white-space:break-spaces` → folds to Normal) all flow through the new convenience path. **Cycle 3 simplification:** policy is read from ONE containing-block style + applied uniformly. **Phase 3 Task 9 cycle 3b sub-cycle 2 shipped — CSS `overflow-wrap` + `word-break`** [PR #36] (historical entry, superseded by Task 9 cycle 3b sub-cycle 3 above). Continues Task 9 from cycle 3b sub-cycle 1 ([PR #35](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/35) merged at `8dc32d1` + post-merge review pass at `10f40f4`). New types in [`src/NetPdf.Layout/Inline/`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Inline/): [`OverflowWrap`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Inline/OverflowWrap.cs) — byte enum (Normal=0, Anywhere=1) per CSS Text L3 §5.1; [`WordBreak`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Inline/WordBreak.cs) — byte enum (Normal=0, BreakAll=1, KeepAll=2) per CSS Text L3 §5.2. **`LineBuilder.Wrap` updates:** new `OverflowWrap overflowWrap = OverflowWrap.Normal` + `WordBreak wordBreak = WordBreak.Normal` parameters (5th + 6th positional, before `cancellationToken`). When `wordBreak == BreakAll`, the flat-build pass upgrades every Prohibited per-glyph opportunity to Allowed (forces aggressive glyph-level wrapping). When `overflowWrap == Anywhere` AND the line would overflow AND no Allowed candidate exists in `[lineStart, cursor)`, a forced break fires at `cursor - 1` (single-glyph-wider-than-line case still emits 1 glyph and starts fresh). Both args validated up-front with descriptive `ArgumentOutOfRangeException`. **Composition rules:** OverflowWrap.Anywhere only fires under overflow + no candidate (preserves UAX #14 candidates as preferred); WordBreak.BreakAll respects Pre/NoWrap's `wrapsAtAllowed=false` rule (Pre's strict no-wrap policy wins over BreakAll). KeepAll has no observable effect for Latin/Cyrillic/Greek content (CJK semantics activate when UAX #24 lands in cycle 4). **Cycle 3b sub-cycle 2 deferrals (sub-cycle 3):** hyphenation via Liang patterns (primitives in `NetPdf.Text.Hyphenation`); `overflow-wrap: break-word` (deprecated alias for `anywhere` with subtle min-content-size differences); per-source-TextRun policy (Task 10). **Phase 3 Task 9 cycle 3b sub-cycle 1 shipped — CSS `white-space` preprocessing + wrap-time `Pre`/`NoWrap` mode** [PR #35] (historical entry, superseded by Task 9 cycle 3b sub-cycle 2 above). Continues Task 9 from cycle 3a ([PR #34](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/34)). Cycle 3a wrapped raw input AS-IS (no white-space preprocessing); cycle 3b sub-cycle 1 ships **CSS Text L3 §4.1 white-space processing** + wrap-time `Pre`/`NoWrap` honoring as the foundation for cycle 3b sub-cycles 2–3 (overflow-wrap, hyphenation). New types in [`src/NetPdf.Layout/Inline/`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Inline/): [`WhiteSpace`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Inline/WhiteSpace.cs) — byte enum (Normal=0, Pre=1, NoWrap=2, PreWrap=3, PreLine=4) covering the 5 most-common CSS Text L3 §3 values. `break-spaces` deferred. New static method on [`LineBuilder`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Inline/LineBuilder.cs): `PreprocessWhitespace(text, mode)` → `string` — applies CSS Text L3 §4.1 collapse / preserve rules per mode. **Algorithm:** Normal/NoWrap collapses any run of {SP, TAB, LF, CR, FF} into a single SP + strips leading/trailing whitespace; Pre/PreWrap pass through unchanged; PreLine collapses SP+TAB runs to single SP but preserves LF+CR (segment breaks) and strips end-of-line trailing SP per §4.1.2. **`LineBuilder.Wrap` updates:** new `WhiteSpace whiteSpace = WhiteSpace.Normal` parameter (4th positional, before `cancellationToken`); when mode is `Pre` or `NoWrap` the wrap loop suppresses Allowed-break wrapping (only Mandatory breaks split lines). Plus `WhiteSpace` value validated up-front with descriptive `ArgumentOutOfRangeException`. **Cycle 3b sub-cycle 1 deferrals (sub-cycles 2/3):** `overflow-wrap: anywhere` + `word-break: break-all` (sub-cycle 2 — forced break at any glyph when no candidate exists); hyphenation via Liang patterns (sub-cycle 3 — primitives already exist in `NetPdf.Text.Hyphenation`); CSS Text L3 §4.1.1 segment-break-transformation rules (CR-LF→LF normalization belongs in the HTML preprocessor, not the inline pass); preserved-tab tab-size handling for Pre mode; per-run white-space mode (cycle 3b currently applies one mode for the whole inline pass — per-source-TextRun white-space lands when InlineLayouter integrates in Task 10); `break-spaces` mode (rarely needed for v1 invoice/report content). New tests: [`LineBuilderWhitespaceTests`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Phase3/LineBuilderWhitespaceTests.cs) — 20 tests covering: 3 PreprocessWhitespace arg-validation (null text, undefined mode, empty text returns empty for all 5 modes); 4 Normal-mode cases (collapse consecutive spaces incl. tabs/CRLF, strip leading/trailing, pure-whitespace collapses to empty); Pre + PreWrap pass-through invariants; NoWrap collapse-like-Normal; PreLine collapse-spaces-preserve-LF + end-of-line-SP-strip + CRLF-preserved; Wrap-time NoWrap suppresses Allowed wrap (one overflowing line) but still honors Mandatory; Wrap-time Pre suppresses Allowed wrap; Wrap-time PreWrap + PreLine wrap at Allowed; Wrap-time undefined-WhiteSpace throws. Tests use the synthetic Latin font (no system-font dependency). Tests: **3917 unit / 4047 solution-wide passing** (+20 unit / +20 solution-wide over cycle 3a's review pass at 3897; 4 skipped). AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green. Active-task pointer advances to **Phase 3 Task 9 cycle 3b sub-cycle 2** — `overflow-wrap` + `word-break` (forced break at any glyph when no candidate exists).)

**Phase 3 Task 9 cycle 3a shipped — `LineBuilder.Wrap` UAX #14 line-break + naive greedy wrapping** [PR #34] (historical entry, superseded by Task 9 cycle 3b sub-cycle 1 above). Continues Task 9 from cycle 2 ([PR #33](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/33)). Cycle 2 wired up shaping (step 3 of the 6-step inline pipeline); cycle 3a ships **steps 4 + 6 — UAX #14 break-opportunity scan + greedy line wrapping** as MVP. New types in [`src/NetPdf.Layout/Inline/`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Inline/): [`ShapedRunSlice`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Inline/ShapedRunSlice.cs) — readonly record struct (`ShapedRunIndex`, `GlyphStart`, `GlyphLength`, `SliceAdvance`) representing one contiguous glyph slice from a single `ShapedRun` that fits on a single line; [`LineFragment`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Inline/LineFragment.cs) — readonly record struct (`Slices[]`, `TotalAdvance`, `EndsWithMandatoryBreak`) representing one wrapped line ready for the painter. New static method on [`LineBuilder`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Inline/LineBuilder.cs): `Wrap(sourceTextRuns, shapedRuns, availableInlineSize, ct)` — returns `LineFragment[]`. **Algorithm:** rebuild concat text; run `LineBreakAlgorithm.FindBreaks` (UAX #14); flatten glyphs across all shaped runs into a `(runIdx, glyphIdxInRun, advance, opportunity)` array indexed by global glyph position; walk with two cursors (`lineStart`, `cursor`) tracking the most recent `Allowed` opportunity in `[lineStart, cursor]`; on overflow snap back to candidate + emit; on `Mandatory` (LF/CR/NEL/¶/etc.) force fragment boundary; when no candidate exists overflow is allowed (cycle 3b adds `overflow-wrap`). Each emit groups consecutive same-run glyphs into one `ShapedRunSlice`. **Cycle 3a deferrals (cycle 3b/c):** white-space variants (`pre`/`pre-wrap`/`pre-line`/`nowrap`); `overflow-wrap: anywhere` + `word-break: break-all`; hyphenation via Liang patterns (primitives already exist in `NetPdf.Text.Hyphenation`); `text-align` (start/end/center/justify); `vertical-align` baseline shifts; RTL fragment-level reversal (cycle 2 already produces RTL glyph arrays in HarfBuzz visual order; cycle 3c reverses fragment-level slice order for RTL paragraphs); UAX #24 per-run script detection; integration with `InlineLayouter` (Task 10). New tests: [`LineBuilderWrapTests`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Phase3/LineBuilderWrapTests.cs) — 14 tests covering empty input, 7 arg validations (null sourceTextRuns/shapedRuns + 5 inline-size cases: zero/negative/NaN/+∞), single short run fits in one line, soft-wrap on space separator (UAX #14 LB18), mandatory break at LF (LB5), long unbreakable run overflows without snap-back (no candidate fallback), multi-shaped-run line emits one slice per run, total-advance equals sum-of-slice-advances invariant, cancellation token observed at line emission. Tests use the synthetic Latin font (no system-font dependency). Tests: **3884 unit / 4014 solution-wide passing** (+14 unit / +14 solution-wide over the cycle 2 review pass's 3870; 4 skipped). AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green. Active-task pointer advances to **Phase 3 Task 9 cycle 3b** — white-space variants + `overflow-wrap` + hyphenation.)

**Phase 3 Task 9 cycle 2 shipped — `LineBuilder.Shape` shaping integration via `HbShaper`** [PR #33] (historical entry, superseded by Task 9 cycle 3a above). Continues Task 9 from cycle 1 (PR #32). Cycle 1 shipped steps 1+2 of the 6-step inline pipeline (bidi → itemize → shape → break-opp → measure → wrap); cycle 2 ships **step 3 — shape — plus the per-run advance measurement** half of step 5. New types in [`src/NetPdf.Layout/Inline/`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Inline/): [`ShapedRun`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Inline/ShapedRun.cs) — readonly record struct (Source ItemizedRun + ShapedGlyph[] + TotalAdvance) carrying HarfBuzz output + the run's summed inline-axis advance for cycle 3's wrap pass; [`IShaperResolver`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Inline/IShaperResolver.cs) — `IDisposable` interface that resolves an `HbShaper` for a given `ComputedStyle` (the line builder doesn't construct shapers itself; resolution + caching is an injected concern so production can ship a font-registry-backed resolver while tests can drive the line builder with a synthetic-font resolver). Tests use a synthetic-font resolver wrapping [`SyntheticFont.Build()`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Text/Fonts/OpenType/SyntheticFont.cs) — no system-font dependency. (Note: `HbShaper` is sealed so the test can't intercept its `Shape` call to pin script/language/direction passthrough at the resolver layer; those invariants are deferred to integration tests in cycle 3 / Task 10 once the full pipeline can be exercised end-to-end with real glyph outputs.) **Phase 3 Task 8 cycle 2 shipped — flow-around-floats + cross-fragmentainer deferral** [PR #31] (historical entry, superseded by Task 9 above). Continues Task 8 from cycle 1 (PR #30). Cycle 1 tracked floats + resolved `clear` but in-flow blocks ignored floats for sizing (visually overlapped). Cycle 2 adds [`FloatManager.GetAvailableInlineRange(blockY, containingStart, containingEnd)`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Layouters/FloatManager.cs) — returns `(InlineStart, InlineEnd)` reduced by any float whose vertical extent intersects `blockY`. Per CSS 2.2 §9.5: a non-floating block shrinks its inline-size to leave room for floats on both sides. **`BlockLayouter` updates:** the outer loop calls `GetAvailableInlineRange` at each child's hypothetical-Y; `borderBoxInlineSize` derives from `availInlineEnd - availInlineStart - margins`; the fragment's `InlineOffset` anchors at `availInlineStart + marginInlineStart` so blocks visually flow PAST left floats. **Cross-fragmentainer float deferral** per Fragmentation L3 §5: new private `WouldFloatOverflow` peek + dispatch — when a float would overflow + the page has prior emitted content, returns `PageComplete` with the float as the resume target (cross-page float per CSS Fragmentation L3 §5). Float-on-empty-page that's taller than ANY page falls back to cycle 1's emit + `PAGINATION-FORCED-OVERFLOW-001`. **Cycle 2 deferrals (subsequent cycles):** nested in-flow blocks use parent's content-area only — they don't dynamically re-query floats at their nested-Y (cycle 3); a single block ignores cycle-2's float-bottom — it doesn't widen below the float's bottom (cycle 3); float CONTAINING block alignment to nested parent vs BFC-wide (cycle 3); inline content + line-boxes flowing around floats (Phase 3 Task 9-10 LineBuilder). The post-PR-30 `PostPr30_trailing_float_overflow_emits_diagnostic` test was rewritten as `PostPr30_trailing_float_overflow_when_no_prior_emission_still_diagnoses` to pin the cycle-2 fallback case (taller-than-any-page floats). **Phase 3 Task 7 cycle 2c shipped — subtree-aware pagination (atomic MVP)** [PR #29] (historical entry, superseded by Task 8 above). Continues Task 7 from cycle 2b (PR #28). Pre-cycle-2c the outer break decision + cursor advance both used the box's OWN `borderBoxBlockSize`, so containers with overflowing block-level descendants silently clipped past the fragmentainer + subsequent siblings visually overlapped the overflow. Cycle 2c adds [`MeasureSubtreeVisualBlockExtent`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Layouters/BlockLayouter.cs) — a pre-measure pass returning the maximum block-axis extent reached by any descendant (max of own border-box + descendant bottoms, applying adjacent-margin collapse). The chunk-fit + cursor-advance both use this measured extent so: (a) oversized subtrees trigger a break-before via the resolver pushing the entire subtree to the next page atomically per CSS Fragmentation L3 §5; (b) subtrees that can't fit any page commit via the existing forced-overflow forward progress + emit `PAGINATION-FORCED-OVERFLOW-001` (pre-fix this case was silent — outer measure missed the overflow); (c) siblings AFTER an overflowing subtree are positioned past the overflow's bottom edge with no visual overlap. Non-flow block kinds (Table/Flex/Grid/Replaced) are atomic to the measure pass — only their own border-box size contributes (same `IsBlockFlowContainerOwnedByBlockLayouter` predicate gating as `EmitBlockSubtreeRecursive`). Recursion uses the existing `MaxRecursionDepth=256` DoS guard. **Cycle 2c MVP scope.** Subtrees are paginated ATOMICALLY (push wholly to next page OR forced-overflow). True mid-subtree splits — parent's first half on page 1 + parent's second half on page 2 — are deferred to **cycle 2d** with a new failing-skip pin (`Cycle2d_oversized_subtree_splits_across_two_pages_at_inner_break`). Mid-splits require recursive continuation tokens (`BlockContinuation.NestedContinuation`) + break consultation inside `EmitBlockSubtreeRecursive` + recursive resume on retry. New tests: 6 cycle 2c regression tests in [`BlockLayouterTests`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Phase3/BlockLayouterTests.cs) — `Cycle2c_nested_overflow_pushes_subtree_to_next_page_when_prior_content_exists` (oversized subtree after a fitting sibling triggers break-before with continuation pointing at parent), `Cycle2c_nested_overflow_on_fresh_page_emits_with_diagnostic` (subtree taller than any page commits via forced-overflow + emits diagnostic — pre-fix silent), `Cycle2c_subsequent_sibling_does_not_overlap_overflowing_subtree` (sibling after an overflowing parent positioned at parent's subtree-extent bottom, not parent's own bottom), `Cycle2c_leaf_box_subtree_extent_equals_own_border_box` (sanity — cycle 1 leaf-only behavior unchanged), `Cycle2c_subtree_extent_respects_margin_collapse_between_nested_siblings` (collapse applied during the measure pass), `Cycle2c_subtree_extent_treats_table_as_atomic_using_own_height` (Table/Flex/Grid/Replaced not recursed into). The cycle 2c deferral pin from cycle 2b is now ACTIVATED + replaced by the 6 explicit tests above. Tests: **3755 unit / 3885 solution-wide passing** (+6 unit / +6 solution-wide over PR #28's 3749; 4 skipped — the 2 cycle-3 deferral pins + 1 capture harness + the new cycle-2d deferral pin; the cycle-2c pin is now removed). AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green. Active-task pointer advances to **Phase 3 Task 7 cycle 2d** — true mid-subtree pagination splits — OR alternatively to **Phase 3 Task 8** (`FloatManager`) if the reviewer prefers to ship the float interaction next.)

**Phase 3 Task 7 cycle 2b shipped — recursive nested-block layout** [PR #28] (historical entry, superseded by cycle 2c above). Continues Task 7 from cycle 2 (PR #26). Cycles 1 + 2 walked `_rootBox.Children` only; a `div > p` tree emitted only the `div` fragment. Cycle 2b adds [`EmitBlockSubtreeRecursive`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Layouters/BlockLayouter.cs) — a private helper that walks each emitted child's block-level descendants + emits a `BoxFragment` for each at correctly nested offsets relative to the parent's content area. The recursion runs from BOTH the Continue path + the forced-overflow path, so nested descendants render even when the outer block is forced through overflow forward-progress. Adjacent-margin collapse (§8.3.1 — same `MarginCollapse.Collapse` helper used by the outer loop) is applied between nested siblings; non-block children still break adjacency. **Cycle 2b deferrals (still — to subsequent commits):** auto-height resolution per §10.6.3 (cycle 3 — `ReadLengthPxOrZero` returns 0 for auto so a container with `height: auto` + children renders with a 0-sized parent fragment but the children still emit at correct offsets); cross-subtree pagination splits (cycle 2c — currently each top-level subtree is atomic for pagination); parent / first-child margin collapse + BFC root suppression (cycle 3 — needs BFC detection); logical-axis property reads (cycle 3); width/height auto resolution (cycle 3). New tests in [`BlockLayouterTests`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Phase3/BlockLayouterTests.cs): `Cycle2b_layouter_emits_fragments_for_nested_block_descendants` (div > p → 2 fragments), `Cycle2b_layouter_recurses_through_three_levels` (root > section > article > h1 → 3 fragments at correctly nested offsets), `Cycle2b_nested_children_apply_inline_offsets_inside_parent_padding` (child's InlineOffset = parent contentLeft + child marginLeft), `Cycle2b_nested_siblings_apply_margin_collapse` (two block siblings inside a parent → collapse applies), `Cycle2b_nested_non_block_children_are_skipped` (TextRun siblings are silently skipped, only the block sibling emits). The cycle-2 deferral pin `Cycle2_Layouter_lays_out_nested_block_descendants` is now ACTIVATED + replaced by these 5 explicit tests. Tests: **3741 unit / 3871 solution-wide passing** (+8 unit / +8 solution-wide over PR #27's 3733; 3 skipped — the 2 cycle-3 deferral pins + 1 capture harness; the cycle-2 nested-recursive-layout pin is now removed). Active-task pointer advances to **Phase 3 Task 7 cycle 2c** — cross-subtree pagination splits — OR alternatively to **Phase 3 Task 8** (`FloatManager`) if the reviewer prefers to ship the float interaction next.)

**Phase 3 Task 7 cycle 2 shipped — adjacent-sibling margin collapse per CSS 2.1 §8.3.1** (historical entry, superseded by cycle 2b above). Continues Task 7 from cycle 1 (PR #22). Cycle 1 laid out blocks by SUMMING adjacent margins (`marginEnd_N + marginStart_{N+1}`); CSS 2.1 §8.3.1 specifies these must COLLAPSE to a single margin per the formula `max(positives) - max(absolute values of negatives)`. **New types:** [`MarginCollapse`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Layouters/MarginCollapse.cs) — pure-static `Collapse(m1, m2)` helper implementing the spec formula. Commutative + tested in isolation; will be shared across `BlockLayouter` + future `FlexLayouter` / `GridLayouter` / `TableLayouter` collapse paths. **`BlockLayouter` updates:** introduces `prevBlockMarginEnd` + `isFirstBlockOnPage` state per attempt; for each block child, computes `effectiveTopGap` (= `marginStart` for first block, else `MarginCollapse.Collapse(prevBlockMarginEnd, marginStart)`) + `topShift` (= `effectiveTopGap` for first, else `effectiveTopGap - prevBlockMarginEnd`); the `BlockOffset` of the emitted fragment becomes `fragmentainer.UsedBlockSize + topShift`. The `marginBoxBlockSize` (drives `chunkBlockSize` for the resolver's fit-check) now uses `topShift`-not-`marginStart` so collapse is reflected in pagination accounting. **Cross-page collapse suppression** per CSS Fragmentation L3 §6.1 — the layouter resets the collapse chain on each page entry: `prevBlockMarginEnd = 0` + `isFirstBlockOnPage = true` at `AttemptLayout` entry, so the first block on a fresh page applies its FULL marginTop without collapsing across the page break. **Cycle 2 deferrals (still — to subsequent commits):** parent/first-child + parent/last-child collapse (cycle 3 — needs recursive layout + BFC detection); BFC root suppression (cycle 3 — needs `display: flow-root` / `overflow` / float / abs-pos detection); empty-box collapse (cycle 3 — synthetic empty-box path); recursive nested-block layout (cycle 2b — separate commit); logical-axis property reads (cycle 3); width/height auto resolution (cycle 3). New tests: [`MarginCollapseTests`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Phase3/MarginCollapseTests.cs) — 24 theory cases covering both-positive, both-negative, mixed-sign, zero-with-negative, commutativity, idempotence on equal margins, plus extreme-magnitude cases. Updated [`BlockLayouterTests`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Phase3/BlockLayouterTests.cs) — 6 new collapse-specific tests (positive-positive max, mixed-sign difference, both-negative most-negative, three-block collapse chain, cross-page first-block-uses-full-marginTop, single-block-no-phantom-collapse) + 2 existing test math updates (`Layouter_stacks_multiple_blocks_with_collapse` rename + offset 220 instead of 225; `Layouter_returns_PageComplete_when_next_block_overflows` cumulative now 490 instead of 500 — the 10px savings is the collapse). The cycle-2 deferral pin `Cycle2_Layouter_collapses_adjacent_margins` is now ACTIVATED by the new tests; the cycle-2 nested-recursive-layout pin remains skipped until cycle 2b ships. Tests: **3699 unit / 3830 solution-wide passing** (+27 unit / +27 solution-wide over cycle 1's 3672; 4 skipped including the 3 cycle-2/3 deferral pins still active). AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green. Active-task pointer advances to **Phase 3 Task 7 cycle 2b** — recursive nested-block layout (or, if reviewer prefers, ship cycle 2 standalone + open cycle 2b as a separate PR).)

**Phase 3 Task 7 cycle 1 shipped — BlockLayouter scaffolding + project-reference flip** (historical entry, superseded by cycle 2 above). Per the Phase 3 plan §"BlockLayouter" — the first real layouter implementing [`ILayouter`](src/NetPdf.Paginate/ILayouter.cs). Walks the block-level children of a root [`Box`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Boxes/Box.cs), stacks them vertically, consults the [`IBreakResolver`](src/NetPdf.Paginate/IBreakResolver.cs) at every block boundary, emits [`BoxFragment`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Layouters/BoxFragment.cs) into an [`IBlockFragmentSink`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Layouters/IBlockFragmentSink.cs) as each box is positioned. **Project-reference flip:** pre-Task-7 [`NetPdf.Paginate.csproj`](src/NetPdf.Paginate/NetPdf.Paginate.csproj) referenced [`NetPdf.Layout.csproj`](src/NetPdf.Layout/NetPdf.Layout.csproj) — but the reference was DEAD (Paginate never used any Layout types). Per the file layout in [CLAUDE.md](CLAUDE.md) layouters live in `NetPdf.Layout` + must implement `ILayouter` from `NetPdf.Paginate` — requiring `Layout → Paginate`, not the reverse. Cycle 1 flips the dependency: Paginate becomes a leaf-ish node (depends only on the facade for the diagnostic parity test); Layout depends on Paginate so layouters can implement `ILayouter` + consume `IBreakResolver` / `FragmentainerContext` / `LayoutCheckpoint` directly. **New types in [`src/NetPdf.Layout/Layouters/`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Layouters/):** [`BoxFragment`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Layouters/BoxFragment.cs) (record struct: Box + InlineOffset + BlockOffset + InlineSize + BlockSize; the layouter's per-box output, ready for Phase 4's painter); [`IBlockFragmentSink`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Layouters/IBlockFragmentSink.cs) (extends `NetPdf.Paginate.IFragmentSink` from Task 5 — `Emit(fragment)` + `Cursor` + `RollbackTo(cursor)` for rewind support); [`ComputedStyleLayoutExtensions`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Layouters/ComputedStyleLayoutExtensions.cs) (decodes typed `ComputedSlot` payloads — cycle 1 covers resolved-px lengths only; cycle 3 will add percentage resolution + auto handling per CSS 2.1 §10.3); [`BlockLayouter`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Layouters/BlockLayouter.cs) (the layouter itself). **Cycle 1 algorithm:** for each block-level child, read margin / padding / border / height as CSS px (auto + percentage default to 0 — cycle 3 wires real resolution); compute margin-box block-axis extent; consult resolver via `BreakOpportunity.Block`; on `Continue` emit fragment + advance `fragmentainer.UsedBlockSize`; on `BreakHere` return `LayoutAttemptOutcome.PageComplete` with `BlockContinuation(ResumeAtChild, ConsumedBlockSize)`; on `Rewind` propagate `LayoutAttemptOutcome.NeedsRewind` with the named checkpoint. Inline / atomic children skipped (Task 10 `InlineLayouter` will handle them). **Cycle 1 deferrals (subsequent commits on this branch):** margin collapsing per CSS 2.1 §8.3.1 (cycle 2); BFC root detection + intrinsic sizing modes (cycle 3); width/height auto resolution per §10.3.3 + §10.6.2 (cycle 3); percentage resolution against containing-block (cycle 3); float interaction (Phase 3 Task 8); avoid-break / break-inside metadata extraction from ComputedStyle (cycle 3 wires the `BreakInside` / `BreakBefore` / `BreakAfter` properties through to `BreakOpportunity` flags). New [`BlockLayouterTests`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Phase3/BlockLayouterTests.cs) — 12 tests covering: single block fits + emits fragment with correct offset/size; inline-axis offset uses MarginLeft + size uses ContentInlineSize - margins; multi-block stacking with correct sequential block-axis offsets; page-break dispatch when next block overflows + `BlockContinuation` shape; resume-from-continuation on the second page; non-block children silently skipped; empty root returns `AllDone`; constructor null-arg validation; `OperationCanceledException` thrown when token fires; force-break dispatch via custom resolver; `IBlockFragmentSink.Cursor` increments on emit + `RollbackTo` truncates. Tests: **3660 unit / 3791 solution-wide passing** (+12 unit / +12 solution-wide over Task 5's 3648 baseline; 1 skipped). AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green. Active-task pointer advances to **Phase 3 Task 7 cycle 2** — margin collapsing per CSS 2.1 §8.3.1.)

**Phase 3 Task 5 shipped — bounded retry coordinator + 6-recommendation review pass + 2 Copilot fixes** (historical entry, superseded by Task 7 above). Per the Phase 3 plan §"Re-layout loop discipline" + Task 5's spec — the orchestrator that drives an [`ILayouter`](src/NetPdf.Paginate/ILayouter.cs) through up to 2 retries with progressively-relaxed [`LayoutAttemptStrategy`](src/NetPdf.Paginate/ILayouter.cs) (Strict → DropAvoidInside → LastResort), emitting [`PAGINATION-FORCED-OVERFLOW-001`](docs/diagnostics-codes.md) when the LastResort attempt fires. **New types in [`src/NetPdf.Paginate/`](src/NetPdf.Paginate/):** [`ILayouter`](src/NetPdf.Paginate/ILayouter.cs) (the layouter-facing contract real layouters implement in Tasks 7+); `LayoutAttemptResult` (record struct with `Outcome` + `Continuation` + `RewindTo` + `Cost` + factory helpers `PageComplete` / `AllDone` / `NeedsRewind`); `LayoutAttemptOutcome` enum (`PageComplete` / `AllDone` / `NeedsRewind`); `LayoutAttemptStrategy` enum (`Strict` / `DropAvoidInside` / `LastResort`); [`LayoutRetryCoordinator`](src/NetPdf.Paginate/LayoutRetryCoordinator.cs) (`MaxRetries=2` per the plan's bound; `Run(layouter, fragmentainer, ref layout, resolver)` returns the layouter's terminal result, never `NeedsRewind` to its caller). **New diagnostic infrastructure in [`src/NetPdf.Paginate/Diagnostics/`](src/NetPdf.Paginate/Diagnostics/):** [`PaginateDiagnostic`](src/NetPdf.Paginate/Diagnostics/PaginateDiagnostic.cs) (record struct mirroring `NetPdf.Diagnostic`); `PaginateDiagnosticSeverity` enum (`Info` / `Warning` / `Error`); [`PaginateDiagnosticCodes`](src/NetPdf.Paginate/Diagnostics/PaginateDiagnosticCodes.cs) (string constants — the diagnostic-codes parity test verifies these match the facade's `NetPdf.DiagnosticCodes.PAGINATION-*`); [`IPaginateDiagnosticsSink`](src/NetPdf.Paginate/Diagnostics/IPaginateDiagnosticsSink.cs) (interface — same pattern as `NetPdf.Css.Diagnostics.ICssDiagnosticsSink`, kept inside Paginate so the assembly doesn't reference the public facade). **Algorithm:** for-loop over `attempt ∈ [0..MaxRetries]`; map attempt to strategy via `AttemptToStrategy`; emit `PAGINATION-FORCED-OVERFLOW-001` BEFORE the LastResort attempt runs (so consumers see the warning even if the layouter has issues); call `layouter.AttemptLayout(fragmentainer, ref layout, resolver, strategy)`; if outcome is not `NeedsRewind`, return; otherwise `RewindTo.RestoreInto(fragmentainer, ref layout)` (per Phase 3 Task 4 review fix #6 the restore reseats `layout.Fragmentainer` if a speculative swap occurred) + advance to next attempt. Defensive: a layouter contract violation (returning `NeedsRewind` on the LastResort attempt) is caught + escalated to a synthetic `PageComplete` rather than infinite-looping. New [`LayoutRetryCoordinatorTests`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Phase3/LayoutRetryCoordinatorTests.cs) — 22 tests covering: `AttemptToStrategy` mapping (5 theory cases including saturation past `MaxRetries`); trivial PageComplete + AllDone (no retries, no diagnostic emission); single-retry success; double-retry success with diagnostic emitted at LastResort; layouter contract violation defense (LastResort still returning `NeedsRewind`); null-sink handling; diagnostic message includes page index; checkpoint restoration via a `StateMutatingMockLayouter` that mutates state on attempt 0 + verifies state is restored on attempt 1; null-arg validation (using try/catch since `ref LayoutContext` can't cross lambda boundaries); `LayoutAttemptResult` factory helpers; `PaginateDiagnosticCodes` string-literal pinning + parity check with facade's `NetPdf.DiagnosticCodes`. **PR #21 review pass — 6 user recommendations + 2 Copilot inline fixes** (a59365e + b9c…): (1) **NeedsRewind requires non-null RewindTo** — `LayoutAttemptResult.ValidateOrThrow` enforces the invariant; coordinator throws `InvalidOperationException` rather than silently retrying from dirty state; the `NeedsRewind` factory is non-nullable so direct construction with null is impossible. (2) **Fragmentainer sync after restore** — coordinator now reassigns its local `fragmentainer` from `layout.Fragmentainer` after every `RestoreInto`, so the next `AttemptLayout` receives the captured (post-speculative-swap-undo) instance. (3) **Fragment-output rollback** — new optional `IFragmentSink` interface; coordinator calls `RollbackTo(checkpoint.FragmentOutputCursor)` on rewind so layouters that emit fragments incrementally can discard them. Layouters that emit only on `PageComplete` leave the sink null. (4) **`IBreakResolver : IDisposable`** — both `BreakResolver` + `OptimizingBreakResolver` implement `Dispose()` returning the final held lease via the lease-token CAS. The integrating layout pipeline drives via `using var resolver = ...`. (5) **Wire `PAGINATION-OPTIMIZER-FALLBACK-001`** — `OptimizingBreakResolver` constructor now accepts an optional `IPaginateDiagnosticsSink`; emits the diagnostic on every batched fallback (with the `FallbackReason` from `OptimizerResult`). Closes the gap where future layouters could silently drop the diagnostic by forgetting to inspect `FellBackToGreedy`. (6) **`CancellationToken` threaded through** — `LayoutRetryCoordinator.Run` + `ILayouter.AttemptLayout` accept a token (default `None`); coordinator checks it before each attempt + layouters check inside long-running inner loops. Mock layouters in tests propagate the token. (7) **Original-page-index in diagnostic** — coordinator captures `fragmentainer.PageIndex` at entry so the forced-overflow message reports the page that originally had problems (rather than 0 after restoration). (8) [Copilot] XML doc on `LayoutAttemptResult.PageComplete` no longer says "zero cost" — accepts any non-negative cost. Tests updated for the new `ILayouter` signature (added `CancellationToken`); 17 new regression tests covering: invariant violation throws, Fragmentainer sync after restore, `RollbackTo` called with captured cursor, two-rewind rollback sequencing, no-rollback when fragmentSink null, resolver `Dispose` returns held lease, `using var resolver` releases on scope exit, `OptimizingBreakResolver` emits fallback diagnostic on `FellBackToGreedy`, no-emit-when-no-fallback, null-sink-no-throw, cancellation before first attempt, cancellation between retries, `PageComplete` non-zero cost. Tests: **3648 unit / 3779 solution-wide passing** (+18 unit / +18 solution-wide over the cycle-1 baseline of 3630; 1 skipped). AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green.

Tests: **3648 unit / 3779 solution-wide passing**. AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green. **Phase 3 Task 4 shipped — bounded DP optimizer + 7-recommendation review pass + 8 Copilot inline fixes** (historical entry, superseded by Task 5 above). Per the Phase 3 plan §"Bounded DP optimizer" — replaces the Task 1 greedy stub with a real cost-minimizing implementation, then hardened with the user's 7 review recommendations + Copilot's 8 inline comments. **Cycle 1 — bounded DP optimizer.** New types in [`src/NetPdf.Paginate/`](src/NetPdf.Paginate/): [`Optimizer`](src/NetPdf.Paginate/Optimizer.cs) (Knuth-Plass-style sliding-window DP with 2-page lookahead — at each page boundary enumerate `(b1, b2)` candidate pairs minimizing `Score(b1) + Score(b2)`, commit `b1` only, slide forward); [`OptimizerResult`](src/NetPdf.Paginate/OptimizerResult.cs) (record carrying `BreakIndices` + `TotalCost` + `FellBackToGreedy` + `FallbackReason`); [`OptimizingBreakResolver`](src/NetPdf.Paginate/OptimizingBreakResolver.cs) (production `IBreakResolver`, delegates batched to `Optimizer.Optimize`, streaming degrades to greedy). [`IBreakResolver`](src/NetPdf.Paginate/IBreakResolver.cs) extended with `ResolveBreaks(opportunities, ctx)`; greedy [`BreakResolver`](src/NetPdf.Paginate/BreakResolver.cs) Task-1 stub gets matching impl. **Cycle 2 — 7 review recommendations + 8 Copilot inline comments.** (1) [Rec #1 + Copilot #2 + Copilot #6] **Terminal-break semantics fix** — pre-fix the DP committed at least one break for any non-empty input even when the entire remainder fit on one page. New early-exit: if the tail past `pageStart` fits on a single fragmentainer AND no forced break is reachable, commit no break. (2) [Rec #2 + Copilot #1 + Copilot #8] **Page-local cost scoring** — added `pageStart` parameter (default 0) to [`CostModel.Score`](src/NetPdf.Paginate/CostModel.cs); the trailing-blank ratio now computes against `(opportunity.UsedBlockSize - pageStart)`, recovering correct per-page measurements when the optimizer batches across pages. Coordinate-space contract clarified in `IBreakResolver` XML doc — streaming uses per-fragmentainer `UsedBlockSize`, batched uses cumulative-across-window. (3) [Rec #3] **Per-window DP budget caps** — new `MaxCandidatesPerPage = 256` (single-page candidate cap) + `MaxPairEvaluations = 65_536` (cumulative pair-evaluation budget across the run); either trip falls back to greedy. Pathological inputs (1000 zero-height candidates piling onto one page) now degrade gracefully rather than blowing the O(k²) inner loop. (4) [Rec #4] **Forced-break tightening** — when an author-forced break is reachable on the current page, commit at exactly its position without running `(b1, b2)` optimization. Section-boundary rewards no longer insert extra earlier breaks before a forced break. (5) [Rec #5] **Paragraph-aware widow scoring** — new `ParagraphId` field on `BreakOpportunity` (default 0); the optimizer counts subsequent same-`ParagraphId` line opportunities for accurate `lineCountAfterBreak` widow scoring. Layouters that don't supply `ParagraphId` get a heuristic fallback counting consecutive `LineBoundary` opportunities. (6) [Rec #6] **`LayoutContext.Fragmentainer` restoration** — [`LayoutCheckpoint.Capture`](src/NetPdf.Paginate/LayoutCheckpoint.cs) now snapshots `layout.Fragmentainer` into a new `CapturedFragmentainerRef` field; `RestoreInto` reseats `layout.Fragmentainer` back to it on rewind. Pre-fix a speculative attempt that swapped to a cloned fragmentainer left `layout.Fragmentainer` pointing at the discarded clone after restore. (7) [Rec #7] **Lease-token pool ownership** — [`LayoutCheckpointPool`](src/NetPdf.Paginate/LayoutCheckpoint.cs) now stamps a unique lease token (via `Interlocked.Increment` on a `long` counter) onto each rented checkpoint; `Return` uses an atomic CAS to compare the caller's lease token against the checkpoint's currently-stamped value. Stale-after-rerent + immediate double-return + concurrent multi-thread Returns are all rejected by a single mechanism — replacing the prior `ConcurrentDictionary<LayoutCheckpoint, byte> _inPool` belt-and-suspenders. New `CheckpointLease` readonly struct wraps the rented checkpoint + the token; `IBreakResolver.RegisterCheckpoint(CheckpointLease)` propagates the lease through the resolver-internal Return path. (8) [Copilot #3, #4, #5] **Single-chunk-too-tall detection** — `CostModel.Score` adds `BreakInsideAvoidViolation` penalty when `ChunkBlockSize > contentBlockSize` regardless of position; greedy fallback in `Optimizer` + `BreakResolver.ResolveBreaks` also commit + apply the overflow cost when a chunk on a fresh page (`pageSoFar == 0`) exceeds the fragmentainer extent. (9) [Copilot #7] **PROGRESS.md duplicate "Last updated" fixed** — only the topmost entry now has the prefix; historical entries demoted to bare paragraphs. New [`PaginationOptimizerTests`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Phase3/PaginationOptimizerTests.cs) — **60 tests** (+24 over cycle 1) covering: cycle-1 scenarios (forced/avoid/overflow/multi-page/section-boundary/streaming/lease-mgmt/null-arg), the new terminal-break semantics (single-fitting + multi-fitting return empty), page-local scoring (`pageStart` validation + recovery), `ChunkBlockSize > page` (cost-model + DP + greedy), paragraph-aware widow scoring, forced-break-displacement-by-section-reward defense, unreachable-forced-break later-iteration commit, per-page cap fallback, pair-eval-budget fallback, fragmentainer restoration after speculative swap, capture stamps `CapturedFragmentainerRef`, stale-lease rejection after re-rent, double-return rejection via lease token, default-lease no-op, `using`-block dispose, lease-token uniqueness, cumulative-`UsedBlockSize` end-to-end. Foundation tests updated for the lease API throughout. Tests: **3599 unit / 3729 solution-wide passing** (+24 unit over cycle-1's 3575; 1 skipped). AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green. Active-task pointer advances to **Phase 3 — Fragmentainer-aware layout + pagination** (Tasks 5-30 ahead — re-layout loop with bounded retry, BlockLayouter, FloatManager, InlineLayouter, TableLayouter, MulticolLayouter, FlexLayouter, GridLayouter, AbsoluteLayouter, @page rules, page-margin boxes, generated content, W3C conformance integration, performance tuning, `0.7.0-beta` tag).)

**Phase 3 Task 1 shipped — pagination foundation** (historical entry, superseded by Task 4 above). Per the Phase 3 plan's strong emphasis on "build the paginator first" the first PR delivers the layouter-facing interfaces every later layouter consumes: [`FragmentainerContext`](src/NetPdf.Paginate/FragmentainerContext.cs) (per-page state — page index, content-area dimensions, used height, named-string carry-forward); [`IBreakResolver`](src/NetPdf.Paginate/IBreakResolver.cs) + [`BreakDecision`](src/NetPdf.Paginate/BreakDecision.cs) + [`BreakAction`](src/NetPdf.Paginate/BreakAction.cs) + [`BreakOpportunity`](src/NetPdf.Paginate/BreakOpportunity.cs) + `BreakOpportunityClass` (the layouter↔paginator API surface); [`LayoutCheckpoint`](src/NetPdf.Paginate/LayoutCheckpoint.cs) + `LayoutCheckpointPool` (mutable + pooled, ConcurrentBag with 64-instance soft cap matching the Phase 2 ComputedStyle pattern); [`LayoutContinuation`](src/NetPdf.Paginate/LayoutContinuation.cs) hierarchy (`BlockContinuation` / `InlineContinuation` / `TableContinuation` / `FlexContinuation` / `GridContinuation`); [`LayoutContext`](src/NetPdf.Paginate/LayoutContext.cs) ref struct (containing-block dimensions + writing mode + bidi block-direction + counter map; lazy-allocated counter dict so a layout pass that doesn't use author counters pays zero allocation); [`WritingMode`](src/NetPdf.Paginate/WritingMode.cs) enum (`HorizontalTb` / `VerticalRl` / `VerticalLr` — sideways-rl/lr emit the existing `CSS-WRITING-MODE-SIDEWAYS-UNSUPPORTED-001`); [`CostModel`](src/NetPdf.Paginate/CostModel.cs) with documented penalty constants from the Phase 3 plan's table (`BreakInsideAvoidViolation = 1_000_000`, `StrandedHeading = 1000`, `Orphan = 500`, `Widow = 500`, `FlexOrGridLineSplit = 400`, `TableRowMidCellSplit = 300`, `LargeBlankTrailingArea = 200`, `SectionBoundaryReward = -100`); [`BreakResolver`](src/NetPdf.Paginate/BreakResolver.cs) Task-1 stub implementation that always picks Continue when the next chunk fits + BreakHere when it doesn't (greedy; the bounded DP optimizer replaces this in Task 4). New diagnostic codes [`PAGINATION-OPTIMIZER-FALLBACK-001`](docs/diagnostics-codes.md) (Info) + [`PAGINATION-FORCED-OVERFLOW-001`](docs/diagnostics-codes.md) (Warning) wired to the registry. New [`PaginationFoundationTests`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Phase3/PaginationFoundationTests.cs) — 23 tests covering FragmentainerContext clone/named-string carry-forward, LayoutCheckpoint pool rent-reset semantics + null-Return safety, LayoutContext counter lazy alloc + IncrementCounter + Read-default-zero, the full CostModel penalty matrix (BreakInsideAvoid effectively-infinite + SectionBoundary negative-reward + Orphan / Widow / TableRowMidCell / LargeBlankTrailing + clean-block-boundary-zero-cost), BreakResolver Continue/BreakHere/RegisterCheckpoint/GetLastCheckpoint + custom-orphan/widow override, BreakDecision.Continue singleton, and continuation-record value-equality. Tests: **3506 unit / solution-wide passing** (+23 over Phase D's 3483; 1 skipped). AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green.
