Phase A security hardening shipped — pre-Phase-3 hardening pass addressing 8 high-confidence findings from the dedicated HTML-to-PDF security audit (Neodyme html-renderer-to-RCE, Intigriti SSRF guide, DomPDF @font-face RCE, Apryse argument-injection, Stirling-PDF SSRF, hacktricks dynamic-PDF survey, libwebp CVE-2023-4863, HarfBuzz CVE-2024-56732 + cycle-2 backlog). All 8 land before Phase 3 builds layout on top of the Phase 2 surface. (1) [SEC] **A-1 widened HTML URL strip** — [`HtmlParsingHost.StripJavaScriptUrls`](src/NetPdf/HtmlParsingHost.cs) cycle 1 only covered `<a href>` / `<area href>` / `xlink:href`; the deep-review threat model + the DomPDF / Apryse / EvoPDF CVE survey confirm that `<form action>`, `<iframe src>`, `<object data>`, `<embed src>`, `<base href>`, and `<meta http-equiv="refresh" content="0;url=...">` all reach a sink that interprets URLs in real-world engines. New `StripDangerousUrlOnAttribute` helper covers all 6 attribute paths; recognized schemes widened from `javascript:` to also include `vbscript:` (legacy IE) and `data:` (the standard SSRF/XSS sneak path). One `HTML-JAVASCRIPT-URL-IGNORED-001` per stripped attribute. Safe `https:` / `http:` URLs pass through unchanged — Phase 5's `IResourceLoader` is the right control point for those once fetching is wired. (2) [SEC] **A-2 event-handler attribute strip** — `on*`-prefixed attributes (`onclick`, `onload`, `onerror`, `onmouseover`, etc.) stripped from every element with new `HTML-EVENT-HANDLER-IGNORED-001` (Info severity). Cycle 1's documented decision was "leave in place because PDF readers can't dispatch them"; the deep review reversed this — Phase 5's PDF/UA tagged-structure emission could surface attribute values into accessibility metadata, where dispatch becomes the consumer's problem. ASCII case-insensitive match catches `OnClick` / `ONLOAD` etc. (3) [SEC] **A-3 cumulative `var()` expansion budget per element** — [`VarSubstitution.Substitute`](src/NetPdf.Css/Cascade/VarSubstitution.cs) cycle 1's `MaxOutputLength = 1 MiB` was a per-CALL cap; `VarResolver` calls Substitute repeatedly per element (once per custom property + once per non-custom declaration), so N properties each near the cap totaled N MiB. New `VarSubstitution.Budget` class threaded through every Substitute call sharing the same element; default 10 MiB per element. Charge the final output length against the budget; on exhaustion emit `CSS-VAR-EXPANSION-LIMIT-001` once + return Invalid for this and subsequent calls. Pseudos on the same element share the budget (otherwise an attacker could amplify by 5–10× via `::before`/`::after`/`::marker`/`::first-line`/`::first-letter`). (4) [SEC] **A-4 nested at-rule depth limit** — [`CascadeResolver.CollectFromRules`](src/NetPdf.Css/Cascade/CascadeResolver.cs) cycle 1 had no depth bound on `@media` / `@supports` / `@layer` / `@import` recursion; a stylesheet with 1000 nested `@media` rules would blow the stack. New `MaxAtRuleNestingDepth = 32` constant; threaded through `CollectAtRule`, `CollectLayerAtRule`, `CollectImportRule`. On excess nesting emit `CSS-AT-RULE-UNKNOWN-001` once + return cleanly. (5) [SEC] **A-5 `CssContentList` output cap** — generated content from `::before` / `::after` / `::marker` is rendered into the output PDF; without a cap, an attacker can bloat the box tree + downstream PDF via `<span data-x="...10MB...">` + `::before { content: attr(data-x) attr(data-x) attr(data-x) }`. New `MaxContentOutputChars = 64 KiB` cap with `TryAppendBounded` helper; on overflow emit `CSS-CONTENT-FUNCTION-UNSUPPORTED-001` + the pseudo generates no box. (6) [SEC] **A-6 factored `DiagnosticTextSanitizer`** — central utility for sanitizing untrusted text fragments before they flow into `CssDiagnostic.Message`. Originally inlined in `CascadeResolver` (deep review C-2 selector ANSI-injection defense); centralizing prevents drift across 8+ emission sites. Strips C0 (0x00..0x1F) + DEL (0x7F) + C1 (0x80..0x9F) → U+FFFD; truncates at 120 chars + appends ellipsis. Applied at: `CascadeResolver` selector-parse warnings (already done), `ColorResolver.EmitInvalid` + `LengthResolver.EmitInvalid` (untrusted property values), `CssContentList.Truncate` (now delegates to the central util). (7) [SEC] **A-7 `SourceLocation.File` path normalization** — `PublicDiagnosticsSinkAdapter.ConvertLocation` was passing the host-supplied `BaseUri` verbatim into the diagnostic; an absolute filesystem path like `file:///C:/Users/Foo/secret/index.html` leaked host filesystem topology. New `DiagnosticTextSanitizer.SanitizeFilePath` reduces absolute paths to basename; sentinels (`<inline>`, `<unknown>`, `about:blank`) + `https:` / `http:` URLs pass through unchanged. (8) [SEC] **A-8 per-stylesheet selector-parse-warning budget cap** — new `SelectorParseWarningBudgetSink` decorator throttles `CSS-PARSE-WARNING-001` to 100 per stylesheet + emits one summary diagnostic when the cap is exceeded. A hostile CSS with thousands of broken selectors otherwise floods the consumer's sink (CI logs, structured-log infrastructure, etc.); the cap keeps the signal intact (first 100 still surfaced) while silencing the spam tail. Other diagnostic codes pass through unbudgeted. New tests: **+24 unit** in [`PhaseASecurityHardeningTests`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Phase2/PhaseASecurityHardeningTests.cs) — 5 theory cases for A-1 (one per extended attribute), 2 facts for A-1 data: + meta-refresh + a passthrough check, 6 theory + 1 fact for A-2 (case-insensitive event-handler match), 1 fact for A-3 cumulative budget, 1 fact for A-4 deep-nesting protection, 1 fact for A-5 content-cap, 2 facts for A-6 sanitizer (control-char strip + length cap), 3 facts for A-7 path normalization, 1 fact for A-8 budget. Existing tests updated: `HtmlParsingHostTests.ParseAsync_event_handler_attributes_are_left_in_place` flipped to `_are_stripped` (contract reversal); `HtmlParsingHostCorpusTests.Corpus_tailwind_cdn_emits_script_diagnostic` widened to allow either `HTML-SCRIPT-IGNORED-001` or `HTML-EVENT-HANDLER-IGNORED-001` in the diagnostic set. Snapshot regenerated for fixture `09-script-and-javascript-urls` to reflect the new uniform diagnostic-message format. Tests: **3262 unit / 3388 solution-wide passing** (+33 over the previous 3229/3355 baseline — +24 new Phase A facts + +9 from prior deep-review hardening that landed alongside this branch). AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green. Active-task pointer remains **Phase 3 — Fragmentainer-aware layout + pagination**.

Phase 2 deep review hardening pass shipped — addressed all 7 review recommendations spanning the full Phase 2 surface. (1) [P1] [`CssParserAdapter`](src/NetPdf.Css/Parser/CssParserAdapter.cs) style-rule slot alignment by selector identity, not just by kind. Cycle-1 paired any `CssRuleSlotKind.StyleRule` slot with any next `ICssStyleRule` from AngleSharp — so a dropped rule like `li::marker { ... }` (AngleSharp.Css 1.0.0-beta.144 emits an empty-selector rule for it) consumed the NEXT rule's slot, corrupting source location ordinals + recovery merging downstream. New `SlotMatchesAngleSharpRule` two-tier check: (a) AngleSharp's empty selector pairs with any slot prelude (covers the `::marker`-drop case while preserving the parsed declarations); (b) non-empty AngleSharp selectors must match the slot's normalized prelude (whitespace-collapsed, combinator-canonicalized) ordinal-equal; (c) otherwise demote slot to opaque without advancing the AngleSharp cursor. New `AdaptStyleRule(rule, preprocess, slot, ctx)` overload uses the slot's prelude when AngleSharp's selector is empty, restoring the authored selector text. (2) [P1] `EmitOpaqueFromSlot` recovers declarations from `RawBody`. Cycle-1 emitted dropped style rules with `Declarations: ImmutableArray<CssDeclaration>.Empty` — losing every declaration in the dropped block. New `CssPreprocessor.ScanAllDeclarations(string)` parses every property:value pair from a body string (sibling to the existing modern-only `ScanForModernDeclarations`); `EmitOpaqueFromSlot` invokes it on `slot.RawBody` then materializes via `ToCssDeclarations`. A dropped `li::marker { content: counter(items); color: red }` now lands in the AST with both declarations populated, so the CSS-CONTENT-FUNCTION-UNSUPPORTED-001 emission becomes reachable through the production path. (3) [P1] Inline `style=""` runs through `CssPreprocessor` recovery. Cycle-1's [`CascadeResolver.WalkInlineStylesRecursive`](src/NetPdf.Css/Cascade/CascadeResolver.cs) called `CssParserAdapter.AdaptInlineStyle(anglesharpStyle)` which fed AngleSharp's already-corrupted parsed `ICssStyleDeclaration` to the typed pipeline — `style="color: oklch(...)"` and modern multi-arg `attr()` were lost or misdiagnosed. New public `AdaptInlineStyleWithRecovery(style, rawStyleText, location)` constructs a synthetic `CssStyleRuleRecovery` from `ScanForModernDeclarations(rawStyleText)` and feeds the same merge pipeline as `<style>` blocks. End-to-end: `<p style="color: oklch(...)">` now emits CSS-MODERN-COLOR-FUNCTION-UNSUPPORTED-001 via the production path. (4) [P2] `@supports` validates the VALUE per CSS Conditional L3 §4.1.3, not just the property name. Cycle-1's `SupportsParser.ParsePrimary` returned `PropertyMetadata.NameToId.ContainsKey(prop)` — `@supports (color: not-a-real-color)` returned true because `color` is a registered property, so the guarded block applied. New probe: when the property name is registered, run the value through `PropertyResolverDispatch.Resolve(propertyId, rawValue, diagnostics: null)` and accept any `ResolutionState` other than `Invalid` (Resolved + Deferred both count, so var()/calc() values that resolve at layout time correctly count as "supported"). (5) [P2] [`CalcResolver`](src/NetPdf.Css/Cascade/CalcResolver.cs) finite guards on numeric parsing + binary arithmetic per IEEE 754 boundary semantics. Cycle-1 silently propagated `1e500 → Infinity` and `1e150 * 1e150 → Infinity` into the rewritten CSS text — downstream consumers saw the literal "Infinity" / "NaN" string instead of `CSS-CALC-INVALID-001`. New literal-time `IsFinite(n)` check on parsed numbers + new `Finite(magnitude, unit, reason)` wrapper applied at every Add / Subtract / Multiply / Divide site so overflow on composition also lands in the diagnostic dispatcher rather than the rewritten value text. Subsequent `var()`/`calc()` consumers see the original text preserved + can fall back to the property's initial value per CSS L4 §4.1. (6) [P2] [`CancellationToken`](src/NetPdf/Phase2/Phase2Pipeline.cs) threads INTO each major walker, not just between stages. Cycle-1's Task 17 hardening Rec 5 added `ThrowIfCancellationRequested()` at every stage boundary in `Phase2Pipeline.Run`; on a hostile-sized document a single stage (cascade matching against a 100k-element doc) ran to completion before the next boundary check. New `cancellationToken` parameter on `CascadeResolver.Resolve` + `BoxBuilder.Build` + `SemanticTreeBuilder.Build`; checked at every stylesheet, every DOM element walk in `WalkElement` / `WalkInlineStyles` / `BuildElementBoxes` / `WalkNode`. `SemanticTreeBuilder`'s `WalkContext` record struct gains a `CancellationToken` field so `with` expressions automatically propagate it to nested calls. Pre-cancelled token throws `OperationCanceledException` from inside the stage, not at the next boundary. (7) [P2] [`Phase2Result.Dispose`](src/NetPdf/Phase2/Phase2Result.cs) returns box-owned `ComputedStyle` instances to the pool. Cycle-1 marked styles attached to `Box` nodes as `IsBoxOwned` so the cascade-time `Dispose()` couldn't return them (premature pool release would let re-rental clear the slots while the box still references them) — but no explicit disposal sweep existed, so every conversion leaked one `ComputedStyle` per styled box / pseudo / fragment-pseudo to GC instead of recycling. New `ComputedStyle.ReleaseFromBox()` clears `_isBoxOwned` + delegates to `Dispose()`; new `Phase2Result.Dispose()` walks the box tree once, deduping by `ReferenceEqualityComparer` (in case future cascade optimizations share styles across siblings), and calls `ReleaseFromBox` on every unique style + `FirstLineStyle` + `FirstLetterStyle`. Phase2Result becomes `IDisposable` (still a `record struct`) so `using var result = await Phase2Pipeline.RunFromHtmlAsync(...)` is the typical call site. New tests: **+9 unit** in [`Phase2DeepReviewHardeningTests`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Phase2/Phase2DeepReviewHardeningTests.cs) — one per Rec, plus an extra calc-overflow case + a Dispose-idempotency case. Tests: **3229 unit / 3355 solution-wide passing** (+9 unit / +9 solution-wide over the previous 3220/3346 baseline). AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green. Active-task pointer remains **Phase 3 — Fragmentainer-aware layout + pagination**.

Phase 2 Task 19 hardening review pass shipped — addressed all 5 review recommendations: (1) [BLOCKER] Made [`ComputedStyleTests.Dispose_then_post_dispose_access_throws`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Css/ComputedValues/ComputedStyleTests.cs) deterministic by adding a test-only `internal static ComputedStyle.RentForExclusiveTesting()` factory that bypasses the production pool. The flake reproduces under xUnit's parallel runner: another test class's `ComputedStyle.Rent()` can race the just-disposed instance from the `ConcurrentBag`, call `Reset()` (which flips `_disposed = false`), and silently neutralize the assertion. The production soft-guard contract documents this race as best-effort by design — the test only needs to verify the soft guard fires when no re-rent occurs. The fix adds a `_excludedFromPool` flag set by the test-only factory; `Dispose()` checks it + skips the `_pool.Add(this)` call, so the disposed flag stays observably true regardless of concurrent rent activity. Verified deterministic across 3 full-suite runs (3220/3346 each). (2) [BLOCKER] 100 KB invoice perf criterion documented honestly. The exit-criterion (`< 50 ms p50`) is not satisfied — measured p50 (extracted from BDN's `*-report-full-compressed.json`) is **51.4 ms** (~2.8% over target). CHANGELOG now lists explicit p25 / p50 / p75 / mean instead of just mean ± error. The criterion is **borderline-waived** for ship: cycle-1 prioritizes correctness over perf; the 100 KB synthetic stresses cascade matching at ~3700 elements (O(rules × elements) hot path); Phase 3 layout/paint will dominate total convert wall-clock anyway (Phase 2 pipeline becomes ~1% once fragmentainer-aware layout lands). Deferring optimization until Phase 3+5 lets us set the perf budget against rendering-bound measurements rather than synthetic-bound ones. Phase 2 doc exit-criterion checkbox updated from ✅ to ⚠️ with waiver rationale. (3) [BLOCKER] [`README.md`](README.md) updated to reflect Phase 2's actual scope: status banner now reads "Phase 1 ✅ + Phase 2 ✅ (pending tag)"; the "every overload throws NotImplementedException" warning correctly cites `0.3.0-alpha` (was `0.1.0-alpha`) and notes that the throws stay until Phase 5 wires the facade (was claimed to land in Phase 2); code samples corrected from `// works at 0.3.0-alpha+` to `// still throws at 0.3.0-alpha; wired at v1.0`; the "What's actually shipped" capability table renamed from "at 0.1.0-alpha" to "at 0.3.0-alpha" with new rows for the Phase 2 surface (HTML parsing host, CSS cascade + var/calc subset contract, box-tree generation, semantic-tree generation, diagnostics emission); the public-facade row clarifies "Phase 5 wires the facade through Phase 2 + 3 + 4". (4) [BLOCKER] CHANGELOG release marker reframed: section header changed from `## [0.3.0-alpha] — 2026-05-07` (implies released) to `## [0.3.0-alpha] — staged for 2026-05-07 (tag pending PR merge)`; the `[Unreleased]` section gains an explanatory paragraph "treat the section as the staged contents of the next release"; the `[Unreleased]` compare-link now points to `0.1.0-alpha...HEAD` (was prematurely `0.3.0-alpha...HEAD`). Maintainer creates the actual `git tag 0.3.0-alpha` after PR merge. (5) [BLOCKER] Aligned CHANGELOG technical claims with implementation. Three corrections: (a) ComputedStyle is a `sealed class` (NOT a struct) holding `[InlineArray]`-backed inline buffers; pooled via a process-wide `ConcurrentBag<ComputedStyle>` (NOT `ArrayPool<T>`); `Rent()` clears via `Reset()` on take, `Dispose()` returns to the bag with a soft-guard `_disposed` flag. (b) `calc` resolver subset contract spelled out: absolute lengths/percentages/angles/times/frequencies/resolutions reduce; font-relative + viewport-relative + container-relative units **defer** to Phase 3's typed-value pipeline; mixed-unit-across-incompatible-dimensions also defers. Length resolver section parallel-corrected — `em`/`rem`/`vh`/`vw`/`vmin`/`vmax` etc. are NOT in the supported-units list; deferred to Phase 3. (c) `:has()` corrected from "parsed + matches" to "parsed + bytecode-flagged; matcher always returns false at runtime in v1 + emits CSS-HAS-RENDERING-NOT-IMPLEMENTED-001 once per flagged sub-group" — the previous wording suggested `:has()` actually matched, when in v1 it deterministically does not. Tests: **3220 unit / 3346 solution-wide passing** (unchanged — Task 19 hardening updates docs + the test-only Rent path; no production-test count impact). AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green across 3 full-suite runs. Active-task pointer remains **Phase 3 — Fragmentainer-aware layout + pagination**.

Phase 2 Task 18 hardening 2 review pass shipped — addressed all 4 review recommendations: (1) [P2] Unified diagnostics capture via the public [`IDiagnosticsSink`](src/NetPdf/Diagnostics/IDiagnosticsSink.cs) so HTML-stage diagnostics land in snapshots alongside CSS-stage. Cycle 1 captured only the internal `ICssDiagnosticsSink`, leaving `HTML-SCRIPT-IGNORED-001` and `HTML-JAVASCRIPT-URL-IGNORED-001` invisible to the snapshot framework. [`SnapshotTests.RunPipelineAsync`](tests/NetPdf.LayoutSnapshots/SnapshotTests.cs) now constructs `new HtmlPdfOptions { Diagnostics = sink }` + lets `Phase2Pipeline.RunFromHtmlAsync` auto-wire `PublicDiagnosticsSinkAdapter.ForOptions(options)` (per Task 17 hardening Rec 4) — the public sink receives both HTML diagnostics directly from `HtmlParsingHost` + CSS diagnostics adapted from `ICssDiagnosticsSink`. [`DiagnosticsSerializer`](tests/NetPdf.LayoutSnapshots/Serialization/DiagnosticsSerializer.cs) was rewritten to take `IReadOnlyList<NetPdf.Diagnostic>` (public type) instead of `IReadOnlyList<CssDiagnostic>` (internal) — the type change keeps the interface natural for callers + matches what production consumers see. New 9th fixture [`09-script-and-javascript-urls`](tests/NetPdf.LayoutSnapshots/Fixtures/09-script-and-javascript-urls/) exercises the HTML diagnostics path: a `<script>alert('x')</script>` element + an `<a href="javascript:doBad()">` link both emit Warnings (`HTML-SCRIPT-IGNORED-001` + `HTML-JAVASCRIPT-URL-IGNORED-001`) end-to-end via the production pipeline, while a sibling `<a href="https://example.com">` survives intact (proves the strip is targeted, not blanket). The semantic-tree golden also captures the 3-state semantic outcome: `<script>` removed entirely (no node), `<a>` with stripped href becomes transparent (an `InlineText "click"` flows up to its parent), `<a>` with safe href emits `Link @href="https://example.com"`. (2) [P2] Source locations now appear in diagnostic snapshots. Previous format `{Code}\t{Severity}\t{Message}` lost regression-detection on, e.g., a CSS-PROPERTY-VALUE-INVALID-001 that started reporting wrong source lines. New format `{Code}\t{Severity}\t{Location}\t{Message}` with three formats for the location field: `<unknown>` for `SourceLocation.Unknown` (today's typical state for CSS-stage until Task 3 wires real positions — explicit placeholder is more honest than a silent `0:0` that would change meaning when Task 3 lands); `<inline>:Line:Column` for HTML diagnostics on documents parsed without a BaseUri (every snapshot fixture, since file-pathed BaseUris would break CI portability); `{File}:Line:Column` verbatim when a real File is set. The format documents the expected snapshot author practice ("BaseUri stays unset for snapshot fixtures"). Fixture 09's diagnostics correctly carry `<inline>:1:28` (script position) + `<inline>:1:82` (javascript: link position) from AngleSharp's `IsKeepingSourceReferences` mode; fixture 08's modern-color diagnostic now carries `<inline>:1:37` from `CssPreprocessor`'s recovery path while the counter() + replaced-pseudo entries still emit `<unknown>` (Task 3 territory). (3) [P2] Codified the v1 semantic-tree policy on generated content. The `05-pseudo-with-attr` box snapshot DOES carry the `"[WIDGET] "` generated text (BoxBuilder materializes it from the cascade), but the semantic snapshot does NOT (SemanticTreeBuilder walks the static DOM, not the rendered box tree — Task 15 cycle 1 deferral Rec 4). The reviewer flagged the gap as ambiguous: drift vs. intent. The hardening adds explicit policy statement to [`SemanticTreeBuilder`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Semantic/SemanticTreeBuilder.cs)'s XML doc — generated text is intentionally absent in v1, with the v1.1 PDF/UA pass routing `::marker` content to `InlineText` (informational) and `::before`/`::after` to either `InlineText` (when carrying `attr()`/`counter()` substitution) or `/Artifact` (purely decorative) per WCAG 1.1.1 + the rendered-tree-driven rebuild. New `PseudoWithAttr_generated_text_is_absent_from_semantic_tree_until_phase_5_pdfua` Fact pins the current state explicitly: the box tree's `::before`/`::after` `InlineBox` carries `"[WIDGET] "` and `"."` text on its TextRun children, while the semantic tree's `AggregateText` reads only `"item description"` (no `[WIDGET]`, no `.`). When Phase 5 changes the policy, the named-test failure tells the future author "you're crossing an intentional v1 boundary" rather than the snapshot drift looking like an accidental regression. (4) [P3] Narrowed `.gitignore` Finder-duplicate patterns from `* [0-9].*` (any extension) to source-shaped extensions only: `*.cs` + `*.csproj` + `*.props` + `*.targets` + `*.json`. Legitimate numbered docs/fixtures/assets (`Sample 2.html`, `screenshot 3.png`, `notes 4.md`) are now tracked normally — verified by creating `tests/sample 2.html` + `tests/notes 3.md` + `tests/asset 5.png` and seeing all three in `git status`, while `tests/cs-dup 2.cs` is correctly ignored. Comment in `.gitignore` documents the `git add -f path/to/file` escape hatch for legitimate numbered source files (rare but possible — e.g., a deliberate partial class file split). Phase 2 Task 18 cycle 1 shipped — layout snapshot test infrastructure. New test project [`NetPdf.LayoutSnapshots`](tests/NetPdf.LayoutSnapshots/) gains three pieces of machinery and 7 golden-file fixtures so future Phase 2 / Phase 3 changes that reshape the box or semantic trees fail loud instead of silently regressing. (a) Deterministic serializers: [`BoxTreeSerializer`](tests/NetPdf.LayoutSnapshots/Serialization/BoxTreeSerializer.cs) walks `Box` trees emitting `{indent}{Kind}{source-tag?}{pseudo-tag?}{text?}` lines with 2-space indent — `BlockContainer @element=p`, `TextRun @element=p "Hello world."`, `Marker @element=li ::marker`, `InlineReplacedElement @element=img`; escapes `\\` `\"` `\n` `\r` `\t` in TextRun text. [`SemanticTreeSerializer`](tests/NetPdf.LayoutSnapshots/Serialization/SemanticTreeSerializer.cs) mirrors the format for `SemanticNode` trees with extra metadata tags `@href` (Link), `@alt=<missing>/<decorative>/"value"` tri-state (Image/Figure per Task 15 Rec 6), `@rowspan`/`@colspan`/`@scope`/`@headers`/`@abbr` (TableCell/TableHeaderCell per Task 15 Rec 5). Both are AOT-clean (no reflection, no LINQ in serialization paths), Span-friendly, and identical-by-bytes across runs. (b) Golden-file comparison: [`SnapshotAssert.MatchesFile(actual, snapshotRelativePath)`](tests/NetPdf.LayoutSnapshots/Serialization/SnapshotAssert.cs) reads the snapshot from `Fixtures/<name>/box-tree.txt` (or `semantic-tree.txt`), normalizes line endings, and throws an `XunitException` with a unified-diff-style report on mismatch (first-divergence + 9 more lines of context, capped at 10 to keep failure output readable). The `NETPDF_UPDATE_SNAPSHOTS=1` (or `=true`) environment variable flips to update mode — writes `actual` to the source-tree fixture instead of comparing. Source-tree path resolution walks up from `AppContext.BaseDirectory` until it finds the `NetPdf.slnx` repo root marker, then descends into `tests/NetPdf.LayoutSnapshots/Fixtures/<...>` so update mode writes the source tree, not the bin/ output. First-run bootstrap behavior: when a fixture file doesn't exist, the helper writes the initial snapshot to the source tree AND fails the test (avoids the silent-green-on-no-snapshot trap). (c) Theory driver: [`SnapshotTests`](tests/NetPdf.LayoutSnapshots/SnapshotTests.cs) runs both serializers against every fixture: `BoxTree_matches_snapshot(fixtureName)` × 7, `SemanticTree_matches_snapshot(fixtureName)` × 7. Each test parses `Fixtures/<name>/input.html`, runs the full Phase 2 pipeline via [`Phase2Pipeline.RunFromHtmlAsync(html, new HtmlPdfOptions())`](src/NetPdf/Phase2/Phase2Pipeline.cs), serializes both trees, and asserts against the goldens. The 7 fixtures cover the principal Phase 2 surface area: `01-simple-paragraph` (`<p>Hello world.</p>` smoke); `02-list-with-markers` (ordered list with 3 items, decimal markers from Task 14); `03-table-with-caption` (table fixup wrapper+grid pair from Task 13, caption preservation, scope+colspan); `04-var-and-calc` (`:root { --base: 8px; --doubled: calc(var(--base) * 2); }` chain from Tasks 8/9); `05-pseudo-with-attr` (`.label::before { content: "[" attr(data-tag) "] "; }` covering Task 14 multi-string-concat + attr() substitution); `06-hidden-and-aria` (display:none + aria-hidden="true" + visible content covering Task 15 Rec 1 hidden filtering); `07-figure-with-img` (figure+figcaption + alt="" decorative + missing alt covering Task 15 Rec 6 alt tri-state). The csproj gains `NetPdf.Css` project ref + `<None Include="Fixtures\**\*.*" CopyToOutputDirectory="PreserveNewest" />` so goldens are co-located with the test binary at runtime. Replaces the original `PhaseZeroSmoke.Solution_Compiles` placeholder. Cycle-1 deferrals: snapshot doesn't yet capture computed-style fields (deferred until Phase 3 layout actually consumes them — capturing them now would lock in cycle-1 internals), pagination output (Phase 3 cost-model owns that), or paint display-list (Phase 4). New tests: **+14 snapshot** in [`NetPdf.LayoutSnapshots`](tests/NetPdf.LayoutSnapshots/SnapshotTests.cs) (7 fixtures × 2 trees). Tests: **3220 unit / 3330 solution-wide passing** (+13 over Task 17 hardening's 3220/3317 — the new project's `PhaseZeroSmoke` placeholder is replaced by 14 theory cases, net +13). AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green. Active-task pointer flipped to **Task 19 — Phase 2 release prep**.

Phase 2 Task 17 hardening review pass shipped — addressed all 6 review recommendations: (1) [P1] Diagnostics sink now threaded through every stage. [`Phase2Pipeline.Run`](src/NetPdf/Phase2/Phase2Pipeline.cs) forwards the supplied `ICssDiagnosticsSink` to `CascadeResolver.Resolve` + `VarResolver.Resolve` in addition to `BoxBuilder.Build`. Cycle 1 only forwarded to BoxBuilder, losing `CSS-CONTAINER-QUERY-UNSUPPORTED-001` / `CSS-AT-RULE-UNKNOWN-001` / `CSS-HAS-RENDERING-NOT-IMPLEMENTED-001` / `CSS-PARSE-WARNING-001` (cascade-emitted) and `CSS-VAR-CIRCULAR-001` / `CSS-VAR-EXPANSION-LIMIT-001` / `CSS-CALC-INVALID-001` / `CSS-CALC-DIV-BY-ZERO-001` (var-resolver-emitted). All now reach the supplied sink. (2) [P1] `CssMediaContext` is now built from `HtmlPdfOptions` instead of the hardcoded `DefaultPrint`. New `BuildMediaContext(options)` helper maps `HtmlPdfOptions.MediaType` (Print/Screen) to the lower-cased media string and projects the viewport from `HtmlPdfOptions.PageSize` (WidthPx + HeightPx). DevicePixelRatio + PreferredColorScheme stay at their defaults until `HtmlPdfOptions` grows matching options (post-v1). Authors who pass `MediaType = Screen` or non-default `PageSize` (Letter / Tabloid / etc.) now get correct `@media`-query evaluation against their actual viewport. (3) [P1] Stylesheet media + disabled metadata preserved per HTML5 §4.2.6. `ExtractStylesheets` now reads each owner element's `media` attribute (authoritative for inline `<style>`) and falls back to `rawSheet.Media.MediaText` when missing (covers `<link>` sheets where AngleSharp populates Media from the link's media attribute). The `IsDisabled` state from `rawSheet.IsDisabled` is also propagated. Cycle 1 hardcoded `mediaQuery: null, isDisabled: false`, so `<style media="screen">` rules applied during print. (4) [P2] New [`PublicDiagnosticsSinkAdapter`](src/NetPdf/Diagnostics/PublicDiagnosticsSinkAdapter.cs) wraps the public `IDiagnosticsSink` as the internal `ICssDiagnosticsSink`, converting each `CssDiagnostic` into the public `Diagnostic` shape (severity 1:1, `CssSourceLocation` → `SourceLocation`). The adapter sits in the facade assembly where both types are visible (NetPdf.Css can't reference NetPdf without a project-cycle). New `ForOptions(options)` static returns null when `HtmlPdfOptions.Diagnostics` is null so downstream stages fast-skip emission. `RunFromHtmlAsync` auto-wires the adapter when no explicit sink is supplied — a single public sink now collects HTML + CSS + layout diagnostics. (5) [P2] `CancellationToken` honored at every stage boundary. New `cancellationToken` parameter on `Run(...)` calls `ThrowIfCancellationRequested()` after parsing + before each of CascadeResolver / VarResolver / BoxBuilder / SemanticTreeBuilder. Pre-cancelled tokens throw immediately. (Stage internals don't yet support cancellation, but stage boundaries are now responsive.) (6) [P2] Owner-node-based stylesheet pairing replaces ordinal-index pairing. `ExtractStylesheets` now reads each `ICssStyleSheet.OwnerNode` to associate the sheet with its `<style>` element directly. Cycle 1's `QuerySelectorAll("style")[styleIdx]` matched by ordinal which silently corrupted when disabled / external `<link>` sheets entered `document.StyleSheets`. New tests: **+14 integration** in [`Phase2HardeningTests`](tests/NetPdf.RealDocuments/Phase2/Phase2HardeningTests.cs) — 3 sink-threading tests (cascade `@container`, var() circular, `:has()`); 4 media-context-from-options tests (print vs screen via `@media print`/`@media screen`, A4 viewport gates `min-width:1000px`, Tabloid passes `min-width:1000px`); 2 media-attribute tests (`<style media="screen">` skipped during print, `<style media="print">` applied during print); 3 adapter tests (public sink receives CSS diagnostics through adapter, severity + location conversion correctness, `ForOptions` returns null for missing sink); 1 cancellation test (pre-cancelled token throws OperationCanceledException); 1 owner-node multi-style-elements test pinning that media metadata is correctly paired across 3 sheets. Tests: **3220 unit / 3317 solution-wide passing** (+14 RealDocs over Task 17 cycle 1's 3220/3303). AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green. Active-task pointer remains **Task 18 — Layout snapshot test infrastructure**.

Phase 2 Task 17 cycle 1 shipped — HTML+CSS → BoxTree end-to-end integration tests. New [`Phase2Pipeline`](src/NetPdf/Phase2/Phase2Pipeline.cs) composition helper stitches every Phase 2 stage (`HtmlParsingHost` → `CssPreprocessor` → `CssParserAdapter` → `CascadeResolver` → `VarResolver` → `BoxBuilder` + `SemanticTreeBuilder`) behind two entry points: `RunFromHtmlAsync(html, options, sink)` for the test-friendly path that parses raw HTML; `Run(document, sheets, sink)` for callers that already have a parsed document. Returns a [`Phase2Result`](src/NetPdf/Phase2/Phase2Result.cs) record struct carrying the box tree, semantic tree, resolved cascade, and adapted stylesheets. This is the canonical pipeline composition the public `HtmlPdf.Convert` facade will eventually invoke (Phase 5 wires the public surface). New tests: **+30 integration** in two new test files: 15 in [`Phase2EndToEndTests`](tests/NetPdf.RealDocuments/Phase2/Phase2EndToEndTests.cs) covering all 4 corpus invoices (smoke + box/semantic-tree non-triviality), diagnostic budget on the classic invoice, cross-stage invariants (`display: none` filters both trees, `aria-hidden=\"true\"` filters semantic only, `var() → calc()` chain lands as 20px on the box, list-item marker numbering, replaced-element pseudo suppression with diagnostic, `attr()` substitution end-to-end, `hidden` attribute filtering, determinism across 3 runs (box-tree shape, semantic-tree shape, diagnostic count); 15 in [`Phase2CompositionTests`](tests/NetPdf.RealDocuments/Phase2/Phase2CompositionTests.cs) covering deeper compositions (3-level var() through calc() reduction, var-with-fallback, both `::before`+`::after` materializing with attr() substitution, content with `counter()` rejected via pipeline, modern color functions theory × 4 (oklch/oklab/color-mix/light-dark) emitting through preprocessor recovery → cascade → resolver, multi-arg attr() emitting through preprocessor recovery + content-list rejection, aria-hidden subtree-drops in semantic tree, `<style>` rule text doesn't leak into semantic InlineText, table wrapper+grid present in box tree end-to-end, `thead`/`tbody`/`tfoot` transparency in semantic tree, mixed `<li>` + `<div display:list-item>` numbering continuously per Task 14 review Rec 3, replaced-pseudo dedup across 5 imgs → 1 diagnostic). New helper `FindPrincipalBoxes(root, localName)` filters out TextRun children that inherit `SourceElement` from the parent inline (caught a bug in initial test draft where `WalkBoxes(...).Where(b => b.SourceElement?.LocalName == \"p\")` matched both the principal `<p>` box AND its TextRun children). External `<link rel=\"stylesheet\">` resource loading is disabled at the AngleSharp boundary; Phase 5 wires the resource pipeline. Phase 2 Task 16 hardening review pass shipped — addressed all 6 review recommendations: (1) [P1] Multi-arg `attr(name type, fallback)` reachable via production path. New `ContainsMultiArgAttr` + `IsAttrIdent` + `IsMultiArgAttrBlock` helpers in [`CssPreprocessor`](src/NetPdf.Css/Parser/Preprocessing/CssPreprocessor.cs) detect modern multi-arg attr() inside declaration values; the recovered raw text is merged over AngleSharp's normalized output by `CssParserAdapter`, so the cascade now delivers the original `attr(name type, fallback)` text to `CssContentList` which emits `CSS-ATTR-MULTI-ARG-UNSUPPORTED-001` end-to-end. Detection: any `,` inside the parens, OR whitespace-separated tokens after the first ident. Bare `attr(name)` doesn't trigger recovery (no need — AngleSharp passes it cleanly). (2) [P1] Modern color function handling unified per CSS Color L4 §6 + §10 + Color L5 §3 + §6. New shared [`ModernColorFunctions`](src/NetPdf.Css/ComputedValues/ModernColorFunctions.cs) `FrozenSet` becomes the single source of truth — `CssPreprocessor.ModernValueFunctions` aliases it; [`ColorResolver.TryParseFunctionalColor`](src/NetPdf.Css/ComputedValues/PropertyResolvers/ColorResolver.cs) consults it after the legacy `rgb`/`rgba`/`hsl`/`hsla` switch. The unified set: `oklch` / `oklab` / `lab` / `lch` / `color` / `color-mix` / `light-dark` — previously the preprocessor recovered 4 (`oklch`/`oklab`/`color-mix`/`light-dark`) while ColorResolver diagnosed 6 (everything except `light-dark`); the mismatch left `light-dark` with the wrong diagnostic (`CSS-PROPERTY-VALUE-INVALID-001` instead of `CSS-MODERN-COLOR-FUNCTION-UNSUPPORTED-001`) and `lab`/`lch`/`color()` without guaranteed raw-value recovery. (3) [P1] Marker fallback fix per CSS Pseudo L4 §3.4. New `MarkerContentResolution` enum (`AbsentOrNormal` / `Supported` / `Unsupported`) + `ResolveMarkerContent` helper replaces the old `MarkerContentFromCascade` so [`BuildListItemMarker`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Boxes/BoxBuilder.cs) distinguishes "no override" (fall back to list-style-type) from "unsupported override" (suppress the marker entirely after `CssContentList` emitted `CSS-CONTENT-FUNCTION-UNSUPPORTED-001`). Previously a `li::marker { content: counter(items) }` rule would render a default disc/decimal — a marker the author explicitly didn't request. Now the marker is suppressed (no glyph) once the cascade delivers the rule (currently blocked by AngleSharp.Css's `::marker` drop, so the forward-looking contract is documented + tested at the `CssContentList` layer). (4) [P2] `CSS-PSEUDO-SUPPRESSED-ON-REPLACED-001` deduped by (rule source location, pseudo name, element tag). New build-scoped `HashSet<string>` threaded through `Build` → `BuildElementBoxes` → `BuildPseudo` → `EmitPseudoSuppressedOnReplaced`. A 100-image page with `img::before { content: 'X' }` now emits 1 diagnostic instead of 100. Distinct (pseudo, tag) combinations still emit independently. When the source location is `Unknown` (synthesized CSS / tests) the dedup key falls back to (pseudo, tag) so emission is at most once per pseudo+tag. (5) [P2] `attr()` name validated as a CSS ident-token per CSS Syntax §4.3.11. New `IsCssIdentChar` + `IsValidCssIdentStart` helpers in `CssContentList`: ASCII subset for cycle 1 — start: letter / `_` / `-` followed by ident continuation; continuation: letter / digit / `-` / `_`. Punctuation like `attr(.foo)` / `attr(123abc)` / `attr(@bad)` / `attr(foo!bar)` / `attr(-)` now rejects the parse + emits `CSS-CONTENT-FUNCTION-UNSUPPORTED-001` instead of being treated as a missing-attribute (empty string). Escape decoding + non-ASCII identifier ranges defer to cycle 2 alongside the typed-value pipeline. (6) [P2] Production-path diagnostic tests added. New `Multi_arg_attr_in_pseudo_content_emits_via_production_path_per_Rec_1` test exercises HtmlParsingHost → CssPreprocessor → CssParserAdapter → CascadeResolver → VarResolver → BoxBuilder for multi-arg attr() (depended on Rec 1's recovery work); 4 new theory entries for `Modern_color_function_emits_via_production_path_per_Rec_2` cover oklch/oklab/color-mix/light-dark through the same pipeline (depended on Rec 2's unification work). New tests: **+17 unit** in [`BoxBuilderDiagnosticsTests`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Layout/Boxes/BoxBuilderDiagnosticsTests.cs) — 1 dedup test (broad selector × 5 imgs → 1 emission), 1 multi-pseudo-tag test (3 unique combinations → 3 emissions); 1 marker-content-unsupported test pinning `CssContentList` rejection behavior; 5 malformed-attr-name theory cases (Rec 5); 4 valid-attr-name theory cases (data-x / _x / --custom / my-attr); 1 multi-arg-attr-via-production-path test; 4 modern-color-via-production-path theory entries. Tests: **3220 unit / 3273 solution-wide passing** (+17 unit / +17 solution-wide over Task 16 cycle 1's 3203/3256). AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green. Active-task pointer remains **Task 17 — Integration test: HTML+CSS → BoxTree end-to-end**.

Phase 2 Task 16 cycle 1 shipped — diagnostics emission for unsupported / silently-dropped CSS features. Four new diagnostic codes registered in [`docs/diagnostics-codes.md`](docs/diagnostics-codes.md) + mirrored in [`src/NetPdf.Css/Diagnostics/CssDiagnosticCodes.cs`](src/NetPdf.Css/Diagnostics/CssDiagnosticCodes.cs) + [`src/NetPdf/Diagnostics/DiagnosticCodes.cs`](src/NetPdf/Diagnostics/DiagnosticCodes.cs): (1) `CSS-CONTENT-FUNCTION-UNSUPPORTED-001` (Warning) — `content:` value used a function/keyword cycle 1 doesn't yet handle (`counter()` / `counters()` / `url()` / `image()` / `image-set()` / `linear-gradient()` / `open-quote` / `close-quote` / `no-open-quote` / `no-close-quote`). [`CssContentList`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Boxes/CssContentList.cs) now takes an `ICssDiagnosticsSink` + `CssSourceLocation` (with a sink-less convenience overload preserved for non-emitting callers); rejected tokens emit the diagnostic naming the offending function/keyword + truncated value text. (2) `CSS-ATTR-MULTI-ARG-UNSUPPORTED-001` (Warning) — modern `attr(name type, fallback)` form rejected (per Task 14 review Rec 4); `ReadAttrArgs` returns a typed `AttrRejectReason` distinguishing multi-arg from malformed-syntax so the caller emits the right code. (3) `CSS-MODERN-COLOR-FUNCTION-UNSUPPORTED-001` (Info severity — distinguishes "known unsupported feature" from generic parse-error Warning) — [`ColorResolver`](src/NetPdf.Css/ComputedValues/PropertyResolvers/ColorResolver.cs) `TryParseFunctionalColor` now returns the lower-cased function name (`oklch` / `oklab` / `lab` / `lch` / `color` / `color-mix`) via a new `out string? modernColorFn` parameter so the dispatcher emits the dedicated code instead of `CSS-PROPERTY-VALUE-INVALID-001`. The pre-existing `Modern_color_functions_are_invalid_until_cycle_2` regression test was updated to assert the new code + Info severity. (4) `CSS-PSEUDO-SUPPRESSED-ON-REPLACED-001` (Info) — `::before` / `::after` rule on a replaced element (`<img>` / `<video>` / `<canvas>` / `<iframe>` / `<object>` / `<embed>`); per CSS Pseudo L4 §3 the pseudo-element is suppressed because replaced elements are atomic. New `EmitPseudoSuppressedOnReplaced` helper in `BoxBuilder` fires only when the cascade actually carried a rule for the pseudo (no noise on replaced elements without rules). [`BoxBuilder.BuildPseudo`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Boxes/BoxBuilder.cs) reorders the early-return so the rule-check happens before the suppression-return; both `::before` and `::after` rules emit independently. [`BoxBuilder.MarkerContentFromCascade`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Boxes/BoxBuilder.cs) now plumbs the sink + declaration source location through to `CssContentList.TryParse` so a `::marker { content: counter(...) }` rule (when AngleSharp.Css preserves it post cycle-2 recovery) emits the content-function-unsupported diagnostic with the correct location. New tests: **+35 unit** — 8 parity tests in [`DiagnosticCodesTests`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Diagnostics/DiagnosticCodesTests.cs) for the 4 new codes (registry-doc match + literal-stability pin); 27 emission tests in new [`BoxBuilderDiagnosticsTests`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Layout/Boxes/BoxBuilderDiagnosticsTests.cs) covering content-function rejection variants (counter/counters/url/open-quote/close-quote/no-open-quote), supported-content non-emission, multi-arg attr rejection (type-only / fallback-only / bare-success), modern color function emission for all 6 function names + standard rgb non-emission + Info severity vs invalid-color Warning differentiation, pseudo-suppressed-on-replaced theory across 6 replaced tags + non-replaced non-emission + replaced-without-rule non-emission + diagnostic-message inspection. Tests use direct `ColorResolver.Resolve` + `CssContentList.TryParse` calls for the modern-color + multi-arg-attr paths because AngleSharp.Css 1.0.0-beta.144 normalizes those tokens before they reach the cascade adapter. Cycle-1 deferrals (cycle 2 work alongside the box-tree-driven SemanticTreeBuilder rebuild + CssPreprocessor recovery): preprocessor-side declaration-dropped diagnostic; 3D transform projection emission; sideways writing-mode emission; subgrid + anchor positioning + sticky position emission. Tests: **3203 unit / 3256 solution-wide passing** (+35 unit / +35 solution-wide over the PR #10 base of 3168/3221). AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green. Active-task pointer flipped to **Task 17 — Integration test: HTML+CSS → BoxTree end-to-end**.

Phase 2 Task 15 hardening review pass shipped — addressed 7 of 8 review recommendations (Rec 4 is a documented cycle-2 deferral): (1) [P1] Hidden-element exclusion per Pseudo + ARIA + cascade. New `IsHidden` filter in [`SemanticTreeBuilder`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Semantic/SemanticTreeBuilder.cs) returns true for: HTML metadata-content elements (`head` / `title` / `style` / `script` / `link` / `meta` / `template` / `base` / `noscript` / `area` / `param` / `source` / `track`); the HTML5 `hidden` attribute; ARIA `aria-hidden="true"`; cascade-resolved `display: none` + `visibility: hidden` (when a `ResolvedCascadeResult` is supplied via the new optional `cascade` parameter on `Build`). Hidden elements + their entire subtrees emit no semantic nodes. Without this, Rec 3's new text-node walking would have leaked CSS rule text from `<style>` blocks as InlineText. (2) [P2] `<a>` without `href` is now transparent per HTML5 §4.6.1 — `MapElement` returns null when the href attribute is missing or empty, flattening the anchor's content into the parent. The previous null-Href Link emission pinned an invalid state. (3) [P2] Loose visible text in transparent containers preserved per Rec 3 — `CollectChildSemantics` now walks `element.ChildNodes` (not just `element.Children`) so text nodes directly under `<body>` / `<div>` / `<section>` become `SemanticKind.InlineText` spans. New whitespace policy: container kinds (Document / List / Table / sectioning) drop pure-whitespace text between structural children (just source indentation); text-leaf kinds (Heading / Paragraph / ListItem / cells) preserve boundary whitespace so word separation between adjacent inline runs survives concatenation. (5) [P2] Table-cell metadata captured per Rec 5. New [`TableCellMetadata`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Semantic/TableCellMetadata.cs) record struct (RowSpan / ColSpan / Scope / Headers / Abbr); attached to TableCell + TableHeaderCell `SemanticNode`s via the new `Cell` property. RowSpan + ColSpan parsed per HTML5 §4.9.10 (non-integer → fallback 1; values < 1 → clamp to 1). Computed header associations (HTML5 §4.9.12 walking the resolved row/column grid) deferred — Phase 3 layout owns that. (6) [P2] Image alt tri-state per Rec 6 + HTML5 §4.8.3. `ResolveAltText` distinguishes: missing alt + missing aria-label → `AltText = null`; explicit decorative `alt=""` → `AltText = ""` + new `HasExplicitDecorativeAlt = true` flag; non-empty alt → normalized accessible name; aria-label fallback when alt is missing entirely. Phase-5 paint can now emit `<img alt="">` as `/Artifact` per PDF/UA §7.1 vs flagging missing-alt as broken. (7) [P2] Aggregate-text replaced with interleaved InlineText spans per Rec 7. New `SemanticKind.InlineText` value; only InlineText nodes carry `Text`, every other kind has `Text = ""` and surfaces text via child InlineText spans interleaved with nested semantic structure. New `SemanticNode.AggregateText` derived property concatenates leaf InlineText `Text` depth-first for accessibility-name composition. The previous double-tagging where a paragraph and its child link both stored the link's text is eliminated. New `NormalizeInlineText` collapses internal whitespace runs but preserves boundary whitespace as a single space (so `"Hello "` + `<span>` + `"!"` reads as `"Hello world!"` after AggregateText concatenation). (8) [P2] `<pre>` + `<code>` preserve whitespace per Rec 8 — new `PreserveWhitespace` flag in `WalkContext` propagates from `<pre>`/`<code>` ancestors to their text-node descendants; `WalkText` takes raw text without `NormalizeInlineText` when the flag is set. The previous `NormalizeText` collapse misrendered preformatted code blocks as single-line text. Cycle-1 deferral: (4) [P2] Generated content bridging — `::before` / `::after` / `::marker` / list labels / `attr(data-...)` text rendered by `BoxBuilder` is absent from SemanticTreeBuilder. Bridging requires either input from the box tree or a duplicate cascade walk — deferred to cycle 2 alongside the rendered-tree-driven rebuild that would also strengthen Rec 1's cascade-aware skipping by switching the source of truth from the static DOM to the rendered BoxTree. The deferral is documented in the SemanticTreeBuilder XML doc. New tests: **+19 unit** in [`SemanticTreeBuilderTests`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Layout/Semantic/SemanticTreeBuilderTests.cs) covering each rec — table-cell metadata defaults / rowspan+colspan / scope+abbr / headers / invalid-attr clamping / non-cell null Cell; `<a>` href-less transparency + href emission; image alt with text / empty=decorative / missing=null / aria-label fallback / normalization / figure aria-label / figcaption fallback; loose text in transparent containers becomes InlineText; metadata text doesn't leak (style/script/title); cascade display:none + visibility:hidden exclusion; hidden attribute + aria-hidden=true + aria-hidden=false (kept); aria-hidden subtree fully excluded; pre/code preserve whitespace; paragraph normalizes whitespace differently; interleaved text+link children with no double-tagging. Refactored 17 existing tests from `node.Text` direct reads to `node.AggregateText` derivation + the InlineText interleaving model. Tests: **3167 unit / 3220 solution-wide passing** (+19 unit over Task 15 cycle 1's 3148/3201). AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green. Active-task pointer remains **Task 16 — Diagnostics emission for unsupported CSS features**.

Phase 2 Task 15 cycle 1 shipped — `SemanticTreeBuilder` parallel pass per the Phase 2 doc. Walks the styled DOM and emits a parallel tree of HTML semantic / accessibility roles for v1.1's PDF/UA tagged-PDF structure-tree emission. Three new files: [`src/NetPdf.Layout/Semantic/SemanticKind.cs`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Semantic/SemanticKind.cs) — byte enum with 26 values mirroring PDF/UA's standard structure types (Document, Heading1..Heading6, Paragraph, BlockQuote, Code, List, ListItem, Table + TableRow + TableHeaderCell + TableCell + TableCaption, Link, Image, Figure, FigureCaption, the seven HTML5 sectioning kinds Header / Footer / Nav / Main / Aside / Article / Section); [`src/NetPdf.Layout/Semantic/SemanticNode.cs`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Semantic/SemanticNode.cs) — sealed class with Kind / SourceElement / Href / AltText / Text / Children; [`src/NetPdf.Layout/Semantic/SemanticTreeBuilder.cs`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Semantic/SemanticTreeBuilder.cs) — static `Build(IDocument)` walker. Walk semantics: each child element is mapped to a SemanticKind via `MapElement`; recognized elements produce a node + recurse; unrecognized elements (`<div>` / `<span>` / `<thead>` / `<tbody>` / `<tfoot>` / `<html>` / `<head>` / `<body>` / etc.) are transparent — their children flatten into the parent's child list with no node of their own. Accessibility-name resolution per the Phase 2 doc + WAI-ARIA: `<img>` uses `alt` then `aria-label`; `<figure>` uses `aria-label` then child `<figcaption>` text. Whitespace normalization for accessibility-name strings — `NormalizeText` collapses whitespace runs to single spaces and trims. Text content captured on "leaf-ish" kinds (Heading1..6, Paragraph, BlockQuote, Code, ListItem, TableHeaderCell, TableCell, TableCaption, FigureCaption, Link); container kinds (Document, List, Table, Figure, Section family) carry only children. Cycle-1 documented limitations: subtree text is captured in full on each leaf node, so a `<p><a>link</a></p>` has the link's text in BOTH the paragraph's `Text` AND the nested Link node's `Text` — Phase 5 paint chooses the right granularity by traversing the tree depth-first; cycle 2 will interleave proper text spans with semantic children. Cycle-1 deferrals: ARIA `role="..."` overrides (cycle 2), form-control roles (Form/Field), MathML, SVG-figure metadata, RUBY (Ruby/RB/RT/RP), TOC hierarchy, the printer-mark roles. Tests: **+35 unit** in [`SemanticTreeBuilderTests`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Layout/Semantic/SemanticTreeBuilderTests.cs) covering each heading level (theory × 6), paragraph text normalization, container vs. leaf text capture distinction, ul/ol both → List, thead/tbody/tfoot transparency, table caption / th vs td, anchor with + without href, image alt → aria-label fallback chain, figure aria-label → figcaption fallback, all 7 HTML5 sectioning elements (theory × 7), div / span transparency, code + pre both → Code, blockquote text, document root invariants, empty HTML, nested H1/article/main structure, link inside paragraph (cycle-1 text overlap documented). **+4 corpus integration** in [`SemanticTreeCorpusTests`](tests/NetPdf.RealDocuments/Semantic/SemanticTreeCorpusTests.cs) — invoice corpus runs through HtmlParsingHost + SemanticTreeBuilder without throwing (theory × 2: classic-pure-css + anvil-running-elements); table rows + cells captured; metadata text doesn't leak (no @page / font-family in semantic tree text). Tests: **3148 unit / 3201 solution-wide passing** (+35 unit + 4 RealDocs over Task 14 hardening's 3113/3161). AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green. Active-task pointer flipped to **Task 16 — Diagnostics emission for unsupported CSS features**.

Phase 2 Task 14 hardening review pass shipped — addressed all 7 review recommendations: (1) [P1] `::before` / `::after` suppressed on replaced elements per CSS Pseudo L4 §3 — `BuildPseudo` early-returns when `HtmlReplacedElements.IsReplaced(host.LocalName)` is true; replaced elements are atomic (intrinsic content) and have no place to host generated content. The cycle-1 hardening test that verified `<img>::before` was routed to `InlineBox` is flipped to assert no pseudo box at all. (2) [P1] `::marker` content override per Pseudo L4 §3.4 — new `MarkerContentFromCascade` queries `markerRules.GetWinner("content")` + parses via `CssContentList`; falls back to the `list-style-type`-derived glyph when content is absent / `normal` / `none` / unsupported. AngleSharp.Css 1.0.0-beta.144 silently drops `::marker` selectors during parse (same class as `display: contents`), so the override path is unreachable in practice today — code is correct + becomes load-bearing once cycle 2's CssPreprocessor recovery preserves `::marker` rules. (3) [P1] List numbering counts `display: list-item` siblings, not just `<li>` per CSS Lists L3 — `ComputeListItemPosition` now takes the cascade and consults each sibling via new `IsListItemElement` helper (cascade rule wins; falls back to UA default for `<li>`). CSS-only authors who put `display: list-item` on a `<div>` get correct numbering. (4) [P2] Modern multi-arg `attr()` rejected per Task 14 review Rec 4 — `CssContentList.ReadAttrArgs` no longer silently strips `type` / `fallback` args + treats as bare `attr(name)`; it requires the close-paren immediately after the name (whitespace OK) and returns false otherwise so the entire content-list parse fails cleanly. Cycle 2 will deliver the typed-value pipeline + fallback handling for the modern form. (5) [P2] `::first-line` / `::first-letter` staging gated to block-container boxes per Pseudo L4 §3.2 / §3.3 — `StageFragmentPseudoStyles` early-returns when `!IsBlockContainer(box.Kind)`. Inline / replaced / table-internal boxes no longer rent + populate fragment-pseudo styles that would never be applied. (6) [P2] Author `::marker` properties filtered to the spec allowlist per Pseudo L4 §3.4 — new `ApplyMarkerApplicableDeclarations` + `MarkerApplicableProperties` allowlist (color / content / cursor / font-style / font-weight / letter-spacing / line-height / list-style-position / list-style-type) replaces the unfiltered `ApplyResolvedDeclarations` call in `BuildListItemMarker`. Arbitrary `display` / `margin-*` / `padding-*` / `background-*` / `position` declarations no longer leak into the marker box. (7) [P2] `lower-greek` properly implemented via new `ToGreek` + `GreekLowerSymbols` — bijective base-24 conversion with Greek alphabet symbols α β γ δ ε ζ η θ ι κ λ μ ν ξ ο π ρ σ τ υ φ χ ψ ω per CSS Counter Styles 3 §6 (final-sigma ς omitted since lists use the medial form). 1..24 → α..ω; 25 → αα; etc. Removed the silent disc fallback that misrendered authored `lower-greek`. New tests: **+20 unit** in [`BoxBuilderPseudoTests`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Layout/Boxes/BoxBuilderPseudoTests.cs) — 6 replaced-pseudo theory cases (img/video/iframe/canvas/object/embed all suppress before+after), 1 marker fallback (counter() unsupported → list-style-type), 1 CSS-only display:list-item div counted alongside `<li>` siblings, 3 first-line/first-letter staging gating tests (inline doesn't stage / replaced doesn't stage / block does), 3 marker property filter tests (padding doesn't leak / margin+display don't leak / font-weight applies via inheritance), 2 lower-greek tests (basic α/β/γ + wrap to αα at 25), 4 new in [`CssContentListTests`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Layout/Boxes/CssContentListTests.cs) for multi-arg attr() rejection (type-only / fallback-only / type+fallback / trailing-whitespace-still-works). 2 existing tests adjusted: `Pseudo_on_replaced_element` flipped from "becomes InlineBox" to "no pseudo box"; `Author_marker_rule_styles_apply_to_marker_box` rewritten to honestly test that color is inherited via anon style (the original test passed for the wrong reason — color was set via inheritance, not via cascade-delivered ::marker rule). Tests: **3113 unit / 3161 solution-wide passing** (+20 unit over Task 14 cycle 1's 3093/3141). AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green. Active-task pointer remains **Task 15 — `SemanticTreeBuilder` parallel pass**.

Phase 2 Task 14 cycle 1 shipped — pseudo-element materialization extensions: (a) `::marker` for list-items per CSS Lists L3 §3 + Pseudo L4 §3.4 — every `BoxKind.ListItem` gets a `BoxKind.Marker` child carrying the marker glyph; supports `disc` / `circle` / `square` (`•` / `◦` / `▪`) plus numeric `decimal` / `decimal-leading-zero` / `lower-roman` / `upper-roman` / `lower-alpha` / `upper-alpha` / `lower-latin` / `upper-latin`; `none` suppresses the marker; new `BuildListItemMarker` helper rents a fresh `ComputedStyle` (inherits from list-item, applies any `::marker` cascade rule); position counting walks parent's `<li>` children for 1-indexed sibling position. (b) UA default `list-style-type` lookup per HTML "Rendering" §15.3.4 — `ApplyDefaults` now skips `PropertyId.ListStyleType` (parallel to its `Display` skip); new `ReadListStyleType(style, element)` walks DOM ancestors when the cascade hasn't set it, returning `decimal` for `<ol>` ancestor / `disc` for `<ul>`/`<menu>` ancestor / `disc` otherwise — without this, `<ol><li>` would inherit the registry's `disc` default and number with bullets. (c) New `list-style-type` + `list-style-position` properties added to `properties.json` + their keyword tables registered in `KeywordResolver` (list-style-type covers the 12 cycle-1 named counter styles; list-style-position is `inside`/`outside`). (d) Extended `::before` / `::after` content parsing — new [`CssContentList`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Boxes/CssContentList.cs) helper handles multi-string concatenation (`"a" "b"` → `"ab"`) + `attr(name)` substitution against the host element (case-insensitive function name; missing attribute → empty string per Generated Content L3 §1.3); replaces the cycle-1 `CssStringParser.TryParseSingleString` call in `BuildPseudo`. (e) `::first-line` / `::first-letter` cascade staging — new nullable `Box.FirstLineStyle` / `Box.FirstLetterStyle` properties carry the resolved styles for Phase 3 line-layout to apply during fragment rendering; `StageFragmentPseudoStyles` queries the cascade for these pseudos on every element and rents + populates the styles when rules exist. Cycle-1 deferrals: `counter()` / `counters()` (needs `counter-reset` / `counter-increment` properties — cycle 2), `image()` / `url()` content (resource pipeline), `open-quote` / `close-quote` (needs quotation-stack with depth tracking + `quotes` property), `list-style-image`, `<ol start>` / `<li value>` attribute overrides, `lower-greek` (cycle 1 falls back to disc), modern multi-arg `attr(name type, fallback)` form (AngleSharp.Css 1.0.0-beta.144 normalizes the value before reaching the cascade). New tests: **+30 unit** — 18 in [`BoxBuilderPseudoTests`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Layout/Boxes/BoxBuilderPseudoTests.cs) covering disc / circle / square / decimal sequence / decimal-leading-zero / lower-alpha / upper-roman / list-style-type:none / `::marker` rule styling / multi-string concat / attr() substitution / missing-attr empty / strings-attr mix / regression for single-string / first-line staging / first-letter staging / no-rule null staging / first-line not a box; 12 in [`CssContentListTests`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Layout/Boxes/CssContentListTests.cs) covering single-string / multi-string / mixed-quotes / attr basic / attr-missing-empty / mix / counter-rejected / url-rejected / open-quote-rejected / empty-input / case-insensitive-attr / escape-decoding. **+2 corpus integration** in [`BoxBuilderCorpusTests`](tests/NetPdf.RealDocuments/Css/BoxBuilderCorpusTests.cs) — synthetic ordered list emits decimal markers in sequence, synthetic unordered list emits disc markers. Two existing hardening tests (`Pseudo_with_unsupported_content_form_emits_no_box`) had `attr(data-label)` and `"PRE" "POST"` removed from the unsupported theory data since cycle 1 now handles them. Tests: **3093 unit / 3141 solution-wide passing** (+30 unit + 2 RealDocs over Task 13 hardening's 3063/3109). AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green. Active-task pointer flipped to **Task 15 — `SemanticTreeBuilder` parallel pass**.

Phase 2 Task 13 hardening review pass shipped — addressed all 5 review recommendations: (1) [P1] Tree-wide orphan fixup pass per Tables L3 §3.1's "Generate Missing Parents" rule — new [`FixupOrphanedTableInternals`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Boxes/BoxBuilder.cs) walks the full tree post-`FixupTable` and wraps misparented table internals (loose `display: table-cell` outside any table, stray `<tr>` outside a row-group, etc.) in synthesized anonymous `Table` wrappers; consecutive orphans share one synthesized wrapper; orphan-runs broken by non-table siblings get separate wrappers; `FixupAnonymousBlocks` re-runs after wrapping in case the synthesized block-level Table introduced inline/block mixing; recursion descends into table internals' content (a `<td>` is a block container that may host further orphans) but skips orphan-checking for table-internal direct children that are already governed by `FixupTable` (avoiding double-restructuring). (2) [P1] Anonymous-box style isolation per CSS 2.1 §17.5.1 / Tables L3 §3.2 — new [`CreateAnonBoxStyle`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Boxes/BoxBuilder.cs) helper rents a fresh `ComputedStyle`, applies registry defaults (initial values for non-inheritable properties like `padding` / `border` / `background` / `display`), then overlays inheritable properties from the parent style; previously the `Box.Anonymous`/`NewAnonTablePart` calls reused the wrapper's style instance directly so wrapper backgrounds / borders / padding leaked onto every synthesized row-group / row / cell; now anon boxes inherit only inheritable properties (`color` / `font-family` / `line-height` propagate; `padding-top` / `border-width` / `background` reset to initial). Applied at every anon-box construction site in table fixup (TableGrid + anon row-groups + rows + cells synthesized at grid / row-group / row levels + the synthesized Table wrapper for orphans). (3) [P1] Replaced-element exception in [`DisplayMapper`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Boxes/DisplayMapper.cs) per Tables L3 §2 — a replaced element (`<img>` / `<video>` / `<canvas>` / `<iframe>` / `<object>` / `<embed>`) specifying a table-internal display value (`table-row` / `table-cell` / `table-column` / `table-caption` / any of the *-group variants) becomes `BoxKind.InlineReplacedElement`, NOT a structural table box; replaced elements are atomic and cannot host the structural roles those display values describe. New `IsTableInternalDisplay` helper centralizes the table-internal-value check. (4) [P2] Irrelevant child removal for `TableColumn` / `TableColumnGroup` per Tables L3 §3.1.4 — new [`DropIrrelevantColumnChildren`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Boxes/BoxBuilder.cs) called from `BuildElementBoxes` after children attach: `TableColumn` accepts no children at all (column is metadata-only — controls i'th column width/styling, no rendered content); `TableColumnGroup` keeps only `TableColumn` children. Stops authors' erroneous `<col>` / `<colgroup>` content (text, padding, nested elements) from leaking into rendered output. (5) [P2] Caption source-order preservation — new [`TableCaptionsSplit`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Boxes/BoxBuilder.cs) struct partitions captions by their position relative to the first non-caption internal: captions seen before any internal land before the synthesized grid, captions seen after at least one internal land after; previously all captions were forced before the grid regardless of source order, losing position info that the box-tree serialization / accessibility tree mapping rely on. Captions interleaved between internals join the after-grid bucket since they appeared after at least one internal. New tests: **+19 unit** in [`BoxBuilderTableFixupTests`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Layout/Boxes/BoxBuilderTableFixupTests.cs) — 6 for orphan fixup (loose cell / loose row / loose row-group / loose caption / consecutive coalescing / break by non-table sibling), 3 for anon style isolation (padding doesn't leak / non-inheritable resets / inheritable color propagates), 4 for replaced-element exception (img with table-cell / table-row / table-caption all become inline-replaced; div with table-cell still becomes TableCell), 2 for column child filtering (column drops all / column-group keeps only columns), 4 for caption order (before / after / both sides / multiple captions before). Tests: **3063 unit / 3109 solution-wide passing** (+19 unit / +19 solution-wide over Task 13 cycle 1's 3044/3090). AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green. Active-task pointer remains **Task 14 — Pseudo-element materialization**.

Phase 2 Task 13 cycle 1 shipped — table fixup in [`BoxBuilder`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Boxes/BoxBuilder.cs) per CSS Tables L3 §3 + §2.1: every `Table` / `InlineTable` wrapper now owns exactly one anonymous `TableGrid` child holding the row-groups (captions stay direct wrapper children so caption-side margins compose against the wrapper, not the grid). Anonymous box generation per §3.1.1–§3.1.2: bare `TableRow` children of a grid get wrapped in an anon `TableRowGroup`; bare `TableCell` children of a grid get wrapped in anon `TableRowGroup` → anon `TableRow`; bare `TableCell` children of an explicit row-group get wrapped in an anon `TableRow`; non-cell content inside any row gets wrapped in an anon `TableCell`; non-row content at grid level gets wrapped in anon `TableRowGroup` → anon `TableRow` → (anon `TableCell` for non-cells, real cells pass through). Whitespace-only `TextRun` children between table internals are stripped per §3.1 (without this, AngleSharp's preserved indentation between `<tr>`/`<td>` elements would become anonymous cells full of whitespace). Recursive fix into explicit row-groups + rows so their bare cells / non-cell content gets wrapped before grid-level fixup runs. New helper [`NewAnonTablePart`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Boxes/BoxBuilder.cs) creates anon table-internal boxes via the public constructor (the `Box.Anonymous` factory is restricted to always-anonymous kinds; table internals can be either source-backed or anonymous). New tests: **17 unit** in [`tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Layout/Boxes/BoxBuilderTableFixupTests.cs`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Layout/Boxes/BoxBuilderTableFixupTests.cs) covering wrapper/grid split, caption preservation, multiple captions, whitespace stripping, bare-row wrapping, bare-cell wrapping, non-cell wrapping in cells, consecutive bare-row coalescing, mixed bare-cell + bare-row sequences, thead/tbody/tfoot pass-through, nested tables, empty tables, caption-only tables. **2 corpus integration** tests added to [`tests/NetPdf.RealDocuments/Css/BoxBuilderCorpusTests.cs`](tests/NetPdf.RealDocuments/Css/BoxBuilderCorpusTests.cs) — the classic-pure-css invoice's table wrappers all own a `TableGrid` + no anon table-cells carry whitespace-only content. Cycle-1 deferral: loose `display: table-cell` outside any table ancestor (Tables L3 §3.1's misparent-up walk synthesizing the table+grid+row-group+row scaffolding) — would need a separate tree-walk pass since FixupTable is wrapper-rooted; defer to a later cycle. Two existing hardening tests (`Cycle1_table_produces_Table_kind_but_no_TableGrid_yet` + `Cycle1_inline_table_also_has_no_TableGrid`) have been flipped to `Task13_*` to assert TableGrid IS now present. Tests: **3044 unit / 3090 solution-wide passing** (+17 unit + +2 RealDocs over Task 12 hardening's 3027/3070). AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green. Active-task pointer flipped to **Task 14 — Pseudo-element materialization**.

Phase 2 Task 12 hardening review pass shipped — addressed all 9 hardening recommendations: (1) [P1] Added metadata-content `display: none` defaults to [`HtmlDefaultDisplay`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Boxes/HtmlDefaultDisplay.cs) (head/title/style/link/meta/template/script/base/noscript/area/param/source/track) per HTML "Rendering" §15.3.1 + §15.5.1 — without these defaults `<title>Invoice 123</title>`/`<style>p{...}</style>` text would have leaked into the box tree; (2) [P1] Fixed [`BoxBuilder.BuildPseudo`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Boxes/BoxBuilder.cs) — pseudo display now defaults to `inline` per CSS Pseudo L4 §3.1 (NOT to the host's UA default — `<div>::before` previously inherited `block` from div's UA default) AND the `DisplayMapper.Map` call passes `null` for the element name so `<img>::before` doesn't get classified as `InlineReplacedElement` (pseudo-elements are never replaced); (3) [P1] Added [`BoxKind.LineBreak`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Boxes/BoxKind.cs) for `<br>` per HTML "Rendering" §15.3.6 (UA stylesheet equivalent: `br { content: "\A"; white-space: pre-line }`) — modeling as its own kind preserves the line-break semantics for Phase 3 line layout; an empty `InlineBox` would silently disappear during line construction; (4) [P2] Added [`CssStringParser`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Boxes/CssStringParser.cs) — parses + decodes a single CSS `<string>` token per CSS Syntax 3 §4.3.5–§4.3.7 (hex escapes incl. line continuation + greedy hex consumption; proper handling of `\\`, `\"`, `\'`); BoxBuilder now silently skips pseudo-elements with non-string content (`counter()`/`attr()`/`url()`/`open-quote`/`close-quote`/multi-token) instead of rendering them as literal text; (5) [P2] Implemented `display: contents` per Display L3 §3.1.1 — `BuildElementBoxes` now returns `IReadOnlyList<Box>` (usually 1 item, empty for `display: none`, N items for `display: contents` after promoting children to grandparent); end-to-end testing deferred to cycle 2 because AngleSharp 1.0.0-beta.144 silently drops `display: contents` during CSS parse (cycle-2 CssPreprocessor work will preserve it); (6) [P2] Widened anonymous-block insertion fixup per Display L3 §2.1 + §3.1 — now triggers on `IsBlockContainer` (Root/BlockContainer/ListItem/AnonymousBlock + InlineBlockContainer + TableCell + TableCaption) instead of just `IsBlockLevel`, so `<span style="display:inline-block"><text><p>block</p><text></span>` correctly wraps the inline runs in `AnonymousBlock`s; (7) [P2] Added cycle-1 incomplete-table tests — verifies `<table>` produces `BoxKind.Table` wrapper but NO `TableGrid` intermediary yet (Tables L3 §2.1 wrapper + grid pair lands with Task 13); also verifies the HTML5-auto-inserted `<tbody>` is in the descendant chain; (8) [P2] BoxBuilder's `ApplyResolvedDeclarations` now passes `winner.OriginalDeclaration.Location` into `PropertyResolverDispatch.Resolve` so any emitted diagnostic keeps line/column origin (the values are `CssSourceLocation.Unknown` until Task 3 wires real positions, but the hookup is in place); (9) [P2] Added production-path corpus tests in [`tests/NetPdf.RealDocuments/Css/BoxBuilderCorpusTests.cs`](tests/NetPdf.RealDocuments/Css/BoxBuilderCorpusTests.cs) — every invoice runs through `HtmlParsingHost` → `CssPreprocessor` → `CssParserAdapter` → `CascadeResolver` → `VarResolver` → `BoxBuilder` without throwing + the classic invoice's metadata text doesn't leak into the box tree + diagnostic noise stays under 50 entries on known-good input. ## Phase 0 — Legal & architecture lock ✅ Complete

- **Tagged:** `0.0.1-phase0`
- **Completed:** 2026-05-01
- **Time:** ~1 day calendar (Claude Opus 4.7 high)

### What was done
Apache-2.0-licensed scaffolding established. 9 src + 11 test + 3 sample projects organized in `NetPdf.slnx` with central package management. Public API surface frozen (`HtmlPdf`, `HtmlPdfOptions`, `PdfRenderResult`, all interfaces). Governance docs in place: clean-room policy, dependency dossier, compatibility matrix, diagnostic codes registry, PDF spec notes. Per-phase execution guides under `docs/phases/`. Project-scoped skills under `.claude/skills/`. Test corpus seeded with 4 invoice samples (classic CSS, Tailwind CDN, responsive Tailwind, Anvil running-elements). NuGet ID `NetPdf` reserved on nuget.org via `0.0.1-phase0` placeholder (unlisted). `NUGET_API_KEY` set up as GitHub Actions repository secret. `CLAUDE.md` session-bootstrap added.

### What's next

## Phase 1 — PDF writer + text foundation ✅ Complete

- **Tagged:** `0.1.0-alpha`
- **Completed:** 2026-05-03
- **Time:** ~3 days calendar (Claude Opus 4.7 high; estimate was 4–6 weeks for solo dev — actual ~10× faster with daily Claude collaboration)
- **Doc:** [`docs/phases/phase-1-pdf-writer-and-text.md`](docs/phases/phase-1-pdf-writer-and-text.md)
- **CHANGELOG entry:** [CHANGELOG.md#010-alpha--2026-05-03](CHANGELOG.md)

### What was done
Programmatic PDF generation works end-to-end. NetPdf can produce well-formed, byte-deterministic PDF 1.7 bytes from internal `PdfDocument` calls — the byte writer, OpenType font subsetting + ToUnicode CMap, WOFF 1.0 / 2.0 decoders, JPEG / PNG / WebP / AVIF / GIF image embedders with content-hash dedup and indirect `/SMask` wiring, full Bidi (UAX #9) / Line break (UAX #14) / grapheme cluster (UAX #29) text shaping, the determinism harness with per-platform pin map, the AOT-clean native smoke binary with enforced JIT/AOT byte-parity gate, and the BenchmarkDotNet baseline with +25%-tolerance regression gate. Public `HtmlPdf.Convert(html)` still throws `NotImplementedException` — that wires up in Phase 2.

### Phase 1 exit criteria
1. ✅ All Phase 1 task tests pass — **1546 unit / 1557 solution-wide passing**.
2. ✅ UCD reference tests pass: UAX #9 **100%**, UAX #14 **99.952%**, UAX #29 grapheme stage **100%**.
3. ✅ Byte-determinism test passes — per-platform SHA-256 pin + 72 property tests.
4. ✅ AOT smoke publishes and runs successfully on `osx-arm64` with enforced JIT/AOT byte-identity gate. Linux + Windows pinned in Phase 5 CI matrix.
5. ✅ Programmatic `PdfDocument` construction produces valid PDF 1.7 bytes (verified via the AOT smoke output: 1791 bytes, opens in Acrobat / Firefox / Chrome / macOS Preview).
6. ⏸️ qpdf `--check` deferred to Phase 5 CI (qpdf not yet a local dev dep; Phase 5 wires it into the cross-platform validation matrix).
7. ✅ Roboto-Regular WOFF 2.0 loads, subsets, and embeds end-to-end.
8. ✅ Performance baseline meets target — 100-page < 500 ms target = 264.7 µs actual ≈ **~1,890× headroom**; memory linear at 2.46 KB/page across 4 orders of magnitude.
9. ✅ CHANGELOG updated, `0.1.0-alpha` tagged.

### What's next
Phase 2 — CSS engine + DOM pipeline. See [`docs/phases/phase-2-css-engine.md`](docs/phases/phase-2-css-engine.md).

### How to verify the Phase 1 baseline
```bash
# Solution-wide tests pass (1546 unit / 1557 total).
dotnet test NetPdf.slnx -c Release --nologo

# AOT smoke publishes and runs; native binary produces byte-identical output to JIT.
./scripts/aot-parity.sh

# Performance regression gate: full benchmark suite + +25% tolerance check.
./scripts/benchmark-gate.sh
```

### Subtasks completed

### Subtasks completed

- **Task 1 — PDF object model + `WriteTo`** ✅ (2026-05-01)
  - `PdfWriter` byte writer over `IBufferWriter<byte>` with cumulative position tracking, plus `Hex` helper.
  - `PdfObject` abstract base + 11 concrete types: `PdfBoolean`, `PdfNull`, `PdfInteger`, `PdfReal`, `PdfName`, `PdfLiteralString`, `PdfHexString`, `PdfArray`, `PdfDictionary`, `PdfStream`, `PdfIndirectRef`. All emit byte sequences conforming to ISO 32000-2:2020 §7.3.
  - `PdfNames` static class with ~85 pre-allocated standard names used throughout the rest of Phase 1+.
  - `PdfDictionary` uses .NET 10's `OrderedDictionary<TKey, TValue>` so insertion order is preserved → byte-deterministic output.
  - 85 unit tests covering primitives, name escaping, literal-string octal escapes, hex-string UTF-16BE-with-BOM, array/dictionary nesting, stream `/Length` auto-set, determinism property test.

- **Task 2 — Indirect-object store + xref table writer** ✅ (2026-05-01)
  - `IndirectObjectStore` — 1-based deterministic numbering, `Allocate`/`Add`/`Assign` for forward references, byte-offset recording, `ValidateAllAssigned` gate before emit.
  - `PdfDocumentWriter` — orchestrates header → indirect objects → xref → trailer → `startxref` → `%%EOF`. Header emits binary marker (4 bytes ≥ 0x80) per §7.5.2. xref entries are **exactly 20 bytes** including the 2-byte ` LF` terminator per §7.5.4. Trailer `/Size` auto-managed.
  - `Version` is a `string` property; facade translates the public `PdfVersion` enum at the API boundary.
  - 30 unit tests covering header/binary marker, all 5 PDF version strings, xref entry byte-exactness, xref offset correctness, `/Size`, `startxref`, EOF marker, determinism, minimal-valid-PDF end-to-end.

- **Hardening pass** ✅ (2026-05-01) — review-driven correctness reinforcement before Task 3.
  - `PdfFormat` constants (xref widths, byte-offset limit, generation max, binary-marker bytes, supported-versions allow-list) — connects emitted bytes to ISO 32000-2 sections explicitly.
  - `PdfObject.EnumerateChildren()` virtual + container overrides — lets graph operations walk the tree without subtype switches.
  - `PdfPreflightValidator` — single structural pass before write: version on allow-list, all refs assigned, `/Root` present + indirect + allocated + `/Catalog`-typed, every reachable indirect ref allocated (no dangling), every ref generation = 0.
  - `PdfIndirectRef.StoreId` — refs allocated by a store carry that store's id; `Assign` rejects synthetic and cross-store refs. Catches the silent-corruption risk of cross-document binding.
  - xref byte-offset limit enforced (`> 9_999_999_999` throws — files larger require xref streams).
  - Dropped unused `NetPdf.Paint` / `NetPdf.Text` / `SkiaSharp` refs from `NetPdf.Pdf.csproj`.
  - 25 new tests; total 141 unit / 152 solution-wide.

- **Task 3 — Trailer `/ID` from content SHA-256** ✅ (2026-05-01)
  - `PdfWriter` gains an optional `IncrementalHash` tee — every emitted byte is fed into the hash sink without buffering. `StopHashing()` detaches before the trailer (the trailer would otherwise self-reference).
  - `PdfDocumentWriter.WriteTo` auto-derives `/ID` when not user-set: SHA-256 of header + indirect objects + xref, first 16 bytes (the conventional 128-bit ID size per §14.4), encoded as `PdfHexString`. The `/ID` array contains the 16-byte digest twice (original-doc id + current-revision id, equal for fresh files).
  - User-provided `/ID` is preserved (writer skips auto-derivation when `Trailer.ContainsKey(/ID)` — pays no hash cost in that path).
  - 7 new tests including a strong correctness assertion that re-derives the hash externally (`SHA256.HashData(bytes[..trailerOffset])`) and compares against the emitted `/ID`. Determinism preserved end-to-end (identical input → identical hash → identical `/ID` → byte-equal output).

- **Post-Task-3 hardening pass** ✅ (2026-05-01) — second review-driven hardening round.
  - **Trailer-graph traversal**: preflight now walks the entire trailer dictionary, not just `/Root`. Catches dangling/foreign refs in `/Info`, `/Encrypt`, future trailer entries.
  - **Foreign-store ref rejection in preflight**: previously only `Assign()` rejected cross-store refs; refs embedded inside arrays/dictionaries could pass with in-range numbers. Validator now rejects `StoreId != 0 && StoreId != store.Id` everywhere.
  - **Path-tracking cycle detection**: switched from "visit-once-and-skip" to "ancestor-set-and-throw."
