### Subtasks completed

- **Task 1 — HTML parsing host (AngleSharp wireup, no scripting)** ✅ (2026-05-04)
  - `src/NetPdf/HtmlParsingHost.cs` — `internal sealed` host that parses HTML through an AngleSharp `IConfiguration` configured with `WithCss()` + `WithDefaultLoader(new LoaderOptions { IsResourceLoadingEnabled = false })`. JavaScript stays permanently off: no `IScripting` service, no `AngleSharp.Js` package reference anywhere in the dependency graph. The host registers a custom `IHtmlParser` constructed with `HtmlParserOptions { IsKeepingSourceReferences = true }` so post-parse DOM walks see populated `IElement.SourceReference` for diagnostic source-location reporting. AngleSharp DOM types stay strictly behind the `internal` boundary — the public 0.1.0-alpha facade is unchanged.
  - **`<script>` handling**: post-parse `QuerySelectorAll("script")` snapshot, then for each element emit `HTML-SCRIPT-IGNORED-001` (Warning) through `HtmlPdfOptions.Diagnostics` with the script's source line/column, and remove it from the DOM tree before returning. Matches the registry contract — *"the element was removed from the rendering tree"*. External `<script src="…">` is treated identically: never fetched, never executed, just diagnosed and stripped.
  - **`HtmlPdfOptions.BaseUri`**: forwarded to AngleSharp via `req.Address(baseUri.AbsoluteUri)`. When unset, `"about:blank"` is used so relative-URL resolution is well-defined for the future resource-loader stages but never reaches the network.
  - **`src/NetPdf/Diagnostics/DiagnosticCodes.cs` (new)**: first emit-side constants file. Houses `internal const string HtmlScriptIgnored001 = "HTML-SCRIPT-IGNORED-001"`. The constant value is parity-tested against the registry doc so a typo at any future emission site is caught immediately.
  - **Test plan honored** per the testing-discipline rule (unit + integration in the same PR):
    - Unit (`tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Css/HtmlParsingHostTests.cs`, 16 tests): simple-HTML round-trip; no-script no-diagnostic; single-script emits with the correct code/severity/message; script removal from tree; multi-script one-per-element; external-script with `src` attribute; head-located script; source-location populated when AngleSharp supplies it (graceful fallback to `SourceLocation.Unknown` when not); BaseUri applied to document.BaseUri; null BaseUri → `about:blank`; null sink doesn't throw on script presence; null html / null options reject; pre-cancelled token throws; malformed HTML survives via HTML5 recovery; deterministic across repeated parses.
    - Unit (`tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Diagnostics/DiagnosticCodesTests.cs`, 2 tests): registry-doc parity (constant matches the row in `docs/diagnostics-codes.md` for both code and severity); literal stability pin.
    - Integration (`tests/NetPdf.RealDocuments/Css/HtmlParsingHostCorpusTests.cs`, 9 tests): all 4 invoice corpus files parse without throwing (parameterized via `[Theory]`); `01-classic-pure-css.html` emits zero diagnostics; both Tailwind-CDN samples emit ≥ 1 `HTML-SCRIPT-IGNORED-001` and finish with an empty `<script>` set; `04-anvil-running-elements.html` parses cleanly with zero diagnostics; BaseUri propagates through a real corpus document.
  - **AngleSharp version note**: the Phase 2 doc snippet referenced `WithStandardLoader`, but AngleSharp 1.1.2 only exposes `WithDefaultLoader` (the `WithStandardLoader` extension is from a later AngleSharp.Io split). Switched the call accordingly; semantics are identical (resource loading is the controlling option).
  - Total tests: **1570 unit / 1590 solution-wide passing** (+18 unit + 9 integration over Phase 2 kickoff baseline of 1552 / 1563).

- **Task 1 review cycle 1 — JavaScript sanitization hardening, source-location contract, no-network gate** ✅ (2026-05-04) — first review-driven round on the new host.
  - **Source-location contract pinned**: the previous test accepted both populated and `Unknown` locations, hiding a regression risk on the *"with source location"* clause of `HTML-SCRIPT-IGNORED-001`. Replaced with three hard contracts: `Line`/`Column` are non-zero; the line number matches the authored 1-indexed position of the `<script>`'s `<` (verified at line 3 with leading filler); `Location.File` reflects `BaseUri.AbsoluteUri` when set and is `null` when unset.
  - **Explicit parser scripting flag** (HTML5 §13.2.5.4.7): added `IsScripting = false` to the registered `HtmlParserOptions`. AngleSharp's struct default is already `false`, so no behavior change today — but the explicit setting locks `<noscript>` content parsing as DOM (the no-JS fallback is what NetPdf renders) against any upstream default flip. Two new tests verify `<noscript><p id=fallback>` is queryable as a real `<p>` element and that `<noscript>` does not emit a diagnostic.
  - **`javascript:` URL stripping (new `HTML-JAVASCRIPT-URL-IGNORED-001`)**: `<a href>` / `<area href>` / SVG `<a xlink:href>` carrying a `javascript:` URL emit the new Warning code and have the attribute removed; the element + its text remain so the link text still renders into the PDF, but Phase 4 link emission has nothing to attach a clickable target to. Detection follows WHATWG URL §3.5: leading C0-control + space stripped, embedded tab/CR/LF/FF in the scheme tolerated, scheme matched case-insensitively. Other URL-bearing attributes (`src`, `action`, `formaction`, `cite`, `data`, `poster`) are intentionally not scanned — no Phase 1–4 emission consumer interprets them as actionable URLs, so stripping would add DOM churn for no security benefit. Event-handler attributes (`onclick`, `onload`, …) are likewise left in place: inert without a JS engine, no PDF reader can dispatch them. Both decisions are documented in the host's XML doc.
  - **No-network regression test**: a parse exercising `<link rel=stylesheet>`, `<style>@import>`, `<img src>`, `<script src>`, and `<iframe src>` against deliberately-bad host `nope.invalid` finishes in well under 1 second (a real DNS failure would take seconds) and `link.Sheet` remains `null`. Locks down `IsResourceLoadingEnabled = false` as an executable boundary, not just a configured option.
  - **CSS-ownership clarified**: code comment near `WithCss()` documents that AngleSharp.Css populates `document.StyleSheets` and Task 2's CSS adapter will consume that CSSOM (rather than re-parsing raw CSS text); AngleSharp.Css types must never leak past `NetPdf.Css.Parser`.
  - **`HtmlPdfOptions.Timeout` boundary documented**: XML remarks on `ParseAsync` explicitly state that the host honors only the `CancellationToken` it is handed; `Timeout` is composed at the public facade in Task 12+ via `CancellationTokenSource.CreateLinkedTokenSource`. Prevents future contributors from re-implementing Timeout enforcement at the wrong layer.
  - **Diagnostic registry parity**: extended `DiagnosticCodesTests` with two new tests covering `HTML-JAVASCRIPT-URL-IGNORED-001` — registry-doc parity (constant value + severity match the markdown row) and literal stability pin. The registry was updated alphabetically within the `HTML-*` section.
  - 31 new unit tests across `HtmlParsingHostTests` (16 javascript-URL + noscript + source-location + no-network) and `DiagnosticCodesTests` (2 new diagnostic-code tests); some are `[Theory]` rows expanded by xUnit into 8 + 9 cases for whitespace/case-insensitive variants and kept-URL counter-cases.
  - Total tests: **1601 unit / 1621 solution-wide passing** (+31 unit on top of Task 1's initial round).

- **Task 2 — CSS parser adapter (AngleSharp.Css → internal AST)** ✅ (2026-05-04)
  - **AST types** under `src/NetPdf.Css/Parser/`: `CssStylesheet` (top-level), `CssRule` (abstract base), `CssStyleRule` (selector + declarations), `CssAtRule` (name + prelude + declarations + child rules — covers both block-form `@media`/`@supports`/`@keyframes` and statement-form `@import`/`@charset`/`@namespace` in one shape), `CssDeclaration` (property + value + `!important`), `CssSelector` (raw text, structural placeholder for Task 6's compiled bytecode), `CssValue` (raw text, structural placeholder for Tasks 9–10's typed value tree). All `internal sealed record`s — public API surface unchanged.
  - **`CssParserAdapter`** static class that translates `ICssStyleSheet` → `CssStylesheet` via type-pattern dispatch over AngleSharp.Css's rule interfaces. Explicit cases for `ICssStyleRule`, `ICssMediaRule`, `ICssSupportsRule`, `ICssKeyframesRule`, `ICssKeyframeRule`, `ICssFontFaceRule`, `ICssPageRule`, `ICssMarginRule`, `ICssImportRule`, `ICssCharsetRule`, `ICssNamespaceRule`, plus a generic `ICssGroupingRule` fallback for grouping at-rules we don't yet have a special case for, plus an unknown-rule fallback that preserves the rule's `CssText` as a prelude for future diagnostic emission. The order of cases is locked: more-specific interfaces first (e.g., `ICssMediaRule` before `ICssGroupingRule`).
  - **Documented fidelity losses**: AngleSharp.Css normalizes during parsing — named colors expand to `rgba(r, g, b, a)`; shorthand declarations expand to longhands (`background: url('x') no-repeat` → 12 separate `background-*` declarations including `initial`-valued ones not in the source); whitespace around combinators is canonicalized (`.a > .b` → `.a>.b`). Cascade and computed-value stages already operate on longhands and normalized colors, so these are beneficial downstream. Documented `@page :first` selector-text loss in AngleSharp.Css 1.0.0-beta.144 — the `:first` pseudo-class is dropped by AngleSharp before reaching the CSSOM; flipping the assertion is gated on either an AngleSharp fix or Phase 2 Task 3's pre-pass tokenizer extracting it.
  - **No-leakage contract enforced**: a property-walker test (`Adapt_emitted_types_declare_no_anglesharp_property_types`) asserts that every public property on every emitted record (and their generic args) declares a non-AngleSharp type. The compile-time type system already enforces this, but the test makes the contract executable so a future accidental `object`-typed field or AngleSharp-typed return wouldn't slip through.
  - **Project wiring**: `tests/NetPdf.RealDocuments` gained a project ref to `src/NetPdf.Css` and a matching `InternalsVisibleTo` entry on `NetPdf.Css.csproj` so corpus integration tests can drive the adapter directly.
  - **Dual-layer tests** per the testing-discipline rule:
    - Unit (`tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Css/Parser/CssParserAdapterTests.cs`, 21 tests): `Adapt(null)` rejection; empty sheet; simple style rule selector + declaration round-trip with named-color normalization; compound selectors with combinators; `!important` flag; shorthand-to-longhands expansion (the pin); `@media` (simple + complex query) with prelude + child rules; `@supports` condition prelude; `@keyframes` name + keyframe-entry children; `@font-face` declarations through the `IEnumerable<ICssProperty>` path; `@page` declarations + named-page selector loss; `@import` with optional media; `@charset`; `@namespace` with + without prefix; source-order preservation across mixed top-level rules; deterministic across repeated calls (with structural rule comparator since records' Equals doesn't deep-compare list contents); no-leakage contract.
    - Integration (`tests/NetPdf.RealDocuments/Css/CssParserAdapterCorpusTests.cs`, 6 tests): all 4 invoice corpus stylesheets adapt without throwing and produce non-empty rules; classic-pure-css mixes style rules + `@page`; Anvil running-elements has multiple `<style>` blocks and the aggregated rule set still contains an adapted `@page` rule.
  - Total tests: **1622 unit / 1648 solution-wide passing** (+21 unit + 6 integration over Task 1 review cycle 1).

- **Task 2 review cycle 1 — stylesheet metadata, typed @import, inline style, AST immutability** ✅ (2026-05-04) — first review-driven round on the CSS adapter.
  - **Source-location scaffolding (Rec 6)**: new `CssSourceLocation(string? Source, int Line, int Column)` record struct with `Unknown` sentinel. Added `Location` field to `CssRule` (abstract base — every rule type inherits) and `CssDeclaration`. All current emitters set `Unknown`; Phase 2 Task 3's pre-pass tokenizer is the planned populator. Tracked as a Task 3 blocker in the active-task plan above.
  - **`ImmutableArray<T>` migration (Rec 7)**: `CssStylesheet.Rules`, `CssStyleRule.Declarations`, `CssAtRule.Declarations`/`ChildRules`, and the new `CssImportRule.ImportedRules` are now `ImmutableArray<T>` instead of `IReadOnlyList<T>`. Real immutability (can't be cast back to a mutable list), value-type allocation, and cascade caching wins. Important caveat captured in tests: `ImmutableArray<T>.Equals` compares the underlying array by **reference** identity, so records with `ImmutableArray<T>` fields still don't compare structurally — the determinism test uses `SequenceEqual`-style traversal.
  - **Stylesheet metadata (Rec 1)**: new fields on `CssStylesheet` — `Href`, `Origin` (`CssStylesheetOrigin` enum: `UserAgent`/`User`/`Author` per CSS Cascade L4 §6.1), `OwnerKind` (`CssStylesheetOwnerKind` enum: `Unknown`/`StyleElement`/`LinkElement`/`Imported`/`UserAgent`), `MediaQuery`, `IsDisabled`, `Order`. The cascade resolver in Task 7 needs every one. Two `Adapt` overloads: a defaults-only convenience (Author/Unknown/0) and a full-metadata version. The corpus integration test for the Anvil invoice's `<style media="print">` block exercises the metadata round-trip end-to-end.
  - **Typed `CssImportRule` (Rec 5)**: new sealed record subtype with `Url`, `MediaQuery`, `LayerName`, `SupportsCondition`, and `ImportedRules` (slot for ResourceLoader integration). The adapter dispatches `ICssImportRule` to `CssImportRule` instead of a stringly-typed `CssAtRule`. Caveat documented in the type's doc + a dedicated test: `LayerName` and `SupportsCondition` stay `null` until Task 3's pre-pass — AngleSharp.Css 1.0.0-beta.144 mangles `@import url(...) layer(name)` and `@import url(...) supports(...)` into a malformed `"not all"` media query before the CSSOM, so the only recovery path is reading the layer/supports clauses from the raw stylesheet text before AngleSharp parses the directive.
  - **`CssParserAdapter.AdaptInlineStyle` (Rec 2)**: new public method translating `ICssStyleDeclaration` (from `IElement.GetStyle()`) to `ImmutableArray<CssDeclaration>`. The cascade resolver (Task 7) walks the DOM and pulls inline styles at iteration time, keeping AngleSharp DOM types behind the `NetPdf.Css.Parser` boundary. Inline shorthands expand to longhands the same way stylesheet declarations do, so the cascade sees a uniform input shape. Corpus test exercises this against the Anvil invoice's many `style="…"` attributes.
  - **AngleSharp gap escalation (Recs 3, 4)**: `@page :first` selector loss and `@page` margin-box loss are now tracked as **named Task 3 blockers** in the active-task plan above. Two unit tests (`Adapt_page_rule_pseudo_selector_loss_is_a_known_task_3_blocker` / `Adapt_page_rule_margin_box_loss_is_a_known_task_3_blocker`) pin current behavior and reference Task 3's recovery plan. The adapter's `AdaptMarginRule` case stays in the dispatch as forward-compat; the case is dead today (AngleSharp never instantiates `ICssMarginRule`) but will catch margin-boxes as soon as Task 3's pre-pass synthesizes them.
  - **`CssParserAdapter` doc expanded** with the full AngleSharp limitations roster (3 named gaps, all linked to Task 3). The page rule's `AdaptPageRule` adapter has an inline comment summarizing the gap so future maintainers find it locally.
  - 11 new unit tests + 2 new integration tests (corpus metadata round-trip, corpus inline-style adaptation), plus updates to existing tests for the new shape (ImmutableArray APIs, `CssImportRule` dispatch, `ChildRules.Length` instead of `.Count`).
  - Total tests: **1633 unit / 1659 solution-wide passing** (+11 unit + 2 integration over Task 2's initial round).

- **Task 3 — Pre-pass CSS tokenizer + preprocessor (Task 2 review-cycle blocker recovery)** ✅ (2026-05-04)
  - **`CssTokenizer`** (`src/NetPdf.Css/Parser/Preprocessing/CssTokenizer.cs`) — minimal position-tracking tokenizer designed for the pre-pass, not a full CSS Syntax L3 token stream. `ref struct` over `ReadOnlySpan<char>` for stack residence + zero allocation. Operations: `PeekChar`/`ReadChar`/`PeekCharAt`, `SkipWhitespaceAndComments` (handles ASCII whitespace + `/* ... */`), `ReadAtKeyword`/`ReadIdentifier` (per a relaxed CSS Syntax L3 §4.3.11), `ReadParenthesizedBlock`/`ReadCurlyBlock` (balanced blocks respecting strings + nested same-kind blocks + comments), `ReadUntilAnyTopLevel(delimiters)` (skip-aware top-level read), `SkipString` (handles backslash escapes + bad-string per Syntax L3 §4.3.5), `SkipRule` (consumes statement-form `;` or block-form `{...}`). Position tracking via newline-counting; line + column 1-indexed. Documented non-goals: CSS escape sequences in identifiers, CDO/CDC tokens, full bad-string/bad-url recovery — added only when a real input demands.
  - **`CssPreprocessor`** (`src/NetPdf.Css/Parser/Preprocessing/CssPreprocessor.cs`) — single static `Process(string css, string? source = null) → CssPreprocessResult` walks raw CSS in source order and produces side-channel data the adapter merges with the AngleSharp-derived CSSOM. Closes all 4 review-cycle 1 blockers:
    1. **`@page` selector recovery**: `ParsePageRule` reads everything between `@page` and the opening `{` (or `;`) into the recovered selector; works for `:first` / `:left` / `:right` / named pages / unnamed pages.
    2. **`@page` margin-box recovery**: walks the page body looking for `@<box-name> { ... }` constructs; each becomes a `CssMarginBoxRecovery` with name + raw declaration text + position. Adapter then constructs `CssAtRule` entries via `BuildMarginBoxRules`/`ParseRawDeclarations` and attaches them as `ChildRules` on the owning `@page` rule.
    3. **`@import` modern syntax recovery**: `ParseImportRule` reads the URL (handles `url("…")`, `url('…')`, `url(...)`, plain `"..."`, `'...'`), then accepts `layer` / `layer(name)` / `supports(condition)` / media query in any order; populates `CssImportRuleRecovery.{Url, MediaQuery, LayerName, SupportsCondition}`. AngleSharp's mangled `"not all"` media query is bypassed entirely when the recovery is present.
    4. **Source positions**: `CssRuleSourcePosition` records line/column for every top-level rule indexed by ordinal. The adapter looks up by AngleSharp's emit order to backfill `CssRule.Location`.
    Robustness: never throws on malformed CSS — whatever it can't parse it skips, advancing past the next `;` or balanced `{...}`. AngleSharp is the canonical parser; the pre-pass only fills gaps.
  - **Recovery records** (`CssPageRuleRecovery`, `CssMarginBoxRecovery`, `CssImportRuleRecovery`, `CssRuleSourcePosition`, `CssPreprocessResult` with `Empty` sentinel) — all `internal sealed record`, `ImmutableArray<T>` for collections.
  - **`CssParserAdapter` integration**: new overload `Adapt(ICssStyleSheet sheet, CssPreprocessResult preprocess, …metadata)` accepts preprocess data and merges into the AST. Backward-compatible: original 7-arg overload now delegates to the new path with `CssPreprocessResult.Empty`. The merge logic uses ordinals — sees AngleSharp emit order, looks up corresponding recoveries by index. `CssPageRuleRecovery` populates `CssAtRule.Prelude` (selector) and `CssAtRule.ChildRules` (margin-boxes via the new `BuildMarginBoxRules` helper). `CssImportRuleRecovery` populates `CssImportRule.{Url, MediaQuery, LayerName, SupportsCondition}` directly. Every adapted rule's `Location` is now populated from the preprocess.
  - **`ParseRawDeclarations`** in the adapter: minimal `property: value [!important];` splitter for margin-box bodies. Uses the `CssTokenizer` for proper string + paren handling. Cascade resolver in Task 7 will be the canonical declaration parser once typed values land in Tasks 9–10; this is a stopgap that gives the cascade something walkable today.
  - **Modern syntax token capture deferred**: the Phase 2 doc Task 3 also called out `oklch()`/`color-mix()`/`light-dark()` and `@container`/`@layer` block-form. These are deferred to a Task 3 follow-up cycle because their consumers (typed value tree from Tasks 9–10, layer cascade from Task 7) don't exist yet — capturing tokens with no downstream consumer would be premature. The pre-pass shape supports adding capture passes later without redesign.
  - **Dual-layer tests** per the testing-discipline rule:
    - Unit (`tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Css/Parser/Preprocessing/CssTokenizerTests.cs`, 24 tests): every operation pinned — `IsEnd`, position tracking through newlines, `SkipWhitespaceAndComments` (including unterminated comment), `ReadIdentifier` (simple, dashed, underscored, non-identifier-start rejection), `ReadAtKeyword`, `ReadParenthesizedBlock` (simple, nested, string-with-unbalanced-paren), `ReadCurlyBlock` (simple, nested, string-with-unbalanced-curly), `ReadUntilAnyTopLevel` (delimiter, paren-skip, string-skip), `SkipString` with escaped quotes, `SkipRule` for statement vs block forms, `GetSubstring`.
    - Unit (`tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Css/Parser/Preprocessing/CssPreprocessorTests.cs`, 25 tests): null rejection, empty, whitespace-only; `@page` recovery for unnamed / `:first` / `:left` / `:right` / named; margin-box recovery for single, multiple, with-page-pseudo; `@import` recovery for plain, with-media, with-named-layer, with-anonymous-layer, with-supports, with-all-three, with-quoted-url; source-position recording across multi-rule input; ordinal indices zero-indexed per kind; robustness on unterminated block / unterminated string / unrelated at-rules / mixed inputs.
    - Integration (`tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Css/Parser/CssParserAdapterPreprocessTests.cs`, 10 tests): full pipeline (raw CSS → preprocessor + AngleSharp → adapter → AST). Every blocker has its end-to-end test pinning the recovered AST shape: `:first` page → prelude; named page → prelude; margin-boxes → `ChildRules` with parsed declarations; `@import layer(name)` → `LayerName`; `@import supports(...)` → `SupportsCondition`; combined layer + supports + media; rule `Location` backfill (every rule's `Line > 0`); empty preprocess fallback; original two-arg overload still works; mixed-rule-set preserves order + recovers everything in one pass.
    - Integration (`tests/NetPdf.RealDocuments/Css/CssParserAdapterCorpusTests.cs`, +1 test): the Anvil running-elements corpus invoice's `@page { @bottom-right { … } @bottom-left { … } }` margin-boxes are recovered through the preprocessor and surface as adapted `CssAtRule` entries on the `@page`'s `ChildRules`. Aggregated across all `<style>` blocks in the document for resilience to corpus reorganization.
  - Total tests: **1692 unit / 1721 solution-wide passing** (+59 unit + 1 integration over Task 2 review cycle 1).

- **Task 3 review cycle 1 — modern at-rule recovery, ordinal-drift fix, token-aware !important, margin-box allowlist** ✅ (2026-05-04) — review-driven hardening on the pre-pass tokenizer.
  - **AngleSharp probe escalation**: review pointed at modern-CSS deferral as P1; probing showed the gap is bigger than described. AngleSharp.Css 1.0.0-beta.144 silently DROPS `@container`, `@layer` block-form, and `@layer` statement-form ENTIRELY (the rules vanish from `ICssStyleSheet.Rules`). It also silently CORRUPTS `oklch(0.5 0.2 30)` → `rgba(9, 0, 0, 1)` and produces empty rule bodies for `color-mix()`/`light-dark()`. The ordinal-drift bug from Rec 2 was real and silently broken: my preprocessor walked 7 source rules but AngleSharp emitted 4, so source positions for normal rules following any modern at-rule pointed at the wrong line.
  - **Unified `RuleSlots` list (Rec 1 + Rec 2)**: replaced `CssPreprocessResult.RulePositions` with a typed `ImmutableArray<CssPreprocessRuleSlot>` ordered by source. Each entry is either `CssAngleSharpRuleSlot` (carries position; the next AngleSharp rule pairs here) or `CssOpaqueAtRuleSlot` (carries name + prelude + position; an at-rule AngleSharp drops, the adapter splices in directly). The preprocessor recognizes the at-keywords AngleSharp drops via a `FrozenSet<string>` allowlist (`"container"`, `"layer"`) and routes them to opaque slots. The adapter's new `AdaptTopLevelRules` walks the slot list — pairing AngleSharp emits sequentially via a cursor, splicing opaque slots inline. This makes the ordinal-drift fix and modern-at-rule capture the same change: modern at-rules become first-class entries in the AST (as `CssAtRule` with `Name = "container"` / `"layer"`, no children, no declarations — opaque pending Task 7's layer cascade and post-v1 container-queries).
  - **Token-aware `!important` recognition (Rec 5)**: the previous `EndsWith("!important")` check would falsely strip the marker from values like `content: "!important"` (the closing-quote bytes precede the literal `!important` text). New `StripTrailingImportant` walks the value text via `CssTokenizer`, skipping strings/comments/parens, and only strips `!important` when found at the value tail outside any token-respecting span. Pinned by an integration test in `CssParserAdapterPreprocessTests`.
  - **Margin-box name allowlist (Rec 6)**: `CssPreprocessor` now validates margin-box names against the 16-entry CSS Paged Media L3 §6.4 list (`top-left-corner`, `top-left`, `top-center`, …, `right-bottom`). Unknown names like `@top-bogus` are silently dropped (treated as malformed CSS) instead of becoming pseudo-margin-boxes. A `[Theory]` covering all 16 names round-trips the recovery; a separate test pins the unknown-name drop.
  - **Nested rule locations now correctly Unknown (Rec 3)**: the previous code threaded the top-level slot list down into `@media`/`@supports`/`@keyframes` child-rule adaptation, so child positions matched random top-level entries. Adapter now has a separate `AdaptNestedRules` path that uses no preprocess data — every nested rule's `Location` is `Unknown`. Recovering nested positions is a future Task 3 follow-up.
  - **Documented limitations (Recs 4 + 7)**: per-property declaration positions inside margin-boxes still resolve to the parent margin-box's location (the tokenizer tracks body-relative positions but converting to absolute requires offset bookkeeping the recovery records don't carry today; documented in `ParseRawDeclarations`). CSS escape sequences in identifiers (`\41 ` = "A") are pinned with a test that locks the current "pass-through verbatim" behavior; generated CSS rarely uses identifier escapes.
  - **Modern value functions still deferred**: `oklch()`/`color-mix()`/`light-dark()` are value-level constructs requiring per-declaration value-text re-parsing — that's plumbed into the typed value tree in Tasks 9–10. AngleSharp's silent corruption of `oklch` to wrong rgba is documented in PROGRESS.md as a Task 9–10 prerequisite.
  - **Adapter API changes**: the preprocess-aware `Adapt(sheet, preprocess, …)` overload now drives the slot-walking path; the simpler `Adapt(sheet, …metadata)` overload still works (delegates with `CssPreprocessResult.Empty` → falls back to AngleSharp-only walk with Unknown positions). Backward compatible.
  - 17 new unit tests (10 in `CssPreprocessorTests` covering modern at-rules, ordinal-drift, allowlist; 7 in `CssParserAdapterPreprocessTests` covering opaque-rule emission, drift fix end-to-end, token-aware !important, unknown margin-box, nested-Unknown). Some existing tests adjusted because `RulePositions` → `RuleSlots`. A `[Theory]` for the 16 spec margin-box names contributes 10 InlineData rows.
  - Total tests: **1716 unit / 1745 solution-wide passing** (+24 unit over Task 3's initial round).

- **Task 3 review cycle 2 — raw-value capture, robust slot merge, RawBody preservation, nested grouping recursion, comment-aware !important** ✅ (2026-05-04) — second-round hardening on the pre-pass tokenizer.
  - **Raw-value capture (Rec 1)** — new `CssDeclarationRecovery` + `CssStyleRuleRecovery` records. The preprocessor's `ScanForModernDeclarations` walks each rule body token-aware, detects calls to `oklch`/`oklab`/`color-mix`/`light-dark` (case-insensitive, outside strings/comments/parens via `ContainsModernValueFunction`), and records the authored property/value/`!important` triple. The adapter's `AdaptDeclarationsWithRecovery` merges: existing properties get their values overridden with the recovered raw text (closing the silent-corruption gap on `oklch`); recovery-only properties (the `color-mix`/`light-dark` case where AngleSharp produces an empty body) are appended. So a sheet that authored `.a { color: oklch(0.5 0.2 30) }` now adapts to a `CssDeclaration` with `Value.RawText = "oklch(0.5 0.2 30)"` instead of AngleSharp's bogus `rgba(9, 0, 0, 1)`. Tasks 9–10 will resolve the typed value from the preserved text.
  - **Robust slot merge (Recs 4 + 5)** — replaced `CssAngleSharpRuleSlot` / `CssOpaqueAtRuleSlot` with a single unified `CssRuleSlot` carrying `Kind` (`StyleRule` / `AtRule`), `AtKeyword`, `Prelude`, `RawBody`, and `NestedSlots`. Every top-level rule produces exactly one slot, regardless of whether AngleSharp will preserve or drop it. The adapter's `AdaptSlot` tentatively pairs each slot with AngleSharp's next emitted rule; if the rule kinds don't match (because AngleSharp dropped a previously-supported at-rule), the slot demotes to opaque and the AngleSharp cursor doesn't advance. This means future AngleSharp regressions that drop new rule types — beyond today's `@container` / `@layer` — won't reintroduce the ordinal-drift bug. The merge is sequential, single-pass, and never throws. The previous hard-coded `AngleSharpDroppedAtRules` allowlist still exists as a hint for the preprocessor's tracking of "expected drops" but isn't load-bearing for correctness.
  - **`RawBody` preservation (Rec 2)** — new field on `CssAtRule`. The preprocessor stashes the raw text inside `{...}` for at-rules whose body AngleSharp can't decompose (today: `@container`, `@layer` block-form, `@font-face` is also captured raw though AngleSharp handles it cleanly). The adapter copies `RawBody` through to the emitted `CssAtRule` so the cascade resolver in Task 7 can re-parse on demand without re-reading the source stylesheet. Statement-form `@layer name, name2;` has empty `RawBody`. Verified end-to-end: `@container (min-width: 800px) { .a { color: red } .b { color: blue } }` adapts to a `CssAtRule { Name = "container", Prelude = "(min-width: 800px)", RawBody = ".a { color: red } .b { color: blue }" }`.
  - **Nested modern at-rule recovery (Rec 3)** — preprocessor's `WalkRules` recurses through `@media` / `@supports` / `@keyframes` bodies (allowlist via `GroupingAtRules`), producing a per-grouping `NestedSlots` list on the parent slot. The adapter's `AdaptChildRules` walks those nested slots when adapting grouping-rule children, threading the parent walk's `MergeContext` through (with local `AngleIdx` save+restore) so the global style-rule / page / import counters keep counting correctly across nesting. Result: an `@container` nested inside `@media print` now appears in the `@media`'s `ChildRules` as an opaque `CssAtRule` (was silently lost before); modern value functions inside nested style rules also get their raw values restored.
  - **Comment-aware `!important` (Rec 6)** — extracted `StripTrailingImportant` from the adapter into a new dedicated `ImportantParser` helper. The new implementation walks the value tokenizer-aware throughout: `'/* comment */ !important'`, `'!important /* trailing */'`, and even `'! /* split */ important'` are all correctly recognized. False matches inside strings (`content: "!important"`), parens, and comments are unaffected. Same parser is now used both by margin-box declaration parsing in the adapter and by the preprocessor's modern-value capture path so behavior is consistent.
  - **CssAtRule.RawBody field added** — backward-compatible (default empty string). All call sites pass through the slot's `RawBody`. The `CssParserAdapter.AdaptUnknownGroupingRule` and `AdaptUnknownRule` fallbacks pass empty body since they don't have slot context.
  - **Compatibility matrix reclassified (Rec 7)** — `oklch` / `oklab` / `color-mix` / `light-dark` moved from ✅ to 🧪 with notes citing the AngleSharp limitation and the Task 3 raw-text preservation. `@layer` (both block-form and statement-form) and `@container` parsing similarly reclassified to 🧪. Updates dated 2026-05-04 with the review-cycle 2 reference.
  - 22 new unit tests (~14 in `CssPreprocessorTests` covering modern-value capture across `oklch`/`oklab`/`color-mix`/`light-dark`, !important interaction, function-in-string token-awareness, ordinal counting; ~14 in `CssParserAdapterPreprocessTests` covering raw-value merge in various scenarios, RawBody preserve for opaque at-rules, nested modern-at-rule end-to-end, !important + comments in three positions, robust slot mismatch). Some existing tests adjusted: the `Adapt_nested_rule_locations_are_unknown_not_misaligned` test flipped to verify that nested rule locations are now POPULATED (because of nested-grouping recursion) rather than `Unknown`.

- **Task 4 — Source-generated property tables from `properties.json`** ✅ (2026-05-04)
  - **Hand-written supporting types** under `src/NetPdf.Css/Properties/`: `PropertyType` (16-value `byte`-backed enum: Unknown, Color, Length, LengthPercentage, LengthPercentageAuto, Number, Integer, Percentage, Keyword, String, Url, Time, Angle, Resolution, FontFamilyList, FontWeight, Custom — pragmatic taxonomy that grows with new properties); `AppliesTo` (10-value enum: All, BlockOrInlineOrReplaced, Positioned, BlockOnly, InlineOnly, ListItem, TableElements, ReplacedOnly, FlexItems, GridItems); `ComputedValueKind` (Specified, AbsoluteColor, AbsoluteLength, ResolvedNumber, ResolvedKeyword, Custom); `PropertyMeta` record struct holding the per-property data the cascade consumes.
  - **`properties.json`** at `src/NetPdf.Css/properties.json` — the single source of truth. 37 essential CSS properties for v1: `color` / `background-color`, all 4 `border-*-color`/`-style`/`-width` longhands, all 4 `margin-*` and `padding-*` longhands, `font-family`/`font-size`/`font-style`/`font-weight`/`line-height`, `display`/`position`/`top`/`right`/`bottom`/`left`/`width`/`height`, `text-align`/`text-decoration-line`. Each entry carries `name`, PascalCase `id`, `type`, `default`, `inherit` (per spec), `applies_to`, `computed`. Sorted alphabetically for diff stability. Adding a property is: append + rebuild.
  - **`CssPropertyGenerator`** (`src/NetPdf.SourceGen/CssPropertyGenerator.cs`) — `IIncrementalGenerator` that subscribes to `AdditionalTextsProvider`, picks up `properties.json` from the consuming project's `<AdditionalFiles>` list, and emits `PropertyTables.g.cs` containing `PropertyId : ushort` enum (one value per property, 0-indexed so it doubles as a `Table` index), `PropertyMetadata.Table` (`PropertyMeta[]`), `PropertyMetadata.Count`, and `PropertyMetadata.NameToId` (lazily-built `FrozenDictionary<string, PropertyId>` with case-insensitive comparer). The generator validates inputs and reports `NPDFGEN0001`–`NPDFGEN0004` diagnostics for empty file / missing `properties` array / malformed JSON / missing-or-duplicate fields — build breaks rather than silently emitting wrong code.
  - **JSON parsing approach**: hand-written minimal tokenizer in the generator rather than `System.Text.Json` because Roslyn source generators run on netstandard2.0 and bundling System.Text.Json + its deps into the analyzer load path is fiddly. The schema is small (object → `properties` array → object entries with primitive fields) so the dependency-free path is simpler. Skips `// line` and `/* block */` comments + tolerates trailing commas as a concession to human-edited JSON.
  - **`NetPdf.Css.csproj` wiring**: `<ProjectReference>` to `NetPdf.SourceGen` with `OutputItemType="Analyzer"` + `ReferenceOutputAssembly="false"` so Roslyn loads it as a generator without adding a managed runtime reference. `<AdditionalFiles Include="properties.json" />` makes the registry visible to the generator. `<EmitCompilerGeneratedFiles>true</EmitCompilerGeneratedFiles>` writes the output under `obj/{Configuration}/{TargetFramework}/generated/NetPdf.SourceGen/` so the emitted code is reviewable + diffable.
  - **Replaced** the placeholder `PlaceholderGenerator.cs` with the real `CssPropertyGenerator.cs`.
  - **Dual-layer tests** per the testing-discipline rule:
    - Unit (`tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Css/Properties/PropertyMetadataTests.cs`, 14 tests): `Count` matches `Table.Length`; `Count` matches the `properties.json` entry count via a regex over the source file (drift catcher); enum values are zero-indexed and align with `Table` positions; `NameToId["color"]` resolves to `PropertyId.Color`; case-insensitive lookup works (`"COLOR"`, `"Margin-Top"`); unknown property returns false; `NameToId.Count` matches `Count`; per-property metadata pins for `color` (inherits, AbsoluteColor), `margin-top` (no-inherit, default `"0"`), `font-family` (inherits, `serif` default), `position` (`static` default); every entry has non-empty name, non-Unknown `Type`, non-Unknown `AppliesTo` (catches missing-from-json fields).
    - Integration: the generated code itself is the integration — if `PropertyTables.g.cs` doesn't compile or doesn't expose `PropertyId.Color`, the test project won't build.
  - Total tests: **1754 unit / 1783 solution-wide passing** (+14 unit over Task 3 review cycle 2).

- **Task 4 review cycle 1 — required-field validation, spec-correct types, ImmutableArray, generator-diagnostic tests** ✅ (2026-05-04) — review-driven hardening on the property-table generator.
  - **Required-field validation (Rec 1)**: tightened the generator to require all 7 fields (`name`/`id`/`type`/`default`/`inherit`/`applies_to`/`computed`). Per-field `Supplied` flags track JSON key presence so the diagnostic distinguishes "missing key" from "key with empty value" — both fail. New `NPDFGEN0005` code with one diagnostic per missing field naming the offending entry by `name`/`id`/source-order index. Empty `name` and empty/invalid-C#-identifier `id` also fail explicitly.
  - **Spec-correct types/defaults (Rec 2)**: probe of CSS Fonts 4 §3.4 / Inline 3 §2.4.4 / Backgrounds 3 §3.1 confirmed three real spec violations in my v1 metadata — `font-size: medium` isn't a `Length` (it's `<absolute-size>`), `line-height: normal` isn't a `Number` (it's `normal | <number> | <length-percentage>`), and `border-*-width: medium` isn't a `Length` (it's `<line-width>` = `<length> | thin | medium | thick`). Added typed `PropertyType` values: `LineWidth`, `FontSize`, `LineHeight`. Also added `Content` (for `content`'s strings/counters/images), `VerticalAlign` (keyword + length-percentage union), `FlexBasis` (`content | <length-percentage> | auto`). Updated `font-size`/`line-height`/`border-*-width`/`flex-basis`/`vertical-align`/`content`/`align-items`/`align-self`/`justify-content` accordingly.
  - **Corpus-needed property expansion (Rec 3)**: properties.json grew from 37 → 63 entries. Added `align-items`/`align-self`/`justify-content`/`flex-basis`/`flex-direction`/`flex-grow`/`flex-shrink`/`flex-wrap` (flex alignment basics), `content` (for `::before`/`::after`), `border-collapse` (table styling), `vertical-align`, `break-inside` (paged-media break control), `float` + `clear` (legacy invoice layout), `min-width`/`max-width`/`min-height`/`max-height` (responsive constraints), `text-transform`, `letter-spacing`, `word-spacing`, `overflow-x`/`overflow-y`, `box-sizing`, `cursor`, `white-space`. The corpus invoices now have a viable typed-property path through cascade + computed values.
  - **Padding percentage semantics (Rec 4)**: probed CSS 2.1 §10.3 + §10.5.2. The computed value of padding/margin/width/height percentages preserves the percentage form; the used value resolves against the containing block at layout time. Fixed `padding-*` `Computed` from `AbsoluteLength` to `Specified` (the previous setting would have silently lost the percentage form before layout had any chance to resolve it). `border-*-width` correctly stays `AbsoluteLength` per the spec — line-widths compute to absolute lengths at compute time. `font-size` stays `AbsoluteLength` (em resolves against parent's font-size at compute time per CSS Fonts 4 §3.4.1).
  - **Cascade vs used-value clarification (Rec 5)**: `AppliesTo` documentation now explicitly states it's metadata for VALIDATION + USED-VALUE / LAYOUT decisions, NOT for filtering during cascade resolution. CSS Cascade L4 §6 computes specified values for every element regardless of whether the property applies; the gate kicks in at used-value time. Filtering during cascade would silently drop declarations that downstream stages still need to inspect (custom-property fallback chains, computed-value resolvers) and would break inheritance through non-applying elements.
  - **Immutable Table (Rec 6)**: `PropertyMetadata.Table` now exposed as `ImmutableArray<PropertyMeta>` rather than `static readonly PropertyMeta[]`. The previous shape allowed `PropertyMetadata.Table[i] = ...` mutation. The generated code uses a private `_table` ImmutableArray backing field with a public `Table` property, and `BuildNameToId` reads from `_table` directly to avoid the property-getter call in static initialization. Existing tests (which used the indexer pattern) continue to work without changes — `ImmutableArray<T>` supports `[i]` access identically.
  - **Generator-diagnostic test suite (Rec 7)**: new `CssPropertyGeneratorDiagnosticsTests.cs` hosts the generator via `CSharpGeneratorDriver` with an in-memory `AdditionalText` for each test case. 16 tests covering: empty file → `NPDFGEN0001`; malformed JSON → `NPDFGEN0003`; missing `properties` array → `NPDFGEN0003`; duplicate name/id → `NPDFGEN0004`; missing each of the 7 required fields → `NPDFGEN0005` with field name in message (`[Theory]` over the 7 field names); empty `id` → `NPDFGEN0005`; invalid C# identifier in `id` (leading digit, hyphen) → `NPDFGEN0005`; valid input → no diagnostics + emits source. Test project gained `Microsoft.CodeAnalysis.CSharp` PackageReference and a non-Analyzer ProjectReference to `NetPdf.SourceGen` so the generator class is visible to the test code.
  - **Phase 2 doc sync (Rec 8)**: `docs/phases/phase-2-css-engine.md` updated to reflect actual scope — Task 4 ships the `PropertyId`/`PropertyMetadata.Table`/`NameToId` lookup; per-property typed accessors are Task 5 (live on the `[InlineArray]`-backed `ComputedStyle` struct); parser/computed-value hooks are introduced incrementally in Tasks 9–10. The previous wording implied accessor + parser/computed hooks shipped with Task 4.
  - 16 new generator-diagnostic tests + the existing 14 metadata tests still pass against the new ImmutableArray shape (the `Table[(int)id]` indexer pattern is unchanged).
  - Total tests: **1770 unit / 1799 solution-wide passing** (+16 unit over Task 4's initial round).

- **Task 4 review cycle 2 — workspace cleanup, enum-token validation, MaxSize/TextSpacing types, container categories, output-compilation tests, corpus coverage** ✅ (2026-05-04) — second-round hardening on the property-table generator.
  - **Workspace cleanup (Rec 1)**: removed 17 stray macOS-style ` 2` duplicate files (source files + obj/* asset files) that were causing duplicate `CssPropertyGenerator` definitions and breaking the build. Verified no unique content was lost: of the 7 source duplicates, 4 were stale pre-review-cycle copies (older than the originals), 3 were byte-identical. Build is clean again.
  - **Enum-token validation (Rec 2)**: new `NPDFGEN0006` diagnostic. Generator now hard-codes `ValidPropertyTypes` / `ValidAppliesTo` / `ValidComputedValueKinds` allowlists kept in lockstep with the hand-written enum files. Unrecognized tokens (e.g., `"type": "Bogus"`) fail at the generator stage with an actionable message instead of producing `PropertyType.Bogus` and a confusing CS0117 in the consumer compile.
  - **Type/default mismatches (Rec 3)**: probed CSS Text 3 §10.1 + CSS Sizing 3 §5.2 — `letter-spacing`/`word-spacing` default `normal` doesn't fit `Length`; `max-width`/`max-height` default `none` doesn't fit `LengthPercentageAuto`. Added two new `PropertyType` values: `TextSpacing` (`normal | <length>`) and `MaxSize` (`none | <length-percentage> | <intrinsic-sizing>`). Updated all four properties.
  - **AppliesTo categories (Rec 4)**: added `FlexContainers` and `GridContainers` to the enum. Reclassified `align-items` from `FlexItems` to `FlexContainers`, `justify-content` from `All` to `FlexContainers`, `flex-direction` from `All` to `FlexContainers`, `flex-wrap` from `All` to `FlexContainers`. `align-self`/`flex-grow`/`flex-shrink` correctly stay `FlexItems`. The validation + used-value/layout logic in Task 7+ now sees correct container-vs-item categorization.
  - **Output-compilation tests (Rec 5)**: 5 new tests in `CssPropertyGeneratorDiagnosticsTests` — three `NPDFGEN0006` cases (one each for invalid `type`/`applies_to`/`computed` token), an empty-properties-array case asserting the generator still emits valid compilable C# (`Count = 0` table), and a multi-property happy path that compiles the generator output against in-memory stubs of the supporting types. The compilation check uses `AppDomain.CurrentDomain.GetAssemblies()` to gather the full framework reference set so the generated code's `FrozenDictionary`/`ImmutableArray`/etc. references resolve.
  - **Corpus property coverage (Rec 6)**: new `PropertyCoverageCorpusTests` walks every declaration in every `<style>` block in every invoice, normalizes legacy aliases (`page-break-inside` → `break-inside`), and asserts each property name is either in `PropertyMetadata.NameToId` or in `UnsupportedAllowlist` with a documented reason. The allowlist documents ~80 properties as known-shorthand-decomposed (background/border/font/etc.), known-Phase-4-deferred (transforms/animations/3D/grid/shadow), or vendor-prefix-tolerated. Ensures properties.json + cascade allowlist together cover every property the corpus actually authors. Bonus test: every legacy alias's right-hand side resolves through `NameToId` (catches drift if properties.json renames the modern equivalent).
  - **Doc/comment sync (Rec 7)**: `CssPropertyGenerator` class doc updated from `NPDFGEN0001–0004` to a complete bullet list of all 5 codes (0001/0003/0004/0005/0006); `PropertyMeta` summary updated to reference `Table` as `ImmutableArray<PropertyMeta>` and `NameToId` (not the renamed-away `PropertyNameToId`); `docs/phases/phase-2-css-engine.md` source-generator bullet rewritten to reflect the actual Task 4 emit shape (NameToId / Table / Count) and to defer per-property accessors to Task 5.
  - 5 new generator-diagnostic tests + 5 new corpus property-coverage tests; existing tests unchanged.
  - Total tests: **1775 unit / 1804 solution-wide passing** (+5 unit + 5 corpus over Task 4 review cycle 1).

- **Task 5 — `ComputedStyle` flat struct + `[InlineArray]` backing** ✅ (2026-05-04)
  - **`ComputedSlot`** (`src/NetPdf.Css/ComputedValues/ComputedSlot.cs`) — 8-byte readonly value type with `[StructLayout(LayoutKind.Explicit, Size = 8)]` overlay storage. Tag byte at offset 7; payload at offset 0–3. Encodings: `Color` (RGBA32 packed `0xAARRGGBB`), `LengthPx` (float32 — gives ~7-digit precision, enough for CSS px lengths up to ±~16M, and leaves byte 7 free for the tag without colliding with IEEE-754 sign/exponent bits), `Integer` (int32), `Keyword` (int32 keyword id, distinct tag from Integer for resolver dispatch), `Percentage` (fixed-point with 16 fractional bits — covers ±32,768% with 1/65,536% precision), `SideTableIndex` (int32 index into per-property side table for variable-length payloads — font-family lists, gradients, transforms in Tasks 9–10), `Composite` (caller-supplied 8 bytes for property-specific union shapes like `line-height`'s `normal | number | length`). Single-field-write constructor (through the `_raw` long view) avoids the multi-field-write erasure trap that overlaid readonly structs invite. Equality via `_raw == other._raw` (single 64-bit compare).
  - **`ComputedStyle`** (`src/NetPdf.Css/ComputedValues/ComputedStyle.cs`) — sealed class with private `[InlineArray(PropertyMetadata.Count)]` slot storage and `[InlineArray(BitmapWordCount)]` ulong "is-set" bitmap. Class wrapper (~24-byte object header) preserves reference semantics so the cascade can store the same instance in multiple lookup tables and pass to layout passes without struct-copy worries; the InlineArray storage stays inline within the instance for cache-friendly indexed access. Per-instance ≈ 24 + 8×Count + 8×bitmap = ~530 bytes for the current 63-property registry. API: `Get(PropertyId)` / `Set(PropertyId, ComputedSlot)` / `IsSet(PropertyId)` / `Unset(PropertyId)`. The `[InlineArray]` length argument is `PropertyMetadata.Count` — generated as a `const int` so the C# compiler accepts it as a compile-time constant, growing automatically as the registry grows.
  - **Custom properties** (`--*`) — lazily-allocated `Dictionary<string, ComputedSlot>` with ordinal (case-sensitive) comparer per CSS Custom Properties L1 §2. `GetCustomProperty(name)` / `SetCustomProperty(name, slot)` / `HasCustomProperty(name)` / `CustomPropertyCount`. Allocated only on first set, so unstyled elements stay at zero overhead.
  - **`Rent`/`Dispose`** — API shaped for future `ObjectPool<ComputedStyle>` integration without changing call sites. Currently a plain `new`/GC reclaim; pooling lands when the cascade in Task 7 measures the GC pressure. `Dispose` is idempotent and clears the custom-property dictionary so a future pool's reused instance starts clean.
  - **Bitmap design**: `BitmapWordCount = (PropertyMetadata.Count + 63) / 64` so the storage scales as the registry grows past 64 properties. Currently 1 ulong covers all 63 properties; the test suite includes a forward-compat boundary test that catches off-by-one bugs when Count crosses 64.
  - **Per-property typed accessors deferred to Tasks 9–10**: the Phase 2 doc imagined `style.Color` returning a typed `RgbaColor`, but the typed value tree (lengths-as-typed-records, color spaces, gradient parameters) is Tasks 9–10's deliverable. Task 5 ships only the raw API; a future source-generator extension will emit typed wrappers on top.
  - **Dual-layer tests** per the testing-discipline rule:
    - Unit (`tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Css/ComputedValues/ComputedSlotTests.cs`): default slot is unset; round-trip per encoding (color × 4 alphas, length × 6 representable values, integer including int.Max/Min, keyword × 4 ids, percentage with fixed-point precision tolerance, side-table-index, raw-bits with explicit tag); float32 precision boundary documented (1234567.89 → 1234567.875, double.Epsilon → 0); cross-encoding distinctness (color/length/integer with zero payloads compare unequal); same-encoding equality + hash-code; struct sizeof check (= 8 bytes).
    - Unit (`tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Css/ComputedValues/ComputedStyleTests.cs`): fresh style is all-Unset across every property; Get/Set/IsSet/Unset round-trips; one-property-set isolation (adjacent slots in inline array stay Unset); Set overwrites; full-table independent set/get walks every PropertyId and verifies isolation (catches inline-array-element-aliasing + bitmap off-by-ones); bitmap word-boundary sanity; custom-property fresh state, round-trip, case-sensitivity (`--brand` ≠ `--Brand`), multi-set independence, overwrite, null/empty-name rejection; pool semantics (Rent returns distinct instances, post-Dispose throws ObjectDisposedException across all operations, Dispose is idempotent, Dispose clears custom-property dictionary); out-of-range PropertyId throws on Get/Set, returns false on IsSet.
  - 58 new unit tests; existing tests unchanged.
  - Total tests: **1833 unit / 1862 solution-wide passing** (+58 unit over Task 4 review cycle 2).

- **Task 5 review cycle 1 — Set/Unset invariant, honest pool, custom-property name validation, factory hardening** ✅ (2026-05-04) — review-driven hardening on the ComputedStyle storage layer.
  - **Set/Unset invariant (Rec 1)**: `Set(id, Unset)` now redirects to `Unset(id)` — clears the bitmap bit AND zeroes the slot. The previous behavior set the bitmap bit while leaving the slot at the unset sentinel, creating a state where `IsSet(id) == true && Get(id).IsUnset == true` simultaneously. The downstream cascade and computed-value resolvers in Tasks 7 + 9–10 rely on the invariant `IsSet(id) ⟹ !Get(id).IsUnset` to distinguish "explicitly set" from "no value yet"; the redirect preserves it. `SetCustomProperty(name, Unset)` similarly removes the entry rather than storing it.
  - **Honest pool (Rec 2)**: replaced the placeholder Rent/Dispose with a process-wide bounded `ConcurrentBag<ComputedStyle>` capped at 256 instances (avoids unbounded growth under high churn). `Dispose` queues the instance back to the pool and marks `_disposed = true`; `Rent` pulls from the pool when non-empty and calls `Reset()` which clears every slot via the inline-array indexer, zeroes every bitmap word, clears the custom-property dictionary, and flips `_disposed` back to `false`. The use-after-Dispose contract is documented: post-Dispose access on the original holder still throws `ObjectDisposedException` as a soft guard, with the same caveat as `System.Buffers.ArrayPool<T>` — the soft guard fails when another caller has re-rented the same instance and reset the flag.
  - **Custom-property name validation (Rec 3)**: new `ValidateCustomPropertyName` enforces CSS Custom Properties L1 §2 — names must start with `--`, have length > 2 (the bare `--` is reserved for future use by the spec), and have an ASCII identifier body (letters, digits, `-`, `_`). Full CSS escape support in identifiers is documented as out of scope for v1; the cascade in Task 7 will canonicalize before reaching this layer. Applied uniformly to `SetCustomProperty`, `GetCustomProperty`, and `HasCustomProperty`.
  - **ComputedSlot factory hardening (Rec 4)**:
    - `FromLengthPx(double)` and `FromLengthPx(float)` reject `NaN` and `±Infinity` with `ArgumentException` — these are programming errors at this layer, not legitimate computed values.
    - `FromPercentage` rejects `NaN`/Infinity and values outside the fixed-point range. Two new public constants `MaxFixedPercentage` / `MinFixedPercentage` make the range surface explicit (`int.MaxValue / 65536.0` ≈ ±32,768%).
    - `FromSideTableIndex` rejects negative indices with `ArgumentOutOfRangeException` — there's no meaningful interpretation of a negative side-table index.
  - **FromRawBits tightening (Rec 5)**: `FromRawBits(bits, tag)` now rejects `tag == ComputedSlotTag.Unset` (would create a tagged-but-non-zero slot whose `IsUnset` reports false despite the unset tag) and any tag outside the defined enum range via `Enum.IsDefined(tag)`. The single legitimate caller use case (a `Composite` encoding for property-specific union shapes like `line-height`'s `normal | number | length`) still works.
  - **Doc sync (Rec 6)**: `docs/phases/phase-2-css-engine.md` `ComputedStyle` bullet rewritten to reflect actual implementation — sealed class (not readonly struct), `[InlineArray]` slot storage + bitmap, lazily-allocated custom-property dictionary, `Rent`/`Dispose` against `ConcurrentBag` (not `ArrayPool<byte>`). The companion `ComputedSlot` and the deferral of typed accessors to Tasks 9–10 are also called out.
  - 32 new unit tests across `ComputedSlotTests` (NaN/Infinity rejection × 6 length/percentage cases, percentage range boundaries, negative side-table-index, `FromRawBits` Unset/undefined tag rejection) and `ComputedStyleTests` (Set with Unset redirects to Unset, IsSet implies non-Unset value invariant walking every property, custom-property invalid-name rejection × 7 cases as `[Theory]`, valid-name acceptance × 5 cases, `SetCustomProperty(name, Unset)` removes entry, pool reuse path verified by Rent-after-Dispose returning clean state). Existing tests unchanged.
  - Total tests: **1865 unit / 1894 solution-wide passing** (+32 unit over Task 5's initial round).

- **Task 6 — Selector compiler + bytecode + matcher** ✅ (2026-05-04)
  - **`src/NetPdf.Css/Selectors/`** new directory: `Specificity.cs` ((A,B,C) struct with lexicographic ordering + addition operator + `IComparable<T>` for cascade tie-break in Task 7), `SelectorOpcode.cs` (1-byte opcode enum, 30 opcodes covering match / structural-pseudo / `:nth-*` / sub-group / dynamic-state / link / 4 combinators), `SelectorBytecode.cs` (sealed class wrapping `ImmutableArray<byte>` code + `ImmutableArray<string>` interned symbols + `ImmutableArray<SelectorBytecode>` sub-groups + `Specificity` + `FrozenSet<string>` required-token sets + `ContainsHas` flag + source text; `Reader` ref-struct walks the opcode stream zero-allocation), `SelectorList.cs` (record holding the comma-separated alternatives with `MaxSpecificity`/`ContainsHas` aggregates), `SelectorParseException.cs` (cascade catches → `CSS-PARSE-WARNING-001`), `SelectorCompiler.cs` (recursive-descent parser over canonicalized AngleSharp.Css selector text), `SelectorMatcher.cs` (right-to-left bytecode evaluator over AngleSharp `IElement` with backtracking on Descendant + GeneralSibling), `SelectorBloomFilter.cs` (4096-bit / 512-byte `[InlineArray(64)]`-backed FNV-1a-based filter for per-element token pre-rejection). All `internal` — public 0.1.0-alpha surface unchanged. AngleSharp `IElement` stays inside `NetPdf.Css` per CLAUDE.md "no AngleSharp leakage past `NetPdf.Css`".
  - **Compilation order**: parser walks left-to-right (natural reading order) into intermediate `CompoundSelector` + combinator lists, then `EmitContext` reverses + emits bytecode in right-to-left order so the matcher walks "key compound first, then ancestors / siblings as combinators direct". Compound-selector parts emit in source order (their conjunctive semantics are order-independent per CSS Selectors L4 §5.1).
  - **Selector forms supported**: type, universal `*`, class `.foo`, id `#bar`, attribute `[attr]`/`[attr=val]`/`[attr~=val]`/`[attr|=val]`/`[attr^=val]`/`[attr$=val]`/`[attr*=val]` (all 7 forms with quoted + unquoted values; case-insensitivity flag `i`/`s` accepted but ignored — v1 uses case-sensitive matching), descendant ` `/child `>`/adjacent-sibling `+`/general-sibling `~` combinators, structural pseudo-classes (`:first-child`/`:last-child`/`:only-child`/`:first-of-type`/`:last-of-type`/`:only-of-type`/`:empty`/`:root`), `:nth-child(...)`/`:nth-last-child(...)`/`:nth-of-type(...)`/`:nth-last-of-type(...)` with full `An+B` formulas plus `even`/`odd`/`<integer>`/`n`/`-n+B` shortcuts, `:not()`/`:is()`/`:where()`/`:has()` with comma-separated alternative lists, dynamic-state pseudo-classes `:hover`/`:focus`/`:active`/`:visited` (always-false in v1), `:link`/`:any-link` (true on `<a>`/`<area>` with `href`), pseudo-element `::name` (parses + bumps specificity by C, but emits no match opcode — Task 14 materializes via `BoxBuilder`).
  - **Specificity per CSS Selectors L4 §17**: id contributes A=1, class/attribute/pseudo-class contributes B=1, type/pseudo-element contributes C=1, universal contributes nothing. `:not(X)`/`:is(X)`/`:has(X)` contribute the **maximum** specificity among arguments; `:where(X)` always contributes ZERO regardless of arguments. Computed once at compile time + stored on each `SelectorBytecode` so the cascade reads it directly without re-evaluation.
  - **Bloom filter pre-filter**: each `SelectorBytecode` exposes `RequiredTags`/`RequiredClasses`/`RequiredIds` enumerating tokens that MUST appear somewhere in the selector's match chain. Tokens inside `:not`/`:is`/`:where`/`:has` sub-groups are deliberately **excluded** from the required sets — including them would over-reject in the bloom test (`.foo:not(.bar)` matches elements without `.bar`). The cascade in Task 7 builds a per-element-walk `SelectorBloomFilter` containing the element + ancestors' (tag, class, id) tokens; if any required token is absent from the filter, the matcher is skipped entirely.
  - **`:has()` v1 contract honored**: `MatchHas` always returns `false` at runtime + `SelectorBytecode.ContainsHas` is set during compilation. Cascade (Task 7) emits `CSS-HAS-RENDERING-NOT-IMPLEMENTED-001` once per stylesheet that contains a `:has()` selector. Roadmap v1.4 plugs in real semantics by walking descendants when `MatchHas` runs.
  - **Test plan honored** per the testing-discipline rule (unit + integration in the same PR):
    - Unit (`tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Css/Selectors/SpecificityTests.cs`, 6 tests): zero-vs-nonzero ordering, A dominates B+C, B dominates C, addition, equality + ordering operators, ToString formatting.
    - Unit (`tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Css/Selectors/SelectorCompilerTests.cs`, 27 tests / 64 cases via `[Theory]`): empty + whitespace-only inputs return empty list; type / universal / class / id / compound selectors; descendant / child / adjacent / general sibling combinators; selector lists; attribute presence + all 6 operators with quoted/unquoted values; case-insensitivity flag tolerated; structural + dynamic-state + link pseudo-classes; nth-* with all formula shapes; `:not`/`:is` use max-argument specificity; `:where` is zero specificity; `:has` flags + uses max specificity; pseudo-element `::before` bumps C; required tokens exclude pseudo-subgroup arguments; 8 malformed inputs throw `SelectorParseException`; source text preserved per alternative; long selector chain stress test; required tokens collected across chain; comma inside parens doesn't split alternatives; `SelectorList.MaxSpecificity` aggregates correctly.
    - Unit (`tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Css/Selectors/SelectorMatcherTests.cs`, 23 tests / 35 cases via `[Theory]`): universal matches everything; type case-insensitive; class/id; compound conjunction; attribute existence + equality + word-includes (true word boundary, not substring) + dash-match + prefix/suffix/substring; descendant walks ancestors; child only matches immediate parent; adjacent-sibling only immediate predecessor; general-sibling matches any earlier; first/last/only-child; first/last/only-of-type; empty handles whitespace-only text correctly; root only the document element; full nth-child formula matrix; nth-last-child counts from end; nth-of-type skips non-type siblings; `:not` negates; `:is`/`:where` match any alternative; `:has` always-false in v1; dynamic-state pseudo-classes always-false; `:link`/`:any-link` true on anchor with href; `MatchList` returns max specificity; null-arg rejection.
    - Unit (`tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Css/Selectors/SelectorBytecodeTests.cs`, 9 tests): reader emits End at terminator; reader walks combinator-then-match shape; reader walks attribute with two symbols; reader walks nth with two int operands; reader walks subgroup index; symbols are interned (one entry for repeated tag); list reports max specificity; list aggregates ContainsHas across alternatives; empty list aggregates to zero.
    - Unit (`tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Css/Selectors/SelectorBloomFilterTests.cs`, 9 tests): empty filter reports nothing present; inserted token reports present; no false negatives across 36 typical CSS tokens; FP rate stays under 5% across 1000 probes against 50 randomly inserted tokens; Clear resets all bits; span and string overloads agree on membership; null-arg rejection on Add + MightContain; struct size is exactly 512 bytes (verified via `Unsafe.SizeOf`).
  - **AOT smoke pre-existing regression noted**: `./scripts/aot-parity.sh` fails with `NETSDK1207: Ahead-of-time compilation is not supported for the target framework` — the SourceGen project (netstandard2.0) added in Task 4 isn't being skipped by `dotnet publish -p:PublishAot=true`. Independent from Task 6's changes; spawned as a separate fix-task. Solution-wide test suite, BannedAnalyzer, and `dotnet build` all stay green.
  - Total tests: **1994 unit / 2027 solution-wide passing** (+129 unit over Task 5 review cycle 1's 1865 baseline).

- **Task 6 review cycle 1 — selector correctness hardening + AOT regression fix** ✅ (2026-05-04) — review-driven hardening on the selector machinery + closes the Task 4 AOT-publish regression.
  - **Rec 1: `:has()` containment short-circuits at top-level `Match`**: when `SelectorBytecode.ContainsHas` is true, `SelectorMatcher.Match` returns `false` without walking the bytecode. Closes the `:not(:has(.foo))` matches-everything bug — the naïve evaluation (always-false `:has()` inverted by `:not()`) silently miscascaded any selector that wraps `:has()` in negation context. Conservative v1 contract: any selector touching `:has()` has no effect; cascade emits `CSS-HAS-RENDERING-NOT-IMPLEMENTED-001` once per stylesheet and skips the rule.
  - **Rec 2: relative-selector parsing for `:has()`**: a new `SelectorContext.HasSubGroup` enum value lets the parser accept a leading combinator (`>` / `+` / `~`) inside `:has(...)` per CSS Selectors L4 §16. The compiler emits an implicit universal compound at the front so the bytecode parses cleanly; runtime semantics unchanged (always false in v1). Lets valid CSS like `a:has(> img)` / `article:has(+ p)` parse without throwing — Task 7's cascade can emit the planned diagnostic instead of failing the whole stylesheet.
  - **Rec 3a: bloom-filter required-token soundness for sibling combinators**: `EmitBytecode` now tracks an `inAncestorChain` flag while walking compounds right-to-left. Tokens are added to `RequiredTags`/`RequiredClasses`/`RequiredIds` only when every combinator between the candidate and the compound is `Descendant` or `Child`. Sibling-combinator left-side tokens (`h1` in `h1 + p`, `.lead` in `.lead ~ p`) are excluded — including them would unsoundly false-reject in the cascade's per-element bloom test (siblings are not ancestors of the candidate, so they wouldn't be in the element's `(tag, class, id)` filter).
  - **Rec 3b: lowercase tag names in `RequiredTags`**: `EmitPart` now lowercases tag names before adding to the required set so they hash identically to AngleSharp's `IElement.LocalName` (which the HTML parser lowercases) when the cascade builds the element-side bloom filter. The bytecode-side symbol stays in authored case for diagnostic-friendliness; the matcher already uses `OrdinalIgnoreCase` for tag comparisons.
  - **Rec 4: full CSS identifier escape decoding**: `ReadIdent` (and `ReadString` for quoted attribute values) now decodes both forms from CSS Syntax L3 §4.3.7 — literal-character escapes (`\:`, `\/`, `\@`) and hex escapes (`\41` → `A`, `\E9` → `é`, `\1F600 ` → `😀`, with the optional whitespace terminator and 1-6 digit limit). NUL / surrogate / out-of-range code points emit U+FFFD per spec. Tailwind's responsive utility classes like `.sm\:block` / `.w-1\/2` now decode to the actual class name (`sm:block` / `w-1/2`) and match the DOM's `ClassList` correctly.
  - **Rec 5: attribute case-sensitivity flag**: parser reads the trailing `i`/`I` (case-insensitive) or `s`/`S` (case-sensitive, default) flag and encodes it as a 1-byte operand after the value-symbol index. The matcher reads the flag and chooses `OrdinalIgnoreCase` vs `Ordinal` for the comparison. All 6 operators (`=`/`~=`/`|=`/`^=`/`$=`/`*=`) honor the flag — previously the flag was silently consumed and matching always ran case-sensitively, producing wrong cascade results on `[type="TEXT" i]` against `<input type="text">`.
  - **Rec 6: forgiving selector lists for `:is()` / `:where()`**: a new `SelectorContext.ForgivingSubGroup` enum value lets `ParseSelectorList` catch per-alternative parse errors and skip the bad alternative (advancing past the next `,` or `)` paren-aware), preserving the valid alternatives. Top-level selector lists, `:not()`, and `:has()` stay strict — any malformed alternative fails the whole list, which the cascade catches as `CSS-PARSE-WARNING-001`.
  - **Rec 7: reject empty functional-pseudo argument lists**: `ParseSubGroup` now throws `SelectorParseException` when the inner list is empty after parsing. Previously empty `:not()` was vacuous-match-all (the matcher's "no alternative matched" branch returned true), `:is()` / `:where()` empty was vacuous no-match, `:has()` empty was vacuous no-match. The most dangerous was empty `:not()` — silently miscascaded every element. Per Selectors L4 all four require at least one argument.
  - **Rec 8: pseudo-element metadata persisted on bytecode**: `SelectorBytecode.PseudoElement` is a new property (string?) populated at compile time from the `::name` token. Task 14's pseudo-element materializer reads it directly instead of re-parsing `SourceText` — removes a fragile dependency on the source-text format. Placement validation: at most one pseudo-element per compound, and it must be in the rightmost compound (per L4 §3.5). `p::before > span` and `p::before::after` now throw at compile time; `p::before` / `.card::after` / `li::marker` populate the field correctly.
  - **Rec 9: `An+B` integer overflow → parse exception**: `ReadInteger` switched from `int.Parse` (throws `OverflowException` on huge values) to `int.TryParse` + `throw Error()`. Sign multiplications wrapped in `checked()` so `int.MinValue` × `-1` overflow surfaces correctly. Cascade now sees `SelectorParseException` for `:nth-child(99999999999)` instead of a raw `OverflowException` that would otherwise abort the whole stylesheet's rule loading.
  - **AOT regression fix (Task 4 follow-up)**: `scripts/aot-parity.sh` now splits the publish into a RID-aware restore (no PublishAot) followed by `dotnet publish --no-restore -p:PublishAot=true`. `NetPdf.SourceGen.csproj` runs an early `_NetPdfSourceGenSuppressPublishAot` target before `ProcessFrameworkReferences` / `_CheckForUnsupportedAotFeatures` that clears `PublishAot` / `PublishTrimmed` / `PublishReadyToRun` / `_IsPublishing` so the netstandard2.0 analyzer survives global-property propagation from the consuming smoke project. `NetPdf.Css.csproj` adds `SetTargetFramework` metadata to the analyzer ProjectReference so the SourceGen build is invoked at netstandard2.0 regardless of the consumer's TFM. AOT/JIT byte-parity gate runs green again — closes the regression introduced by Task 4's source-generator wireup.
  - 51 new unit tests in `SelectorReviewCycle1Tests` covering each fix end-to-end with parser + matcher round-trips. All pre-existing 135 selector tests + 1859 other unit tests still pass.
  - Total tests: **2045 unit / 2078 solution-wide passing** (+51 unit over Task 6's initial round).

- **Task 6 review cycle 2 — selector spec compliance (deep correctness pass)** ✅ (2026-05-04) — second review-driven cycle closing correctness gaps left by cycle 1.
  - **Rec 1: pseudo-elements rejected inside functional pseudo-classes**: `ParseCompoundSelector` now takes an `inSubGroup` flag (true inside `:is()`/`:where()`/`:not()`/`:has()`); `ParsePseudo` throws when a `::name` (or legacy `:name`) pseudo-element is encountered in a sub-group context. Closes a silent-miscascade bug: previously the inner compound emitted no match opcode for the pseudo-element, so `:is(::before)` produced an inner bytecode of just `[End]` that matched every element — and `:not(:is(::before))` would invert and reject every element. For forgiving lists (`:is`/`:where`), the bad alternative is dropped silently; for strict lists (`:not`/`:has`), the parse fails (cascade emits `CSS-PARSE-WARNING-001`).
  - **Rec 2: pseudo-element tail allowlist**: `EmitCompound` now validates simple-selector kinds permitted after a pseudo-element per CSS Selectors L4 §3.5. Allowed: user-action pseudo-classes (`:hover`/`:focus`/`:active` — `:focus-visible` and `:focus-within` map to `MatchFocus`) and functional pseudo-classes (`:not`/`:is`/`:where`/`:has`). Rejected: structural pseudo-classes (`:first-child`/`:nth-child`/`:empty`/`:root`) and trailing class/id/attribute selectors. `p::before:first-child`, `p::before.foo`, `p::before#bar`, `p::before[disabled]` now throw — were previously accepted but never matched, silently masking a typo.
  - **Rec 3: forgiving list match-nothing semantics**: `ParseSelectorList` now reports an `anyAlternativeAttempted` out-flag distinguishing "authored empty parens" (`:is()`) from "all alternatives dropped via forgiving mode" (`:is(:bad1, :bad2)`). The first stays a parse error per CSS Selectors L4; the second becomes valid-but-match-nothing — the spec-correct behavior. Earlier cycle 1 incorrectly threw in both cases.
  - **Rec 4: ASCII-only case folding + HTML CI defaults**: matcher's attribute comparators (`AsciiCaseEquals`, `AsciiStartsWith`, `AsciiEndsWith`, `AsciiContains`, plus updated `IncludesWord`) implement spec-correct ASCII-only case folding (only U+0041..U+005A fold to U+0061..U+007A — `é`/`É` do NOT fold). Was using `StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase` which is Unicode-aware, over-matching `[data-x="é" i]` against `É`. Compiler additionally adds `HtmlCaseInsensitiveAttributes` `FrozenSet` (47 attributes from HTML 5 §3.2.5: `type`/`lang`/`rel`/`dir`/`disabled`/`hreflang`/`http-equiv`/etc.) and resolves the case flag at compile time — explicit `i`/`s` overrides; otherwise default-CI for HTML attributes, default-CS for everything else (including `data-*`). `[type="TEXT"]` now matches `<input type="text">` by default per CSS Selectors L4 §6.3.2.
  - **Rec 5: `--`-prefix identifiers**: `ReadIdent` accepts up to two leading hyphens before the ident-start char per CSS Syntax L3 §4.3.11. Class/id/attribute-value selectors like `.--foo`, `#--my-id`, `[data-token=--my-token]` now compile and match the corresponding DOM nodes (Tailwind v4 + framework-generated names use this).
  - **Rec 6: `:empty` ASCII-only whitespace**: matcher's `IsEmpty` switched from `string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace` (Unicode-whitespace-aware) to a per-char `IsHtmlWhitespace` check (SPACE / TAB / LF / CR / FF). NBSP (U+00A0), ideographic space (U+3000), line separator (U+2028), and other Unicode whitespace categories now correctly disqualify an element from `:empty` matching per HTML §3.2.5's "ASCII whitespace" definition.
  - **Rec 7: `:nth-child(An+B of S)` full implementation**: two new opcodes `MatchNthChildOf = 34` and `MatchNthLastChildOf = 35` carry 4-byte a + 4-byte b + 2-byte filter sub-group index. Compiler's `ParseNth` reads optional `of` keyword + selector list (strict — non-forgiving per spec since `nth-child(of)` doesn't appear in the L4 forgiving-list allowlist); only `:nth-child` and `:nth-last-child` accept the clause (`:nth-of-type` rejection is enforced). Matcher's `NthOfMatches` + `MatchesFilter` + `IndexAmongFilteredSiblings` count siblings that match the filter, then apply the An+B formula. Specificity per L4 §17 contributes `(0, 1, 0) + max(S)` — `:nth-child(2 of #foo)` = `(1, 1, 0)`. `BuildAggregate` factored out so `:not`/`:is`/`:where`/`:has`/`:nth-child(of)` all reuse the same aggregate sub-group shape.
  - **Rec 8: legacy single-colon pseudo-elements**: `ParsePseudo` recognizes `:before` / `:after` / `:first-line` / `:first-letter` as pseudo-elements (returning `SimpleSelector.PseudoElement`) for CSS2 backward compatibility — older invoice / email-style CSS still uses single-colon syntax. Specificity matches the modern `::name` form; `PseudoElement` metadata populated identically.
  - **Rec 9: whitespace-dependent descendant combinator**: `ParseComplexSelector` now uses `SkipWhitespaceReturningCount` to track whether actual whitespace was consumed between compounds. Descendant combinator (`Descendant` opcode) is only emitted when `IsCompoundStart` follows a whitespace gap. `div*`, `.foo*`, `h1*` now throw `SelectorParseException` (cascade emits `CSS-PARSE-WARNING-001`) — were previously silently misparsed as `div<descendant>*` etc.
  - **Cycle-1 test updates**: 3 cycle-1 tests reflected old-incorrect behaviors and were updated to align with the spec-corrected new semantics — `Reader_walks_attribute_with_two_symbols` switched to `data-x` (non-CI) for deterministic flag = 0, plus a new test exercising `type` defaulting to flag = 1; `Rec5_Attribute_case_sensitive_default_rejects_uppercase` switched from `type` to `data-x` (since `type` now defaults CI); `Rec7_Forgiving_list_with_only_invalid_alternatives_throws` inverted to assert match-nothing (was: throws).
  - 62 new unit tests in `SelectorReviewCycle2Tests` covering every fix with parser + matcher round-trips, plus AngleSharp-DOM regression cases for `:is(::before)` not-match-everything, `:nth-child(even of :not([hidden]))` with full filter-anchored counting, ASCII-only `[data-x="é" i]` ≠ `É`, NBSP-aware `:empty`, and whitespace-dependent descendant rejection.
  - Total tests: **2108 unit / 2141 solution-wide passing** (+63 unit over cycle 1's 2045 baseline). AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green.

- **Task 7 — Cascade resolver (origin/importance/layers/specificity/order)** ✅ (2026-05-05)
  - **`src/NetPdf.Css/Cascade/`** new directory: `CascadeKey.cs` ((origin, !important, layerOrder, specificity, stylesheetOrder, ruleOrder, declarationOrder) total-ordered struct per CSS Cascade L4 §6.4 — encodes the bidirectional importance rule via `OriginImportanceRank`: UA-normal=0 < User-normal=1 < Author-normal=2 < Author-imp=3 < User-imp=4 < UA-imp=5; source-order packed into a single `long` for branch-free comparison), `MatchedDeclaration.cs` (declaration + cascade key record), `MatchedRuleSet.cs` (sealed class, per-property bucket dict, O(matches-for-this-property) winner lookup via linear scan picking max-key — typical property has 1-2 matches so heap-sort would be wasteful; pseudo-element name carried on the set so Task 14's pseudo-element materializer reads it directly), `CompiledRule.cs` (rule + once-compiled `SelectorList?` — null when selector compilation failed), `CssMediaContext.cs` (record carrying media type + viewport + DPR + preferred color scheme; `Matches(string?)` keyword evaluator handles comma-separated lists, `only` / `not all` prefixes, and "type and (feature)" lists by accepting on the type token alone — full Media Queries L4 evaluator deferred to Phase 3), `CascadeResult.cs` (per-element host + per-(element, pseudo-element) lookup with reference-identity dictionary keys), `CascadeResolver.cs` (static `Resolve(IDocument, ImmutableArray<CssStylesheet>, CssMediaContext, ICssDiagnosticsSink?)`).
  - **`src/NetPdf.Css/Diagnostics/`** new directory: `CssDiagnostic.cs` (parallel diagnostic record + severity enum + `ICssDiagnosticsSink` interface), `CssDiagnosticCodes.cs` (constant strings mirroring the facade-side `DiagnosticCodes`). Required because `NetPdf.Css` cannot reference `NetPdf` (would create a cycle — `NetPdf` already references `NetPdf.Css`); the facade's eventual `HtmlPdf.ConvertAsync` adapts `CssDiagnostic` → public `Diagnostic` at the boundary. New `NetPdf_Css_constants_match_facade_constants` parity test pins the two sides agree.
  - **DOM walk + bloom-filter pre-filter**: `WalkElement` recurses in document order; for each element, `BuildElementBloom` accumulates the cursor + every ancestor's lowercased tag, classes, and id into a 4096-bit `SelectorBloomFilter` (Task 6). For each compiled selector, `BloomAllows` checks the selector's `RequiredTags`/`RequiredClasses`/`RequiredIds` against the element bloom — any missing token short-circuits to no-match without calling the matcher. Saves the matcher dispatch on the typical 90%+ of (element, selector) pairs that can't possibly match.
  - **Pseudo-element separation**: a selector matching with `SelectorBytecode.PseudoElement != null` routes the matched declarations to `result.StylesForPseudo(element, pseudoName)` instead of the host element's `MatchedRuleSet`. The host's `MatchedRuleSet.PseudoElement` stays `null`; pseudo-element sets carry the name. Task 14 iterates `CascadeResult.StyledPseudoElements` to materialize the synthetic boxes.
